RKNĀ_1.4–1.9	namaḥ tārāyai yasmin avajñā naraka prasūtiḥ bhaktiḥ ca sarva abhimata pradāyinī avyāhatam yaḥ jagat eka bandhuḥ sa jñāyate sarva vid atra nirmalam iha hi dharma jñāt aparam anavaśeṣa jñam anicchan api kumārilaḥ dharma jñaḥ eva kevale pratiṣiddhe vedam upādeyam abhimanyamānaḥ paṭhati dharma jña tva niṣedhaḥ tu kevalaḥ atra upayujyate sarvam anyat vijānan tu puruṣaḥ kena vāryate iti 
RKNĀ_1.13–1.20	 tat ayam ācāryaḥ api sarva sarvajña caraṇa reṇu sanātham yāvat ākāśam jagat icchan api tribhuvana cūḍāmaṇī bhūta saparikara heya upādeya tattva jña puruṣa puṇḍarīka prasādhanāt api apramāṇaka jaḍa vaidika śabda rāśi pramukha sakala durmati pravāda pratihatiḥ iti antarnayan āha heya upādeya tattvasya sa abhyupāyasya vedakaḥ yaḥ pramāṇam asauviṣṭaḥ na tu sarvasya vedakaḥ ityādi tat idānīm upayukta sarvajñam eva tāvat prasādhayāmaḥ paryante tu sarva sarvajña doha dam api apaneṣyāmaḥ svāsthyam āsthīyatām yaḥ yaḥ sa ādara nirantara dīrgha kāla abhyāsa sahita cetaḥ guṇaḥ sa sarvaḥ sphuṭībhāva yogyaḥ yathā yuvati ākāraḥ kāminaḥ puruṣasya yathā ukta abhyāsa sahita cetaḥ guṇāḥ ca amī catur ārya satya viṣayāḥ ākārāḥ iti svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ 
RKNĀ_1.23	 tatra na tāvāt āśraya dvāreṇa hetu dvāreṇa vā asiddhi sambhāvanā saṃkalpa rūḍhānām catur ārya satya ākārāṇām cetaḥ guṇa mātrasya ca hetoḥ pratyātma vedya tvāt na api sa ādara nirantara dīrgha kāla abhyāsa lakṣaṇam hetu viśeṣaṇam asambhāvanīyam tathā hi saṃsāra svabhāvam duḥkha atiśayam apanetum iyam saṃkalpa ārūḍhā catur ārya satya ākāra bhāvanā prārabdhā asyāḥ ca asambhāvanā nāma kim bhāvyasya saṃkalpa ārūḍha tva asambhavāt anarthi tvāt heya rūpā niścayāt heyasya nitya tvāt tasya ahetu tvāt tad hetoḥ nitya tvāt heya hetu aparijñānāt tad bādhaka abhāvāt bādhakā parijñānāt cittasya doṣa ātmaka tvāt tasya vyavasthita guṇa tvāt bhava antara abhāvāt dhvasta doṣa punar udbhavāt vā iti trayodaśa vikalpāḥ 
RKNĀ_2.7–2.11	 tatra na tāvat ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ sa parikara heya upādeya ātmakasya catur ādi asati ākārasya bhāvyasya vikalpa ārūḍhasya pratyātma vedya tvāt na api dvitīyaḥ duḥkha mātrasya api parityāga arthi tvena vyāpteḥ sarva jana anubhava siddha tvāt na api tṛtīyaḥ saṃsāra ātmanaḥ duḥkha svarūpasya pratīteḥ katham asya duḥkha ātmaka tvam iti ced saṃkṣepataḥ kathitam sākṣāt duḥkha prakṛti narakam preta tiryakkha rūpam martye śama kvacana tat api grastam eva asukhena devānām ca kṣayam upagate puṇya pātheya piṇḍe caṇḍa jvālā vyatikara mucaḥ hanta bhogāḥ te eva iti 
RKNĀ_2.17–2.20	 na ca caturthaḥ vārtamānika pañca skandha ātmakasya duḥkhasya utpāda darśanāt na ca pañcamaḥ duḥkhasya kādācid ka tvāt na api ṣaṣṭhaḥ kāryakādācitka tvasya anitya hetuka tvena vyāpta tvāt na api saptamaḥ duḥkhe viparyāsa tṛṣṇā pravṛtti śakti karmabhiḥ sahitasya ātma dṛṣṭi lakṣaṇasya hetoḥ sāṃsārika pañca skandha lakṣaṇa kāryāni atha anupapattitaḥ niścayāt yat āhuḥ ahaṃkāraḥ tāvat tadanu mamakāraḥ tad ubhaya prasūtaḥ rāga ādiḥ tat ahita mateḥ dveṣa dahanaḥ tatas śeṣaḥ kleśaḥ tatas udayinaḥ karma visarāt visārī saṃsāraḥ śaraṇa rahitaḥ dāruṇataraḥ tasmāt tṛṣṇā viparyāsau ātma dṛṣṭi puraḥsarau aṃsāri skandha janakau nirṇītau kārya hetutaḥ 
RKNĀ_2.29–3.2	 ātma darśanasya ca avidyā tvam ātma pratikṣepataḥ draṣṭavyam tad abhāve api kṣaṇa bhaṅga prastāve para loka ādikam anākulam avasthāpitam na ca aṣṭamaḥ ātma dṛṣṭi rūpāyāḥ avidyāyāḥ pratipakṣa bhūtasya nairātmya darśanasya sambhavāt na api navamaḥ nairātmya darśanasya mārga śabda vācyasya pramāṇataḥ niścita tvāt daśamaḥ api asambhavī doṣa avasthāyām cittasya saṃskāra apekṣa tvāt yaḥ hi yat svabhāvaḥ tasmin svabhāve vyavasthitaḥ na saṃskāram apekṣate yathā doṣam apanīya tapanīyam akṣaya daśāyām avasthitam apekṣate ca cittam avidyā avasthāyām saṃskāram iti vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhiḥ pratiṣedhyasya tad svabhāva tvasya yat vyāpakam saṃskāra nirapekṣa tvam tat viruddham tad apekṣa tvam iti cittasya doṣa ātmaka tva kṣatiḥ 
RKNĀ_3.7–3.12	 ekādaśaḥ api ayuktaḥ cetasaḥ tad tad samskāra atiśaye prajñā atiśaya darśanāt na ca dvādaśaḥ para loka prasādhanāt tathā hi yat cittam tat citta antaram pratisandhatte yathā idāni intanam cittam cittam ca maraṇa kāla bhāvi iti svabhāva hetuḥ na ca arhat carama cittena vyabhicāraḥ tasya āgama mātrataḥ pratīta tvāt niḥkleśa citta antara jananāt vā hetoḥ vā kleśe satī iti viśeṣaṇāt iti anāgata bhava siddhiḥ evam yat cittam tat citta antara pūrvakam yathā idāni intanam cittam cittam ca janma samaya bhāvi iti arthataḥ kārya hetuḥ iti atīta bhava siddhiḥ 
RKNĀ_3.15	 na ca trayodaśaḥ doṣa kāraṇasya ātma darśanasya yat viruddham nairātmya darśanam tasya nirupadrava tvāt bhūta artha tvāt svabhāva tvāt ca sarvadā avasthiteḥ tat na ayam viśeṣaṇā siddhaḥ api hetuḥ tathā api īdṛśaḥ abhyāsaḥ na kasyacid dṛśyate iti ced na dṛśyatām sambhāvanā tāvat aśakya pratiṣedhāḥ idānīntana jana pravṛttiḥ ca avyāhata iti na aparam gamyate atas eva idam sambhāvanā anumānam ucyate 
RKNĀ_3.20	 na ca eṣa viruddhaḥ hetuḥ sa pakṣe kāminī ākāre sambhavāt na ca anaikāntikaḥ abhyāsa sahita cetaḥ guṇa sphuṭa pratibhāsayoḥ kārya kāraṇayoḥ ghaṭa kumbha kārayoḥ iva sarva upasaṃhāreṇa pratyakṣa anupalambhataḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhau abhyāsa sahita cetaḥ guṇa tvasya sādhanasya sphuṭa pratibhāsa karaṇa yogya tayā vyāpti siddheḥ tathā hi vyāpti adhikaraṇe kāmātuḥ avartini yuvati ākāre sa ādara nirantara dīrgha kāla abhyāsa sahita cetaḥ guṇāt pūrvam anupalabdhiḥ sphuṭa ābhasya paścāt abhyāsa saṃvedanam sphuṭa ābha saṃvedanam iti trividha pratyakṣa anupalambha sādhyaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ sphuṭa pratibhāsa abhyāsa saciva citta ākārayoḥ iyam upapannā sarva upasaṃhāravatī vyāptiḥ atas anaikāntika tā api asambhavinī iti anavadyaḥ hetuḥ 
RKNĀ_3.29–4.3	 nanu katham anumānataḥ sarvajña siddhi pratyāśā tasya parokṣa tvena tad pratibaddha liṅgā niścayāt kim ca sarvajña sattā sādhane sarvaḥ hetuḥ na trayīm doṣa jātim atipatati sarvajñe hi dharmiṇī asiddha tvam asarvajñe hi viruddha tvam ubhaya ātmake api anaikāntika tvam iti api ca abhyāsāt kāraṇāt kāryasya sphuṭa ābhasya pratītau na avaśyam kāraṇāni kāryavanti bhavanti iti anaikāntika tā atha sphuṭībhāva yogya tā anumīyate sā api śaktiḥ ucyate sā ca kārye anantarā sāntarā vā atra ādyā kārya samadhigamyā na ca adhigata kāryasya tayā kaścid upayogaḥ dvitīyā tu kārya avasāyam aikāntikam na sādhayet 
RKNĀ_4.7–4.11	 na ca kāryā pratītau yogya tā niścayaḥ sambhavī na api yogya tā mātra sādhane kṛtārthaḥ sādhana vādī sarvajña jñāne kārye vivādasya tādavasthyāt bhavatu sphuṭībhāvasya siddhiḥ tathā api kaḥ prastāvaḥ sarvajña vivāde sādhanam ārabdhavataḥ sphuṭa tvam cetasaḥ sādhayitum kim ca prasiddha anumāne bhū talasya dharmiṇi kumbhakāra ghaṭayoḥ api dharmayoḥ pratīta tvāt kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ grahītum śakyataḥ eva prastute tu kāmātuḥ asantāna vartinaḥ yuvati ākārasya dharmiṇaḥ tad pragata abhyāsa sphuṭa tvayoḥ api dharmayoḥ parokṣa tvāt katham kārya kāraṇa gṛhītiḥ yathā ca naiyāyikam prati yuṣmābhiḥ ucyate pratyakṣataḥ na kārya mātram puruṣa vyāptam sidhyati kim tu avāntaram eva ghaṭa jātīyam kāryam iti tathā na ākāra mātram abhyāsa pūrvakam sidhyati kim tu avāntaram eva yuvati ākāra sāmānyam iti vyaktam eva na ca abhyāsa kāryaḥ sphuṭībhāvaḥ tad abhāve api svapne darśanāt 
RKNĀ_4.18	 kim ca sarva vidaḥ api yadi catur ārya satya parijñānataḥ sarvajña tā sthitiḥ tarhi ghaṭa ādi katipaya vastu jñāne api sarvajñā iti sādhvī śuddhiḥ api ca jñānavān mṛgyate kaścid tad ukta pratipattaye ajña upadeśa karaṇe vipralambhana śaṅkibhiḥ iti yuṣmābhiḥ eva ucyate na ca sarva jñānavān viśeṣa niṣṭhatayā adhigantum śakyate na ca asya sattā mātra siddhau kaścid upayogaḥ pravṛtteḥ anaṅga tvāt iti sarvam asamañjasam 
RKNĀ_4.24	 atra ucyate na vayam sākṣāt sarvajña sattā pratijñāyām hetu vyāpāram anumanyāmahe bhūdhara adhīna vahni sattāvat kim tu catur ārya satya ākāra svarūpe dharmiṇi sphuṭa ābha tvasya sādhyasya ayoga vyavaccheda artham parvate agni mātra ayoga vyavaccheda vat sphuṭa ābha tvam tu kāminī ākāra ādi dṛṣṭānte dṛṣṭam eva tat ca parvatīya agni vat pakṣa dharmatā balataḥ satya catuṣṭaya adhikaraṇam sidhyat sarvajña tām ācakṣmahe yathoktam iti abhyāsa balāt parisphuṭa daśā koṭiḥ sphurat sambhavī heya ādeyatad aṅga lakṣaṇa guṇaḥ sarvajña tā sā eva naḥ iti 
RKNĀ_4.31	 tat atra abhyāsa sahita catur ārya satya ākāraḥ samagraḥ dharmī sāmagryam abhyāsa viśiṣṭa cetaḥ guṇa tva mātram hetuḥ sphuṭībhāva yogya tā asādhyam yathā sa agni tva an agni tva san dehe parvata ātmā pramāṇa pratītaḥ dharmī tathā atra api sarvajña tvā sarvajñatva vivāde api pratyātma viditaḥ satya catuṣṭaya ākāraḥ dharmī tasmāt sphuṭa ābha tvena sādhyena dṛṣṭānte vyāpti siddheḥ asti eva tad pratibaddha liṅga niścayaḥ sādhyasandehe api dharmiṇaḥ catur ārya satya ākārasya siddheḥ na trividha doṣa jāteḥ avasaraḥ yogyatāyāḥ prasādhanena ca kāraṇāt kārya pratītau anaikāntika tvam iti api anabhyupagama pratihatam yogyatā ca sa antarā eva sādhyate iyam ca na gamayatu nāma ekāntataḥ kārya sattvam anupapadyamānam punar asya sambhavam ākṣipati eva tadā bhāvini kārye sandehe api kāraṇa yogya tā niścīyate eva brīhi ādau bhāvi phalā niścaye api yogya tā niścayena pravṛtteḥ anyathā śilā śakala ādeḥ api upādāna prasaṅgaḥ 
RKNĀ_5.10–5.12^1	 tad jātīyasya śarāva stha paṅkoptasya sāmarthyam upalabdham iti ced atra api kāminī ākāre bhāvanā jātīyasya sphuṭībhāva karaṇa yogya tā dṛṣṭā iti samānam evam yogyatā mātra sādhanena eva kṛtārthaḥ sādhana vādī sarvajña kāraṇa bhāvāt tad abhāva vādinām nirdalanāt kāryasya ca traikālikasya sambhāvanā prasādhanāt muttkī arthinām ca pravṛtteḥ avirodhāt vādinaḥ api tanmātra sādhanasya abhipreta tvāt atas eva kaḥ prastāvaḥ sarvajña sattā vivāde sphuṭībhāva sādhanasya ityādi api anavakāśam sarvajña śabdena sphuṭībhāva yogya tāyāḥ vivakṣita tvāt tathā kārya kāraṇa pratītiḥ api sambhavati eva tathā hi kāminī abhyāsa santati sahacāri sambhramkārī avacaḥ darśanam eva kāminī ākārasya tad bhāvanāyāḥ ca darśanam tathābhūta kāya vacaḥ adarśanam eva bhāvanāyāḥ adarśanam evam sphuṭa pratibhāsa santati sahacāri viśiṣṭakā yavacaḥ darśanam sphuṭa pratibhāsa darśanam 
RKNĀ_5.12^2	 tathā avasthita kāya vacaḥ adarśanam eva sphuṭa pratibhāsā darśanam iti asati eva prastute api pratyakṣa anupalambhataḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva pratītiḥ iyam ca tathā avasthakā mātuḥ aśarīra vacana grahaṇe tad eka deśa bhūta yuvati ākāra abhyāsa sphuṭa pratibhāsa grahaṇa vyavasthā vyāvahārikeṇa avaśyam svīkartavyā anyathā citta caitya rūpa rasa gandha sparśa paramāṇu puñja ādi ātmakasya kumbhakāra ghaṭa pradeśa ādeḥ api rūpa eka deśa grāhakam cakṣuḥ pratyakṣam na samudāya vyavasthāpakam iti sarva vyāvahārika pramāṇa uccheda prasaṅgaḥ tathā bāhya ghaṭakām ityādīnām śakti kṛtasya mahataḥ jāti bhedasya sambhavāt anya jātīya vyāpti grahe anya jātīyāt buddhimat anumānam ayuktam saṃkalpa ārūḍhānām tu jala jvalana yuvati ākāra ādīnām bāhya tvena adhyastānām api vijñāna eka svarūpa tayā eka jātīya tvam asti iti bhāva nā sahita ākāra mātreṇa eva vaiśadya vyāptiḥ astu 
RKNĀ_5.30	 na ca svapne sphuṭa tā avyabhicāraḥ bhāvanā siddha lakṣaṇayoḥ hetvoḥ jāti bhede tad kāryayoḥ ekatva abhimāne api jāti bhedasya avaśyam svīkartavya tvāt dṛśyate hi siddha sādhyāḥ vaiśadya jātiḥ anapekṣya viparīta bhāvanām nidrā vicchede vicchidyamānāḥ bhāvanā bhāvinī tu na vinā vipakṣa abhyāsam jāgrataḥ api yat āhuḥ svapne api sphuṭa tā tathā eva na tathā api eka tvam eva anayoḥ na prākāra sama tvam eva sama tām jāteḥ samām aṅgati anyat niddha nirodha bādhyam itarat bādhyam pratyatnaiḥ punar vaiśadyam viparīta bhāvana balāt nairghṛṇya bhede yathā iti 
RKNĀ_6.5^1	 yat api ghaṭa ādi katipaya jñāne api sarvajñaḥ syāt iti uktam tatra api ghaṭa ādi prakṛta aśeṣa vedane api bhayam bhavāt dheyata yadi kaḥ doṣaḥ saḥ api sarvajña tām vrajet saṃsāra duḥkha mokṣāya spṛhayantaḥ vayam punar bhajema tad upāya jñam sthātum tad gīta vartamani iti uttaram draṣṭavyam tathā sattā mātre vipratipannān prati sattā eva kevalā prasādhitā viśeṣa jijñāsāyām tu pramāṇa upapanna kṣaṇika nairātmya vādinaḥ eva sugatasya bhagavataḥ sarvajña tā atas etat api nirastam yat āha bhaṭṭaḥ sugataḥ yadi sarvajñaḥ kapilaḥ na iti kā pramā 
RKNĀ_6.5^2	 atha ubhau api sarva jñau mata bhedaḥ katham tayoḥ iti tasmāt ukta krameṇa muniḥ ājanaye pramāyāḥ śaktiḥ vyanakti gatim apramitām kṛpām ca anyatra tu dvayam udastam adaḥ asta māne tena ekaḥ eva śaraṇam sa nirātma vādī iti viśeṣa siddhiḥ api anavadeyā iti sarvam anākulam ākula ādhayaḥ pare na pratipadyante sādhane asmin avadye api durnīti dahana dagdha buddhayaḥ punar api etat ācakaṣate bādhaka pramāṇa sadbhāvāt sarvajñasya asat vyavahāraḥ yuktaḥ sat vyavahāra pratiṣedhaḥ vā prasādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt vā iti 
RKNĀ_6.25–6.27	 atra vicāryate kim punar asya bhagavataḥ bādhakam pramāṇam pratyakṣam anumānam śabda ādikam vā iti vikalpāḥ na tāvat pratyakṣam pratyakṣam hi kevala pradeśa ādau pravartamānam sva pravṛtti yogyam eva tatra vastu pratiṣedhati na vastu mātram na ca sarvajñasya pratyakṣa pravṛtti yogya tā asti svabhāva viprakṛṣṭa tvāt tasya 
RKNĀ_7.1	 syāt etat na vayam pratyakṣam pravartamānam abhāvam sādhayati iti brūmaḥ kim tarhi nivartamānam tathā hi yatra vastuni pratyakṣasya nivṛttiḥ tasya asadbhāvaḥ yathā śaśaviṣāṇa ādeḥ yatra tu pratyakṣasya pravṛttiḥ tasya sadbhāvaḥ yathā ghaṭa ādeḥ asti ca sarvajñe pratyakṣa nivṛttiḥ tat asya api abhāvaḥ kena nivāryate iti 
RKNĀ_7.5–7.9	 ucyate nivartamānam pratyakṣam abhāvam sādhyati iti kaḥ arthaḥ kim pratyakṣasya yā nivṛttiḥ tatas abhāva siddhiḥ nivṛtti sahitāt vā pratyakṣāt nivṛttāt vā pratyakṣāt iti na ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ sati api vastuni pratyakṣa nivṛtteḥ upalabhyamānāyāḥ vastu abhāva niyata tva asiddheḥ na api dvitīyaḥ svābhāvena saha kasyacid sāhitya anupapatteḥ anyathā tad nivṛtta tva anupapatteḥ 
RKNĀ_7.11–7.19	 na ca tṛtīyaḥ tathā hi nivṛttāt pratyakṣāt abhāva siddhiḥ iti asataḥ pratyakṣāt iti uktam bhavati na ca asataḥ hetu bhāvaḥ sambhavati sarva samarthya viraha lakṣaṇtvāt tasya na hi tat ca na asti tena ca pratipattiḥ iti nyāyam atas na tāvat pratyakṣam sarvajña bādhakam na api anumānam tat dhi trividha liṅga ja tvena trividham tatra kārya svabhāvayoḥ vidhi sādhana tvāt pratiṣedhe sādhye anavasaraḥ na ca dṛśya anupalambhaḥ tad prabhedaḥ vā kārya anupalabdhi ādiḥ yogyā anupalambhaḥ vā para abhimataḥ atra pramāṇam sarvajña tāyāḥ svabhāva viprakṛṣṭa tvena adṛśya tvāt nanu kāraṇa anupalambhāt eva sarvajña tā pratiṣedhaḥ sidhyati tathā hi tad kāraṇam indriya vijñānam vā mānasam vā bhāvanā bala jam vā bhāvanā bala jam api cākṣuṣam vā mānasam vā iti vikalpāḥ 
RKNĀ_7.22	 tatra na tāvat cakṣuḥ indriya vijñānam aśeṣa artha grāhi tasya pratiniyata artha viṣaya tvāt deśa antare kāla antare ca tathā eva pratiniyamaḥ anyathā hetu phala bhāva abhāva prasaṅgāt aneka indriya vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt ca tathā ca kārikā eka indriya pramāṇena sarvajñaḥ yena kalpyate nūnam sa cakṣuṣā sarvān rasa ādīn pratipadyate yad jātīyaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ ca yat jātīya artha darśanam bhavet idānīm lokasya tathā kāla antare api abhūt iti tatas ca evam prayogaḥ kartavyaḥ buddha cakṣuḥ na atīta ādi viṣayam cakṣuḥ tvāt asmad ādi cakṣuḥ vat acakṣuḥ vā atīta ādi viṣaya tvāt śabda vat iti sarvam etat śrotra ādau api draṣṭavyam na cakṣuḥ ādi prakarṣaḥ sva artham atikramya dṛṣṭaḥ kārikā yatra api atiśayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ sa sva artha an atilaṅghanāt dūra sūkṣma ādi vṛttau syāt na rūpe śrotra vṛttitaḥ bṛhaṭṭīkā ca śrotra gamyeṣu śabdeṣu dūra sūkṣma upalabdhitaḥ puruṣa atiśayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na rūpa ādi upalambhanāt cakṣuṣā api ca dūra stha sūkṣma rūpa upalambhanam kriyate atiśaya prāptyā na tu śabda ādi darśanam 
RKNĀ_8.13	 na ca etat vaktavyam yadi nāma ekaikena indriyeṇa tad jñānena vā sarvasya agrhaṇam tathā api pañcabhiḥ indriyaiḥ tad jñānaiḥ vā sva sva viṣaya pravṛttaiḥ eva atiśaya prāptaiḥ bhaviṣyati iti ekaikasya api niḥśeṣa sva viṣaya grahaṇa adarśanāt para citta ādi ati indriyāṇām grahaṇa abhāvāt ca tat evam indriya vijñānam vā na aśeṣa grāhī iti na prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ 
RKNĀ_8.17–8.22	 na api dvitīyaḥ tathā hi yadi api tat mānasam sarva artha viṣayam tathā api na tasya svātantryeṇa artha grahaṇe vyāpāraḥ asti manasaḥ bahis asvātantryāt anyathā andha vadhiḥ ādya bhāva prasaṅgaḥ teṣām api manasaḥ bhāvāt pāratantrye cetndriya jñāna parigṛhīta artha viṣaya tvāt atīta anāgata dūra sūkṣma vyavahita para citta ādeḥ arthasya indriya parijñāna agocarasya manasā paricchedaḥ na prāpnoti iti katham sarvajña tā na ca bhāvanā bala jam sarva artha grāhī iti tṛtīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tathā hi tad bhāvanā bala jam api yadi indriya āśritam iti caturthaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā saḥ asaṅgataḥ indriyasya tat jñānasya ca niyata viṣaya viṣaya tva pratipādanāt 
RKNĀ_8.25	 atha bhāvanā balena tathāvidham utpannam manaḥ vijñānam sarva artha grāhī iti pañcamaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā anvartha tvāt pratyakṣa śabdasya tasya ca bhāvanā bala avalambinaḥ api anakṣaja tvāt na artha sākṣāt kāri tvam asti iti pratipādanīyam kim ca sva viṣaya sīmānam anatipatya eva prakarṣaḥ api dṛśyate na tu sarva viṣaya tvena iti katham tena api sakala artha jāta ādi vedanam yatas na kasyacid abhyāse api atīndriya artha darśi tvam upalabdham 
RKNĀ_8.30	 bṛhaṭṭīkāḥ ye api sa atiśayāḥ dṛṣṭāḥ prajñā medhā balaiḥ narāḥ stoka stoka antara tvena na te atīndriya darśanāḥ prājñaḥ api ca naraḥ sūkṣmān atha an draṣṭum kṣamaḥ api san sajātīḥ anatikrāman na atiśete parān api eka avavaraka sthasya pratyakṣam yat pravartate śaktiḥ tatra eva tasya syāt na eva avavaraka antare ye ca arthāḥ dūra vicchinnāḥ deśa parvata sāgaraiḥ varṣa dvīpa antaraiḥ ye ca kaḥ tān paśyet iha eva san atra varṣaḥ kāla viśeṣaḥ evam śāstra vicāreṣu dṛśyate atiśayaḥ mahān na tu śāstra antara jñānam tanmātreṇa eva sidhyati jñātvā vyākaraṇam dūram buddhiḥ śabda apaśabdayoḥ ākṛṣyate na nakṣatra tithi grahaṇa nirṇaye jyotiḥ vid ca prakṛṣṭaḥ api candra arka grahaṇa ādiṣu na bhavati ādi śabdānām sādhu tvam jñātum arhati tathā veda itihāsa ādi jñāna atiśayavān api na svarga devatā pūrva pratyakṣīkaraṇe kṣamaḥ daśa hasta antaram vyomnaḥ ye nāma utplutya gacchati na yojanam asau gantum śaktaḥ abhyāsa śataiḥ api tasmāt atiśaya jñānaiḥ ati dūra gataiḥ api kiñcid eva adhikam jñātum śakyate na tu atīndriyam iti 
RKNĀ_9.20	 pratyakṣa sūtre tu kāśika ākāraḥ para matam āśaṅkya āha tat na avagata viṣaya tvāt bhāvanāyāḥ na ca akasmāt avagateḥ utpattiḥ sambhavati sarva utpattimatām kāraṇavat tvāt atha pramāṇa antara avagatam bhāvyate kim bhāvanayā tatas eva tad siddheḥ kim ca tad pramāṇam na tāvat anumānam dharma adharmayoḥ pūrvam agrahaṇena tad vyāpta liṅga saṃvedanā sambhavāt jagat vaividhya artha āpatteḥ api hi kim api kāraṇam asti iti etāvat unnīyate na tu kaścid viśeṣaḥ na ca anirdiṣṭa viśeṣa viṣayā bhāvanā bhavati yoga śāstreṣu api hi viśeṣāḥ eva dhyeyatayā upadiśyante dhyeyaḥ ātmā prabhuḥ yaḥ asau hṛdi dīpaḥ iva sthitaḥ ityādibhiḥ āgama mānāt tarhi avagatam bhāvayiṣyate yadi pramāṇāt tadā tatas eva avagateḥ kim bhāvanayā hāna upādāna artham hi vastu jijñāsyate te ca tatas eva siddhe iti vyarthāḥ bhāvanā kāruṇikaḥ api hi dharma āgamān eva śiṣyebhyaḥ vyācakṣīta na bhāvanā bhedam anubhavet 
RKNĀ_10.3	 atha vipralambha bhūyiṣṭha tvāt āgāmānām pramāṇam āgamaḥ na vā iti vicikitsamānaḥ bhāvanayā jijñāsate tat na tatas api tad asiddheḥ bhāvanā bala priniṣpannam api jñānam anāśvsanīya artham eva abhūtasya api bhāvyamānasya aparokṣa arthavat prakāśanāt yathā hi taiḥ eva uktam tasmāt bhūtam abhūtam vā yat yat eva abhibhāvyate bhāvanā pariniṣpattau tat sphuṭā kalpa dhīḥ phalam api ca bhāvanā bala jam apramāṇam gṛhīta grahaṇāt yāvat eva hi gṛhītam tāvat eva bhāvanayā viṣayīkriyate mātrayā api adhikam na bhāvanā gocarayati yoga abhyāsa āhita saṃskāra pāṭava nimittā hi smṛtiḥ eva bhāvanā iti gīyate sā ca pramāṇam iti sthitam eva na ca tad uttara kālam sākṣātkāri jñānam udeti iti pramāṇam asti indriya sannikarṣam antareṇa artha sākṣātkārasya kvacid adarśanāt yoginām dharma adharmayoḥ aparokṣa pratibhāsam jñānam na asti indriya sannikarṣa abhāvāt asmad ādi vat 
RKNĀ_10.14–10.17	 vācapatiḥ tu kaṇikāyām āha satyam śruta anumāna gocara cāriṇī bhāvanā viśada ābha jñāna hetuḥ iti na avajānīmahe kin tu yat viṣaya jātam tat eva viśada pratipatti gocaraḥ na jātu rūpa bhāvanā prakarṣaḥ rasa viṣaya vijñāna vaiśadyāya kalpate nanu na viṣaya antara vaiśadya hetu bhāvam bhāvanāyāḥ saṅgirāmahe kintu śruta anumāna viṣaya vaiśadya hetu tām eva tad viṣayaḥ ca samasta vastu nairātmyam iti tad bhāvanā prakarṣaḥ samasta vastu nairātmyam viśadayan samasta vastu viśada tām antareṇa tad upapatteḥ samasta vastu vaiśadyam āvahati iti uktam 
RKNĀ_10.21	 satyam uktam ayuktam tu tat tathā hi na āgama anumāna gocara tvam nirātmanām vastu bhedānām parama artha satām na hi te eteṣām anya nivṛtti mātra avagāhinī parama artha satsvalakṣaṇam gocarayitum arhataḥ na api tad viṣayā bhāvanā tat agrāhyam api sva lakṣaṇam tat adhyavaseya tayā tad viṣayaḥ iti tad yoniḥ api bhāvanā tat viṣaya iti tad prakarṣaḥ tad vaiśadya hetuḥ iti ced na tat adhyavaseyasya api parama artha sattva abhāvāt tathā hi yat anumānena gṛhyate yat ca adhyavasīyate te dve api anya nivṛttī na vastunī sva lakṣaṇa avagāhi tve abhilāpa saṃsarga yogya pratibhāsā anupapatteḥ 
RKNĀ_10.28^1	 mā bhūt tayoḥ sva lakṣaṇam viṣayaḥ tad prabhava bhāvanā prakarṣa paryanta janmanaḥ tu viśada ābhasya cetasaḥ bhaviṣyati kāmīnī vikalpa prabhava bhāvanā prakarṣāt iva kāmātuḥ asya kāminī sva lakṣaṇa sākṣātkāraḥ kari kumbha kaṭhora kuca kalaśa hāriṇi hariṇa śāva lola locane campaka dala avadāta gātra late lāvaṇya sarasi nirantara lagna lalita doḥkandalī mūlam āliṅganam aṅgane preya sitare prayaccha sañjīvaya jīviteṣu ari patitaḥ asmi tava caraṇa nalinayoḥ iti vacana kāya ceṣṭayoḥ upalabdheḥ asti ca vikalpa avikalpayoḥ kathañcid samāna viṣaya tā iti na ati prasaṅgaḥ iti ced 
RKNĀ_10.28^2	 satyam sambhavati ayam anubhavaḥ na punar asya arthe prāmāṇya sambhavaḥ atad utpatteḥ atada ātmanaḥ tad avyabhicāra niyama ayogāt atādātmyam ca arthasya vijñānāt atirekāt anatireke api ca vijñānānām anyonyasya bhedāt atādātmyāt ekasya vijñānasya itara vijñāna vedanā anupapatteḥ vijñāna sva lakṣaṇa eka tva abhyupagame ca tat nityam ekam advitīyam brahma abhyasanīyam iti kṣaṇika nairātmya abhyāsa abhyupagamaḥ datta jala añjaliḥ prasajyeta tat na tādātmyāt tasya avyabhicāraḥ na api tad kāryatvāt bhāvanā prakarṣa kāryam khalu evat na viṣaya kāryam 
RKNĀ_10.28^3	 yadi ucyeta pāramparyeṇa tad kāryam anumāna vat yathā hi vahni sva lakṣaṇāt dhūma sva lakṣaṇam tatas dhūma anubhavaḥ tatas dahana vikalpaḥ tatas ca anumānam utpannam iti pāramparyeṇa vahni pratibandhāt prāpakam ca vahneḥ dāha pāka kāriṇaḥ tathā idam api anumāna janita bhāvanā prakarṣa paryanta jam pāramparyeṇa artha prasūta tayā tad avyabhicāra niyamāt tatra pramāṇam iti tat kim anumānena vahnim vyavasthāpya bhāvayataḥ yat vahni viṣayam ati viśada vijñānam tat pramāṇam iti om iti brubāṇasya parvata nitamba ārohaṇe sati indriya sannikarṣa janmanaḥ dahana vijñānasya bhāvanā ādhipatya viśada ābha vijñānena saha saṃvāda niyama prasaṅgaḥ 
RKNĀ_10.28^4	 visaṃvādaḥ ca bahulam upalabhyate lakṣaṇa yogini ca vyabhicāra sambhave tad lakṣaṇam eva bādhitam iti viśada ābham api prātibham iva saṃśaya ākrāntam apramāṇam tad bhāvanāyāḥ bhūtārtha tvam na tad javi śat ābhavijñāna prāmāṇya hetuḥ vyabhicārāt etan ca prāsarpakasya iva saktu karkarī prāpti mūla lābha manoratha paramparā hitaḥ draviṇa sambhāra sākṣātkāraḥ tathāgatasya nirātmaka samasta vastu sākṣātkāraḥ iti āpatitam sarva artha vastu bhāvanā parikarmita citta santāna varti vijñānam pratyālambana pratyaya tvam artha mātrasya 
RKNĀ_11.27^1	 tathā ca tad utpatteḥ tat avyabhicāra niyamaḥ iti ced na arthasya hi ālambana pratyaya tva vijñānam pratīndriya apekṣa tvena vyāptam tat ca asmāt sva viruddha upalabdhyā vyāvartamānam ālambana pratyaya tām api arthasya nivartayati na khalu indhana viśeṣaḥ dhūma hetuḥ iti vinā api dahanam sastreṇa api saṃskāraiḥ dhūmam ādhatte tad ādhāne vā samasta kārya hetu anumāna uccheda prasaṅgaḥ bhāvanāyāḥ ca bhūta arthāyāḥ artha anapekṣāyāḥ eva viśada vijñāna janana sāmarthyam upalabdham kāma ātura ādi vartinyā iti bhūtārthā api tad nirapekṣā eva samartha iti na arthasya ālambana pratyaya tvam śakya avagamam api ca ālambana pratyaya api te eva asya kṣaṇāḥ yujyante ye tasya purastāt tanāḥ avyavadhānāḥ tathā ca te eva asya grāhyāḥ na punar pūrvatarāḥ 
RKNĀ_11.27^2	 tad kālāḥ anāgatāḥ ca iti na sarva viṣaya tā atha dṛśyamānāḥ dhātu traya paryāpannāḥ prāṇabhṛtaḥ janma antara parivarta upātta atīta anāgata skandha kadamba kopādāna upādeya ātmāna iti tad darśanam dṛśyamāna tādātmyena tad viśeṣaṇa tayā atīta anāgatam api gocarayati na ca asmad ādi darśanasya api tathā tva prasaṅgaḥ rāga ādi mala āvṛta tvāt tasya ca bhagavataḥ nirmṛṣṭa nikhila kleśa upakleśa malam vijñānam anāvaraṇam paritas pradyotamānam ālambana pratyayam sarva ākāram gocarayet tasya ca sākṣāt paramparayā ca kathañcid sarveṇa sambandhāt deśa kāla viprakīrṇa vastu mātra viśiṣṭa svabhāva tayā tathā eva gocarayet na ca etat sarva grahaṇam antareṇa iti sarva viṣayam asya vijñānam anāvaraṇam siddham 
RKNĀ_12.16^1	 tat anupapannam vicāra asaha tvāt tathā hi iyam ālambana pratyayasya sarva viśiṣṭa ātma tā bhāvikī na vā bhāvikī ced na tāvat sarvasmin ālambana pratyaye ca ekā sambhavati ekasya aneka vṛtti tva anupapatteḥ nānā ced ālambana pratyayāḥ ca sarve ca iti tattvam tathā ca na sambandhaḥ iti na tad grahaṇe sarva grahaṇam vikalpa āropita tayā tu avikalpakam samasta vastu viṣayam sarvatra pratīyate iti subhāṣitam sva ālambana pratyaya mātra gocaram eva avikalpakam samasta vastu viśiṣṭa ālamba nādhyavasāya jananam tena adhyavasāya anugata vyāpāram avikalpakam api samasta vastu viṣayam bhavati 
RKNĀ_12.16^2	 yat āha vyavasyanti īkṣaṇāt eva sarva ākārān mahā ādhiyaḥ iti ced atha katipaya vaḥ tu ālambana anubhavasya kutastyaḥ eṣa mahimā yatas samasta vaḥ tu avasāyaḥ iti rāga ādi āvaraṇa vigamāt iti ced tarhi yathāvat vastūni paśyet na punar asmāt apārtha tvam asya iti tat ayuktam vikalpa nirmāṇa kauśalam asya yujyeta tattva āvaraka tā hi sulabha malānām kleṣa ādīnām na punar vikalpa nirmāṇa pratibandha tā tasmāt bhāvanā prakarṣa mātraja tvāt artha avi abhicāra niyama abhāvāt viśada ābham api saṃśaya ākrānta tvāt apramāṇam apratyakṣam ca iti sāmpratam 
RKNĀ_13.1^1	 yat api sat artha prakāśanam buddheḥ svabhāvaḥ asat artha tvam ca āgantukam iti asati bādhake sat artha tvam eva iti tat ayuktam anumita bhāvita vahni viṣaya viśada ābha jñāna prāmāṇya prasaṅgāt tadvidhasya kvacid bādha darśanāt aprāmāṇyam iha api samānam anyatra abhiniveśāt tat iha yadi viśada ābha vijñāna hetu tvam bhāvanāyāḥ viśeṣaṇa traya yogena sādhyate tatas siddha sādhanam bhavatu tathāgataḥ tathābhūta vijñānavān na tu etat vijñānam asya pratyakṣam apramāṇa tvāt tathā ca apakṣa dharma tayā hetoḥ asiddha tā prasiddha dharmaṇaḥ dharmiṇaḥ aji jñāsita viśeṣa tayā anumeya tva abhāvāt atha pratyakṣa vijñāna hetu tāḥ bhāvanāyāḥ param pratyasiddhā sādhyate tathā ca sati sādhya viparyaya vyāpteḥ viruddha tā hetoḥ viśeṣaṇa trayavatyā api bhāvanāyāḥ viśada ābha bhrānta vijñāna janaka tvāt dṛṣṭāntasya ca sādhya hīna tvāt 
RKNĀ_13.1^2	 yadā ca bhūta artha bhāvanā janita tve api na asya prāmāṇyam abhūta artha tvāt tadā yat ucyate nirupadrava bhūta artha svabhāvasya viparyayaiḥ na bādhā yatnavat tve api buddheḥ tad pakṣa pātataḥ iti tat anupapannam bhūta artha tve api hi buddheḥ tad pakṣa pātitāḥ bhūta arthaiḥ pratipakṣaiḥ bādhaḥ na bhavet abhūta arthā tu iyam sā ātmībhāvam āpannā api ātma ātmīya dṛṣṭiḥ iva sambhavat bādhā tasmāt pratipakṣa vivṛddhi mātram na tu ātyantikī vivṛddhiḥ sambhavati yayā sa mūla kāṣam kaṣitāḥ doṣāḥ na punar udbhaviṣyanti atas eva asthiḥ āśraya tve api apunar yatna apekṣa tve api asya na ātyantikī niṣṭhā sambhavati ātmā ātmīya dṛśaḥ iva virodhi pratyaya sambhavāt tad sambhavaḥ ca abhūta artha tvāt śruta anumita viṣayam tu pratyakṣam na sambhavati eva tayoḥ parokṣa rūpa avagāhi tvāt pratyakṣasya ca tad viparīta tvāt tad gata bhūtā bhūta artha anuvidhāyi tvena sva viṣaye śruta anumāna jñāna apekṣayā prāmāṇya anupapatteḥ ca 
RKNĀ_13.23	 tat siddham etat bhūta artha bhāvanā prakarṣa paryanta javi jñānam apratyakṣam arthe aprāmāṇyāt yat apramāṇam tat apratyakṣam arthe yathā kāmātuḥ asya kāminī vijñānam apramāṇam ca tat nitānta viśat a ābha tve sati bhāvanā prakarṣa ja tvāt yat nitānta viśat a ābha tve sati bhāvanā prakarṣa jam vijñānam tat apramāṇam 
RKNĀ_14.1^1	 yathā anumita bhāvita vahni viśada vijñānam iti samāna hetu ja tvam samāna rūpa tayā vyāptam yat āha tad atad rūpiṇaḥ bhāvāḥ tad atad rūpa hetu jāḥ iti tat asya prāmāṇyam nivartamānam tulya hetu ja tvam api nivartayati na ca eṣa bhūta artha bhāvanā prakarṣa paryanta jaḥ anindriya sannikṛṣṭa anumita bhāvita vahni vaiśadye ca nirātmaka samasta vastu vaiśadye ca viśiṣyate na ca rāga ādi āvaraṇa virahaḥ viśeṣaḥ na khalu ete kambala ādi vat āvarakāḥ vijñānasya kim tu tad ākṣipta manāḥ vividha viṣaya bheda tṛṣṇā ādi pariplutaḥ na śaknoti bhāvayitum iti bhāvanā ādara mātraḥ eva tad viraha upayogaḥ 
RKNĀ_14.1^2	 asti ca iha api śiśira bhara sambhṛta jaḍima mantharatara kāya kāṇḍasya anumita vahni bhāvanā abhiyogaḥ iti na hetu bhedataḥ pratibandha siddhiḥ na ca eka pārthiva aṇu samavāyi kāraṇa janmabhiḥ abhinnauṣṇya apekṣā eka vahni saṃyoga asamavāyi kāraṇaiḥ gandha rasa rūpa sparśaiḥ nānā svabhāvaiḥ vyabhicāraḥ sāmarthya vaicitryāt eka tve api pārthivasya paramāṇoḥ tad vaicitryam ca kārya vaicitrya upalambhāt tat ca nitya samavetam nityam kāraṇa sāmarthya prakrameṇa ca pārthiva avayavini kārye jāyate iti avadātam pariśiṣṭam tu grantha vyākhyāna samaye vyākhyāsyāmaḥ tadā āstām tāvat 
RKNĀ_14.16	 trilocanaḥ tu nyāya prakīrṇake prāha iha kila duḥkha samudaya nirodha mārga ākhyāni āryāṇām satyāni catvāri teṣām satyānām svarūpa sākṣātkāri jñānam yogi pratyakṣam tatra duḥkham phala bhūtāḥ pañca upādāna skandhāḥ tat ca svarūpataḥ jñātavyam te eva hetu bhūtāḥ samudayaḥ sa ca prahātavyaḥ niḥkleśa avasthā cittasya nirodhaḥ sa ca sākṣātkartavayaḥ tad avasthā prāpti hetuḥ nairātmya kṣaṇika tva ādi ākāraḥ citta viśeṣaḥ mārgaḥ sa ca bhāvayitavyaḥ iti saugata matam 
RKNĀ_14.22	 atra ucyate mārgaḥ tāvat pramāṇa pariśuddhaḥ na bhavati iti uktam prāk atas abhūta viṣayasya vikalpasya abhyāsāt asatya artha vijñānam syāt na saṃvādi api ca pramāṇa pariśuddha mārga vādī śākyaḥ pramāṇam pṛṣṭaḥ san sattva ākhya liṅga jam vikalpam brūyāt tatas yāvat vikalpena darśita rūpam tat sarvam asat śabda saṃsṛṣṭa tvāt tasmin ca bhāvyamāne sattve bhāvakasya vikalpakasya bhāvanā upahite viśada ābha tve śabda samsṛṣṭa grāhya nimittam vikalpaka tvam nivartate tad vyāvṛttau grāhyam api śabda saṃsṛṣṭam nivartate atas nirvikalpakam api yogi jñānam nirviṣayam prasaktam yat tu pāramārthikam vastu ātmakam na tad pramāṇa pariśuddham śuddhau vā bhāvanayā bhāvyasya sākṣāt vijñāta tvāt na ca anyasmin śabda saṃsṛṣṭe bhāvyamāne sphuṭam anyat rūpam bhavati śokātuḥ asya api niruddha indriya vyāpārasya tanaya bhāvanāyām mitra ādi pratibhāsa prasaṅgāt 
RKNĀ_15.4	 kṣaṇika tve bhāvye samāropite vāstavam kṣaṇika tvam eva yogi vijñāna pratibhāsi iti ced na satya asatyayoḥ ekatva abhāva ātmake hi bhede asatya bhāvane api yadi satya pratibhāsaḥ tarhi satya tanaya abhyāse api śabda sāmyāt abhedinaḥ tanaya saṃjñakasya kasyacid aparasya svarūpa pratibhāsa prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt abhūta viṣaya abhyāsam nirvikalpakam api saṃvādāt na pramāṇam iti na sarvajña siddhiḥ 
RKNĀ_15.9^1	 api ca bhāvyasya vastunaḥ punar punar cetasi niveśanam abhyāsaḥ sa ca brahmacaryeṇa tapasā sa ādaram dīrgha kālam nirantaram āsevitaḥ dṛḍha bhūmiḥ asphuṭa ākārasya vikalpasya sphuṭa ābha tva jananaḥ iṣṭaḥ sa kṣaṇika tva nairātmya vādinā draḍhayitum aśakyaḥ tathā hi bhāvya grāhī yādṛśaḥ vikalpaḥ utpannaḥ tādṛśaḥ eva niranvayam nirudhyate tasmin ca niruddhe punar punar utpadyamānaḥ pratyayaḥ tādṛśaḥ eva apūrvaḥ utpadyate tat anena paryāyeṇa kalpa sahasre api apūrva utpatteḥ aviśeṣāt na tad janyaḥ saṃskāraḥ abhyāsaḥ utpadyate etena viśiṣṭa vijñāna utpādaḥ abhyāsaḥ vyākhyātaḥ niranvaya niruddham hi pūrva pūrva vijñānam katham uttara avasthā antaram viśiṣtam janayet sarvathā krama bhāvibhiḥ pratyayaiḥ avasthitam eva rūpam śakyam saṃskartum anavasthitam tu sva utpāda vyaya yogi mātram iti aviśiṣṭam syāt 
RKNĀ_15.9^2	 tasmāt pratyāvṛtti bhāvya vastu pratyaya jaḥ saṃskāraḥ vyutthāna pratyaya saṃskāra virodhī yasya asti tasya eva ātmanaḥ prakṛṣṭaḥ api bhāvya sākṣāt kāri pratyaya hetuḥ iti yuktam paśyāmaḥ kim ca cittam ekāgram vyavasthāpayitum vikṣepa tyāga artham abhyāsaḥ anuṣṭhīyate na ca kṣaṇika vādinām vikṣiptam cittam asti pratyartha niyata tayā sarvasya vitta ekāgra tvāt tathā hi yadi sa ākāram vikalpa vijñānam sva pratibhāsa niyata tvāt ekāgram eva tat katham vikṣipyate atha nirākāram tathā api vikalpakam prati vikalpyam bhinnam eva na tu sarva vikalpānām vikalpyam asti tatas nirākāram api vijñānam niyata ālambana tvāt ekāgram eva na vikṣiptam sarvathā na asti kṣaṇika vādinām ekam aneka artham avasthitam cittam yat ekāgram kartum iṣyate tat evam abhyāsa anupapatteḥ asarvajñavatyām citta santatau na ca vijñāna viśeṣaḥ sarvajñaḥ sidhyati iti 
RKNĀ_15.30–16.1	 nyāya bhūṣaṇa kāraḥ tu āha sarva jñānānām nirālambana tve saṃveda mātra tve ca yogi itara pratyayayoḥ kaḥ viśeṣaḥ śuddha aśuddha tvam iti ced bhavatu nāma evam tathā api catur ārya satya ādi viṣaya tvam ayuktam na hi sva ātma mātra vedanena catur ārya satya ādikam sākṣātkṛtam iti yuktam atiprasaṅgāt tad ākāra tvena tat viṣaya tvam iti ced tat kim idānīm sautra antika matam abhyupagatam satyam tathā api atīta anāgata viṣaya tvam katham na hi asataḥ kaścid ākāraḥ asti dṛṣṭa śruta anumita ākāraḥ ca yadi bhāvanā balataḥ spaṣṭaḥ eva avabhāti tathā ca sati bhrāntam eva yogi pratyakṣam syāt avidyamānasya vidyamāna ākāra tayā pratibhāsanāt svapna vat tathā avisaṃvādi tvāt na bhrāntam na anumāna jñānasya bhrānta tve api avisaṃvādi tva abhyupagamāt 
RKNĀ_16.7	 atha bhrāntasya api saṃvādi tvena prāmāṇyam tathā api pratyakṣa lakṣaṇasya abhrānta tva viśeṣaṇam virudhyate na ca avisaṃvādi tvam api tvad mate yuktam yatas prāpya artha darśaka tvam vā pravṛtti viṣaya upadarśaka tvam vā avabhātāt artha kriyā niṣpattiḥ vā bhavatām avisaṃvādi tvam abhipretam na ca etat atīta ādi artha jñāne sambhavati vartamāna artha jñānasya api kṣaṇika tva pakṣe na upapadyate eva tasmāt saugatānām yogi pratyakṣa upavarṇanam ayuktam eva iti 
RKNĀ_16.12	 kim ca idam api vaktum ucitam yadi anumāna pūrvakam artheṣu bhāvanā bala ja jñānam āśvāsa bhājanam tadā āstām tāvat anumāna pauruṣa pratyāśā pratyakṣeṇa api cakṣuḥ dahana ādikam gṛhītvā bhāvanā prakarṣa paryante jātam sthirataram tad ākāra vijñānam syāt yāvat na viparīta bhāvanā abhiyoga paryantaḥ astam gataḥ ca tad viṣayaḥ avasthānatara prāptaḥ vā iti katham pramāṇa upanīta vastu gocara tve api saṃvāda āśvāsaḥ api ca yadā hālikaḥ eva havya aśanam anumāya bhāvanayā sphuṭayet tadā na tad yogi jñānam parama artha viṣaya abhāvāt iti pratyakṣa antara prasaṅgaḥ 
RKNĀ_16.19	 kim ca tad yogi jñānam indriya jñānāt bhinnam abhinnam vā abheda pakṣe na yogi jñānam nāma pratyakṣeṇa bhinnam indriya jñānena eva saṅgrahāt na ca bhāvanā upaskṛta santānasya tathā udayāt bheda vyavasthā rasāyana ādi saṃskāra apekṣayā api pratyakṣa antara vyavasthā prasaṅgāt bheda pakṣe ca bhāvanā sambhavam jñānam kṣaṇika sākṣāt kāri indriya jñānam ca syaiḥ yagrāhi iti sādhvī siddhiḥ indriya jñānasya api tad avasthāyām asthairya grhaṇe kṛtam yogi jñānena na ca tasya ākasmikaḥ kṣaṇikatva avabodhaḥ bhāvanā udbhūta vaiśadyasya hi tad bodhaḥ na ca indriya jñānasya bhāvanā api tu manaḥ vijñāne tām antareṇa api sākṣāt kriyā lābhe ca bhāvanā vaiyarthyam iti kāraṇa abhāvāt eva sarvajña pratihatiḥ 
RKNĀ_16.28^1	 atra abhidhīyate yat tāvat sarva padārtha saṃvedanasya kāraṇam kim indriya jñānam ityādi valgitam tatra bhāvanā bala jam manaḥ vijñānam eva sarva padārtha grāhī iti pañcamaḥ eva asmākam pakṣaḥ atas pakṣa antara bhāvinaḥ doṣāḥ anubhyupagama pratihatāḥ yat ca asmad abhyupagate pañcame pakṣe dūṣaṇam uktam anartha tvāt pratyakṣa śabdasya tasya ca bhāvanā bala avalambinaḥ api anakṣaja tvāt na artha sākṣāt kāri tvam asti iti tat asaṅgatam tathā hi pratyakṣa śabdasya tāvat akṣa āśrita tvam vyutpatti nimittam artha sākṣātkāri tvam tu pravṛtti nimittam iti pratipāditam na ca bhāvanā bala avalambinaḥ manaḥ vijñānasya ānakṣa āśrita tve api artha sākṣa arka raṇe kaścid asti śakti pratighātaḥ yathā hi cakṣuḥ indriyam sva sāmarthyān atikrameṇa yogya deśa stham artham apekṣya sva vijñāna janane pravartate tathā sarva avidyā paripanthi bhūta artha bhāvanā sahitam manaḥ indriyam api yogya deśa stham artham prāpya sva vijñāna janane pravartiṣyate aprāpya kāritāyāḥ ubhayoḥ sādhāraṇa tvāt arthavat tāyāḥ ca manasaḥ api tadānīm iṣṭa tvāt 
RKNĀ_16.28^2	 pṛthagjanasya tu na tādṛśī śaktiḥ yatas netra śrotra vat manaḥ api tādṛś maryādayā yogya deśa stham artha sahakāriṇam āsādya vedanam utpādayet sarva avidyā unmūlakasya bhāvanā viśeṣasya sahakāriṇaḥ abhāvāt iti na ati prasaṅgaḥ tad avasthāyām tu śruti nayanayoḥ iva manasaḥ api kiyat dūreṇa viṣaya sannidhi vyavasthitikaḥ eva pramātum kṣamaḥ kevalam etāvat ucyate yāvat tena śakyam adhigantum sva ākāra arpaṇa samartham sahakāri vastu tāvat itarajanāsā dhāraṇam truṭyat rūpa tayā tasya gocarībhavati iti atas eva artha ākāraḥ vastutas na bhāvanā mātra janitaḥ iti na visaṃvāda śaṅkā api bhāvanayā punar tadīya santāne netre iva añjana viśeṣeṇa śaktiḥ atiśayavatī kācid arpitāḥ yat parajanāsā dhāraṇa darśanam asya tasmāt anakṣaja tve api amnaḥ vijñānasya artha sākṣāt kāri tvam sambhavati nanu manasaḥ bahis asvātantryam anyathā andha badhira ādi abhāva prasaṅgāt uktam ca yoginām dharma adharmayoḥ aparokṣa pratibhāsam jñānam na asti indriya sannikarṣa abhāvāt asmad ādi vat iti 
RKNĀ_17.18	 api ca arthasya hi ālambana pratyaya tvam indriya apekṣa tvena vyāptam tat ca asmāt sva viruddha upalabdhyā vyāvarta manam ālambana pratyaya tām api tasya nivartayati na khalu indhana viśeṣaḥ dhūma hetuḥ iti vinā api dahanam sahasreṇa api saṃskāraiḥ dhūmam ādhatte tad ādhāne samasta kārya hetuka anumāna uccheda prasaṅgaḥ na ca bhāvanā balena kasyacid atīndriya darśi tvam sarvajña tvam vā dṛṣṭam iti ced 
RKNĀ_17.23	 atra ucyate manaḥ śabdena tāvat asmākam anakṣajam vijñānam eva abhipretam na ca asmin andha badhira ādi abhāva prasaṅgaḥ sarva avidyā pratipakṣa bhūta artha bhāvanā lakṣaṇasya saha kāri viśeṣasya andha ādīnām abhāvāt indriya sannikarṣa abhāvāt iti tu artha sākṣātkāri tva mātra apekṣayā sandigdha vyatireki tve anaikāntikī kāraṇa anupalabdhiḥ asmadvidha artha sākṣāt kāritva apekṣayā punar siddha sādhanam 
RKNĀ_17.28	 asmad ādi viśeṣaṇa śūnyasya artha sākṣātkāri tva mātrasya eva indriya adhīna tva darśanāt anaikāntika tvam asambhavi iti ced yadi evam artha sākṣātkāri tva mātrasya indirya vat āloka adhīna tvam upalabdham iti na santamase paśyeyuḥ ulūka ādayaḥ atha vyabhicāra darśanāt ālokasya avyāpaka tvam vyabhicāra śaṅkayā tarhi indriyasya api avyāpaka tvam vyāptyā śaṅkā khaṇḍyate iti ced śaṅkā sambhavāt vyāptiḥ eva asambhavinī yadi prathamatas eva vyāptiḥ vyabhicāraḥ api na dṛśyeta 
RKNĀ_18.1	 tasmāt vyabhicāra darśanam vyāpti śaithilyāt eva sati ca vyāpti śaithilye śaṅkā api nyāyāt āpatantī kena pratihanyate ulūka ādīnām bhinna jātīya tvāt āloka abhāve api artha sākṣātkāri tvam astu iti ced tarhi bhagavataḥ api bhūta artha bhāvanā prakarṣa paryanta mahāpralaya vāyunā nirastānādya avipakṣasya saṃsāra kūpa patitebhyaḥ prāṇibhyaḥ asti eva at bhūta vaijātyam iti yuktam asya avidyā pratipakṣa bhāvanā atiśaya sahita ātmaka antara pratyayāt ālambana pratyayāt ca sākṣāt utpannasya indriyam antareṇa artha sākṣāt kāri tvam atas kāraṇa anupalabdhiḥ kāśika ākārasya vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhiḥ ca vācaspateḥ sandigdha vyatireki tvāt anaikāntikī sandigdha vyatireki tvam tu dūṣaṇam asmad īśvara dūṣaṇe prasādhitam 
RKNĀ_18.10	 tasmāt sādhāraṇa karma nirjātānām asmad ādīnām artha sākṣāt kāri tvam indirya apekṣa tvena vyāptam iti siddha sādhanam prasiddha anumānasya ca na kṣatiḥ dṛśya tva upādheḥ dhūma ādeḥ pratyakṣa anupalambhataḥ vyāpti grahaṇa avirodhāt sāṃsārikā gocara artha sākṣātkāri tva mātra apekṣayā tu sandigdha vyatireki tvam adṛśyasya pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām kenacid vyāpti grahaṇa ayogāt viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇasya ca asambhavāt iti na ca atīndriya darśi tvam sarvajña tvam vādarśane api niṣeddhum śakyate adṛśya anupalambhataḥ niṣedha ayogāt kāraṇa anupalambataḥ tat niśedhaḥ iti ced kāraṇa abhāvaḥ api adarśana mātrataḥ na sidhyati iti tad avasthaḥ paribhavaḥ 
RKNĀ_18.18^1	 yat api kāśika ākāreṇa abhihitam atha pramāṇa antara avagatam bhāvyate kim bhāvanayā tatas eva tad siddheḥ iti tat api asaṅgatam pramāṇa antaram hi anumānam na ca catur ārya satya svarūpe vastu tattve niścite sākṣātkāram antareṇa kleśa jñeya āvaraṇa kṣatiḥ iti sva artham api tāvat bhāvanā yuktimatī tattva sākṣāt kāriṇi ca citta santāne sati śakya sākṣāt kriyam idam iti anye api niścaya anantaram sākṣātkriyāyai pravartyante tad upadiṣṭa svarga sādhanam ca artha bhāvanayā anusaranti iti svarga apavarga lakṣaṇa para artha siddhaye ca bhāvanā saphala iti anyathā tattva asa akṣātkāriṇaḥ lokān atikrāntasya vacanam anādeyam eva syāt iti kva para artha vārtā api 
RKNĀ_18.18^2	 yat ca kim ca tad pramāṇam ityādi ārambhya tasmāt bhūtam abhūtam vā iti etat paryantena dharma adharmayoḥ anumāna apravartanam uktam tatra dharma adharma śabdena kim abhipretam yadi kṣaṇika nirātmaka vastu tattvam tadā tasya pratyakṣeṇa aniścaye api yathā viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa balena vyāpti saṃvedanam tathā kṣaṇa bhaṅga sādhana avasare vyavasthāpitam atha vastūnām svarga ādi sādhana tvam abhipretam tadā tad viṣaya parijñāna aprasādhane api na asmākam kācid kṣatiḥ sa parikara saṃsāra nirvāṇa parijñānena eva upayukta sarvajña prasādhanāt yat āhuḥ heya upadeya tattvasya ityādi 
RKNĀ_18.32	 yat api api ca bhāvanā bala jam gṛhīta grahaṇāt apramāṇam iti uktam tatra gṛhītam nāma pratyakṣeṇa anumānena vā pramāṇa antarasya abhāvāt na tāvat pratyakṣam kṣaṇika tva ādau arvācīnasya kasyacid asti anumānena ca eka vyāvṛtti viśiṣṭe vastu tattve avasite api sarva ātmanā spaṣṭa vastu tattva sākṣātkāri pratyakṣam na gṛhīta grāhi anumānena vastu tattva asparśanāt na ca tad uttara kālam ityādi tu kāraṇa anupalabdhi dūṣaṇa prastāve prativyūḍham iti 
RKNĀ_19.5	 yat api vācaspatinā satyam ityādinā punar punar uttarottaram āśaṅkya tat kim anumānena vahnim vyavasthāpya ityādinā bhāvanā bala jasya anumāna pūrvaka tve visaṃvādam upadarśya upasaṃhṛtam tat na bhāvanāyāḥ bhūtārtha tvam tat javi śadavijñāna prāmāṇya hetuḥ vyabhicārāt iti tat asaṅgatam tathā hi ayam vahni viṣaye anumāna pūrvaka bhāvanā balataḥ spaṣṭa vahni pratyayaḥ kim vahneḥ api utpannaḥ tathā bhūta bhāvanā mātrāt eva vā 
RKNĀ_19.10–19.12	 parathampakṣe visaṃvādaḥ ca bahulam upalabhyate iti yat uktam tat durbhāṣitam sākṣāt arthāt utpannasya api visaṃvāda sambhave anyasya api pratyakṣasya hastaka tyāga prasaṅgāt dvitīya pakṣe tu bhāvanā prakarṣa mātra jasya arthāt anutpannasya bahulam visaṃvāda upalambhe api bhāvanā arthābhyām sākṣāt utpannasya yogi pratyakṣasya api visaṃvāda sambhavaḥ iti sthavīyasī bhrāntiḥ 
RKNĀ_19.15^1	 nanu yadi indriyam vinā api bhāvanā arthābhyām yogi jñānam utpadyate tarhi parvate bhāvanā vahnibhyām vahni jñānam utpadyatām avisaṃvādi visaṃvādaḥ ca bahulam upalabhyate iti ced na sākṣāt vahneḥ utpāde sati visaṃvāda abhāvāt kevalam utpādaḥ eva durāpaḥ na hi vayam pramāṇa dṛṣṭa vastu bhāvanā sahitam manaḥ indiryam artha svarūpa grāhi jñānam janayati iti brūmaḥ api tu asat dṛṣṭi lakṣaṇa avidyā paripanthi kṣaṇika nairātmya lakṣaṇa sarva vastu tattva bhāvanā sahitam na ca vahni tvam sarva vastu tattvam kim tu kṣaṇika nairātmyam eva iti kṣaṇa bhaṅga prasādhanataḥ pratipāditam iti 
RKNĀ_19.15^2–19.28	 kim ca sva manīṣā parikalpitaḥ khalu ayam anumita bhāvita vahni viṣaya viśadaḥ pratyayaḥ na punar asya loke sambhavaḥ tathā hi niṣprayojanam anunmattaḥ na kaścid bhāvayati prayojanam ca śiśira bhara mantha kāya kāṇḍasya api dāha ādi mātram eva tat ca anumitena eva vahninā tad deśa upasarpaṇāt sidhyati anupasarpaṇe bhāvānā vaiyarthyam purastāt tu bhāvite parisphurati tat atha apekṣayā bhrāntiḥ prāsarpakasya iva ityādi upahāsyam api asya kṣata ātmanaḥ durnīti pūti gavī bhakṣaṇa adhmāta jarat gomāyoḥ udgāraḥ iva satām asahyaḥ yat api tatas anantaram āśaṅkya arthasya ālambana pratyaya tvam indriya apekṣi tvena vyāptam iti prasādhitam tat pūrvam eva pratyuktam tathā bhāvanayāḥ ca ityādi āśaṅkya arthasya ālambana pratyaya tvam aśakya avagamam iti yat uktam tat api asambaddham 
RKNĀ_19.31^1	 cakṣuḥ indriyasya api artham antareṇa dvi candra keśoṇḍukā ādau viśada bhrānta jñana janana sāmarthyam upalabdham iti artha sahitam api kevalam eva samartham atas ghaṭa ādeḥ api ālambana pratyaya tvam aśakya avagamam iti indriya pratyakṣam api pratihatam syāt iti tathā api ca ālambana pratyaya api te eva yujyante ityādiḥ na punar vikalpa nirmāṇa pratibandha tā iti paryantaḥ vyarthaḥ asmābhiḥ evaṃvidhasya prastute anabhyupagata tvāt atas eva tasmāt bhāvanā prakarśa mātraja tvāt artha avi abhicāra niyama abhāvāt viśada ābham api saṃśaya ākrānta tvāt apramāṇam apratyakṣam ca iti sāmpratam iti upasaṃhāraḥ api dhikkāraḥ 
RKNĀ_19.31^2	 sarveṣām eva hetūnām asiddha tvāt bhāvanā bala jasya arthāt api utpatteḥ indriya pratyakṣa vat sat artha prakāśanam buddheḥ svabhāvaḥ ityādi asmākam api manoharam bhāvanāyāḥ ca sāmānyena sphuṭa ābha jñāna hetu tvam sādhyate pramāṇa upanna catur ārya satya viṣaya niṣṭhāyām tu sāmarthyāt pratyakṣa pramāṇa hetutā api sādhyate atas eva kāminī pratibhāsasya apramāṇa tve api apratyakṣa tve api sphuṭa ābha tvasya sādhya dharma sāmānyasya sambhavāt na viruddhaḥ hetuḥ na api dṛṣṭāntasya sādhya śūnyatā iti na ca nairātmya dṛṣṭiḥ sambhavat bādhā arthāt utpatteḥ abhūta artha tva abhāvāt 
RKNĀ_20.11	 śruta anumita viṣayam pratyakṣam na sambhavati iti api ayuktam āgama anumānayoḥ dvividhaḥ viṣayaḥ grāhyaḥ adhyavaseyaḥ ca tatra grāhyaḥ su a ākāraḥ adhyavaseyaḥ tu pāramārthika vastu sva lakṣaṇa ātmā asya ca parokṣa tve anumāna sāmagrī sambhave anumāna viṣaya tvam pratyakṣa sāmagrī sambhave ca krameṇa pratyakṣa viṣaya tvam dṛṣṭam eva tat siddham iti ādi upasaṃhāraḥ api paryākulaḥ eva apramāṇa tvāt iti hetuḥ ca prathamaḥ asiddhaḥ bhāvanā bala jasya arthāt api utpatteḥ pramāṇa śakti sambhavāt indriya pratyakṣa vat bhāvanā bala ja tvāt iti dvitīyaḥ tu sandigha vyatireki tvāt anaikāntikaḥ tathā yathā anumita bhāvita vahni viṣaya viśada jñānam iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ api asambhavi iti pratipāditam bhavatu vā tathā api yogi jñānasya tena saha tulya hetu tvam asiddham tat dhi pramāṇa dṛṣṭa vastu bhāvanā mātra jam yogi jñānam tu avidyā pratipakṣa sarva vastu tattva bhāvanā viṣayābhyām utpannam iti mahāntam api viśeṣam asau durmati prapāta patitaḥ na avagāhataḥ iti upekṣaṇīyaḥ 
RKNĀ_20.21–20.23^1	 nyāya prakīrṇe tu mārgaḥ tāvat pramāṇa pariśuddhaḥ na bhavati iti uktam yat tat tad prasādhaka pramāṇena eva prayuktam yat ca api ca ityādi ārabhya yogi jñānam nirviṣayam prasaktam iti uktam tatra kā iyam nirviṣayatā nāma kim vikalpa ākāra nivṛttau nirākāra tā artha ākārāt visadṛśa ākāra tā atha tad ākāra tve api tad vastu saṃsparśitāḥ na tāvat prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ kṣamaḥ jñānasya nirākāra tā anupapatteḥ na api dvitīyaḥ kāminī ādi bhāvanāyāḥ tad ākārasya eva viśadasya darśanāt na ca tṛtīyaḥ artha samarpita ākāra saṃsparśam apāsya anyasya artha saṃsparsasya ayogāt tathā ca uktam arthena ghaṭayati enām 
RKNĀ_20.23^2	 ityādi tayoḥ ca eka tvena adhyavasāyāt bāhyaḥ eva pravṛtti nivṛttī vyāvahārikasya sphuṭībhāvaḥ api bahis abhimatasya paryante vikalpa upādeya kṣaṇasya eva sphuṭasya udayaḥ tāvatā eva sa viṣayaḥ tena sākṣātkṛtaḥ iti vyavahāraḥ kevalam arthāt api utpattau anyathā vyabhicārāt aprāmāṇyam na ca vikalpa upadarśitam api rūpam avastu jñāna ātmaka tvāt anātmaka tve prakāśa ayogāt tad bhāvanā eva ca artha bhāvanā tad sphuṭībhāvaḥ eva bāhya sphuṭībhāvaḥ prakāra antareṇa bāhya sparśa ayogāt etena yat pāramārthikam ityādi na sarvajña siddhiḥ iti paryantam prayuktam 
RKNĀ_21.6	 yat ca api ca ityādi na yuktam paśyāmaḥ iti paryantena dūṣaṇam uktam tat api asaṅgatam tathā hi yādṛśaḥ eva bhāvya grāhī pratyayaḥ prathamaḥ niranvayaḥ niruddhaḥ tādṛśa eva aparaḥ utpadyate iti niyama niścaya kāraṇam na kiñcid asti caṇḍa devatā sparśāt anyat kṣaṇika tvāt iti ced nanu kṣaṇika tvam sthāyitayā virudhyate na visadṛśa utpādena tat dhi prācīnam niranvaya nirodhe yathā sadṛśa kṣaṇa antaram ārabhate tathā sva hetu gata sāmarthya yogāt kārya utpāda anumeyāt yadi viśeṣa leśa viśiṣṭam kṣaṇa antaram utpādayati tadā na kācid kṣatiḥ na hi bhavataḥ iva bhāvasya api kṣaṇikatāyām pradveṣaḥ nāma tasmāt na kṣaṇika tva uttara viśiṣṭa kṣaṇa janaka tvayoḥ virodhaḥ iti na apārthakaḥ abhyāsaḥ 
RKNĀ_21.14	 yat ca idam kiñca ityādinā kṣaṇika tve cittam avikṣiptam āveditam tat api asādhu nairātmya ādi tattva parāṅmukhasya sarvasya eva vikṣipta tvāt bhāvanā balena tattva sākṣāt kāriṇaḥ samāhita tvāt atha ca tattva sākṣāt kriyā lābhāt grāhaka ākāra avagraha sambhavāt ca vyāvahārikam api vikṣiptam asti cittam yatas mama eva doṣa kṣayaḥ bhāvi iti mārgāmi āsa pravṛttiḥ abhyāhata iti paramārthataḥ prāpya ādīnām abhāve api tad saṃkalpasya eva anādya vidyā prabhāvitasya sarvatra pravartaka tvāt atas eva mārga satya abhyāsāt siddhaḥ sarvajñaḥ 
RKNĀ_21.21^1	 nyāya bhūṣaṇasya api yoga ācāra apekṣayā dūṣaṇam aprastutam bahis artha abhyupagamena eva sādhana prakramāt yat ca uktam tathā api atīta anāgata viṣaya tvam katham na hi asataḥ kaścid ākāraḥ asti iti tat etat prastāvān avagāhana phalam upayukta sarvajña adhikāreṇa hi sarva kṣaṇika nirātmaka vastu bhāvanā upakṣepaḥ na sarva sarvajña apekṣayā tatas atīta anāgatam apratīyamānam api na bādhakam tāvatā eva duḥkha nirodha siddheḥ parasmai ca kṣaṇika tva ādi niṣṭhakasya deśanā avatārāt na ca sarva sarvajña hastaka tyāgaḥ 
RKNĀ_21.21^2–22.1	 tathā hi catur ārya satya sākṣātkāra prāptau nirāvaraṇa antaḥkaraṇasya kāruṇya atiśayāt sarva ākāra para artha para tayā sakala gocara cāriṇi cetasi cira virūḍha utsāhasya tādṛś upāya viśeṣa adhigamaḥ bhavaṣyati yam anutiṣṭhataḥ tad utpattim antareṇa api devatā ādhipatyāt satya svapna vat pratiparamāṇu sarva viṣayam yathā deśa kāla ākāra pratyavasthā anukāri sphuṭataram jñānam udiyāt tadā na tāvat vastu vyabhicāra kṛtam visaṃvādi tvam vastūnām eva pratibhāsanāt utpatti sārūpyābhyām vedya sthitiḥ iti tu pṛthagjana apekṣayā yoginaḥ tu sārūpya mātreṇa eva grahaṇam iti nyāyaḥ yat vārttikam aviśuddha dhiyaḥ prati grāhya grāhaka cintā iyam acintyā yoginām gatiḥ iti 
RKNĀ_22.4	 tat evam bhāvi bhūtayoḥ ajanakayoḥ api yogi jñāne sphuraṇam abādhyam bhāvi bhūtayoḥ tarhi yadi svarūpasya sphuraṇam vartamāna tā eva syāt atha svarūpam asannihitam jñānam eva tat ākāram iti nirālambanam niyamena tat api na asti yasmāt asannihite api arthe bhāvanā balāt tad deśa kāla ākāra anukāri vijñānam katham anālambanam tathā tvena adhyavasāyāt ca adhyavasita kāla viśiṣṭasya eva satya svapna vat tasya prāpteḥ yat bhāṣyam yathā sa dṛṣṭaḥ śarad ādi kāla yuktaḥ tathā tasya na bādhita tvam tad kāla yuktaḥ tu na tena dṛṣṭaḥ tathā pratītau api na asti doṣaḥ jñāna mātrasya tu tattvataḥ sphuraṇāt ca na vartamāna tā prasaṅgaḥ saṅgataḥ tathā kṣaṇika tva pakṣe api ekatva adhyāropasāmarthyāt na vyavahārikam prati pramāṇasya kācid kṣatiḥ iti śāstre prapañcitam 
RKNĀ_22.17	 yat api kiñ ca idam api vaktum ucitam ityādi ārabhya bhāvanā bala jasya anumāna pūrvaka tve api pratyakṣa pūrvaka tve api vyabhicāra abhidhānam tad arthāt api bhāvanā bala jasya sākṣāt utpatti svīkārāt apahastitam yathā indriya jasya api dvi candra ādi jñānasya arthāt anutpatteḥ aprāmāṇyam artha indriyābhyām utpattau tu prāmāṇyam evam pramāṇa pūrvakasya api bhāvanā mātrāt utpannasya aprāmāṇyam bhāvanā arthābhyām utpannasya tu prāmāṇyam 
RKNĀ_22.22	 yadi yogi jñānasya arthāt utpattiḥ pramāṇa pūrvakatva apekṣayā na kiñcid prayojanam iti ced na deśa kāla vastu viśeṣam apāsya sāmāneyana sarva diś kāla varti vastu mātram kṣaṇika nirātmakam iti aniścaye mahā prayāsa sādhya puruṣa āyuṣa vyāpinyām bhāvanāyām eva pravṛtteḥ abhāvāt na ca hālikaḥ havya aśanam anumāya sphuṭīkaroti yena pratyakṣa antara tva prasaṅgaḥ asāmarthya vaiyarthyābhyām tad asambhava pratipādanāt 
RKNĀ_22.27	 yat api uktam yoginaḥ jñānam indriya jñanāt abhinnam bhinnam vā tatra prathama pakṣe tāvat na vastu doṣaḥ tādṛś puruṣa viśeṣasya siddha tvāt vyavasthā dūṣaṇam api na asti sādhya tayā eva tādṛś daśā viśeṣasya loka atikrānta atiśayasya parama puruṣa artha rūpasya sādhana viśeṣa pratipādanāya pṛthagjana sādhāraṇa indriya jñānāt bhedena nirdeśāt parama puruṣa artha viṣaya tva abhāvāt eva ca rasāyana ādi saṃskāra jasya api jñānasya na pratyakṣa antara tā bheda pakṣe api na tāvat sthairya itara sphuraṇa kṛta upālambha sambhavaḥ indriya jñānena api vastu sarva ātmanā gṛhṇatā truṭyat rūpasya eva grahaṇāt adhyavasāyaḥ hi pūrvam durllabhaḥ idānīm tu bhāvanā bala nirdalita avidye citta santāne saḥ api indriya jñānena janyate iti viśeṣaḥ 
RKNĀ_23.3–23.7	 nanu yoginaḥ manaḥ vijñāna indriya jñānābhyām paśyate ākāra dvaya sphuraṇa prasaṅgaḥ iti ced satyam satya jñāna ākāraḥ tāvat vastunaḥ na bhinna deśaḥ anyatara bhrānti prasaṅgāt atas tau ākārau apratimau kayā gatyā sphurataḥ iti kaḥ nirṇetum kṣamaḥ yat āha acintyā yoginām gatiḥ iti sarvathā tu na yogi jñānasya kṣatiḥ iti siddham tat evam kāraṇa anupalambhāt api na sarvajña tā bhāvaḥ 
RKNĀ_23.9	 nanu yadi nāma yuṣmad abhimatasya anumānasya na bādhakam tathā api asati eva anumānam bādhakam tathā hi śakyam idam abhidhātum sugataḥ asarva jñaḥ jñeya tvāt prameya tvāt sattvāt puruṣa tvāt vakṛtvāt idriya ādimattvāt ityādi rathyā puruṣa vat tathā ca bṛhaṭṭīkāḥ yasya jñeya prameya tva vastu sattva ādi lakṣaṇāḥ nihantum hetavaḥ śaktāḥ kaḥ nu tam kalpayiṣyati kārikā api pratyakṣa ādyavi saṃvādi prameya tva ādi yasya ca sadbhāva vāraṇe śaktam kaḥ nu tam kalpayiṣyati 
RKNĀ_23.21–23.24	 atra ucyate kim ete jñeya tva ādayaḥ sarvajña tvena sākṣāt viruddhāḥ paramparayā vā aviruddha vidhāne pratiṣedha ayogāt sa ca sākṣāt virodhaḥ paraspara parihāra sthiti lakṣaṇaḥ vā bhāva abhāva vat saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇaḥ vā dahana tuhina vat iti na tāvat ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ yat vyavacchedana antarīyakaḥ yasya paricchedaḥ tayoḥ eva paraspara parihāra sthiti lakṣaṇaḥ virodhaḥ na ca jñeya tva ādi sarvajña tva vyavacchedena sthitam kim tarhi ajñeya tva ādi vyaca= chedena tathā sarvajña tvam asarvajña tva vyavacchedena na tu jñeya tva vyavacchedena 
RKNĀ_23.28–23.32	 na api dvitīyaḥ virodhaḥ yasya hi avikala kāraṇasya bhavataḥ yat sannidhānāt abhāvaḥ tayoḥ eva saha anavasthāna lakṣaṇaḥ virodhaḥ na ca sarvajña tvam prāk pravṛttam avikala kāraṇam dṛṣṭam yena paścāt jñeya tva ādi sadbhāve nirvartate iti syāt tathā tve sati deśa ādi niṣedhaḥ eva bhavet na tu sarvathā ucchedaḥ iti na ca paramparayā virodhaḥ sa hi bhavat niṣedhyasya sarvajña tvasya vyāpaka viruddha tvāt kāraṇa viruddha tvāt kārya viruddha tvāt svabhāva viruddha kārya tvāt vyāpaka viruddha kārya tvāt kāraṇa viruddha kārya tvāt kārya viruddha kārya tvāt svabhāva viruddha vyāpta tvāt vyāpaka viruddha vyāpta tvāt kāraṇa viruddha vyāpta tvāt kārya viruddha vyāpta tvāt vā bhavet tatra sarvajña tvasya asattvāt vyāpaka kāraṇa kāryāṇām asiddheḥ tad viruddha kārya vyāpya abhāvāt na prameya tva ādayaḥ sarvajña tvena paramparayā api viruddhāḥ 
RKNĀ_24.5–24.13	 nanu vaktṛ tvam virudhyate eva sarva viṣaya nirvikalpa jñāna viruddha vikalpa kārya tvāt vaktṛ tvasya na etat yuktam sa vikalpa avikalpayoḥ yugapada vṛtteḥ vikalpa tvena sarvajñasya avirodhāt kaḥ tarhi pṛthagjanāt asya bhedaḥ iti ced ucyate yathā māyā kāraḥ nirmita aśva ādi viṣayam vijñānam nirviṣaya tvena niścinu an= abhrāntaḥ tad anyasmāt ca śreṣṭhaḥ tathā bhagavān api śuddha laukika vikalpa sammukhībhāve api na bhrāntaḥ na api pṛthagjana samānaḥ iti tatas ca nirvikalpaka sarvajña jñāna vikalpayoḥ virodha abhāvāt vaktṛ tvam sarvajña tvena saha aviruddham eva etena ed api nirastam yat āha kāśika ākāraḥ samādheḥ vyutthāya upadekṣyate iti ced na vyutthitasya hi abhilāpinī pratītiḥ bhrānta bhāṣitam apramāṇam bhavet iti 
RKNĀ_24.15^1	 yat api uktam bṛhaṭṭīkāyām yadā ca upadiśet ekam kiñcid sāmānya vaktṛ vat eka deśa jña gītam tat na syāt sarvajña bhāṣitam tat api nirastam vikalpena ekasya kasyacid āmukhīkṛtvā upadeśe api nirvikalpena sarvam avabudhyamānasya vacanānām sarvajña bhāṣita tvāt eva yat punar kārikāyām uktam sānnidhya mātrataḥ tasya puṃsaḥ cintāmaṇeḥ iva niścaranti yathākāmām kuḍya ādibhyaḥ api deśanāḥ evam ādi ucyamānam hi śraddadhānasya śobhate kuḍya ādi niḥsṛta tvāt tu na āśvāsaḥ deśanāsu naḥ kin nu buddha praṇītāḥ syuḥ kim vā kaiścid durātmabhiḥ adṛśyaiḥ vipralambha artham piśāca ādibhiḥ īritāḥ bṛhaṭṭīkāyām api tasmin dhyāna samādhi sthe cintā ratna vat āsthite 
RKNĀ_24.15^2	 niścaranti yathākāmam kuḍya ādibhyaḥ api deśanāḥ tābhiḥ jijñāsitān arthān sarvān jānanti mānavāḥ hitāni ca yathāyogam kṣipram āsādayanti te ityādi kīrtamānam tu śraddadhānasya śobhate vayam aśraddadhānāḥ tu ye yuktīḥ arthayāmahe kuḍya ādi niḥsṛtānām ca na syāt āpta upadiṣṭa tā viśvāsaḥ ca na tāsu syāt kena etāḥ kīrtitāḥ iti kin nu buddha praṇītāḥ syuḥ kim vā brāhmaṇa vañcakaiḥ krīḍadbhiḥ upadiṣṭāḥ syuḥ dūra stha prati śabdakaiḥ kim vā kṣudra piśāca ādyaiḥ adṛṣṭaiḥ parikalpitāḥ tasamān na tāsu viśvāsaḥ kartavyaḥ prājña mānibhiḥ etat api anabhyupagamena eva nirastam śuddha laukika vikalpa saṃmukhībhāvena eva tasya deśaka tva abhyupagamāt iti 
RKNĀ_25.11^1	 atha vā yathā cakrasya uparate api daṇḍa preraṇā vyāpāre pūrva āvega vaśāt bhramaṇam evam bhagavati pratyasta mita samasta vikalpa jāle api sthite yadi pūrva praṇidhāna ahita satata an ābhoga vāhinī deśanā syāt tadā kaḥ virodhaḥ vivakṣā abhāve katham vacana pravṛttiḥ iti na vaktavyam tad abhāve api nidrāṇasya tad tad pravyakta vacana sandarśanāt vacana mātrasya vivakṣayā vyāpteḥ abhāvāt tasmāt yathā pūrva abhyāsataḥ jhaṭiti prabodhitasya ariṇā prahāra ādi dānena anurūpaḥ eva prakramaḥ śastra uddharaṇa ādikaḥ tathā sarva vedinaḥ api sakalāḥ kalāḥ iti anākulam yat āha alaṅkāraḥ śatru sānnidhya mātreṇa pravartante avikalpataḥ 
RKNĀ_25.11^2	 prāk eva tad nirākāri prakramāḥ kopa nirmitāḥ yat punar uktam piśāca ādi kṛta śaṅkayā na atra āśvāsaḥ satām yuktaḥ iti tat asaṅgatam yatas sambhinna ālāpa hiṃsā ādi kutsita artha upadarśanam krīḍā śīla piśāca ādeḥ kāryam tāsu na vidyate pramāṇa dvaya saṃvādi matam tad viṣaye akhile yasya bādhā pramāṇa abhyām aṇīyasi api na īkṣate yathā atyanta rokṣe api na pūrva apara bādhitam karuṇā ādi guṇa utpatteḥ sarva puṃsām pravartakam sarva anuśaya saṃdoha pratipakṣa abhidhāyakam nirvāṇa gara dvāra kapāṭa puṭa bhedam tat ced krīḍana śīlānām rakṣasām vā vacaḥ bhavet te eva santu sambuddhāḥ sarva tad lakṣaṇa sthiteḥ 
RKNĀ_26.3–26.9	 na ca nāmni vivādaḥ na ca nāma nivṛttau vastu nirvartate pratyuta vedasya eva krīḍana śīla piśāca ādi praṇīta tvam yuktam sambhāvayitum yena go śava ādiṣu yogeṣu agamyā gamana ādayaḥ asatya samudācārāḥ saṃprakāśitāḥ loka prasiddhiḥ ca trayaḥ vedasya kartāraḥ muni bhaṇḍa niśācarāḥ iti alam ati nirbandhena nanu sarvajña tvam vīta rāga ādi tvena vyāptam iṣyate tad viruddham ca rāga ādi yogi tvam tat kāryam ca vacanam tat etat vyāpaka viruddha kārya bhūtam vacanam sarvajña abhāvam sādhayati paramparayā viruddha tvāt iti ced na rāga ādīnām vacasaḥ ca kārya kāraṇa bhāva asiddheḥ tathā hi vacana viśeṣaḥ rāga ādi kāryam yaḥ rāgeṇa eva janitaḥ vacana mātram vā 
RKNĀ_26.13^1	 tatra na tāvat prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ tādṛśasya vacanasya niścaya upāya asambhavāt asabhya maithuna ācāra prakāśakam vacanam tat kāryam iti ced na abhiprāyasya durlakṣya tvāt viraktaḥ api rakta vat ceṣṭate raktaḥ api virakta vat iti abhiprāyaḥ durbodaḥ tatas ca viśiṣṭa vyavahārasya sāṃkaryeṇa na tatra ekāntena rāga anumānam yujyate na api vacana mātram rāga ādi kāryam asaṃmukhībhūta rāga ādayaḥ api hi sva abhimata devatā stuti vidhāne mātrā ādi guru jana sambhāṣaṇa ādau ca vacana mātram uccārayantaḥ samupalabhyante na ca yat yad abhāve bhavati tasya tat kāryatā ucyate atiprasaṅgāt 
RKNĀ_26.13^2	 rāga ādi yogya tā tarhi vacasaḥ kāraṇam tayā vinā upala khaṇḍala ādau vacanasya adarśanāt iti ced na karaṇa guṇa vaktu kāmate hi vacanasya hetuḥ tad abhāvāt eva upala khaṇḍala ādau nivartate na rāga ādi yogya tāyāḥ abhāvāt yadi kāraṇa guṇa ādi sakala tad anya kāraṇa bhāve api rāga ādi yogya tā bhāvāt na utpadyate vacanam iti sidhyet tasyāḥ kāraṇa tvam upala khaṇḍala ādau tu vaktu kāma tā na asti tat katham tad kāraṇa tvam vacasām iti evam tarhi vaktu kāma tā eva rāgaḥ astu iṣṭa tvāt na kiñcid bādhitam syāt nāmni vivāda abhāvāt paramārthataḥ punar nitya sukha ātmā ātmīya darśana ākṣiptam sa āśrava viṣayam cetasaḥ abhiṣvaṅgam rāgam āhuḥ 
RKNĀ_26.28–27.1	 niṣpanna sarva sampatteḥ vivakṣā api na yujyate iti ced adoṣaḥ ayam para artha tva ādi vivakṣāyāḥ vīta rāge artha asaṅga abhāvāt kathm parārthā api pravṛttiḥ iti ced na āsaṅgam antareṇa karuṇayā api pravṛtteḥ sā eva rāgaḥ iti ced iṣṭa tvāt adoṣaḥ rāgasya tu svarūpam uktam kāruṇikasya api niṣphala ārambhaḥ na yuktaḥ iti ced na para arthasya eva phalatvāt iṣṭa lakṣaṇa tvāt phalasya iti yat kiñcid etat nanu nirvikalpasya bhagavataḥ katham tasyām avasthāyām karuṇā sambhavaḥ duḥkha vikalpa prabhavā hi karuṇā iti anvaya vyatirekābhyām anya tvena niścitam 
RKNĀ_27.3	 tatas ca kāraṇa abhāvāt katham kārya sambhavaḥ iti ced na yathā kumbhakāra nivṛttau api sva santāna mātra bhāvinī ghaṭa ādi sthitiḥ tathā utthāpaka vikalpa abhāve api samanantara pratyaya balāt anālambana karuṇā pravṛtteḥ avārya tvāt yat āhuḥ guruvaḥ sattāra upakṛtaḥ api bhāvana vaśāt kāṭhinyam āpad tathā śaithilye api yathā asya duḥkha hataye sāndraḥ tathā eva śramaḥ utpāde tu phalasya hetu niyamaḥ no tu prabandha sthitau tasmāt duḥkha dṛśaḥ kṣaye api vilasat maitrī a ādaye asmai namaḥ etena etat api nirastam yat āha kārikāyām rāga ādi rahite ca asamin nirvyāpāre vyavasthite deśanā anya praṇītā eva syāt ṛte pratyavekṣaṇāt 
RKNĀ_27.13–27.15	 nanu yadi nāma eva vaktṛ tvam sarvajña tvena saha aviruddham deha indriya buddhi ādi yogi tvam tu viruddham eva sarvajña tā vyāpaka vīta rāga tva viruddha rāga ādi kāraṇa tvāt deha ādīnām tatas ca pratiṣedhya vyāpaka viruddha kāraṇa upalambhāt sarvajña abhāvaḥ iti ced ucyate deha ādīnām hetu tve api na eṣām kevalānām sahakāri mātrāṇām ātma abhiniveśa lakṣaṇa upādāna kāraṇa vikalānām rāga ādi janaka tvam iti agamakāḥ eva deha ādayaḥ sarvajña abhāvasya tasmāt jñeya tva ādīnām api asāmarthyāt na para parikalpita anumānataḥ api sarvajña abhāvaḥ 
RKNĀ_27.20	 na api sva vikalpitam śābda ādikam bhagavataḥ bādhakam tathā hi yadi api teṣām sati prāmāṇye anumānaḥ eva antarbhāvaḥ anantarbhāve ca aprāmāṇyam eva iti sthūlam dūṣaṇam asti tathā api tad prāmāṇyam abhyupagamya api brūmaḥ yat tāvat pauruṣeya vacanam tad apramāṇam eva bhavatām na ca vaidikam kiñcid vacanam sarva narā sarvajña tva pratipādakam upalabhyate pratyuta nimitta nāmni śākhā antare sphuṭataram eva sarvajñaḥ pratipāditaḥ tathā hi sa vetti viśvam na ca tasya vettā ityādinā ca sarvajñaḥ vede pratipāditaḥ na api upamānāt tad abhāvaḥ sidhyati tathā hi smaryamāṇam eva gavā ādi vastu puras varti gavaya ādi sādṛśya upādhi gavā ādi upādhi vā sādṛśyam upamānena pratīyate iti sthitiḥ na ca sarvajña santāna vartīni cetāṃsi kenacid sarvajñena anubhūtāni yatas smaraṇena viṣayīkriyeran para citta vitteḥ ayogāt 
RKNĀ_28.1–28.6	 yat punar uktam kumārilena narān dṛṣṭvā tu asravajñān sarvān eva adhunātanān tad sādṛśya upamānena śeṣa asarvajña niścayaḥ tat api ayuktam adhunātana sarvajña tvā niścayāt niścaye ca ātmani eva sarvajña tva abhyupagama prasaṅgāt na api arthāpattiḥ bādhikā yatas dṛṣṭaḥ śrutaḥ vā arthaḥ anyathā na upapadyate iti adṛṣṭa artha parikalpanam arthāpattiḥ ucyate na ca asarvajña tvam antareṇa sarva nareṣu kaścid arthaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ śrutaḥ vā na upapadyate yatas tad artha āpattyā parikalpyeta nanu saṃsārasya tāvat anādi tvam pramāṇena pratītam tat ca na sarvajñena jñāyate tad jñāna avadheḥ parastāt asattve anādita akṣati prasaṅgāt tat anyathā anupapadyamānam sarva bhāvānām anādi tvam sarvajña abhāvam sādhayati iti ced 
RKNĀ_28.12	 ucyate upayukta sarvajña apekṣayā tāvat idam adūṣaṇam tasya anādi tva ajñāne api upayukta sarvajña tva avyāhateḥ sarva sarvajñasya api abhāve sādhye asamartheyam arthāpattiḥ tathā hi yathā saṃsārasya anādi tve pūrva pūrva vastu sattāyāḥ anavadhi tvam tathā sarvajña jñānasya api pūrva pūrva vastu sattā vyāpaka tvena anavadhi prasaratā iti ajñātasya ekasya api vastunaḥ anavasthiteḥ sati api sarvajñe anādi tvam upapadyamānam na sarvajña abhāvam ākṣipati tatas ca arthāpattiḥ api na sarvajñasya bādhikā 
RKNĀ_28.18	 na ca abhāva pramāṇa bādhyaḥ sarvajñaḥ pramāṇa pañcaka nivṛttiḥ abhāva pramāṇam iṣyate tatra nivṛttiḥ iti prasajya vṛttyā pramāṇa anutpatti mātram abhipretam atha vā paryudāsa vṛttyā vastu antaram vastu antaram api jaḍa rūpam jñāna rūpam vā jñānam api jñāna mātram eka jñāna saṃsargi vastu jñānam vā iti vikalpāḥ 
RKNĀ_28.22	 tatra na tāvat nivṛtti mātram abhāva pramāṇam upapadyate tat khalu nikhila śakti vikala tayā na kiñcid yat ca na kiñcid tat katham prameyam paricchindyāt tad viṣayam vā vijñānam janayet pratītam vā tat katham iti sarvam andhakāra nartanam yathā uktam na hi abhāvaḥ kasyacid pratipattiḥ pratipatti hetuḥ vā tasya api vā katham pratipattiḥ iti 
RKNĀ_28.27	 na api vastu antara tā pakṣe jaḍa rūpaḥ pramāṇa abhāvaḥ saṅgacchate tasya prameya pariccheda ayogāt paricchedasya jñāna dharma tvāt na api jñāna mātra svabhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ deśa kāla svabhava viprakṛṣṭasya api tatas abhāva prasaṅgāt tad apekṣayā api vijñāna mātra tvāt tasya atha eka jñāna saṃsargi svabhāvaḥ anumanyate tadā kṣatam abhāva pramāṇa pratyāśayā adhyakṣa viśeṣasya eva abhāva pramāṇa nāma karaṇāt tasya ca asmābhiḥ dṛśya anupalambha ākhya sādhana tvena svīkṛta tvāt dṛśya anupalambhaḥ ca bhagavat abhāva sādhane asamarthaḥ iti pūrvam eva āveditam 
RKNĀ_29.1	 kim ca kaḥ punar ayam pramāṇa abhāvaḥ abhimataḥ bhavatām sva pramāṇa gaṇa nivṛttiḥ atha sarva prāṇi gaṇa pramāṇa nivṛttiḥ tatra sva pramāṇa gaṇa nivṛttiḥ vyabhicāriṇī tasyām satyām api vyavahitasya arthasya anapahnava tvāt para pramāṇa nivṛttiḥ tu asarva vidaḥ asiddhāḥ yat āha sarva adṛṣṭiḥ ca sandigdhā svādṛṣṭiḥ vyabhicāriṇī vindhya adri randhra dūrvā ādeḥ adṛṣṭau api sattvataḥ iti tat evam na abhāva pramāṇataḥ api sarvajña niṣedhaḥ iti sthitam 
RKNĀ_29.8	 nanu tathā api sat vyavahāra artham sādhakam api asya na vidyate tathā hi sarva vidaḥ atīndriya tvāt na tāvat asmad ādi pratyakṣam asya sādhakam yathā ca asmābhiḥ asau na upalabhyate tathā asmad jātīyaiḥ api apratyakṣa svabhāva niyamāt na ca ayam kāla antare abhūt iti ca kalpanā yujyate yathā hi kāla tvāt idānīntana kāla vat iti anena anumānena nirākartum śakyate na tathā sādhayitum kārikā sarvajña kalpanā tu anyaiḥ vede vā apauruṣeya tā tulya vat kalpyate yena tena idam saṃpradhāryate sarvajñaḥ dṛśyate tāvat na idānīm asmad ādibhiḥ nirākaraṇa vat śakyā na ca āsīt iti kalpanā iti na api anumānataḥ sarvajña siddhiḥ tad pratibaddha liṅgā niścayāt 
RKNĀ_29.19	 kim ca sarvajña sattā sādhane sarvaḥ hetuḥ trayīm doṣa jātim na ativartate asiddha tvam viruddha tvam anaikāntika tvam ca iti tathā hi sarvajñe dharmaṇi kriyamāṇe na tad dharmaḥ hetuḥ siddhaḥ tasya eva dharmiṇaḥ sādhya tvena asiddha tvāt siddhau vā vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt asarva jñe dharmiṇi na sarvajña siddhiḥ hetoḥ sarvajña viparīta sādhana tvena viruddha tvāt na api sarvajñā sarva jña dharmaḥ hetuḥ tasya anaikāntika tvāt tasmāt na anumānataḥ api sarvajña siddhiḥ kārikā dṛṣṭaḥ na ca eka deśaḥ asti liṅgam yaḥ vā anumāpayet iti 
RKNĀ_29.27	 na api āgama gamyaḥ āgamaḥ hi dvividhaḥ pauruṣeyaḥ nityaḥ ca tatra pauruṣeyaḥ api āgamaḥ tadīyaḥ vā tatra pramāṇam nara antara praṇītaḥ vā na tāvat tadīyaḥ anyonya saṃśraya āpatteḥ tathā hi āgamasya sarvajña ukta tve prāmāṇyam asya ca prāmāṇye sati asmāt sarvajña siddhiḥ iti nara antara praṇītaḥ tu pramāṇa tvena anabhimataḥ eva iti atas api na sarvajña siddhiḥ 
RKNĀ_30.1	 kim ca sarvajña praṇītāt vacanāt sarvajña siddhau kim aparāddham sva vacanena yena atas api asau na gamyeta na api nitya āgama gamyaḥ sarvajñaḥ tathāvidhasya sarvajña pratipādakasya nitya āgamasya abhāvāt yat ca upaniṣad ādau sarvajña pratipādaka vākyam tasya anya artha tvam draṣṭavyam na ca nitya vākyasya anitya sarvajña tva pratipādaka tvam nirviṣaya tu a prasaṅgāt 
RKNĀ_30.5	 kim ca yadi aṅgīkṛtaḥ nitya āgamaḥ kim sarvajña kalpanayā nityaḥ eva āgamaḥ dharme pramāṇam bhaviṣyati kārikā na ca āgamena sarvajñaḥ tadīye anyonya saṃśrayāt nara antara praṇītasya prāmāṇyam gamyate katham na ca api evam paraḥ nityaḥ śakyaḥ labdhum iha āgamaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ ced arthavāda tvam tad pare syāt anitya tā āgamasya ca nitya tve siddhe tad kalpanā vṛthā yatas tam pratipatsyante dharmam eva tatas narāḥ bṛhaṭṭīkā api na ca āgama vidhiḥ kaścid nityaḥ sarvajña bodhakaḥ ityādi saptacatvāriṃśat ślokāḥ sa prapañcam etam artham pratipādayanti tat evam āgamataḥ api na sarvajña siddhiḥ 
RKNĀ_30.18–30.24	 na api upamāna pramāṇa samadhigamyaḥ upamānam hi sadṛśa grahaṇana āntarīyaka pravṛttikam asannikṛṣṭa artha gocaram yathā gavana grahaṇa dvāreṇa goḥ smaraṇam na ca sarvajña sadṛśaḥ kaścid asti kārikā sarvajña sadṛśam kañcid yadi paśyema samprati upamānena sarvajñam jānīyāmaḥ tatas vayam na api arthāpattitaḥ sarvajña siddhiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ śrutaḥ vā arthaḥ anyathā na upapadyate iti adṛṣṭa artha parikalpanam arthāpatti lakṣaṇam na ca atra pramāṇa pratītam kiñcid vastu asti yat sarvajñam anatareṇa anupapadyamānam tat sattām upanayet tat na artha āpattiḥ api sarvajña sādhanī 
RKNĀ_30.27	 na ca pramāṇa pañcaka abhāva svabhāvāt abhāva pramāṇāt asya siddhiḥ vastu abhāva sādhana tvāt asya pratyutā ayam eva asya abhāvam sādhayati iti pratipāditam yat api idam kārikā bṛhaṭtīkayoḥ ekaṣaṣṭyā ślokaiḥ sarvajña siddhaye bauddhasya sādhanam āśaṅkya dūṣitam tat api ghṛṇā akaram iti grantha vistara bhayāt na likhitam 
RKNĀ_31.1–31.6	 tathā hi etāni kila saugataiḥ sarvajña sādhanāya sādhanāni abhidhīyante sarvajñaḥ asti iti satyam sarvajña ukta tvāt dharma abhyupadeśaka tvāt buddhaḥ sarvajñaḥ iti cira pravṛtta dṛḍha smṛteḥ prathamataram aśeṣa śiṣya jana vargasya anekavidha citta caitta ādi parijñānāt sakala padārtha rāśi tattva upadeśāt iti tasmāt sthitam etat na atīndriya darśī sākṣāt asti api tu nitya vacana dvāreṇa eva tasya darśanam iti tat evam sarvathā sarvajña sādhaka pramāṇāsa bhavāt ayuktaḥ bauddhānām sarvajñe sat vyavahāraḥ iti 
RKNĀ_31.9	 atra ucyate anumānāt anyatas asiddhau siddha sādhanam anumānāt api iti asiddham anumānasya pūrvam ukta tvāt tad pratibaddha liṅgā niścayāt ityādi dūṣaṇa prabandhaḥ api prativyūḍhaḥ iti upayukta sarva jñaḥ tāvat trailokya ālokaḥ siddhaḥ sarva sarvjña pakṣe api idam sādhanam yat pramāṇa saṃvādi niścita artha vacanam tat sākṣāt paramparayā vā tad artha sākṣāt kāri jñāna pūrvakam yathā dahanaḥ dāhakaḥ iti vacanam pramāṇa saṃvādi niścita artha vacanam ca idam kṣaṇikāḥ sarvajña saṃskārāḥ iti arthataḥ kārya hetuḥ na asya asiddhiḥ sarva bhāva kṣaṇa bhaṅga prasādhanāt asya vacanasya satya artha tvāt na api virodhaḥ sa pakṣe bhāvāt na ca anaikāntikaḥ vacana mātrasya saṃśaya viparyāsa pūrvaka tve api pramāṇa niścita artha vacanasya sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa tad artha sākṣāt kāri jñāna pūrvaka tvāt anyathā niyamena pramāṇa saṃvāda ayogāt 
RKNĀ_31.22	 ayam ca bhāṣya kārīyaḥ sarva sarvajña prasādhaka prayogaḥ paṇḍita jita aribhiḥ prapañcitaḥ iti tatas eva pracayataḥ aavadhārya iti durvāra prativādi vikramam anādṛtya pramā prauḍhitaḥ sarvajñaḥ jagat eka cakṣuḥ udagāt eṣa prabhāvaḥ atra ca sambuddha sthiti medinī kula gireḥ asmad guroḥ kin tu ayam saṃkṣepaḥ mama ratna kīrti kṛtinaḥ tad vistara trāsinaḥ viśvam astu śubhāt asmāt yatheccham ratimat mataḥ mañjuvajraḥ ca paryante tad pādam sat phala pradam ahan ca mañjuvajraḥ syām mañjughoṣaḥ atha mañju vāc mañjuśrīḥ vādirāṇma mañjukumāraḥ jina dhūrdharaḥ 
RKNĀ_32.4–32.9	 om namaḥ tārāyai sūkta ratna āśraya tvena jita ratna ākarāt idam guroḥ vāc ambudheḥ smartum kiñcid ākṛṣya likhyate rītiḥ sudhā nidhiḥ iyam sattame madhya vartini vidveṣiṇi viṣa jvālā kiñcid jñe tu na kiñcana iha ete naiyāyika ādayaḥ vivāda padasya kṣitidhara ādeḥ svarūpa upādāna upakaraṇa saṃpradāna prayojana vibhāga pravīṇam sarvajña tā ādi guṇa viśiṣṭam puruṣa viśeṣam icchanti yat āhuḥ ekaḥ vibhuḥ sarva vid eka buddhi samāśrayaḥ śāśvataḥ īśvara ākhyaḥ pramāṇam iṣtaḥ jagataḥ vidhātā svarga apavarga arthibhiḥ arthanīyaḥ iti sa ca katham sidhyati iti paryanuyuktāḥ sādhanam idam ācakṣate vivāda adhyāsitam buddhimat hetukam kāryatvāt yat kāryam tad buddhim adhetukam yathā ghaṭaḥ kāryam ca idam tasmāt buddhim adhetukam iti 
RKNĀ_32.21–32.24	 hetoḥ parokṣa artha pratipādaka tvam anubhūteṣu hetvābhāseṣu na śakyam āvedayitum hetvābhāsāḥ ca pañca yathā uktam savyabhicāra viruddha prakaraṇa sama sādhya sama atīta kālāḥ iti tatra na tāvat ayam sādhya samaḥ hetuḥ asiddhaḥ hi sādhya samaḥ kathyate sa ca saṃkṣepataḥ vibhajyamānaḥ dvidhā vyavatiṣṭhate āśraya asiddha tvāt vā asiddhaḥ yathā surabhi gagana aravindam aravinda tvāt iti sati api ca āśraye pramāṇena sambandha asiddheḥ asiddhaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ sāvayava tvāt iti na ca ābhyām prakārābhyām prastutasya hetoḥ asiddhiḥ asti kṣmāruha ādau dharmiṇi pramāṇa sam adhigate kāryatvasya sādhanasya pramāṣ pratīta tvāt cira utpanna parvata ādau ca dharmiṇi kāryatvam sāvayava tvena hetunā boddhavyam tat yathā vivāda padam kāryam sāvayava tvāt yat sa avayavam tat kāryam yathā vastram tathā ca idam tasmāt kāryam iti 
RKNĀ_33.10	 nanu sāvayava tvena hetunā dravyāṇām eva kārya tvam sidhyati na tu tad samavetānām guṇa karma ādīnām teṣām avayava sambandha abhāvāt iti ced satyam teṣām kārya guṇa ādi tvena hetu antareṇa kāryatvam adhigantavyam tathā hi janma bhājaḥ vivāda adhyāsita nitya itara samavāyinaḥ guṇa ādayaḥ kārya guṇa ādi tvāt yaḥ yaḥ kārya guṇa ādiḥ sa sarvaḥ tathā yathā ghaṭa ādi rūpa ādiḥ tathā ca ete tasmāt janma bhājaḥ iti kāryañca na sva kāraṇa samavāyaḥ sāmānya viśeṣaḥ vā boddhavyam yena asya pradhvaṃsa avyāpaka tvāt bhāga asiddha tā syāt kim tu kāraṇa adhīna svarūpa mātram tat ca śabda ādiṣu iva pradhvaṃsa ādau api pratyakṣeṇa adhigatam iti na tāvat ayam asiddhaḥ hetuḥ na api viruddhaḥ tathā hi yaḥ vipakṣaḥ eva vartate sa khalu sādhya viparyaya vyāpteḥ sādhya viruddham sādhayan viruddhaḥ abhidhīyate yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti na ca ayam tathā prasiddha kartṛkeṣu ghaṭa ādiṣu sa pakṣeṣu sadbhāva darśanāt 
RKNĀ_33.24	 nanu buddhimat pūrvaka tve sādhye siddha sādhanam abhimatam hi pareṣām api karma ja tvam kārya jātasya karmaṇaḥ ca cetanā ātmaka tvāt cetanā hetuka tvāt vā tad hetuka tvam ca jagataḥ sarvajña pūrvaka tve tu sādhye vyāptiḥ svapne api na upalabdhā dṛṣṭāntaḥ ca sādhya hīnaḥ kulāla ādīnām asarvajña tvāt viruddha tā ca hetoḥ asarvajña pūrvaka tvena eva kumbha ādau kāryatvasya vyāpteḥ upalabdheḥ na ca upalabdhimat pūrvakatva mātram sādhana viṣayaḥ tad viśeṣasya tu sarvajña pūrvaka tvasya atad viṣayasya api tatas siddhiḥ iti sāmpratam tathā hi yadi asau viśeṣaḥ na sādhana viṣayaḥ katham atas tad siddhiḥ sidhyan vā katham aviṣayaḥ viṣayaḥ ced katham ananvaya doṣam na spṛśet iti ced 
RKNĀ_33.32^1	 ucyate sāmānya mātra vyāptau api antar bhāvita viśeṣasya sāmānyasya pakṣa dharma tā vaśena sādhya dharmiṇī anumānāt viśeṣa viṣayam anumānam bhavati eva itarathā sarva anumāna uccheda prasaṅgāt tathā hi vahni anumānam api na sāmānya mātra viṣayam tasya prāk eva siddha tvāt na api tad viśiṣṭa giri gocaram vahni tva sāmānyasya tad sambandha abhāvena tad viśeṣaṇa tva anupapatteḥ itarathāḥ go tva samavāyāt iva gāvaḥ śābaleya ādayaḥ parvataḥ api vahni tva samavāyāt vahniḥ prasajyeta asti eva gireḥ vahni tvena saṃyukta samavāyaḥ sambandhaḥ iti ced tarhi na apratipadya parvata saṃyuktam vahni viśeṣam asau śakya pratipattiḥ iti vahni viśeṣasya api ananumānam tathā ca ananvaya doṣa prasaṅgaḥ indriya anumāne api ayam eva nyāyaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ yathā indriya lakṣaṇa karaṇa viśeṣa siddhiḥ 
RKNĀ_33.32^2	 tathā hi tatra api na indriya karaṇikā kācid kriyā upalabdhāḥ na khalu cchid ādyaḥ kriyāḥ indriya sādhanāḥ vraścana ādīnām anindriya tvāt na ca vraścana ādi sādhanā sambhavati rūpa ādi paricchitti lakṣaṇā kriyā tasmāt yathā kriyā tva sāmānyasya karaṇa mātra adhīna tva vyāpta tve pakṣa dharma tā vaśāt indriya lakṣaṇa karaṇa viśeṣa siddhiḥ tathā iha api sati api kāryatvasya upādāna upakaraṇa saṃpradāna prayojana jña kartṛ mātra vyāpta tve api vivāda adhyāsiteṣu pakṣa dharma tā vaśāt upādāna ādi abhijña sāmānyasya ākṣipta viśeṣasya eva siddhiḥ anyathā sāmānyasya api vyāpaka abhimatasya na siddhiḥ syāt nirviśeṣasya asambhavāt viśeṣasya vā tasya anupapatteḥ asarvajñasya ca atra adṛṣṭa ādi bheda vijñāna sahitasya adhiṣṭhātṛ bhāva asambhavāt sarvajña ātmakaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ balāt āpatati 
RKNĀ_34.17	 nanūpādāna ādi abhijña kartṛ mātreṇa iva asarvajña tva dehitva ādibhiḥ api vyāptiḥ aśakya parihārāḥ vyabhicāra adarśanasya samāna tvāt iti ced na sarvajña tvā sarvajña tvayoḥ dehi tvā dehi tvayoḥ vā kārya utpattau anupayogāt na hi sārvajñyam kartṛṇām yogyatām upasthāpayati asarvajñebhyaḥ kumbhakāra ādibhyaḥ kumbha ādīnām aprasava prasaṅgāt na api asārvajñyam kumbhakārāt eva keyūra ādīnām api utpatti prasaṅgāt tathā na dehi tvam kārya utpattau upayogi kumbhakārāt eva keyūra ādīnām utpatti prasaṅgāt na adehi tvam kumbhakārāt ghaṭa ādīnām anutpāda prasaṅgāt tatas ca upādāna ādi abhijña puruṣa pūrvaka tvam eva kāryatvasya vyāpakam tat eva ca buddhimat puruṣa pūrvaka tva śabda vācyam tena yadi api buddhimat pūrvakatva mātram vyāpti viṣayaḥ tathā api tad viśeṣasya sarvajña tvasya pakṣa dharma tā balāt pratilambhaḥ iti viśeṣa viṣayam anumānam na ca ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ tasya sādhya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ dharma vikalpāt utkarṣa apakarṣa lakṣaṇa paryanuyogasya sarva anumāna sādha araṇyena anumāna mātra prāmāṇya pratikṣepa hetu tvāt 
RKNĀ_34.29–34.31	 etena yat uktam kaṇikāyām yadi kulāla ādīnām katipaya upakaraṇa ādi jñānam na samasta upakaraṇa ādi jña tā tarhi tena eva nidarśanena īśvarasya api tad upakaraṇa ādi mātra jñānam tanmātra jñāne na sarvajña tā siddhiḥ katipayajñaḥ hi tathā sati syāt na vā tanmātra jñānam api īśvarasya bāla ādi vat iti āha bāla unmatta ādīnām sva kārya prayojana aparijñāne api nirabhiprāyāṇām tatra tatra pravṛtti darśanāt na ca kulāla ādayaḥ nidarśanam na bāla ādayaḥ iti atra niyama hetuḥ asti iti tat nirastam 
RKNĀ_35.3	 īśvarasya hi katipaya ati indriya upakaraṇa ādi jñāne tad kāraṇasya sarvatra samāna tvāt aśeṣa upakaraṇa ādi jña tāyāḥ durvāra tvāt kāraṇam ca tad jñāne sattām antareṇa na anyat dharma adharma ādīnām laukika pratyāsatti hetūnām tatra asambhavāt kāraṇa abhede ca kārya abhedaḥ anyathā katipaya ati indriya jñānam api na syāt yathā hi kulāla ādiḥ tulya darśana sāmagrīkeṣu na akiñcijjñaḥ tathā atīndriya upakaraṇa ādiṣu api īśvaraḥ sāmarthyasya aviśeṣāt na ca bāla unmatta ādi nidarśanena katipaya upakaraṇa jña tā niṣedhaḥ yuktaḥ bīja dṛṣṭāntena buddhimat mātrasya api niṣedha abhidhāna prasaṅgāt tasmāt yathā upādāna ādi abhijñasya api sambhavāt bīja ādibhiḥ na vyabhicāra abhidhānam tathā bāla unmatta ādibhiḥ api iti kulāla ādīnām eva dṛṣṭānta tā yuktimatī upādāna ādi abhijña buddhi vat mātra kārya tvayoḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ tatra prasiddha tvāt tathā jñāna vat īśvarasya cikīrṣā prayatnau nityau iti atra api 
RKNĀ_35.14	 yat abhihitam nityau ced kim īśvarasya jñānena cikīrṣā prayatna upayoginā tayoḥ nitya tvāt sva utpāda upayoga anapekṣaṇāt itya ādi tat api asāram ajñāta kartṛ tva anupaptteḥ jñānam hi yatra cikīrṣā pratyatnau anityau tatra tau upasthāpayat upakaraṇa ādikam upadarśayati yatra tu tau nityau tatra upakaraṇa ādikam upadarśayat api saphalam tasmāt sati api cikīrṣā pratyatnayoḥ nitya tve saphalam īśvara jñānam sākṣātkārya upattau anupayogi api atas eva ca saḥ ayam īdṛśaḥ viśeṣaḥ vicāra asahaḥ katham pakṣa dharma tā balāt api sādhya dharmiṇī upasaṃhriyate iti ādiḥ api pralāpaḥ eva īśvara jñānasya avyāhatau sarvajña tā viśeṣasya durvāra tvāt 
RKNĀ_35.22	 yat abhihitam prekṣāvatām pravṛttiḥ prayojanavat tayā vyāptā na ca īśvarasya prekṣāvataḥ jagat nirmāṇe prayojanam utpaśyāmaḥ prāpta nikhila prāpaṇīyasya prāptavyābhāvāt tat api sāvadyam tad abhiprāyasya durbodha tvāt prayojana abhāva asiddheḥ vyāpaka anupalabdheḥ sandigdha tvāt vicitrā hi puruṣa mātrasya cetaḥ vṛttiḥ prāk eva viśvasya kartuḥ prāpta nikhila prāpaṇīyasya api karuṇayā api para artha pravṛtteḥ sambhāvyamāna tvāt na ca asya naraka ādi nirmāṇa pravṛttiḥ kāruṇikatām upahanti pratyuta pituḥ putra gaṇḍa pāṭana vṛttiḥ iva alpa duḥkha dānena prabhūta dāruṇa duḥkha apanayanāt karuṇā atiśayam eva gamayati prekṣāvatām iva asya api niyata sthira pravṛtti siddheḥ prayojana anumitiḥ eva nyāya prāptā
