RKNĀ_35.31–36.3^1	 yat ca idam udīritam yadi hi sarva kāryāṇām ekaḥ kartā syāt tatas ajñasya tattva anupapatteḥ sarvajña tā syāt adya punar ekaikam kāryam ekaikena kartrā janyate iti yaḥ yat janayati sa tad kāraṇa mātra jñaḥ eva na tu sarvajñaḥ iti atra ucyate kārya liṅga aviśeṣāt ekaḥ kartā sat iti jñāna aviśeṣāt satta eka tva vat kutaścid liṅgāt anumitasya vastunaḥ nānātvasya liṅga antara anumeya tvāt nānātvam upapādayitum pramāṇa antaram vaktavyam yathā ātma nānātvam avasthāpayadbhiḥ sukha ādibhiḥ nānātva vyavasthāpanam ucyate na ca iha kartuḥ aneka tva adhigame pramāṇa antaram asti eka tve tu na pramāṇātaram anveṣṭavyam ekasya kartuḥ abhāve bahūnām vyāhata manasām svātantryeṇa paraspara virodhena mithas sva anukūla abhiprāyānavabodhena yugapad kārya anutpattiḥ utpannasya vā vilopa ādi prasaṅgaḥ syāt iti eka tve tu siddhe sarvajña tā siddhiḥ avirodhinī 
RKNĀ_36.3^2	 na ca īśvarasya sakala kṣetrajña samavāyi dharma adharma jñāna kāraṇa abhāvena tad ajñānam tad samavetānām jñāna cikīrṣā pratyatnānām nitya tvāt na ca buddhi tad nitya tvayoḥ kaścid virodhaḥ na ca buddheḥ anitya tāyāḥ tatra tatra upalabdheḥ īśvara buddheḥ api tathātvam yuktam rūpa ādīnām api anityānām tatra tatra upalabdheḥ toya ādi paramāṇu samavetānām api rūpa ādīnām anitya tva prasaṅgāt para puruṣa samaveta dharma adharma adhiṣṭhānam api asya yuktam eva saṃyukta saṃyogi samavāyasya sambandhasya sadbhāvāt saṃyuktāḥ khalu īśvareṇa paramāṇavaḥ taiḥ ca kṣetrajñāḥ tad samavetau ca dharma adharmau iti 
RKNĀ_36.17	 tat evam kaṇikāyām vācaspateḥ īśvara dūṣaṇam yathāsāram utthāpya vyudastam asmābhiḥ aparam ca busa prāyam anabhyupagama prasiddha siddhānta grastam iha grantha vistara bhayāt na likhitam tat evam abhimatasya eva sarvajña tā lakṣaṇasya viśeṣasya siddheḥ na eṣa viśeṣa viruddhaḥ hetuḥ na api karmabhiḥ siddha sādhanam iti sthitam 
RKNĀ_36.21–36.24	 na ca anaikāntikaḥ sa hi bhavan asādhāraṇaḥ vā syāt yathā nityā pṛthvī gandhavat tvāt iti anupasaṃhāryaḥ vā yathā sarvam nityam prameya tvāt iti sādhāraṇaḥ vā yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ asparśavat tvāt iti tatra na tāvat ādimau pakṣau sa pakṣa sadbhāva darśanena pratikṣipta tvāt na api antimaḥ adhigata kartṛ nivṛtteḥ vyoma ādeḥ vipakṣāt vyāvṛtteḥ upalabdheḥ 
RKNĀ_36.26	 nanu puruṣa vyāpāram antareṇa tṛṇa ādīn udayamānān avalokayan lokaḥ kārya mātram puruṣa pūrvakam iti vyāptim eva na pratipadyate iti ced evam tarhi prasiddha anumāna sthitiḥ api datta jala añjaliḥ tatra api hi vyāpti pratīti kāle eva vyāghra ādi paryākula ati durga pradeśe vahni vyāpāram antareṇa dhūmam puruṣa vyāpāram vinā pūrvam siddham ghaṭam vā vilokayan lokaḥ dhūma mātram vahni pūrvakam ghaṭa mātram vā puruṣa pūrvakam iti vyāptim eva na pratipadyate iti vaktum śakya tvāt 
RKNĀ_37.1	 tatra vahni puruṣayoḥ deśa kāla viprakṛṣṭa tvāt apratikṣepaḥ iti ced yadi evam tṛṇa ādau api puruṣasya svabhāva viprakṛṣṭa tvāt apratikṣepaḥ iti sarvam samānam anyatra abhiniveśāt puruṣa vyāpāra pūrvaka tā tāvat na pratīyate tṛṇa ādīnām sā ca puruṣasya adṛśya tvāt asattvāt vā na pratīyatām kim anena vicāritena sarvathā kiñcid kāryam apūrva puruṣa pūrvakam apaśyat na vyāptim kārya mātrasya puruṣeṇa kaścid cetanāvān avagacchati iti ced yadi evam vahni mātra pūrvaka tā tāvat na pratīyate dhūmasya puruṣa mātra pūrvaka tā ca ghaṭasya sā ca vahneḥ deśa viprakṛṣṭa tvāt asattvāt vā puruṣasya kāla viprakṛṣṭa tvāt asattvāt vā na pratīyatām kim anena vicāritena sarvathā dhūma mātram vahni vyāpāra pūrvakam apaśyan ghaṭa mātram vā puruṣa pūrvakam apaśyan avyāptim eva dhūmasya vahni mātreṇa ghaṭasya puruṣa mātreṇa vā kaścid cetanāvān adhigacchati iti api ucyamānam na vaktram vakrīkaroti tat kim anena prasiddha anumāna apalāpinā jāti uttareṇa 
RKNĀ_37.12–37.14	 syāt etat na sa pakṣāsa pakṣayoḥ darśana adarśana mātreṇa avyabhicāra niścayaḥ atada ātmanaḥ atad utpatteḥ ca avyabhicāra niyama abhāvāt tat idam kārya tvam sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tvena asādhanam atra ucyate na asti vipakṣāt dhetoḥ vyāvṛtti sandehaḥ dhūma analayoḥ iva kārya buddhimatoḥ upalambhān upalambha sādhanasya kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya siddha tvāt 
RKNĀ_37.16	 kārya viśeṣasya eva tad utpāda siddhiḥ na kārya sāmānyasya yathā dhūma ādi vartinaḥ vastu tva ādeḥ na anala ādi janya tva niścayaḥ iti ced na viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt upalambha anupalambhayoḥ tad utpatti sādhana tvena iṣṭayoḥ aviśeṣāt kārya viśeṣasya iva kārya sāmānyasya prabodha āśraya āyattatā siddheḥ yathā hi kāryam vastra ādi upādāna vat dṛṣṭam iti kārya antaram api adṛṣṭa upādānam upādāna vat kāryatvāt vyavasthāpyate tathā tat eva kāryam vastra ādi dṛṣṭa kartṛkam iti adṛṣṭa kartṛkam api kāryatvāt kartṛmat vyavasthāpyate upādānasya iva kartuḥ api kāryeṇa anukṛta an vyavyatireka tvāt tanmātra nibandhana tvāt ca sarvatra kārya kāraṇa vyavahārayoḥ tasmāt yathā kāryam ca syāt nirupādānam ca iti na śakyam āśaṅkitum kārya mātrasya upādāna mātrāt utpāda siddheḥ tathā kāryam ca bhavet akartṛkam ca iti na aśaṅkanīyam kārya mātrasya kartṛ mātrāt utpāda siddheḥ aviśeṣāt 
RKNĀ_37.26	 nanu brūyāḥ nāma kiñcid tathā api na kārya mātrāt buddhimat anumānam api tu kārya viśeṣāt eva yad darśanāt akriyā darśinaḥ api kṛta buddhiḥ syāt na ca anapekṣita tattva anugamāt śabda mātra sāmyāt sādhya siddhiḥ yuktāḥ go śabda vācya tā mātreṇa vāc ādīnām viṣāṇi tva anumiti prasaṅgāt iti ced tat etat svastha uttaram anuttara arham kārya sāmānyasya eva vyāpti prasādhanāt api ca kā punar iyam kṛta buddhiḥ kim apekṣita para vyāpāra avasāyaḥ atha puruṣa kṛtam etat iti pauruṣeya tva niścayaḥ iti 
RKNĀ_38.1	 yadi ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ sa katham kṣiti ādiṣu na asti kāraṇa vyāpāra ātma lābha lakṣaṇasya kāryatvasya kumbha ādi vat kṣiti ādiṣu aviśeṣāt atha puruṣeṇa kṛtam iti pauruṣeya tva niścayaḥ kṛta buddhiḥ abhimatā tadā api tādṛśī kṛta buddhiḥ kasya na asti iti vaktavyam kim kāryatvāt iti hetoḥ avinā abhāva vedinaḥ āhosvit tad viparītasya na ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ avinā abhāva vedinaḥ sādhya apratipatteḥ ayogāt atha tad viparītasya sādhya buddhiḥ na bhavati iti kṛta buddhi hetuka tvam avani tanu mahīruha ādiṣu na asti iti buddhimataḥ anumānam pratikṣipyate 
RKNĀ_38.8	 nanu evam sati sarva anumāna ucchedaḥ syāt sarva hetūnām agṛhīta avinābhāvam prati agamaka tvāt tasmāt na kṛta buddhi hetu tva viśeṣaḥ bhavatu vā kaścid anirūpita rūpaḥ viśeṣaḥ tathā api kim anena kārya mātrasya eva dhūma mātrasya iva vyāpti pratīteḥ na ca kāryatvena hetunā saha mṛd vikārasya sama kakṣatā tasya sva sādhyena dṛśya kumbhakāreṇa saha vyabhicārasya śataśas darśanāt kāryatvasya tu dṛśya adṛśya sādhāraṇena buddhimat mātreṇa tad yogāt iti na ayam anaikāntikaḥ 
RKNĀ_38.14–38.19	 na api prakaraṇa samaḥ apratipakṣa tvāt na hi asya pratipakṣa upasthāpakam dharma antaram asti yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ vastu tve sati anupalabhyamāna anitya dharma tvāt iti asya anityaḥ śabdaḥ vastu tve sati anupalabhyamāna nitya dharma tvāt iti pratipakṣa kṛtam dharma antaram asti na ca idam bādhakam vaktavyam na īśvara kartṛkam jagat vastu tva sattvāt ityādi īśvara kartṛka tvasya vastu tvāt iti virodha abhāvāt iti na ayam prakaraṇa samaḥ api na ca kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ pratyakṣa anumāna āgamaiḥ bādhita viṣayasya tathā abhāvāt asya ca taiḥ avirodhāt tatra pratyakṣa viruddhaḥ anuṣṇaḥ tejaḥ avayavī kṛtaka tvāt anumāna viruddhaḥ sa avayavāḥ paramāṇavaḥ mūrta tvāt āgama viruddhaḥ śucina 
RKNĀ_ra	 śiraḥ kapālam prāṇi aṅga tvāt iti tatra na tāvat ayam pratyakṣa viruddhaḥ sādhya viparyayasya pratyakṣa aviṣaya tvāt na api anumāna viruddhaḥ dharmi grāhiṇa anumānena ābādhita viṣaya tvāt na ca āgama viruddhaḥ āgamena sādhya viparyayasya aparicchedāt saugata ādi āgamaiḥ viparīta paricchedāt iti ced na teṣām kṣaṇika tva ādi artha visaṃvāda upalambhena prāmāṇya abhāvāt veda āgamaḥ api bādhaka tvena na aśaṅkanīyaḥ sahasra śīrṣā puruṣaḥ ityādinā tatra kartuḥ eva pratipādanāt tathābhūta puruṣa atiśaya pūrvaka tva abhāve satya prāmāṇyāt ca iti na ayam atikrānta kālaḥ hetuḥ tat evam apanīta hetu abhāsa vibhramāt atas sādhanāt upādāna ādi abhijñaḥ buddhimān abhimataḥ kartā sidhyati saḥ eva bhagavān asmākam īśvaraḥ iti sthitam 
RKNĀ_39.1	 tathā asya siddhaye śaṅkaraḥ sādhanam idam abhipraiti jagat etat prabodha āśraya āyatta prasavam abhilāṣa prīti paramāṇu mūrti ādhāra paratva aparatva anumeya sāmānya samavāyāntya viśeṣa tad eka artha samaveta parimāṇa eka tva pṛthaktu a guru tva sneha apārthiva rūpa rasa sparśā api adrava tva amūrta saṃyoga tad itaretara abhāva anutpatti rūpā rūpam asmad ādi vinirmitā itarat acetana upādāna tvāt yat ittham tat tathā yathā kalasaḥ tathā ca idam tasmāt idam api tathā iti asya ayam arthaḥ jagat iti dharmī prabodha āśraya āyatta prasavam iti sādhyam abhilāṣa ityādi anutpatti rūpā rūpa paryantena dharmi viśeṣeṇa ākāśa ādi nitya varga parihāraḥ asmad ādi vinirmitā itarat iti anena api dharmi viśeṣeṇa prasiddha kartṛka ghaṭa ādi parihāraḥ abhilāpaḥ ca prītiḥ ca paramāṇu mūrtiḥ ca āsām ādhāraḥ ākāśaḥ ātmā paramāṇuḥ paratva aparatva anumeyau diś kālau sāmānya ādayaḥ tu yathāprasiddhāḥ grahītavyāḥ 
RKNĀ_39.15–39.28	 tathā narasiṃhaḥ prāha vijñāna ādhāra adhīna janma ajanma avacchinna ātma ubhaya vādya vivāda āspada puruṣa pūrvakavyatireki bhāva anubhāvi prameya jātam utpattimat tvāt yat yat ākhyāta sādhana sambandhi tat tat ukta sādhya dharma adhikaraṇam yathā vāsaḥ tathā ca idam tasmāt idam api tathā iti asya ayam arthaḥ prameya jātam dharmi vijñāna ādhāra adhīna janma iti sādhyam ajanma avacchinna ātmā iti dharmi viśeṣaṇam etena ākāśa ādi nitya varga parihāraḥ ubhaya vādya vivāda āspada puruṣa pūrvakavyatireki iti anena api prasiddha kartṛka ghaṭa ādi parihāraḥ bhāva anubhāvī iti vastu rūpam etena pradhvaṃsa ādi parihāraḥ yat yat ākhyāta sādhana sambandhī iti vyāpti vacanam yat dharmi rūpam kathita sādhana yogī iti arthaḥ trilocanaḥ tu vyatirekiṇam imam prayogam āha sarvam kāryam prabodha vat hetukam utpatti dharmaka tvāt yat nityam dṛṣṭam abodha vat hetukam tasya ākāśa ādeḥ tathā utpattiḥ na asti iti dṛṣṭam utpatti dharmakam ca pakṣīkṛtam asmad ādi vinirmitā itarat tasmāt bodha vat hetukam iti 
RKNĀ_40.1	 punar dvi aṇukeśvara siddhau trilocanaḥ eva prāha vivāda āspadībhūtam dvi tvam ātma utpattau kasyacid ekaika viṣayām buddhim apekṣate dvi tva saṃkhyā tvāt yat yat dvi tvam tat tathā yathā dve dravye tathā ca idam dvi aṇuka gatam dvi tvam tasmāt tathā iti yasya ca atra buddhiḥ apekṣyate sa bhagavān īśvaraḥ tathā ca vācaspatiḥ pramāṇayati vivāda adhyāsita tanu taru giri sāgara ādayaḥ upādāna ādi abhijña kartṛkāḥ kāryatvāt yat yat kāryam tat tat upādāna ādi abhijña kartṛkam yathā prāsāda ādi tathā ca vivāda adhyāsitāḥ tanu ādayaḥ tasmāt tathā iti evam sthitvā sthitvā pravṛtti dharmaka tvāt sanniveśavat tvāt artha kriyā kāritvāt ityādayaḥ hetavaḥ kathita pañca avayava krameṇa boddhavyāḥ iti 
RKNĀ_40.16	 tat etat durmati vispanditam jagat andhīkaraṇam na satām upekṣitum ucitam iti kiñcid ucyate iha khalu buddhimat kārya mātrayoḥ sādhya sādhanayoḥ sarva upasaṃhāravatī vyāptiḥ tāvat avaśyam grahītavyā anyathā gamya gamaka bhāva ayogāt sā ca gṛhyamāṇā kim kāraṇa kārya mātrayoḥ iva viparyaya bādhaka pramāṇa balāt grāhyā yat vā agni dhūmayoḥ iva viśiṣṭa anvaya vyatireka grahaṇa pravaṇa viśiṣṭa pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām boddhavyā uta sva vyavasthayā sa pakṣāsa pakṣayoḥ bhūyos darśana adarśanābhyām pratyetavyāḥ āhosvit sa pakṣa āsa pakṣayoḥ sakṛt darśanābhyām jñātavyā iti catvāraḥ vikalpāḥ 
RKNĀ_40.23	 na tāvat ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ sādhya viparyaye buddhi mat abhāve kāryatva sāmānyasya sādhanasya bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt nanu bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvaḥ asiddhaḥ tathā hi idam kārya tvam yathā buddhimatā vyāptam iṣyate tathā deśa kāla svabhāva niyata tvena api kadācika kāraṇa sannidhimat tayā api sāmagrī kārya tvena api vyāptam upalabdham sa ca deśa ādi niyamaḥ kādācitka kāraṇa sanndhiḥ sāmagrī vā buddhimat pūrvikā siddhāḥ yadi punar acetanāni cetanā anadhiṣṭhatāni kāryam kuryuḥ tatas yatra kvacana avasthitāni janayeyuḥ iti na deśa kāla svabhāva niyata prasavam kāryam upalabhyeta 
RKNĀ_40.30^1	 hetu samavadhān a janma tayā na kāryam pratyekam kāraṇaiḥ janyate iti ced samavadhānam eva tu kāraṇānām kutas kādācid ka paripākāt adṛṣṭa viśeṣāt iti ced nanu ayam acetanaḥ katham yathāvat kāraṇāni sannidhāpayet no khalu kvacid avasthitāni daṇḍa ādīni vinā kumbhakāra prayatnam adṛṣṭa viśeṣa vaśāt eva parasparam sannidhīyante sannihitāni vā kāryāya prabhavanti iti buddhimatā deśa kāla svabhāva niyamasya kādācitka kāraṇa sannidheḥ sāmagryāḥ ca vyāpti siddhiḥ buddhi mat abhāve ca eṣām vyāpakānām nivṛttau nivartamānam kārya tvam buddhimat pūrvaka tvena vyāpyate iti pratibandha siddhaye vyāpaka anupalambha trayam upanyastam 
RKNĀ_40.30^2	 tathā na kāryam buddhimat parityāgāt ahetukam eva bhavati iti sambhāvyam deśa kāla svabhava niyama abhāva prasaṅgāt na api buddhimataḥ anyasmāt eva bhavati iti śaṅkanīyam sakṛt api utpāda abhāva prasaṅgāt na ca anyasmāt asmāt api bhavati iti sambhāvyam aniyata hetu tve ahetu tva prasaṅgāt tathā buddhimantam antareṇa acetanena karaṇe sarvadā kriyāyāḥ avirāma prasaṅga ḥ ca iti api viparyaya bādhakam atiprasaṅga catuṣṭayam vyāpti prasādhakam iti kāryatvasya hetu pūrvaka tvam iva buddhimat pūrvaka tvam api avāryam iti ced 
RKNĀ_41.12	 atra ucyate sidhyati eva idam manaḥ rājyam yadi deśa kāla svabhāva niyamasya kādācitka kāraṇa sannidheḥ samagryāḥ ca buddhimat pūrvaka tvena vyāptiḥ sidhyati kevalam etat eva durāpam buddhi mat abhāve api hi sva hetu bala samutpanna sannidheḥ pratiniyata deśa kāla śaktinā acetanena api sāmagrī lakṣaṇa kāraṇa viśeṣeṇa kriyamāṇāni deśa kāla svabhāva niyamakāt citka kāraṇa sannidhi sāmagrī kārya tvāni yujyante iti sandigdha asiddhāḥ vyāpaka anupalabdhayaḥ 
RKNĀ_41.18	 buddhi mat abhāve samavadhānam eva kutas iti ced tat api cetanā anadhiṣṭhita yathā ukta acetana sāmagrī viśeṣāt eva saḥ api tādṛśāt iti anādya cetana sāmagrī paramparātaḥ api deśa ādi niyama sambhāvanāyām na avaśyam buddhimat apekṣā ghaṭa ādeḥ deśa kāla svabhāva niyamaḥ kādācitka kāraṇa sannidhiḥ ca sāmagrī ca buddhimat pūrvikā dṛṣṭā iti aparopi deśa kāla svabhāva niyama ādiḥ tathā eva iti ced yadi evam ghaṭa ādikam api kāryam bahuśas buddhimat pūrvakam upalabdham iti sarvam eva kāryam tathā astu kim anena vyāpaka anupalambha upanyāsa durvyasanena ghaṭa ādeḥ bahuśas buddhimat pūrvakatva darśane api na sarvatra kārya mātrasya tathā abhāva niścayaḥ ced deśa ādi niyama ādīnām api idam samānam iti katham atra api śaṅkā vyudāsaḥ 
RKNĀ_41.27–42.5	 astu tadā pratyakṣam eva sarvatra vyāpti grāhakam iti ced na tarhi viparyaya bādhaka pramāṇa balāt vyāpti graha nirvāhaḥ pratyakṣam ca tatra aśaktam iti dvitīya vikalpa avasare nivedayiṣyate tathā asiddhe kārya kāraṇa bhāve dhūmasya ahetuka utpattau anyasmāt eva utpattau anyasmāt api utpattau sambhāvyamānāyām deśa ādi niyama abhāva sakṛt utpāda abhāva ahetutva prasaṅgāḥ saṅgacchante prastute tu buddhimat kārya mātrayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ na adya api siddhaḥ sādhayitum vā śakyaḥ na ca acetanasya kartṛ tve kriyāyāḥ avirāma prasaṅgaḥ saṅgataḥ na hi acetanam iti eva sarvadā sāmarthya yogi tasya api sva hetu paramparā pratibaddha sāmarthya tvāt iti acetana kāraṇa viśeṣa paramparā sambhāvanāyām na avaśyam buddhimat ākṣepaḥ iti sva mata vyāla upa viklava vikrośita mātram eva idam na punar atra nyāya gandhaḥ api tat evam vyāpti sādhana artham upanyastam vyāpaka anupalambha trayam sandigdhā siddham atiprasaṅga tucaṣṭayam ca buddhimat kārya mātrayoḥ vyāpti asiddhau asaṅgatam atas kārya tvam sādhanam sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tvāt anaikāntikam 
RKNĀ_42.8–42.19	 atra vācaspatiḥ prāha sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tvam nāma hetu doṣaḥ eva na bhavati tat katham nirasyate tathā hi yaḥ eva vipakṣe dṛṣṭaḥ hetuḥ saḥ eva prameya tva ādi vat abhimatam na sādhyet yaḥ tu mahatā api prayatnena mṛgyamāṇaḥ asapakṣe na upalakṣitaḥ sa katham sādhyam na sādhayet avaśyam śaṅkayā bhāvyam niyāmakam apaśyatām iti tu datta avakāśā laukikam aryādā atikrameṇa saṃśaya piśācī labdha prasarāḥ na kvacid na asti iti na ayam kvacid pravarteta sarvasya eva arthasya kathañcid śaṅkā āspada tva darśanāt anartha śaṅkāyāḥ ca prekṣāvatām nivṛtti aṅga tvāt antatas snigdha anna pāna upayoge api maraṇa darśanāt tasmāt prāmāṇika lokayātrām anupālayatā yathādarśanam śaṅkanīyam na tu adṛṣṭam api viśeṣa smṛti apekṣaḥ hi saṃśayaḥ na asmṛteḥ bhavati na ca smṛtiḥ ananubhūta care bhavati tat uktam mīmāṃsā vārttika kṛtāḥ adhyuṣṭa sahasrikāyām na āśaṅkā niḥpramāṇikā iti 
RKNĀ_42.21	 tathā tena eva bṛhaṭṭīkāyām utprekṣeta hi yaḥ mohāt ajātam api bādhakam sa sarva vyavahāreṣu saṃśaya ātmā kṣayam vrajet iti tat etat pralāpa mātram na hi mahatā api prayatnena vipakṣe mṛgyamāṇasya hetoḥ adarśana mātreṇa vyatirekaḥ sidhyati tathā hi vipakṣe hetuḥ na upalabhyate iti anena tad upalambhaka pramāṇa nivṛttiḥ ucyate pramāṇam ca prameyasya kāryam na akāraṇam viṣayaḥ iti nyāyāt na ca kārya nivṛttau kāraṇa nivṛttiḥ upalabdhā nirdhūmasya api vahneḥ upalambhāt yadi punar pramāṇa sattayā prameya sattā vyāptā syāt tadā yuktam etat kevalam iyam eva vyāptiḥ asambhavinī sarvasya sarva darśi tva prasaṅgāt tat na adarśana mātreṇa vyatireka siddhiḥ yathā uktam sarva adṛṣṭiḥ ca sandigdhā svādṛṣṭiḥ vyabhicāriṇī vindhya adri randhra dūrvā ādeḥ adṛṣṭau api sattvataḥ iti sakala vipakṣasya arvācīnam prati adṛśya tvāt 
RKNĀ_43.4	 yat ca uktam saṃśaya piśācī labdha prasarāḥ na kvacid na asti iti na kvacid pravarteta iti tat asaṅgatam artha saṃśayasya api prekṣāvatām pravṛtti aṅga tvāt pravṛttiḥ avirodhinī eva anartha sandehaḥ sarvatra kartum śakyate antatas snigdha anna pāna upayoge api maraṇa darśanāt apravṛttiḥ iti ced durjñānam etat tathā hi artha sandehaḥ anartha sandehaḥ vā iti na ayam ṣaṣṭhī samāsaḥ kin tu artha unmukhaḥ sandehaḥ artha sandehaḥ anartha unmukhaḥ sandehaḥ anartha sandehaḥ iti śāka pārthiva ādi vat madhya pada lopī samāsaḥ evam sati snigdha anna pāna ādau artha sandehaḥ eva tad jātīyasya sva para santāne dṛṣṭi puṣṭi ādi arthasya koṭiśas karaṇa darśanāt maraṇa ādeḥ anarthsya kvacid kadācid darśanāt etad viparītaḥ anartha sandehaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ tasmāt pramāṇāt iva artha saṃśayāt api prekṣāvatām tatra tatra pravṛttiḥ durvāra eva 
RKNĀ_43.13	 yat api idam lapitam yathādarśanam śaṅkanīyam na adṛṣṭa pūrvam api viśeṣa smṛti apekṣaḥ hi saṃśayaḥ ityādi tat asambaddham sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt eva paryudāsa vṛttyā vastu antara rūpāt sarvatra saṃśaya utpatteḥ kim ca viśeṣa smṛti apekṣaḥ eva ayam saṃśayaḥ tathā hi lakṣaṇa yogitva ayogi tvābhyām eva tad jātīya ātad jātīye vaktavye anyathā lakṣaṇa praṇayanam anarthakam syāt evam ca sati tādātmya tad utpatti lakṣaṇa pratibandha viyogi tvena sādhāraṇena dharmeṇa prameya tva dhūma tva kārya tva ādīnām tvad matena sajātīya tvāt prameya tva vyabhicāra darśanam eva śaṅkām upasthāpayati iti yathādarśanam eva idam āśaṅkitam 
RKNĀ_43.20	 yaḥ ca kumārilasya sākṣi tvena upanyāsaḥ sa khalu dadhi bhāṇḍe viḍālaḥ sākṣī iti pravādam na atipatati iti kim atra vaktavyam tat evam vipakṣe adarśana mātreṇa hetoḥ vyatireka asiddheḥ sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tvam nāma hetu dūṣaṇam durvāram eva atas eva asya upanyāsaḥ adoṣodbhāvanam nāma nigraha sthānam iti yat anena āveditam tat api sāvadyam pratyutā asmin hetoḥ sat dūṣaṇe parihartavye na ayam hetu doṣaḥ atas na parihartavyaḥ asya ca upanyāsaḥ adoṣodbhāvanam nāma nigraha sthānam iti bruvan ayam eva tapasvī sva matena niranuyojya anuyoga lakṣaṇena nigraha sthānena nigṛhyate iti kṛpām arhati tat evam viparyaya bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt avyāpteḥ asiddheḥ sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tvāt anaikāntikaḥ kāryatva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ 
RKNĀ_43.30	 atha agni dhūmayoḥ iva viśiṣṭa anvaya vyatireka grahaṇa pravaṇa viśiṣṭa pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām vyaptiḥ niścīyate iti dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ atra ucyate kim dṛśya śarīra upādhinā buddhimat mātreṇa vyāpti gṛhyate āhosvit dṛśya śarīra upādhi vidhureṇa dṛśya adṛśya sādhāraṇena iti vikalpau yadi ādyaḥ pakṣah tadā tathābhūta sādhyam antareṇa api utpadyamāne viṭapa ādau kāryatva darśanāt prameya tva ādi vat sādhāraṇa anaikāntikaḥ hetuḥ 
RKNĀ_44.2	 nanu vṛkṣa ādayaḥ pakṣīkṛtāḥ katham taiḥ vyabhicāraḥ trividhaḥ hi bhāva rāśiḥ sandigdha kartṛkaḥ yathā vṛkṣa ādiḥ prasiddha kartṛkaḥ yathā ghaṭa ādiḥ akartṛkaḥ yathā ākāśa ādiḥ tatra prasiddha kartṛke ghaṭa ādau pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām vyāptim ādāya sandeha pade kṣmāruha ādau kāryatvam upasaṃhṛtya buddhimān anumīyate na punar asu vyabhicāra viṣayaḥ bhavitum arhati 
RKNĀ_44.8^1	 yat āha na sādhyena eva vyabhicāraḥ iti ayuktam etat na hi vyabhicāra viṣayaḥ eva pakṣe bhavitum arhati sandigdhe hetu vacanāt vyastaḥ hetoḥ anāśrayaḥ iti nyāyāt vyabhicāra viṣaya tā ca dṛśya śarīra upādheḥ buddhimat mātrasya tṛṇa ādi utpattau dṛśya anupalambhena pratikṣipta tvāt tatas ca kṣmādhara ādiḥ eva sandigdha kartṛkaḥ pakṣīkartum ucitaḥ kṣmāruha ādiḥ tu acetana kartṛkaḥ iti caturthaḥ bhavarāśiḥ na iṣṭavyaḥ atha vyabhicāra camatkārāt trividha bhāva rāśi vyavasthāpana artham ca viṭapa ādau pratyakṣa apratikṣiptena dṛśya adṛśya sādhāraṇena buddhimat mātreṇa vyāptiḥ avagamyate iti dvitīyaḥ saṅkalpaḥ tadā viṭapa ādau buddhimat mātrasya sambhāvyamāna tvāt na sādhāraṇa anaikāntika tām brūmaḥ 
RKNĀ_44.8^2	 kim tarhi vyāpti grahaṇa kāle dṛśya adṛśya sādhāraṇasya buddhimat mātrasya sādhyasya adṛśyatayā dṛśya anupalambhena vyatireka asiddheḥ vyāpteḥ abhāvat sandigdha vyāvṛttika tvam ācakṣmahe tathā hi yadā kumbhakāra vyāpārāt pūrvam kumbhasya vyatirekaḥ pratyetavyaḥ tadā na sādhya abhāva kṛtaḥ ghaṭa vyatirekaḥ pratyetum śakyaḥ yathā hi viṭapa ādi janma samaye buddhimat mātrā asya adṛśya tvena niṣeddhum aśakya tvāt sattā sambhāvanā tathā ghaṭa ādau api vyatireka niścaya kāle buddhimat mātrasya adṛśya tvāt sattva sambhāvanāyām sādhya abhāva prayuktasya sādhana abhāvasya asiddha tvena vyāpteḥ abhāvāt katham na sandigdha vyatirekaḥ hetuḥ 
RKNĀ_44.25^1	 yat ca ukta yathā kāryam ca syāt nirupādānām ca iti na aśaṅkanīyam tathā kāryam ca bhavet akartṛkam ca iti na aśaṅkanīyam iti tatra api kāryam ca syāt nirupādānam ca bhavet iti na vaktavyam iti kena evam pratāritaḥ asi yadi hi atra pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām vyāptiḥ gṛhyate tadā katham upādāna pūrvakam kārya mātram sidhyati vyāpti grahaṇa prakāra antaram ca tvayā api na upanyastam dṛśya adṛśya sādhāraṇayoḥ upādāna kārya mātrayoḥ dṛśya viṣayābhyām pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām vyāpteḥ abhyūhitum aśakya tvāt sva mata vyālopa prasaṅgaḥ tu pramāṇa cintā avasare aprāpta avakāśaḥ viparyaya bādhaka pramāṇa balāt vā atra vyāpti siddhiḥ tathā hi yathā aṅkura ādikam kāryam niyata deśa kāla svabhāva tvena vyāptam tathā śāli tvā ādinā api jāti bhedena vyāptam upalabdham tatas ca anupādāna pūrvaka tvāt vipakṣa ātmanaḥ śāli tvā ādi jāti bhedasya vyāpakasya nivṛttau nivartamānam kāryatvam upādāna pūrvaka tve viśrāmyat tena vyāptam sidhyati 
RKNĀ_44.25^2	 na ca anupādānena api kriyamāṇaḥ śāli tvā ādi jāti bhedaḥ yujyate upādānam vinā kṛtāt anupādānāt eva kevalāt eka jātīya kāraṇāt tad atad jātīya kārya utpattau kārya bhedasya ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt tat uktam tat atad rūpiṇaḥ bhāvāḥ tad atad rūpa hetu jāḥ iti anyathā anupādānāt eva kṣiti ādeḥ aṅkura ādikam utpadyeta iti aṅkura arthinaḥ bījam na anusareyuḥ tasmāt viparyaya bādhaka pramāṇa balāt eva kāryatvasya hetu mātra pūrvaka tvena iva upādāna pūrvaka tvena api vyāpti siddhiḥ iti nyāyaḥ na ca evam kārya mātra kartṛ tva mātrayoḥ api vyāpti prasādhakam viparyaye bādhakam pramāṇam asti pūrva uktasya vyāpaka anupalambha trayasya atiprasaṅga catuṣṭayasya ca prāk eva pratyākhyāta tvāt tasmāt kāryam ca syāt na ca dhīmat kartṛ pūrvakam iti śaṅkām kurvāṇaḥ prativādī vinā caraṇa mardana ādinā niṣeddhum aśakyaḥ 
RKNĀ_45.13	 nanu yadi dṛśya agni dhūma sāmānyayoḥ iva dṛśyāḥ eva kārya kāraṇa sāmānyayoḥ pratyakṣa anupalambhataḥ vyāptiḥ tadā para citta anumāna kṣatiḥ sva para santāna sādhāraṇena adṛśyena cit mātreṇa pratyakṣataḥ dṛśya viṣayāt vyāpti grahaṇa ayogāt iti api na vācyam bāhya artha sthitau hi sva para santāna sādhāraṇasya cit mātrasya svarūpeṇa adṛśya tve api dṛśya śarīreṇa saha ekasāmagrī pratibandhāt avinirbhāga varti tvam asti eva tatas yathā ghaṭa viṣayam pratyakṣam rūpa eka deśa pravṛttam api avyabhicārāt samudāya upasthāpakam tathā deha grāhakam eva pratyakṣam deha avinirbhāga varti sva para santāna sādhāraṇam cit mātram kampa ādeḥ vyāpakam adhigacchanti tat evam dṛśya ātmanaḥ dṛśyā vinirbhāga vartinaḥ vā padārthasya vyāvahārika paṭu pratyakṣataḥ siddhiḥ vyāpti grahaḥ ca na tu tathātva vinākṛta adṛśya sādhāraṇa cit mātrasya iti santāna antara anumānam ucitam tasmāt yadi pratyakṣa anupalabhābhyām vyāpti grahaḥ tadā dṛśyena eva dṛśyasya iti nyāyaḥ 
RKNĀ_45.24–45.30^1	 tat ayam saṃkṣepa arthaḥ kāryatvasya vipakṣa vṛtti hataye sambhāvyate atīndriyaḥ kartā ced vyatireka siddhi vidhurā vyāptiḥ katham sidhyati dṛśyaḥ atha vyatireka siddhi manasā kartā samāśrīyate tad tyāge api tadā tṛṇa ādikam iti vyaktam vipakṣe kṣaṇam atas na pratyakṣa anupalmbhābhyām api vyāpti siddhiḥ nanu bhūyas darśana adarśanābhyām pratibandhaḥ pratīyate iti tṛtīyaḥ eva asamākam pakṣaḥ kevalam sa pratibandhaḥ na tad utpatti lakṣaṇaḥ grahītavyaḥ kin tu svābhāvikaḥ saḥ eva darśana adarśanābhyām pratīyate tathā ca etam eva artham vācaspatiḥ prāha na sa pakṣāsa pakṣayoḥ darśana adarśanābhyām kāryatvasya gamaka tvam api tu svābhāvika pratibandha balāt iti brūmaḥ saḥ eva tu sa pakṣāsa pakṣayoḥ darśana adarśanābhyām vakṣyamāṇena krameṇa pratīyate iti tad upakṣepaḥ api yuktaḥ tena yasya asau svābhāvikaḥ pratibandhaḥ niyataḥ siddhaḥ saḥ eva gamakaḥ gamyaḥ ca itaraḥ sambandhī iti yujyate tathā hi dhūma ādīnām vahni ādibhiḥ saha sambandhaḥ svābhāvikaḥ na tu vahni ādīnām dhūma ādibhiḥ 
RKNĀ_45.30^2	 te hi vinā dhūma ādibhiḥ upalambhyante yadā tu ārdra indhana ādi sambandham anubhavanti tadā dhūma ādibhiḥ sambadhyante tasmāt vahni ādīnām ārdredhana ādi upādhi kṛtaḥ sambandhaḥ na tu svābhāvikaḥ tatas na niyataḥ svābhāvikaḥ tu dhūma ādīnām vahni ādibhiḥ sambandhaḥ tad upādheḥ anupalabhyamāna tvāt kvacid vyabhicārasya adarśanāt anupalabhyamānasya api kalpanā anupapatteḥ na ca anupalabhyamānaḥ darśanān arha tayā sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvena sandihyamānaḥ upādhiḥ sambandhasya svābhāvika tvam pratibadhnāti iti yuktam yathā uktam prāk sā iyam saṃśaya piśācī ityādi tasmāt upādhim prayatnena anviṣyantaḥ anupalabhyamānā na asti iti avagamya svābhāvika tvam niścinumaḥ 
RKNĀ_46.14	 syāt etat anyasya anyena saha kāraṇena ced svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ bhavet sarvam sarveṇa sambadhyeta tathā ca sarvam sarvasmāt gamyeta atha anyat ced anyasya kāryam kasmāt sarvam sarvasmāt na bhavati anya tva aviśeṣāt tatas ca saḥ eva atiprasaṅgaḥ yadi ucyeta svabhāvāḥ na paryanuyojyāḥ tasmāt anya tva aviśeṣe api kiñcid eva kāraṇam kāryam ca kiñcid iti nanu eṣa svabhāvān anuyogaḥ akārya kāraṇa bhūtānām api svabhāva pratibandhe tulyaḥ eva tasmāt yat kiñcid etat api 
RKNĀ_46.20	 kim asya sambandhasya vyāpti grāhakam pramāṇam iti ced ucyate bhūyas darśana gamyā hi vyāptiḥ sāmānya dharmayoḥ iti prasiddham eva asya ayam arthaḥ kāśika ākāreṇa vyākhyātaḥ prācīna aneka darśana janita saṃskāra sahāye carame cetasi cakāsti dhūmasya agni niyata svabhāva tvam ratna tattvam iva parīkṣakasya śabda tattvam iva vyākaraṇa smṛti saṃskṛtasya brāhmaṇa tvam iva mātā pitṛ sambandha smaraṇa sacivasya ityādi na hi etat sarvam āpātataḥ na pratibhātam iti purastāt api pratibhāsamānam anyathā bhavati iti 
RKNĀ_46.27–47.1	 trilocanena punar ayam arthaḥ kathitam bhūyas darśanena bhūyas darśana sahāyena manasā tad jātīyānām sambandhaḥ gṛhītaḥ bhavati atas dhūmaḥ agnim na vyabhicarati tad vyabhicāre api upādhi rahitam sambandham atikrāmet hetoḥ vipakṣa śaṅkā nivartakam pramāṇam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta upādhi viraha niścaya hetuḥ anupalambha ākhyam pratyakṣam eva tatas siddhaḥ svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ tathā iha api iti sva matam vyavasthāpitam iti vācaspatinā api idam uktam abhijāta maṇi bheda tattva vat bhūyas darśana janita saṃskāra sahāyam indriyam eva dhūma ādīnām vahni ādibhiḥ svābhāvika sambandha grāhī iti yuktam iti 
RKNĀ_47.3	 atra ucyate abhede sati tad utpatteḥ anyaḥ svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ śabda āsphālana mātram eva idam na khalu nirūpyamāṇaḥ prāpyate tathā hi svābhāvikaḥ tu dhūma ādīnām vahni ādibhiḥ sambandhaḥ tad upādheḥ anupalabhyamāna tvāt kvacid vyabhicārasya adarśanāt iti tvayā eva asya lakṣaṇam uktam etat ca asiddham yatas upādhi śabdena svatas artha antaram eva apekṣaṇīyam abhidhātavyam na ca artha antaram dṛśyatā niyatam adṛśyasya api deśa kāla svabhāva viprakṛṣṭasya sambhavāt tatas ca dhūmasya api hutāśena saha sambandhe syāt upādhiḥ na ca upalakṣyate iti katham adarśanāt na asti eva yatas svābhāvika sambandha siddhiḥ 
RKNĀ_47.11	 atha yadi arthānataram apekṣaṇīyam syāt katham dhūmaḥ iti eva pāvaka sattā niyamaḥ iti ced nanu idam eva cintyate tad utpatteḥ asvīkāre sahasraśas darśane api kim sarvatra dhūme sati avaśyam agniḥ sambhavī na vā iti kadācid artha antaram upādhim apekṣya dhūmaḥ api syāt na agniḥ iti kim atra niṣṭaṅka kāraṇam tad upādheḥ anupalabhyamāna tvāt kvacid vyabhicārasya adarśanāt iti tu yat uktam tat pratyuktam eva adṛśyasya api upādheḥ sambhāvyamāna tvāt vyabhicārasya ca pratyaya antara vaikalyena āhatya adarśane api niṣeddham aśakya tvāt atas eva tayoḥ bādhaka abhāve api sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt śaṅkā sambhavati eva na punar tava amunā viklava vikrośita mātreṇa vyāvartate na ca etavatā prāmāṇika lokayātrā atikramaḥ prāmāṇikaiḥ eva sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa abhāve nyāya prāptasya saṃśayasya vihita tvāt na ca sarvatra apravṛtti prasaṅgaḥ pamāṇāt artha saṃśayāt ca pravṛtteḥ upapatteḥ na ca anartha sandehaḥ sarvatra kartum śakyate kvacid artha unmukha tāyāḥ eva darśanāt 
RKNĀ_47.22	 yat ca anya tva aviśeṣe api kiñcid eva kāraṇam kāryam ca kiñcid iti svabhāvaḥ yathā na paryanuyojyaḥ tathā eṣa svabhāvān anuyogaḥ a kārya kāraṇa bhūtānām api svabhāva pratibandhe tulyaḥ eva iti grāmya jana dhandhīkaraṇam vandīkaraṇam ati lāghavam āviskaroti vācaspateḥ tathā hi vastu tva aviśeṣe api agniḥ dahati na ākāśam iti atra yathā na ati prasaṅgaḥ saṅgataḥ pramāṇa siddha tvāt asya arthasya tathā bheda aviśeṣe api kiñcid eva kasyacid kāraṇam kāryam ca kiñcid iti atra api na ati prasaṅga avatāraḥ bhede sati tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna lakṣaṇasya kārya kāraṇa bhāvasya pramāṇa siddha tvāt eva na ca evam svābhāvika sambandha śabda vācyaḥ arthaḥ pramāṇa siddhaḥ kaścid asti tad lakṣaṇasya asiddha tvāt ukta tvāt na ca pratijñā siddhe vastuni atiprasaṅgaḥ nābha edhātavyaḥ sarveṣām sarvatra tad rūpa abhyupagama mātreṇa vijetṛ tva prasaṅgāt yat āha alaṅkāra kāraḥ yat kiñcid ātma abhimatam vidhāya niruttaraḥ tatra kṛtaḥ pareṇa vastu svabhāvaiḥ iti vācyam ittham tathā uttaram syāt vijayī samastaḥ iti 
RKNĀ_48.4	 kim ca svābhāvika sambandhaḥ iti kaḥ arthaḥ kim svatas bhūtaḥ sva hetutaḥ bhūtaḥ ahetukaḥ vā iti trayaḥ pakṣāh na tāvat ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ sva ātmani kāritra virodhāt dvitīya pakṣe tu tad utpattiḥ eva sambandhaḥ mukha antareṇa svīkṛtaḥ iti na kaścid vivādaḥ ahetuka tve tu deśa kāla svabhāva niyama abhāva prasaṅgāt iti asaṅgataḥ svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ 
RKNĀ_48.8	 etena yat uktam na sa pakṣāsa pakṣayoḥ darśana adarśanābhyām kāryatvasya gamaka tvam api tu svābhāvika sambandha balāt iti brūmaḥ saḥ eva tu sa pakṣāsa pakṣayoḥ darśana adarśanābhyām vakṣyamāṇena krameṇa pratīyate iti tad iṣṭa kāma tā mātra āviṣkaraṇam iti mantavyam svābhāvika sambandhasya hi upādhi nirapekṣa niyata tvam lakṣaṇam uktam tasya ca ukta nyāyena asiddhau bhūyas darśana janita saṃskāra sahāye carame cetasi manasi vā tathābhūtam niyata tvam parisphurati iti sahṛdayena vaktum aśakya tvāt 
RKNĀ_48.14	 yat ca śabda tattvam iva brāhmaṇa tvam iva iti dṛṣṭāntīkṛtam tat dvayam api asmān pratyasiddham iti dṛṣṭāntayitum anucitam abhijāta maṇi bheda tattvam tu parisphurati iti yuktam tasya hi upadeśa paramparātaḥ māṇikyavat tena api kaṣṭena indradhanuḥ ākāra jyotiḥ ādikam lakṣaṇam niścitam na ca evam svābhāvika sambandha lakṣaṇam tvayā sva kapola racitam api pramāṇena niścitam yena asya api tādṛśī vyavasthā syāt iti yat kiñcid etat 
RKNĀ_48.20	 kim ca bhavatu tāvat ayam anavadhārita rūpaḥ svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ tathā api darśana adarśanābhyām asya grahaṇam ati durlabham tathā hi yadi prācīna aneka darśana janita saṃskāra sahāyena carama cetasā dhūmasya agni niyata tvam grāhyam tadā sa pakṣāsa pakṣayoḥ koṭiśas pravṛtta darśana adarśana janita saṃskāra sahāyena carama cetasā pārthiva tvasya api loha lekhya tva niyata tvam gṛhyate iti pārthiva tvāt api loha lekhya tva siddhiḥ astu atha pārthiva tvasya loha lekhya tva niyata tvam eva na asti vajre vyabhicāra darśanāt tat katham pratyakṣeṇa niyata tva grahaḥ tarhi dhūmasya vahni niyata tvam eva na asti vyabhicāra abhāvasya darśayitum aśakya tvāt tat katham carama cittena niyama grahaḥ iti api tulyam 
RKNĀ_48.28^1	 vyabhicāra adarśanāt avyabhicāraḥ iti ced nanu vyabhicāra adarśanāt avyabhicāraḥ iti kaḥ arthaḥ kim vyabhicāra adarśanāt avyabhicāraḥ vyabhicāra abhāvāt vā prathame pakṣe vyabhicāraḥ bhavatu mā vā vyabhicāra adarśanāt eva avyabhicāraḥ iti niṣṇātam pāṇḍityam atha dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā vyabhicāra abhāvaḥ kutas jñātaḥ adarśanāt iti ced tat kim adarśana mātram dṛśya adarśanam vā prathamam aśaktam na hi adarśane api vyabhicāraḥ na asti iti abhidhātum śakyate cira kāla naṣṭa brāhmaṇī vyabhicāra vat āhatya adarśane api ati cira kāla vyavadhānena vyabhicāra darśanāt 
RKNĀ_48.28^2	 dvitīyam ca asambhavi kvacid kadācid kenacid vyabhicāra darśana sāmagryām satyām vyabhicāra darśanāt darśana sāmagrībhāve tu pratyaya antara vaikalyāt deśa kāla antara varti tvāt vā vyabhicārasya sa lakṣaṇa prāpta tva abhāvāt tasmāt sati api vyabhicāre tad upalambha sāmagrya bhāvāt vyabhicāra anupalambhaḥ prakāra antareṇa vā tad utpatti lakṣaṇena avyabhicāre vyabhicāra anupalambhaḥ iti ubhayathā api vyabhicāra upalambha nivṛttiḥ astu tvayā tu yat avyabhicāra pratipatti nibandhanam darśana adarśanam upavarṇitam tad pārthiva tva ādau vyabhicārāt dhūme api na avyabhicāra nibandhanam iti dhūmaḥ api tvad mate na āśvāsa bhājam iti prasaktam 
RKNĀ_49.9–49.13	 asmad mate tu pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām ekatra kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhau na vyabhicāra śaṅkā sambhavaḥ tad abhāve tu hetumat tām vilaṅghayet iti nyāyāt na saṃśaya piśāca avasaraḥ tat evam bhūyas darśana adarśanābhyām api na vyāpti siddhiḥ tarhi sakṛt sa pakṣāsa pakṣayoḥ darśana adarśanābhyām vyāpteḥ niścayaḥ iti caturthaḥ eva pakṣaḥ astu tathā hi kāryatvasya buddhimat mātra pūrvaka tvena anvayaḥ ghaṭa ādau dṛṣtaḥ ākāśa ādau buddhimat kāraṇa nivṛttau kāryatvasya vyatirekaḥ tatas ca sakṛt anvaya vyatireka siddhau vyāpteḥ siddha tvāt kutas anaikāntika tā 
RKNĀ_49.17	 atra abhidhīyate yadi buddhimat kāraṇa kārya tvayoḥ ekatra pratibandhaḥ pramāṇa pratītaḥ syāt tad ākāśa ādau buddhiman= nivṛttau kāryatvasya nivṛttiḥ iti yuktam sa ca pratibandhaḥ tādātmyam tad utpattiḥ svābhāvikaḥ anyaḥ vā na sidhyati sādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt iti anantaram eva āveditam tatas ca ākāśa ādau buddhimat nivṛttiḥ api syāt na ca kāryatvasya nivṛttiḥ iti sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tvāt anaikāntikam kāryatvam 
RKNĀ_49.22	 nanu ākāśasya asamat mate nitya tvam tvad mate ca asattvam tat katham atas kāryatva vyatirekaḥ sandigdhaḥ iti ced ucyate na hi ākāśe kāryatva vyāvṛtti mātram vyatirekaḥ kin tu sādhya abhāva prayuktaḥ sādhana abhāvaḥ vyatirekaḥ sa ca ākāśe grahītum aśakyaḥ yathā tatra buddhimat kāraṇa nivṛttiḥ tathā acetanasya api kāraṇasya nivṛttiḥ tat kasya abhāva prayuktaḥ kārya abhāvaḥ pratīyatām yena vyatirekaḥ sidhyati 
RKNĀ_49.27	 nanu satyam eva etat yathā ākāśe buddhimat kāraṇa nivṛttiḥ tathā kāraṇa mātrasya api tatra nivṛttiḥ na buddhimat kāraṇa vyatireka anuvidhāyi tvam kāryatvasya niścetum śakyate tathā api ghata ādau kāryatvasya buddhimatā anvaya darśana ākāśe api buddhi mat abhāva prayuktaḥ kāryatva abhāvaḥ pratīyate tat katham vyatireka asiddhiḥ iti ced hanta ghaṭa ādau api na kāryatvasya sattā mātram anvayaḥ kim tu sādhya sadbhāva prayuktaḥ sādhana sadbhāvaḥ sa ca ghaṭe grahītum aśakyaḥ yathā hi tatra buddhimat bhāvaḥ tathā kaṭa kuḍya ādi bhāvaḥ api tat kaḥ evam jānātu kim buddhimat bhāve kāryatvasya bhāvaḥ yat vā kaṭa kuḍya ādi bhāve bhāvaḥ iti tasmāt atra viśiṣṭa anvaya vyatireka grahaṇa pravaṇa viśiṣṭa pratyakṣa anupalambhau anusartavyau yat dṛśyayoḥ eva kārya kāraṇayoḥ tad utpatti siddhau anvaya vyatirekau sidhyataḥ 
RKNĀ_50.4–50.15^1	 na ca pratibandha sādhakam pramāṇam svapne api asti iti caturthaḥ api pakṣaḥ kṣataḥ tat evam buddhimat kārya mātrayoḥ vyāpteḥ asiddhau adhikaraṇa siddhānta nyāyāt upādāna ādi abhijñaḥ sarvajñaḥ puruṣa viśeṣaḥ sidhyati iti pratyāśā durāśā eva yat ca kriyā sāmānyasya pakṣa dharma tā vaśāt cakṣuḥ lakṣaṇa karaṇa viśeṣa siddhiḥ iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ darśitaḥ saḥ api sādhya abhinnaḥ tatra hi rūpa jñānāni atha anupapattyā siddhasya kāraṇa antarasya eva cakṣuḥ indriyam iti nāmakaraṇāt rūpa jñāna janakatva atiriktasya cakṣuḥ lakṣaṇa viśeṣasya asiddha tvāt atha rūpa jñāna janaka tvam eva cakṣuṣṭvam ucyate 
RKNĀ_50.4–50.15^2	 bhavatu kaḥ doṣaḥ etat eva asmābhiḥ kāraṇa antaram ucyate tathā eva yadi tvayā api buddhimat sāmānya āśraya mātrasya puruṣa viśeṣaḥ iti nāma kriyate tadā na asmākam kādacid vipratipattiḥ paramārthataḥ buddhimat sāmānya āśraye sarvajña tva ādi viśeṣaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi viśeṣa vat sidhyati iti tatra vivadāmahe ubhayoḥ api dṛṣṭānta dārṣṭa antikayoḥ viśeṣa sādhana sāmarthya abhāvāt tat ayam saṃkṣepa arthaḥ dṛśye tu sādhye vyabhicāraḥ eva dṛśyam na ced na vyatireka siddhiḥ sādhāraṇa tvāt atha vā vipakṣa sandehataḥ sādhyam atas na sidhyati iti īśvaraḥ dattā jala añjaliḥ 
RKNĀ_50.21	 idānīm sādhana svarūpam nirūpyate yat etat meru mandara medinī ghaṭa paṭa ādi sādhāraṇam kārya mātram sādhanam upanyastam yāvat asya buddhimat anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānam ekatra na avadhāryate tāvat gamaka tvam ayuktam na ca tat svapne api pratyetum śakyam tathā hi kumbhakāra vyāpāre sati mṛd piṇḍāt ghaṭa lakṣaṇam kāryam upalabhyatām nāma na tu vyāpārāt pūrvam ghaṭa vat kārya mātrasya vyatirekaḥ pratyetum śakyaḥ kumbhakāra vyatireke api śoṣa bhaṅga ādi lakṣaṇasya kāryasya mṛd piṇḍe darśanāt na ca yat vinābhūtam yat upalabhyate tat tasya kāryam atiprasaṅgāt tṛṇa ādi vat mṛd piṇḍasya śoṣa bhaṅga ādi kārya mātram api pakṣīkṛtam iti ced kriyatām buddhimat vyatireke kārya mātra vyatirekaḥ tu ektrā api pratipādyatām yena vyāpti siddhau tṛṇa ādiḥ iva śoṣa bhaṅga ādeḥ api buddhimat anumānam syāt ākāśa ādi vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ tu pūrva pratihataḥ buddhimat pūrvaka tvasya iva kāraṣ mātra pūrvaka tvasya api tatra sambhavāt kiṃprayuktaḥ kāryatva abhāvaḥ iti aparijñānāt 
RKNĀ_51.3	 etena yat uktam na vyabhicāra upalambhāt prātisvika viśeṣa parityāgena ghaṭa ādīnām abhūtvā abhavanāt anya rūpam viśeṣam upalakṣayāmaḥ yat niṣṭham puruṣa pūrvaka tvam vyavasthāpayāmaḥ iti tat api prativyūḍham kumbhakāra ādi a bhāve api mṛd piṇḍa ādau śoṣa bhaṅga ādi kārya darśanāt abhūtvā bhāva lakṣaṇasya kārya mātrasya vyatireka asiddheḥ vyāpteḥ abhāvāt 
RKNĀ_51.8	 nanu yadi kāryatva mātrasya na buddhimatā pratyakṣatas vyāpti grahaḥ vyatireka abhāvāt tvayā api tarhi katham kṛtaka tvasya anitya tvena vyāptiḥ avadhāraytaḥ iti ced anapekṣā lakṣaṇa viparyaya bādhaka pramāṇa balāt iti brūmaḥ tat ca atad rūpa parāvṛttasya eva kṛtaka tvasya vipakṣāt vyatirekam sādhayati na ca tvayā viparyaya bādhaka pramāṇam abhidhātum śakyate iti prāk eva pratipāditam sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tvāt anaikāntikam idam kāryatva mātram 
RKNĀ_51.14–51.18	 etena yat etat naiyāyikānām ākṣepa parihāra viḍambanam iha khalu dve kāryatve kārya mātram viśiṣṭam ca tatra ādyasya pratibandhā siddheḥ anaikāntika tvam viśiṣṭasya bhūdhara ādiṣu asambhavāt asiddha tvam iti tat asaṅgatam kāryatva mātrasya eva pratibandha upapādanāt yat ca uktam viśiṣṭam kāryatvam iti kīdṛśam punar tat iti vaktavyam atha yat kāryam puruṣa anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyitayā tad pūrvakam upalabdham yat dṛṣṭeḥ akriyā darśinaḥ api kṛta buddhiḥ utpadyate tat kāryam sakala prāsāda ādi anugatam bhūdhara ādi vyāvṛttam viśiṣṭam iti abhidhīyate tat asundaram vikalpa anupapatteḥ 
RKNĀ_51.22–51.26^1	 tathā ca āha śaṅkaraḥ kṛta buddhiḥ kim sādhya buddhiḥ kim vā sādhana buddhiḥ sādhya buddhiḥ api yadi gṛhīta vyāptikasya sā bhavati eva atha agṛhīta vyāptikasya kim anyatra api sā bhavantī dṛṣṭā atha sādhana buddhiḥ tarhi sva upagama virodhaḥ sarvasya bhāvasya kṛtaka tva upagamāt iti vācaspatiḥ punar atra āha idam atra nipuṇataram nirūpayatu bhavān kim buddhimat anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānam viśeṣaḥ āhosvit tat darśanam yat parvata ādiṣu nasti iti abhidhīyate yadi pūrvakaḥ kalpaḥ sa buddhimat hetuka tvam tanu bhuvana ādīnām ātiṣṭhamānaiḥ abhyupeyate eva na hi kāraṇam kāryān anuvihita bhāva abhāvam anyaḥ vakti ahrīkāt atha tad darśanam iti caramaḥ kalpaḥ na tarhi akriyā darśinaḥ kṛta buddhi sambhavaḥ yaḥ eva hi ghaṭaḥ anena buddhimat anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyī dṛṣṭaḥ saḥ eva kāryaḥ na tu vipaṇi vartī 
RKNĀ_51.26^2	 tad jātīyasya tad anvayavytiḥ eka anuvidhāna darśanāt adṛṣṭa anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānam api tat jātīyam tathā iti ced hanta utpattimat ghaṭa ādi buddhimat anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi iti anyat api tanu bhuvana ādikam tathā bhavat na daṇḍena parāṇudyate ghaṭa jātīyam utpattimat buddhimat pūrvakam iti ced nanu prāsāda ādi tad hetukam na bhavet aghaṭa jātīya tvāt atha yat jātīyam anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi dṛṣṭam tad jātīyam eva adṛṣṭa anvaya vyatirekam api tad hetukam tat kim kārya jātīyam prāsāda ādi buddhimat hetukam na dṛṣṭam yena utpattimat tanu bhuvana ādi tathā na syāt na khalu tad jātīya tve kaścid viśeṣaḥ iti 
RKNĀ_52.8^1	 vittokaḥ tu āha bhavatu vā kaścid anirūpita rūpaḥ viśeṣaḥ kim punar anena viśeṣam pratipādayatā abhipretam kim kāryatva sāmānyasya asiddha tvam atha kārya viśeṣasya atha kārya mātrasya buddhimat kartṛ vyabhicāraḥ atha sādhya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ vaidharmya mātram kim ca atas yadi tāvat kārya sāmānyasya asiddha tvam tat na asti viśvambhara ādiṣu api kāraṇa vyāpāra janya tvasya ubhaya siddha tvāt atha kārya viśeṣasya kumbha ādi vartinaḥ pakṣe asiddhiḥ abhidhīyate tadā na kācid atra kṣatiḥ viśeṣasya hetu tvena anupādānāt yadi kārya sāmānyasya kartṛ vyabhicāraḥ pratipādayitum iṣṭaḥ 
RKNĀ_52.8^2	 sa na śakyaḥ vipakṣe adarśanāt tṛṇa ādeḥ ca pakṣīkṛta tvāt śaṅkā mātrasya sarvathā aniṣiddha tvāt sandigdha vyatireki tvam naiyāyikānām niranuyojya anuyogaḥ bauddhānām adoṣa udbhāvanam nigraha sthānam iti tu pratipāditam tathā api bādhaka pramāṇāni abhiditāni eva tasmāt na pratibandha asiddheḥ sarvatra vyabhicāra āśaṅkā atha sādhya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ vaidharmya udbhāvanam tat na tasya sarvatra sulabha tvāt yadi sādhya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ vaidharmya mātrāt sādhya asiddhiḥ nivṛtta idānīm anumāna vārtā api nikuñja mahānasayoḥ api dhūmavat tve api kathañcid vaidharmya upapatteḥ iti sakalam yat kiñcid etat iti 
RKNĀ_52.22^1	 tat ayam atra saṃkṣepa arthaḥ yat tāvat kāryatva mātram tat eva uktena krameṇa pratibandha siddheḥ bhūdhara ādiṣu dṛṣṭam puruṣam anumāpayati iti asmākam abhimata sādhya siddhiḥ upapannā eva iti kim asmākam adhika cintayā iti aṅgīkṛtya api uktam viśiṣṭa kārya tvam tat eva tu na asti iti punar vistareṇa pratipāditam iti tat api sarvam anavadheyam eva tathā hi kāryatva mātrasya tāvat uktena krameṇa vyāpteḥ asiddha tvāt anaikāntika tvam anirvāyam yat ca viśiṣṭa kārya tvam vikalpya dūṣitam tasya asmābhiḥ anabhyupagata tvāt tad dūṣaṇāya prabandhaḥ prayāsa eka phalaḥ na hi kārya tvam dvividham abhimatam ekam sarva kārya anugatam aparam parvata ādi vyāvṛttam ghaṭa paṭa prāsāda ādi anuyāyi iti kim tu kāryam aneka jātīyakam 
RKNĀ_52.22^2	 tatra yadi nāma paṭasya prāsāda ādibhiḥ saha vastu tva saṃsthāna viśeṣa yogi tva kārya tva ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ sajātīya tvam asti tathā api na tān dharmān buddhimat pūrvakān adhigacchati vyāvahārikam pratyakṣam kāryatva ādīnām buddhimat vyatireka anuvidhāna abhāvāt tat katham prāsāda parvata ādiṣu kārya tva ādi darśanāt buddhimat anumānam astu kim tu yasya eva ghaṭa jātīya kārya cakrasya vyatireka siddhiḥ tasya buddhimat vyāpta tvam pratyakṣataḥ sidhyati iti uktam tena deśa kāla antare ghaṭa jātīyāt eva buddhimat anumānam yadā tu prāsāda jātīyakam api buddhimat hetukam ekatra pṛthak avadhāryate tadā tad jātīyāt api buddhimat siddhiḥ evam tad tad jātīya sarāva udañcana śakaṭa paṭa keyūra prabhṛtteḥ kārya cakrāt buddhimat pūrvaka tvena pṛthak pṛthak avadhāritāt buddhimat anumānam anavadyam 
RKNĀ_52.22^3	 amum eva artham abhisandhāya ācārya pādaiḥ abhihitam siddham yādṛś adhiṣṭhātṛ bhāva abhāva anuvṛttimat sanniveśa ādi tat yuktam tasmāt yat anumīyate iti evam ghaṭa paṭa parvata dīnām kāryatva vastu tva ādibhiḥ dharmaiḥ sajātīya tve a pi avāntaram ghaṭa paṭa parvata tva ādi jāti bhedam ādāya lokasya vyāpti grāhakam pratyakṣam pravartate iti darśayitum saṃvyavahāra pragalbha puruṣa buddhi apekṣayā yad darśanāt akriyā darśinaḥ api kṛta buddhiḥ bhavati iti uktam na tu śāstra para vaśa buddhi puruṣa apekṣayā tathā hi śāstra saṃskāra rahitasya vyavahāra pragalbhasya puruṣasya devakula jātīyakam puruṣa pūrvakatayā avadhāritavataḥ nagarāt vanam praviṣṭasya parvata devakulayoḥ darśane tayoḥ dvayoḥ api akriyā darśinaḥ api devakule kṛta buddhiḥ bhavati na parvate 
RKNĀ_52.22^4	 tat anayoḥ devakula parvatayoḥ kārya tva ādinā eka jāti tve api kṛta buddhi bhāva abhāvau na tayoḥ parvata devakula tva lakṣaṇa avāntara jāti bhedam anavasthāpya sthātum prabhavataḥ jāti bhede ca siddhe devakula jātīye vyāpteḥ grahaṇāt na parvata jātīyasya na ca prāsāda jātīyasya vyāpti siddhiḥ iti na tatas buddhimat anumānam yadā tu prāsādasya api pṛthak vyāpti grahaḥ tadā tad jātīyāt api buddhimat anumānam astu na kṣitidharā ādi jātīyasya svapne api vyāpti grahaḥ krīḍā parvata ādeḥ nāma mātrā bhede api parvata ādibhiḥ ekāntataḥ bhinna svarūpa tvāt yat ca pṛṣṭam kā iyam kṛta buddhiḥ ityādi tatra kāmam sādhya buddhiḥ eva iti brūmaḥ yat ca atra uktam sādhya buddhiḥ api yadi gṛhīta vyāptikasya sā bhavati eva atha agṛhīta vyāptikasya kim anyatra api sā bhavatī dṛṣṭā iti 
RKNĀ_53.23	 atra ucyate gṛhīta vyāptikasya anumānam bhavati agṛhīta vyāptikasya na bhavati iti atra asmākam na kācid vipratipattiḥ kevalam gṛhīta vyāptikaḥ asmin viṣaye na sambhavati iti brūmaḥ ukta krameṇa vyatireka asiddheḥ vyāvahārika pratyakṣeṇa kāryatvasya vyāpta tva aniścayāt tasmāt avāntara jāti bheda prasiddhi artham vyāvahārika puruṣa apekṣayā eva asyāḥ buddheḥ bhāva abhāvau uktau jāti bhede ca prayojanam pūrvam eva pratipāditam 
RKNĀ_53.28–54.1	 yat api atra nipuṇam anyena vācaspattinā kathitam tat kim kārya jātīyam prāsāda ādi buddhimat hetukam na dṛṣṭam yena utpattimat tanu bhuvana ādi tathā na syāt na khalu tad jātīyaka tve kascit viśeṣaḥ iti tat asaṅgatam tathā hi bhavatu prāsāda parvata ādīnām kāryatva ādinā sajātīya tvam tat tu na vyāvahārika pratyakṣeṇa buddhimat vyāptam pratyetum śakyam vyāpti grahaṇa samaye dṛṣṭānte buddhi mat abhāva prayuktasya kārya mātra vyatirekasya darśayitum aśakya tvāt tat ayam saṃkṣepa arthaḥ kāryatva mātrasya avyatirekāt avyāptasya āgamaka tvam avāntaram tu ghaṭa prāsāda ādi sādhāraṇam kāryatva mātram asmābhiḥ api na svīkṛtam eva yathā tu ghaṭa tva paṭa tva ādi prātisvika aneka jāti puraskāreṇa prasiddha anumāna vyavasthā sā ca anavadyam avasthāpitā iti 
RKNĀ_54.5	 saṃprati sādhya ātmā vicāryate nanu vādinā sādhane samupanyaste tad dūṣaṇa upanyāsam apāsya sādhyasvarūpavikalpanam nāma naiyāyika mate niranuyojya anuyogaḥ saugata mate tu adoṣa udbhāvanam nigraha sthānam iti ced tat etat jālma jalpitam tathā hi sādhya svarūpe apariniṣṭhite tad anusāriṇī pakṣa sa pakṣa vipakṣa vyavasthā kutas tad asiddhau ca asiddhatā ādayaḥ doṣāḥ pakṣa dharmatā ādayaḥ ca guṇāḥ na vyavasthitāḥ iti uktam na idānīm hetoḥ doṣa guṇa kathā iti mūkena prativādinā sthātavyam tasmāt dhetu doṣa upanyāsā eva iyam sādhya niruktiḥ iti ayam eva vādī sva mate niranuyojya anuyoga dūṣaṇena nigraha sthānena nigṛhyate iti kim atra nirbandhena 
RKNĀ_54.13–54.16	 yat etat kārya tvam sādhanam kim anena viśvasya buddhimat mātra pūrvaka tvam sādhyate āhosvit eka tva vibhu tva sarvajña tva nitya tva ādi guṇa viśiṣṭa buddhimat pūrvaka tvam prathama pakṣe siddha sādhanam dvitīye tu vyāpteḥ abhāvāt anaikāntika tā nanu sāmānyena vyāptau pratītāyām api pakṣa dharma tā balāt viśeṣa siddhiḥ yathā agneḥ parvata ayoga vyavaccheda ādi siddhiḥ anyathā sarva anumāna ucchedaḥ anumāna dveṣī hi evam jalpati anumāna bhaṅga paṅke asmin nimagnāḥ vādi dantinaḥ viśeṣe anugama abhāvaḥ sāmānye siddha sādhya tā 
RKNĀ_54.21^1	 atra ucyate sidhyati eva pakṣa dharmatā balataḥ viśeṣaḥ na tu sarvaḥ yena hi vinā pakṣa stham sādhanam na upapadyate sa viśeṣaḥ sidhyatu yathā vahneḥ eva parvata varti tva ādi viśeṣaḥ na pañca varṇa śikhā kalāpa kamanīyaḥ na ca girīṇām tarūṇām kārya tvam kartuḥ eka tva vibhu tva sarvajñatva ādikam antareṇa na upapadyate tad itareṣu api darśanāt tasmāt pakṣā yoga vyavaccheda bheda mātre na dūṣaṇam iṣṭa siddhi anvaya abhāvāt atirikte tu dūṣaṇam yadi evam sva svarūpa upādāna upakaraṇa saṃpradāna prayojana abhijñaḥ eva kartā sādhyate svarūpam iha ca dvi aṇukam kāryam 
RKNĀ_54.21^2	 upādānam iha paramāṇu jāti catuṣṭayam upakaraṇam samasta kṣetrajña samavāyi dharma adharmau sampradanam kṣetrajñāḥ yān ayam bhagavān sva karmabhiḥ abhipraiti prayojanam sukha duḥkha upabhogaḥ kṣetrajñānām evaṃbhūte buddhimati sādhye kutas siddha sādhanam na ca avyāptiḥ kulāla dṛṣṭānte upādāna ādi abhijña tvasya sambhavāt tathā ca vācaspatiḥ pramāṇyati vivāda adhyāsitāḥ tanu giri sāgara ādayaḥ upādāna ādi abhijña kartṛkāḥ kāryatvāt yat yat kāryam tat tat upādāna ādi abhijña kartṛkam yathā prāsāda ādi tathā ca vivāda adhyāsitāḥ tanu ādayaḥ tasmāt tathā iti 
RKNĀ_55.8	 evam atas sādhanāt upādāna ādi abhijña kartṛ mātram prasādhya tasya sarvajña tva sādhanāya vācaspatiḥ eva punar api idam āha bhavatu tāvat upādāna ādi abhijña kartṛ mātra siddhiḥ pāriśeṣyāt tu vyatireki dvitīya nāmnaḥ anumānāt viśeṣa siddhiḥ tathā hi tanu bhuvana ādi upādāna ādi abhijñaḥ kartā na anitya asarva viṣaya buddhimān tat kartuḥ tad upādāna ādi anabhijña tva prasaṅgāt na hi evaṃvidhaḥ tad upādāna ādi abhijñaḥ yathā asmad ādiḥ tad upādāna ādi abhijñaḥ ca ayam tasmāt tathā iti 
RKNĀ_55.16–55.18	 no khalu paramāṇu bhedān kṣetrajña samavāyinaḥ ca karma āśaya bhedān aparimeyān anyaḥ śaktaḥ jñātum ṛte tādṛś īśvarāt iti atra ucyate yāvanti dvi aṇukāni bhinna deśa kāla svabhāvāni kāryāṇi santi teṣu sarveṣu eva kim ekaḥ eva buddhimān vyāpriyate anekaḥ vā yat vā sva sva viṣaya mātra upādāna ādi vedinaḥ paraspara vyāpāra anabhijñāḥ bhinna deśa kāla svabhāvāḥ pratidvi aṇukam anyaḥ eva buddhimantaḥ vyāpriyante iti trayaḥ pakṣāḥ 
RKNĀ_55.22–55.27	 na tāvat prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ deśa kāla svabhāva bhinnānām sarveṣām dvi aṇukānām kartuḥ ekatva asiddheḥ yat ca eka tva sādhanāya kārya liṅga aviśeṣāt ityādi api sādhanam upanyastam tat asaṅgatam dhūma liṅga aviśeṣe api hi agneḥ aneka tva vat tatra api tad śaṅkā sambhavāt sat iti liṅga aviśeṣāt iti tu dṛṣṭāntaḥ asmān pratyasiddhaḥ eva tasmāt yathā mayā nānā tva sādhanāya pramāṇam vaktavyam tathā tvayā api eka tva sādhanāya sādhanam abhidhānīyam atha manyate aneka tva sādhana abhāvāt ekatva siddhiḥ iti yadi evam eka tva sādhana abhāvat aneka tvam eva kim na avagacchasi 
RKNĀ_55.29	 yat api uktam eka tve tu na pramāṇa antaram anveṣṭavyam ekasya kartuḥ abhāve bahūnām vyāhata manasām ityādi tat api cintyatām bahubhiḥ karaṇe yugapad kārya anutpattiḥ iti kim bhinna deśa kālānām kāryāṇām anutpattiḥ vivakṣitā ekasya eva vā mahāvayavinaḥ kṣiti ghaṭa ādi rūpasya tatra ekasmin api kārye bahubhiḥ karaṇe utpatti virodhinam na paśyāmaḥ bahūnām parasparam vaimatya niyama abhāvāt paraspara avyāghāta puruṣa tvayoḥ dvividhasya api virodhasya asambhavāt puruṣa tvam hi apuruṣa tvena viruddham na tu paraspara avyāghātena 
RKNĀ_56.5	 ye tu ananta deśa kāla svabhāva bheda bhinnāḥ teṣu sutarām eva aneka vyāpāra niṣedhaḥ asambhavi iti dvitīyaḥ api pakṣaḥ vyudastaḥ na ca kartuḥ ekatvena dṛṣṭā vyāpti siddhiḥ anekena api svatantreṇa sva sva prayojana arthinā grāma praviṣṭa hariṇa ādi māraṇa eka kārya darśanāt tasya api pakṣīkaraṇe eka kartṛ pūrvaka abhimatasya api pakṣīkaraṇe ātma kartṛ pūrvaka tvam astu tat evam na sarva dvi aṇukānām kartuḥ ekatva siddhiḥ tathā ca uktam eka kartuḥ na siddhau tu sarvajña tvam kim āśrayam 
RKNĀ_56.11–56.13	 atas eva dvitīyaḥ api pakṣaḥ kṣīṇaḥ saveṣu dvi aṇukeṣu ekasya api kartuḥ apravṛttau bahūnām sutarām apravṛtteḥ tṛtīyaḥ tu pakṣaḥ yadi bhavet tadā sva sva vyāpāra viṣaya mātra upādāna ādi abhijña tve api na ekaḥ kaścid sarvajñaḥ sidhyati na ca jñāna sattā mātreṇa katipaya ati indriya darśana vat sarva artha grahaṇam yena tad abhedāt prastuta paramāṇu vat sarvasya eva aviśeṣeṇa grahaṇāt sarvajña tā syāt anumānataḥ hi katipaya ati indriya darśane siddhe api īśvarasya tad kāraṇa yogi tvam niścīyate na tu jñāna sāttā mātreṇa prakāra antareṇa iti niścayaḥ iti kutas sarvajña tā 
RKNĀ_56.19	 nanu atīndriyam paramāṇu ādikam jānataḥ na katham sārvajñyam iti ced tat kim idānīm asarva darśi tveṣu atīndriya darśana mātreṇa sarvajña tā pratyaya āśā evam eva iti ced hanta yadi nāma nyāya vihastena tvayā īdṛśaḥ hasta samāracitaḥ sarvajñaḥ paribhāvitaḥ tathā api anyeṣām apāra dūra deśa kāla vartinām dvi aṇuka ādīnām upādāna ādiṣu januṣā andha prakhyasya parama puruṣa artha āvedinaḥ vā lokaiḥ prāmāṇikaiḥ ca na asya sārvajñyam anumanyate 
RKNĀ_56.24	 asmākan tu na ati indriya darśi mātre pradveṣaḥ evam ca kartuḥ ekatva asiddhau vyatireki api hetuḥ asamarthaḥ viśveṣām ekasya kartuḥ asiddhau tad upādāna ādi abhijña bhāvasya asiddha tvāt yaḥ ca yat mātra kāraḥ sa tanmātra upādāna ādi abhijñaḥ bhavat na sarvajñaḥ aneka āśrayeṇa api upādāna ādi abhijña sāmānyasya caritārtha tvāt tat evam upādāna ādi abhijña puruṣa mātra siddhau api na eka tva sarvajña tva ādi viśiṣṭa puruṣa viśeṣa siddhiḥ puruṣa mātre ca siddha sādhanam uktam buddhimat mātra pūrvaka tām icchatām upādāna ādi abhijña buddhimat pūrvaka tve sādhye katham siddha sādhanam iti ced na tad apekṣayā siddha sādhyatāyāḥ janita tvāt kevalam asiddha uddhāre a bhimate viśeṣe siddhe api naiyāyikasya api na abhimata siddhiḥ iti brūmaḥ 
RKNĀ_57.3	 saugatasya tāvat aniṣṭa siddhiḥ iti ced na sva abhimata sādhya sādhanena eva hi parasya aniṣṭam api sādhanīyam anyathā mātṛ śoka smaraṇa ādinā api tad aniṣṭa siddhiḥ syāt iti asya saṅgrahaḥ pareṣṭa siddhiḥ na para iṣṭa bādhakam prasādhane vedana yatna mātrayoḥ ananvayaḥ abhīṣṭa viśeṣa sādhane vipakṣa sandeha sahantu sādhanam sādhya cintā adhikāraḥ tṛtīyaḥ 
RKNĀ_57.11–57.14	 evam anye api hetavaḥ yathāyogam abhyūhya dūṣaṇīyāḥ tat evam tāvat īśvarasya sat vyavahāraḥ niṣiddhaḥ asat vyavahāra arthan tu tad lakṣaṇa vilakṣaṇa kṣaṇa bhaṅga sādhakam sattā ādi sādhanam eva draṣṭavyam iti iti abodha jana kartṛ vikalpa vyāpi moha timira pratirodhi ratna kīrtiḥ acana amala ramya jyotiḥ astu ciram apratirodhi 
RKNĀ_58.4–58.9	 namaḥ tārāyai apohaḥ śabda arthaḥ nirucyate nanu kaḥ ayam apohaḥ nāma kim idam anyasmāt apohyate asmāt vā anyat apohyate asmin vā anyat apohyate iti vyutpattyā vijāti vyāvṛttam bāhyam eva vivakṣitam buddhi ākāraḥ vā yadi vā apohanam apohaḥ iti anya vyāvṛtti mātram iti trayaḥ pakṣāḥ na tāvat ādimau pakṣau apoha nāmnā vidheḥ eva vivakṣita tvāt antimaḥ api asaṅgataḥ pratīti bādhita tvāt tathā hi parvata uddeśe vahniḥ asti iti śābdī pratītiḥ vidhi rūpam eva ullikhantī lakṣyate na anagniḥ na bhavati iti nitrṛtti mātram āmukhayantī yat ca pratyakṣa bādhitam na tatra sādhana antara avakāśaḥ iti ati prasiddham 
RKNĀ_58.13	 atha yadi api nivṛttim aham pratyemi iti na vikalpaḥ tathā api nivṛtta padārtha ullekhaḥ eva nivṛtti ullekhaḥ na hi anantr bhāvita viśeṣaṇa pratītiḥ viśiṣṭa pratītiḥ tatas yathā sāmānyam aham pratyemi iti vikalpa abhāve api sādhāraṇa ākāra parisphuraṇāt vikalpa buddhiḥ sāmānya buddhiḥ pareṣām tathā nivṛtta pratyaya ākṣiptā nivṛtti buddhiḥ apoha pratīti vyavahāram ātanoti iti ced 
RKNĀ_58.18–58.23	 nanu sādhāraṇa ākāra parisphuraṇe vidhi rūpa tayā yadi sāmānya bodha vyavasthā tat kim āyātam asphurat abhāva ākāre cetasi nivṛtti pratīti vyavasthāyāḥ tatas nivṛttim aham pratyemi iti evam ākāra abhāve api nivṛtti ākāra sphuraṇam yadi syāt kaḥ nāma nivṛtti pratīti sthitim apalapet anyathā asati pratibhāse tad pratīti vyavahṛtiḥ iti gavā ākāre api cetasi turaga bodhaḥ iti astu atha viśeṣaṇtayā antarbhūtā nivṛtti pratītiḥ iti uktam tathā api yadi agavāpa ūḍhaḥ iti īdṛśa ākāraḥ vikalpaḥ tadā viśeṣaṇa tayā tad anupraveśaḥ bhavatu kim tu gauḥ iti pratītiḥ tadā ca sataḥ api nivṛtti lakṣaṇasya viśeṣaṇasya tatra anud kalanāt katham tad pratīti vyavasthā 
RKNĀ_58.27–59.4	 atha evam matiḥ yat vidhi rūpam sphurati tasya parāpohaḥ api asti iti tad pratītiḥ ucyate tadā api sambandha mātram apohasya vidhiḥ eva sākṣāt nirbhāsī api ca evam adhyakṣasya api apoha viṣaya tvam anivāryam viśeṣataḥ vikalpāt eka vyāvṛtta ullekhinaḥ akhilāni avyāvṛttam īkṣamāṇasya tasmāt vidhi ākāra avagrahāt adhyakṣa vat vikalpasya api vidhi viṣaya tvam eva na anya apoha viṣaya tvam iti katham apohaḥ śabda arthaḥ ghuṣyate atra abhidhīyate na asmābhiḥ apoha śabdena vidhiḥ eva kevalaḥ abhipretaḥ na api anya vyāvṛtti mātram kin tu anya apoha viśiṣṭaḥ vidhiḥ śabdānām arthaḥ tatas ca na pratyeka pakṣa upanipāti doṣa avakāśaḥ 
RKNĀ_59.7^1	 yat tu goḥ pratītau na tad ātmā apara ātmā iti sāmarthyāt apohaḥ paścāt niścīyate iti vidhivādinām matam anya apoha pratītau vā sāmarthyāt anya apoḍhaḥ avadhāryate iti pratiṣedha vādinām matam tat asundaram prāthamikasya api pratipatti krama adarśanāt na hi vidhim pratipadya kaścid arthāpattitaḥ paścāt apoham avagacchati apoham vā pratipadya anya apoḍham tasmāt goḥ pratipattiḥ iti anya apoḍha pratipattiḥ ucyate yadi api ca anya apoḍha śabdānullekhaḥ uktaḥ tathā api na apratipattiḥ eva viśeṣaṇa bhūtasya apohasya agavāpa ūḍhaḥ eva go śabdasya niveśita tvāt 
RKNĀ_59.7^2	 yathā nīlotpale niveśitāt indīvara śabdāt nīlotpala pratītau tad kāle eva nīlim a sphuraṇam anivāryam tathā go śabdāt api agavāpoḍhe niveśitāt go pratītau tulya kālam eva viśeṣaṇtvāt agaḥ apoha sphuraṇam anivāryam yathā pratyakṣasya prasajya rūpa abhāva agrahaṇam abhāva vikalpa utpādana śaktiḥ eva tathā vidhi vikalpānām api tad anurūpa anuṣṭhāna dāna śaktiḥ eva abhāva grahaṇam abhidhīyate paryudāsa rūpa abhāva grahaṇam tu niyata svarūpa saṃvedanam ubhayoḥ aviśiṣṭam anyathā yadi śabdāt artha pratipatti kāle kalitaḥ na parāpohaḥ katham anya parihāreṇa pravṛttiḥ tatas gām badhāna iti coditaḥ aśva ādīn api badhnīyāt 
RKNĀ_59.21	 yat api avocat vācaspatiḥ jātimatyaḥ vyaktayaḥ vikalpānām śabdānām ca gocaraḥ tāsām ca tadvatīnām rūpam atajjātīya parāvṛttim iti atas tad avagateḥ na gām badhāna iti coditaḥ aśva ādīn badhnāti tat api anena eva nirastam yatas jāteḥ adhikāyāḥ prakṣepe api vyaktīnām rūpam atajjātīya parāvṛttam eva ced tadā tena eva rūpeṇa śabda vikalpayoḥ viṣayī bhavantīnām katham atad vyāvṛtti parihāraḥ 
RKNĀ_59.26–60.6	 atha na vijātīya vyāvṛttam vyakti rūpam tathā apratītam vā tadā jāti prasādaḥ eṣaḥ iti katham arthataḥ api tad avagatiḥ iti ukta prāyam atha jāti balāt eva anyatas avyāvṛttam bhavatu jāti balāt sva hetu paramparā balāt vā anya vyāvṛttam ubhayathā api vyāvṛtta pratipattau vyāvṛtti pratipattiḥ asti eva na ca āgavāpoḍhe go śabda saṅketa vidhau anyonya āśraya doṣaḥ sāmānye tadvati vā saṃkete api tad doṣau akāśāt na hi sāmānyam nāma sāmānya mātram abhipretam turage api go śabda saṃketa prasaṅgāt kim tu go tvam tāvatā ca saḥ eva doṣaḥ gavā ādi parijñāne go tva sāmānya aparijñānāt go tva sāmānya aparijñāne go śabda vācya aparijñānāt tasmāt eka piṇḍa darśana pūrvakaḥ yaḥ sarva vyakti sādhāraṇaḥ iva bahis adhyastaḥ vikalpa buddhi ākāraḥ tatra ayam gauḥ iti saṃketa karaṇe na itaretara āśraya doṣaḥ 
RKNĀ_60.8–60.16	 abhimate ca go śabda pravṛttau ago śabdena śeṣasya api abhidhānam ucitam na ca anya apoḍhā anya apohayoḥ virodhaḥ viśeṣya viśeṣaṇa bhāva kṣatiḥ vā paraspara vyavaccheda abhāvāt sāmānādhikaraṇya sadbhāvāt bhū tala ghaṭa abhāva vat svābhāvena hi virodhaḥ na parābhāvena iti ābāla prasiddham eṣa panthāḥ śrudhnam upatiṣṭhate iti atra api apohaḥ gamyate eva aprakṛta patha antara apekṣayā eṣaḥ eva śrudhna pratyanīka aniṣṭa sthāna apekṣayā śrudhnam eva araṇya mārgavat viccheda abhāvāt upatiṣṭhate eva sārtha dūta ādi vyavacchedena panthāḥ eva iti pratipadam vyavacchedasya sulabha tvāt tasmāt apoha dharmaṇaḥ vidhi rūpasya śabdāt avagatiḥ puṇḍarīka śabdāt iva śvetim aviśiṣṭasya padmasya yadi evam vidhiḥ eva śabda arthaḥ vaktum ucitaḥ katham apohaḥ gīyate iti ced uktam atra apoha śabdena anya apoha viśiṣṭaḥ vidhiḥ ucyate tatra vidhau pratīyamāne viśeṣaṇa tayā tulya kālam anya apoha pratītiḥ iti 
RKNĀ_60.19	 na ca evam pratyakṣasya api apoha viṣaya tva vyavasthā kartum ucitā tasya śābda pratyayasya iva vastu viṣaya tve vivāda abhāvāt vidhi śabdena ca yathā adhyavasāyam atad rūpa parāvṛttaḥ bāhyaḥ arthaḥ abhimataḥ yathāpratibhāsam buddhi ākāraḥ ca tatra bāhyaḥ arthaḥ adhyavasāyāt eva śabda vācyaḥ vyavasthāpyate na sva lakṣaṇa parisphūrtyāḥ pratyakṣa vat deśa kāla avasthā niyata pravyakta sva lakṣaṇa asphuraṇāt yat śāstram śabdena avyāpṛta akṣasya buddhau apratibhāsanāt arthasya dṛṣṭau iva iti indriya śabda svabhāva upāya bhedāt ekasya eva arthasya pratibhāsa bhedaḥ iti ced atra api uktam jātaḥ nāma āśrayaḥ anyānyaḥ cetasām tasya vastutas ekasya eva kutas rūpam bhinna ākāra avabhāsi tat 
RKNĀ_60.29–61.3	 na hi spaṣṭāspaṣṭe dve rūpe paraspara viruddhe ekasya vastunaḥ staḥ yatas ekena indriya buddhau pratibhāseta anyena vikalpe tathā sati vastunaḥ eva bheda prāpteḥ na hi svarūpa bhedāt aparaḥ vastu bhedaḥ na ca pratibhāsa bhedāt aparaḥ svarūpa bhedaḥ anyathā trailokyam ekam eva vastu syāt dūra āsanna deśa vartinoḥ puruṣayoḥ ekatra śākhini spaṣṭa aspaṣṭa pratibhāsa bhede api na śākhi bhedaḥ iti ced na brūmaḥ pratibhāsa bhedaḥ bhinna vastu niyataḥ kim tu eka viṣaya tva abhāva niyate iti tatas yatra artha kriyā bheda ādi sacivaḥ pratibhāsa bhedaḥ tatra vastu bhedaḥ ghaṭa vat anyatra punar niyamena eka viṣaya tām pariharati iti eka pratibhāsaḥ bhrāntaḥ 
RKNĀ_61.7	 etena yat āha vācaspatiḥ na ca śabda pratyakṣayoḥ vastu gocara tve pratyaya abhedaḥ kāraṇa bhedena pārokṣya apārokṣya bheda upapatteḥ iti tat na upayogi parokṣa pratyayasya vastu gocara tva asam artha tāt parokṣata āśrayaḥ tu kāraṇa bhedaḥ indriya gocara grahaṇa viraheṇa eva kṛtārthaḥ tat na śābde pratyaye sva lakṣaṇam parisphurati kim ca sva lakṣaṇa ātmani vastuni vācye sarva ātmanā pratipatteḥ vidhi niṣedhayoḥ ayogaḥ tasya hi sadbhāve asti iti vyartham na asti iti asamartham asadbhāve tu na asti iti vyartham asti iti asamartham asti ca asti ādi pada prayogaḥ tasmāt śābda pratibhāsasya bāhya artha bhāva abhāva sādhāraṇyam na tat viṣaya tām kṣamate 
RKNĀ_61.15	 yat ca vācaspatinā jātimat vyakti vācya tām sva vācā eva prastutya antaram eva na ca śabda arthasya jāteḥ bhāva abhāva sādhāraṇyam na upapadyate sā hi svarūpataḥ nityā api deśa kāla viprakīrṇa aneka vyakti āśraya tayā bhāva abhāva sādha araṇībhavanti astināsti sambandha yogyā vartamāna vyakti sambandhitā hi jāteḥ astitāḥ atīta anāgata vyakti sambandhi tā ca na astitā iti sandigdha vyatireki tvāt anaikāntikam bhāva abhāva sādhāraṇyam anyathā siddham vā iti vikalpitam tat aprastutam tāvatā tāvat na prakṛta kṣatiḥ jātau bharam nyasyatā sva lakṣaṇa vācya tvasya svayam svīkārāt kim ca sarvatra padārthaya sva lakṣaṇa svarūpeṇa eva astitva ādikam cintyate jāteḥ tu vartamāna ādi vyakti sambadhī astitva ādikam iti tu bāla pratāraṇam evam jātimat vyakti vacane api doṣaḥ vyakteḥ ced pratīti siddhiḥ jātiḥ adhikā pratīyatām mā vā na tu vyakti pratīti doṣāt muktiḥ 
RKNĀ_61.25–62.1	 etena yat ucyate kaumārilaiḥ sa bhāga tvāt eva vastunaḥ na sādhāraṇya doṣaḥ vṛkṣa tvam hi anirdhārita bhāva abhāvam śabdāt avagamyate tayoḥ anyatareṇa śabda antara avagatena sambadhyate iti tat api asaṅgatam sāmānyasya nityasya pratipattau anirdhārita bhāva abhāva tva ayogāt yat ca idam na ca pratyakṣasya iva śabdānām artha pratyāyana prakāraḥ yena tat dṛṣṭaḥ iva asti ādi śabda apekṣā na syāt vicitra śakti tvāt pramāṇānām iti tat api aindriya kaśābda pratibhāsayoḥ eka svarūpa grāhi tve bhinna avabhāsa dūṣaṇena dūṣitam vicitra śakti tvam ca pramāṇānām sākṣātkāra adhyavasāyābhyām api caritārtham tatas yadi pratyakṣa artha pratipādanam śābdena tadvat eva avabhāsaḥ syāt abhavan ca na tad viṣaya khyāpanam kṣamate 
RKNĀ_62.6–62.8	 nanu vṛkṣa śabdena vṛkṣa tva aṃśaḥ codite sattva ādi aṃśa niścayana artham asti ādi pada prayogaḥ iti ced niraṃśa tvena pratyakṣa samadhigatasya sva lakṣaṇasya kaḥ avakāśaḥ pada antareṇa dharma antara vidhi niṣedhayoḥ pramāṇa antareṇa vā pratyakṣe api pramāṇa antara apekṣā dṛṣṭā iti ced bhavatu tasya aniścaya ātmaka tvāt anabhyasta svarūpa viṣaye vikalpaḥ tu svayam niścaya ātmakaḥ yatra grāhī tatra kim apareṇa asti ca śabda liṅga antara apekṣā tatas na vastu svarūpa grahaḥ 
RKNĀ_62.13	 nanu bhinnāḥ jāti ādayaḥ dharmāḥ parasparam dharmiṇaḥ ca iti jāti lakṣaṇa eka dharma dvāreṇa pratīte api śākhini dharma antara vat tayā na pratītiḥ iti kim na bhinna abhidhāna adhīnaḥ dharma antarasya nīla cala uccais tara tva ādeḥ avabodhaḥ tat etat asaṅgatam akhaṇḍa ātmanaḥ sva lakṣaṇasya pratyakṣe api pratibhāsāt dṛśyasya dharma dharmi bhedasya pratyakṣa pratikṣit pata tvāt anyathā sarvam sarvatra syāt iti atiprasaṅgaḥ kālpanika bheda āśrayaḥ tu dharma dharmi vyavahāraḥ iti prasādhitam śāstre 
RKNĀ_62.19	 bhavatu vā pāramārthikaḥ api dharma dharmi bhedaḥ tathā api anayoḥ samavāya ādeḥ dūṣita tvāt upakāra lakṣaṇā eva pratyāsattiḥ eṣitavyāḥ evam ca yathā indriya pratyāsattyā pratyakṣeṇa dharmi pratipattau sakala tad dharma pratipattiḥ tathā śabda liṅgābhyām api vācya vācaka ādi sambandha pratibaddhābhyām dharmi pratipatau niravaśeṣa tad dharma pratipattiḥ bhavet pratyāsatti mātrasya aviśeṣāt 
RKNĀ_62.24	 yat ca vācaspatiḥ na ca eka upādhinā sattvena viśiṣṭe tasmin gṛhīte upādhi antara viśiṣṭaḥ tad grahaḥ svabhāvaḥ hi dravyasya upādhibhiḥ viśiṣyate na tu upādhayaḥ vā viśeṣya tvam vā tasya svabhāvaḥ iti tat api plavate eva na hi abhedāt upādhi antara grahaṇam āsañjitam bhedam punar kṛtyā eva upakāraka grahaṇe upakārya grahaṇa prasañjanāt na ca agni dhūmayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ iva svabhāvataḥ eva dharma dharmiṇoḥ pratipatti niyama kalpanam ucitam tayoḥ api pramāṇa asiddha tvāt pramāṇsiddhe ca svabhāva upavarṇanam iti nyāyaḥ 
RKNĀ_63.3	 yat ca atra nyāya bhūṣaṇena sūrya ādi grahaṇe tad upakārya aśeṣa vasturāśi grahaṇa prasañjanam uktam tad abhiprāyān avagāhana phalam tathā hi tvad mate dharma dharmiṇoḥ bhedaḥ upakāra lakṣaṇā eva ca pratyāsattiḥ tadā upakāraka grahaṇe samāna deśasya eva dharma rūpasya eva ca upakāryasya grahaṇam āsañjitam tat katham sūrya upakāryasya bhinna deśasya dravya antarasya vā dṛṣṭa vyabhicārasya grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ saṅgataḥ tasmāt eka dharma dvāreṇa api vastu svarūpa pratipattau sarva ātma pratīteḥ kva śabda antareṇa vidhi niṣedha avakāśaḥ asti ca tasmāt na sva lakṣaṇsya śabda vikalpa liṅga pratibhāsi tvam iti sthitam 
RKNĀ_63.10–63.14	 na api sāmānyam śābda pratyaya pratibhāsi saritaḥ pāre gāvaḥ caranti iti gavā ādi śabdāt sāsnā śṛṅga lāṅgūla ādayaḥ a kṣara ākāra parikaritāḥ sajātīya bheda aparāmarśanāt sampiṇḍita prāyāḥ pratibhāsante na ca tat eva sāmānyam varṇa ākṛti akṣara ākāra śūnyam go tvam hi kathyate tat eva ca sāsnā śṛṅga ādi mātram akhila vyaktau atyanta vilakṣaṇam api sva lakṣaṇena ekīkriyamāṇam sāmānyam iti ucyate tādṛśasya bāhyasya aprāpteḥ bhrāntiḥ eva asau keśa pratibhāsa vat tasmāt vāsanā vaśāt buddheḥ eva tad ātmanā vivartaḥ ayam astu asat eva vā tad rūpam khyātu vyaktayaḥ eva vā sva jātīya bheda tiraskāreṇa anyathā bhāsantām anubhava vyavadhānāt smṛti pramoṣaḥ vā abhidhīyatām sarvathā nirviṣayaḥ khalu ayam sāmānya pratyayaḥ kva sāmānya vārtā 
RKNĀ_63.21^1	 yat punar sāmānya abhāve sāmānya pratyayasya akasmika tvam uktam tat ayuktam yatas pūrva piṇḍa darśana smaraṇa sahakāriṇā tiricyamāna viśeṣa pratyaya janikā sāmagrī nirviṣayam sāmānya vikalpam utpādayati tat evam na śābde pratyaye jātiḥ pratibhāti na api pratyakṣe na ca anumānataḥ api siddhiḥ adṛśya tve pratibaddha liṅgāt adarśanāt na api indriya vat asyāḥ siddhiḥ jñāna kāryataḥ kādācid kasya eva nimitta antarasya siddheḥ yadā piṇḍa antare antarāle vā go buddheḥ abhāvam darśayet tadā śāvaleya ādi sakala go piṇḍānām eva abhāvāt abhāvaḥ go buddheḥ upapadyamānaḥ katham artha antaram ākṣipet atha go tvāt eva gopiṇḍaḥ 
RKNĀ_63.21^2	 anyathā turagaḥ api gopiṇḍaḥ syāt yadi evam gopiṇḍāt eva go tvam anyathā turaga tvam api go tvam syāt tasmāt kāraṇa paramparātaḥ eva gopiṇḍaḥ go tvam tu bhavatu mā vā nanu sāmānya pratyaya janana sāmarthyam yadi ekasmāt piṇḍāt abhinnam tadā vijātīya vyāvṛttam piṇḍa antaram asamartham atha bhinnam tadā tat eva sāmānyam nāmni param vivādaḥ iti ced abhinnā eva sā śaktiḥ prativastu yathā tu ekaḥ śakta svabhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ tathā anyaḥ api bhavan kīdṛśam doṣam āvahati yathā bhavatām jātiḥ ekā api samāna dhvani prasava hetuḥ anyā api sva rūpeṇa eva jāti antara nirapekṣā tathā asmākam vyaktiḥ api jāti nirapekṣā sva rūpeṇa eva bhinnāḥ hetuḥ 
RKNĀ_64.7–64.15	 yat tu trilocanaḥ aśva tvagotva ādīnām sāmānya viśeṣāṇām sva āśraye samavāyaḥ sāmānyam sāmānyam iti abhidhāna pratyayoḥ nimittam iti yadi evam vyaktiṣu api ayam eva tathā abhidhāna pratyaya hetuḥ tu kim sāmānya svīkāra pramādena na ca samavāyaḥ sambhavī iha iti buddheḥ samavāya siddhiḥ iha iti dhīḥ ca dvaya darśanena na ca kvacid tad viṣaye tu apekṣā sva kalpanā mātram atas abhyupāyaḥ etena sā iyam pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ anuvṛtta vastu anuyāyinī katham atyanta bhedinīṣu vyaktiṣu vyāvṛtta viṣaya pratyaya bhāva anupātinīṣu bhavitum arhati iti ūhā pravartanam asya pratyākhyātam jātiṣu eva paraspara vyāvṛtta tayā vyaktīyamānāsu anuvṛtta pratyayena vyabhicārāt 
RKNĀ_64.19	 yat punar anena viparyaye bādhakam uktam abhidhāna pratyaya anuvṛttiḥ kutaścid nivṛttya kvacid eva bhavantī nimittavatī na ca anyat nimittam ityādi tat na samyak anuvṛttam anyatreṇa api abhidhāna pratyaya anuvṛtteḥ atadrūpa parāvṛtta svarūpa viśeṣāt avaśyam svīkārasya sādhita tvāt tasmāt tulye bhede yayā jātiḥ pratyāsattyā prasarpati kvacid na anyatra sā eva astu śabda jñāna nibandhanam 
RKNĀ_64.24	 yat punar atra nyāya bhūṣaṇa uktam na hi evam bhavati yayā pratyāsattyāḥ daṇḍa sūtra ādikam prasarpati kvacid na anyatra sā eva pratyāsattiḥ puruṣa sphaṭika ādiṣu daṇḍi sūtri tva ādi vyavahāra nibandhanam astu kim daṇḍa sūtra ādinā iti tat asaṅgatam daṇḍa sūtrayoḥ hi puruṣa sphaṭika pratyāsannyoḥ dṛṣṭayoḥ daṇḍi sūtri tva pratyaya hetu tvam na āpalapyate sāmānyam tu svapne api na dṛṣṭam tat yadi idam parikalpanīyam tadā varam pratyāsattiḥ eva sāmānya pratyaya hetuḥ parikalpyatām kim gurvyā parikalpanayā iti abhiprāya aparijñānāt 
RKNĀ_65.1	 atha idam jāti prasādhakam anumānam abhidhīyate yat viśiṣṭa jñānam tad viśeṣaṇa grahaṇana antarīyakam yathā daṇḍi jñānam viśiṣṭa jñānam ca idam gauḥ ayam iti arthataḥ kārya hetuḥ viśeṣaṇa anubhava kāryam hi dṛṣṭānte viśiṣṭa buddhiḥ siddhā iti atra anuyogaḥ viśiṣṭa buddheḥ bhinna viśeṣaṇa grahaṇana antarīyaka tvam vā sādhyam viśeṣaṇa mātra anubhavana antarīyaka tvam vā 
RKNĀ_65.6–65.10	 prathama pakṣe pakṣasya pratyakṣa bādhā sādhana avadhānam anavakāśayati vastu grāhiṇaḥ pratyakṣasya ubhaya pratibhāsā bhāvāt viśiṣṭa buddhi tvam ca sāmānya hetuḥ anaikāntikaḥ bhinna viśeṣaṇa grahaṇam antareṇa api darśanāt yathā sva rūpavān ghaṭaḥ go tvam sāmānyam iti vā dvitīya pakṣe tu siddha sādhanam sva rūpavān ghaṭaḥ ityādi vat go tva jātimān piṇḍe iti parikalpitam bhedam upādāya viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvasya iṣṭa tvāt ago vyāvṛtta anubhava bhāvi tvāt gauḥ ayam iti vyavahārasya tat evam na sāmānya siddhiḥ bādhakam ca sāmānya guṇa karma ādi upādhi cakrasya kevala vyakti grāhakam paṭu pratyakṣam dṛśya anulambhaḥ vā prasiddhaḥ 
RKNĀ_65.15	 tat evam vidhiḥ eva śabda arthaḥ sa ca bāhyaḥ arthaḥ buddhi ākāraḥ ca vivakṣitaḥ tatra na buddhi ākārasya tattvataḥ saṃvṛtyāḥ vā vidhi niṣedhau sva saṃvedana pratyakṣa gamya tvāt anadhyavasāyāt ca na api tattvataḥ bāhyasya api vidhi niṣedhau tasya śābde pratyaye apratibhāsanāt atas eva sarva dharmāṇām tattvataḥ anabhilāpya tvam pratibhā asādhya vasāya abhāvāt tasmāt bāhyasya eva sāṃvṛttau vidhi niṣedhau anyathā saṃvyavahāra hāni prasaṅgāt tat evam 
RKNĀ_65.21–65.26	 na ākārasya na bāhyasya tattvataḥ vidhi sādhanam bahis eva hi saṃvṛtyā samvṛtya api tu na ākṛteḥ etena yat dharma uttaraḥ āropitasya bāhya tvasya vidhi niṣedhau iti alaukikam anāgamam atārkikī iyam kathayati tat api apahastitam nanu adhyavasāye yadi adhyavaseyam vastu na sphurati tadā tat adhyavasitam iti kaḥ arthaḥ apratibhāse api pravṛtti viṣayīkṛtam iti yaḥ arthaḥ apratibhāsā viśeṣe viṣaya antara parihāreṇa katham niyata viṣayā pravṛttiḥ iti ced ucyate yadi api viśvam agṛhītam tathā api vikalpasya niyata sāmagrī prasūta tvena niyata ākāra tayā niyata śakti tvāt niyatā eva jala ādau pravṛttiḥ dhūmasya parokṣa agni jñāna janana vat 
RKNĀ_66.1	 niyata viṣayāḥ hi bhāvāḥ pramāṇa pariniṣṭhita svabhāvāḥ na śakti sāṃkarya paryanuyoga bhājaḥ tasmāt tad adhyavasāyi tvam ākāra viśeṣa yogāt tad pravṛtti janaka tvam na ca sādṛśyāt āropeṇa pravṛttim brūmaḥ yena ākāre bāhyasya bāhye vā ākārasya āropa dvāreṇa dūṣaṇa avakāśaḥ kim tarhi sva vāsanā vipāka vaśāt upajāyamānā eva buddhiḥ apaśyanti api bāhyam bāhye pravṛttim ātanoti iti viplutā eva tat evam anya abhāva viśiṣṭaḥ vijāti vyāvṛttaḥ arthaḥ vidhiḥ saḥ eva ca apoha śabda vācyaḥ śabdānām arthaḥ pravṛtti nivṛtti viṣayaḥ ca iti sthitam 
RKNĀ_66.8–66.19	 atra prayogaḥ yat vācakam tat sarvam adhyavasitā tad rūpa parāvṛtta vastu mātra gocaram yathā iha kūpe jalam iti vacanam vācakam ca idam gavā ādi śabda rūpam iti svabhāva hetuḥ na ayam asiddhaḥ pūrva uktena nyāyena pāramārthika vācya vācaka bhāvasya abhāve api adhyavasāya kṛtasya eva sarva vyavahāribhiḥ avaśyam svīkarttavya tvāt anyathā sarva vyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgāt na api viruddhaḥ sa pakṣe bhāvāt na ca anaikāntikaḥ tathā hi śabdānām adhyavasita vijāti vyāvṛtta vastu mātra viṣaya tvam anicchadbhiḥ paraiḥ paramārthataḥ vācyam sva lakṣaṇam upādhiḥ upādhi yogaḥ sa upādhiḥ astu yadi vā kṛtiḥ astu buddhaḥ gati antara abhāvāt aviṣaya tve ca vācaka tva ayogāt tatra ādi antayoḥ na samayaḥ phala śaktihāneḥ madhye api upādhi virahāt tritayena yuktaḥ tat evam vācya antarasya abhāvāt viṣayavat tva lakṣaṇasya vyāpakasya nivṛttau vipakṣataḥ nivarttamānam vācaka tvam adhyavasita bāhya viṣaya tvena vyāpyate iti vyāpti siddhiḥ 
RKNĀ_67.3–67.11	 namaḥ tārāyai ākṣipta vyatirekā yā vyāptiḥ anvaya rūpiṇī sādharmyavati dṛṣṭānte sattva hetoḥ iha ucyate yat sat tat kṣaṇikam yathā ghaṭaḥ santaḥ ca amī vivāda āspadībhūtāḥ padārthāḥ iti hetoḥ parokṣa artha pratipādaka tvam hetvābhāsa tva śaṅkā nirākaraṇam antareṇa na śakyate pratipādayitum hetvābhāsāḥ ca asiddha viruddha anaikāntika bhedena trividhāḥ tatra na tāvat ayam asiddhaḥ hetuḥ 
RKNĀ_67.12	 yadi nāma darśane darśane nānā prakāram sattva lakṣaṇam uktam āste artha kriyā kāritvam sattā samavāyaḥ svarūpa sattvam utpāda vyaya dhrauvya yogi tvam pramāṇa viṣaya tvam sat upalambhaka pramāṇa gocara tvam vyapadeśa viṣaya tvam ityādi tathā api kim anena aprastutena idānīm eva niṣṭaṅkitena yat eva hi pramāṇataḥ nirūpyamāṇam padārthānām sattvam upapannam bhaviṣyati tat eva vayam api svīkariṣyāmaḥ 
RKNĀ_67.15–67.20	 kevalam tat etat artha kriyā kāritvam sarva jana prasiddham āste tat khalu atra sattva śabdena abhisandhāya sādhana tvena upāttam tat ca yathāyogam pratyakṣa anumāna pramāṇa prasiddha sadbhāveṣu bhāveṣu pakṣīkṛteṣu pratyakṣa ādinā pramāṇena pratītam iti na svarūpeṇa āśraya dvāreṇa vā asidhi sambhāvanā api na api viruddha tā sa pakṣīkṛte ghaṭe sadbhāvāt 
RKNĀ_67.20b	 nanu katham asya sa pakṣa tvam pakṣa vat atra api kṣaṇa bhaṅga asiddheḥ na hi asya pratyakṣataḥ kṣaṇa bhaṅga siddhiḥ tathā tvena aniścayāt na api sattva anumānataḥ punar nidarśana antara apekṣāyām anavasthā prasaṅgāt na ca anyat anumānam asti sambhave vā tena eva pakṣe api kṣaṇa bhaṅga siddheḥ alam sattva anumānena iti ced 
RKNĀ_67.24–68.3	 ucyate anumāna antaram eva prasaṅga prasaṅga viparyaya ātmakam ghaṭe kṣaṇa bhaṅga prasādhakam pramāṇa antaram asti tathā hi ghaṭaḥ vartamāna kṣaṇe tāvat ekām artha kriyām karoti atīta anāga takṣaṇayoḥ api kim tām eva artha kriyām kuryāt anyām vā na vā kām api kriyām iti trayaḥ pakṣāḥ na atra prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ yuktaḥ kṛtasya karaṇa ayogāt 
RKNĀ_68.4–68.6	 atha dvitīyaḥ abhyupagamyate tat idam atra vicāryatām yadā ghaṭaḥ vartamāna kṣaṇa bhāvi kāryam karoti tadā kim atīta anāga takṣaṇa bhāvini api kārye śaktaḥ aśaktaḥ vā yadi śaktaḥ tadā vartamāna kṣaṇa bhāvi kārya vat atīta anāga takṣaṇa bhāvi api kāryam tadā eva kuryāt tatra api śakta tvāt śaktasya ca kṣepā yogāt anyathā varttamāna kṣaṇa bhāvinaḥ api kāryasya akaraṇa prasaṅgāt pūrva apara kālayoḥ api śakta tvena aviśeṣāt samarthasya ca sahakāri apekṣāyāḥ ayogāt 
RKNĀ_68.9–68.11	 atha aśaktaḥ tadā ekatra kārye śakta aśakta tva viruddha dharma adhyāsāt kṣaṇa vidhvaṅsaḥ ghaṭasya durvāra prasaraḥ syāt na api tṛtīyaḥ pakṣaḥ saṅgacchate śakta svabhāva anuvṛtteḥ eva yadā hi śaktasya padārthasya vilambaḥ api asahyaḥ tadā dūra utsāritam akaraṇam anyathā vārtamānikasya api kāryasya akaraṇam syāt iti uktam 
RKNĀ_68.14–68.17	 tasmāt yat yadā yat janana vyavahāra pātram tat tadā tat kuryāt akurvat ca na janana vyavahāra bhājanam tat evam ekatra kārye samartha itara svabhāva tayā pratikṣaṇam bhedāt ghaṭasya sa pakṣa tvam akṣatam atra prayogaḥ yat yadā yat janana vyavahāra yogyam tat tadā tat janayati eva yathā antyā kāraṇa sāmagrī sva kāryam atīta anāga takṣaṇa bhāvi kārya janana vyavahāra yogyaḥ ca ayam ghaṭo vartamāna kṣaṇa bhāvi kārya karaṇa kāle sakala kriyā atikrama kāle api iti svabhāva hetu prasaṅgaḥ 
RKNĀ_68.20–68.25	 asya ca dvitīya ādi kṣaṇa bhāvi kārya karaṇa vyavahāra gocara tvasya prasaṅga sādhanasya vārtamānika kārya karaṇa kāle sakala kriyā atikrama kāle ca ghaṭe dharmiṇi para abhyupagama mātrataḥ siddha tvāt asiddhiḥ tāvat asambhavinī na api viruddha tā sa pakṣe antya kāraṇa sāmagryām sadbhāva sambhavāt nanu ayam sādhāraṇa anaikāntikaḥ hetuḥ sākṣāt ajanake api kuśūla ādi avasthita bīja ādau vipakṣe samartha vyavahāra gocara tvasya sādhanasya darśanāt iti ced 
RKNĀ_68.26–69.1	 na dvividhaḥ hi samartha vyavahāraḥ pāramārthika aupacārikaḥ ca tatra yat pāramārthikam janana prayuktam janana vyavahāra gocara tvam tat iha sādhana tvena upāttam tasya ca kuśūla ādi avasthita bīja ādau kāraṇa kāraṇa tvāt aupacārika janana vyavahāra viṣaya bhūte sambhava abhāvāt kutas sādhāraṇa anaikāntika tā na ca asya sandigdha vyatirekitā viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa sadbhāvat 
RKNĀ_69.1a	 tathā hi idam janana vyavahāra gocara tvam niyata viṣaya tvena vyāptam iti sarva jana anubhava prasiddham na ca idam nirnimittam deśa kāla svabhāva niyama abhāva prasaṅgāt na ca jananāt anyat nimittam upalabhyate tad anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna darśanāt yadi ca jananam antareṇa api janana vyavahāra gocara tvam syāt tadā sarvasya sarvatra janana vyavahāraḥ iti aniyamaḥ syāt niyataḥ ca ayam pratītaḥ tatas janana abhāve vipakṣe niyata viṣaya tvasya vyāpakasya nivṛttau nivartamānam janana vyavahāra gocara tvam jananaḥ eva viśrāmyati iti vyāpti siddheḥ anavadyaḥ hetuḥ 
RKNĀ_69.8–69.11	 na ca eṣa ghaṭaḥ varttamāna kārya karaṇa kṣaṇe sakala kriyā atikrama kāle ca atīta anāga takṣaṇa bhāvi kāryam janayati tatas na janana vyavahāra yogyaḥ sarvaḥ prasaṅgaḥ prasaṅga viparyaya niṣṭhaḥ iti nyāyāt atra api prayogaḥ yat yadā yat na karoti na tat tadā tatra samartha vyavahāra yogyam yathā śāli aṅkuram akurvan kodravaḥ śāli aṅkure na karoti ca eṣa ghaṭaḥ vartamāna kṣaṇa bhāvi kārya karaṇa kāle sakala kriyā atikrama kāle ca atīta anāga takṣaṇa bhāvi kāryam iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ bhinatti samartha kṣaṇāt asamartha kṣaṇam 
RKNĀ_69.15–69.20	 atra api asiddhiḥ na asti vartamāna kṣaṇa bhāvi kārya karaṇa kāle sakala kriyā atikrama kāle ca atīta anāga takṣaṇa bhāvi kārya karaṇasya ayogāt na api virodhaḥ sa pakṣe bhāvāt na ca anaikāntika tā pūrva uktena nyāyena samartha vyavahāra gocara tva janaka tvayoḥ vidhi bhūtayoḥ sarva upasaṃhāravatyā vyāpteḥ prasādhanāt yat punar atra uktam yat yadā yat na karoti na tat tadā tatra samartham iti atra kaḥ karoti arthaḥ kim kāraṇa tvam uta kārya utpāda anuguṇa sahakāri sākalyam ahosvit kārya avyabhicāraḥ kārya sambandhaḥ vā iti tatra kāraṇa tvam eva karoti arthaḥ tatas pakṣa antara bhāvinaḥ doṣāḥ anabhyupagama pratihatāḥ 
RKNĀ_69.24–69.28	 na ca atra pakṣe kāraṇa tva sāmarthyayoḥ paryāya tvena vyāpaka anupalambhasya sādhya aviśiṣṭa tvam abhidhātum ucitam samartha vyavahāra gocara tva abhāvasya sādhya tvāt kāraṇatva samartha vyavahāra gocara tvayoḥ ca vṛkṣa śiṃśapayoḥ iva vyāvṛtti bhedaḥ asti iti anavasaraḥ eva evaṃvidhasya kṣudra pralāpasya tat evam prasaṅga prasaṅga viparyaya hetu dvaya balataḥ ghaṭe dṛṣṭānte kṣaṇa bhaṅgaḥ siddhaḥ tat katham sattvāt anyat anumānam dṛṣṭānte kṣaṇa bhaṅga sādhakam na asti iti ucyate na ca evam sattva hetoḥ vaiyarthyam dṛṣṭānta mātre eva prasaṅga prasaṅga viparyayābhyām kṣaṇa bhaṅga prasādhanāt
