RKNĀ_70.1–70.1a	 nanu ābhyām eva pakṣe api kṣaṇa bhaṅga siddhiḥ astu iti ced astu kaḥ doṣaḥ yaḥ hi pratipattā prativastu yat yadā yat janana vyavahāra yojyam tat tadā tad janayati iti ādikam upanyasitum analasaḥ tasya tatas eva kṣaṇa bhaṅga siddhiḥ yaḥ tu prativastu tat nyāya upanyāsa prayāsa bhīruḥ sa khalu ekatra dharmiṇi yat yadā yat janana vyavahāra yogyam tat tadā tat janayati ityādi nyāyena sattva mātram asthairyavyāptam avadhārya sattvāt eva anyatra kṣaṇika tvam avagacchayatīi katham apramattaḥ vaiyarthyam asya ācakṣīta 
RKNĀ_70.6–70.10	 tat evam eka kārya kāriṇaḥ ghaṭasya dvitīya ādi kṣaṇa bhāvi kārya apekṣayā samartha itara svabhāva viruddha dharma adhyāsāt bhedaḥ eva iti kṣaṇa bhaṅgi tayā sa pakṣatām āvahati ghaṭe sattva hetuḥ upalabhyamānaḥ na viruddhaḥ na ca ayam anaikāntikaḥ atra eva sādharmyavati dṛṣṭānte sarva upasaṃhāravatyā vyāpteḥ prasādhanāt nanu viparyaya bādhaka pramāṇa balāt vyāpti siddhiḥ tasya ca upanyāsavārtā api na asti tat katham vyāptiḥ prasādhitā iti ced 
RKNĀ_70.11–70.15	 tat etat tarala buddhi vilasitam tathā hi uktam etat vartamāna kṣaṇa bhāvi kārya karaṇa kāle a tīta anāga takṣaṇa bhāvi kārye api ghaṭasya śakti sambhave tadānīm eva tad karaṇam akaraṇe ca śakta aśakta svabhāva tayā pratikṣaṇam bhedaḥ iti kṣaṇika tvena vyāptā eva sā artha kriyāśaktiḥ nanu evam anvaya mātram astu vipakṣāt punar ekāntena vyāvṛttiḥ iti kutas labhyate iti ced 
RKNĀ_70.16–70.17	 vyāpti siddheḥ eva vyatireka sandehe vyāpti siddhiḥ eva katham iti ced na dvividhā hi vyāpti siddhiḥ anvaya rūpā ca kartṛ dharmaḥ sādhana dharmavati dharmiṇi sādhya dharmasya avaśyambhāvaḥ yaḥ vyatireka rūpā ca karma dharmaḥ sādhya abhāve sādhanasya avaśyam abhāvaḥ yaḥ enayoḥ ca ekatara pratītiḥ niyamena dvīti apratītim ākṣipati anyathā ekasyāḥ eva asiddheḥ 
RKNĀ_70.20	 tasmāt yathā viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa balāt niyamavati vyatireke siddhe anvaya viṣayaḥ saṃśayaḥ pūrvam sthitaḥ api paścāt parigalati tatas anvaya prasādha artham na pṛthak sādhanam ucyate tathā prasaṅga tad viparyaya hetu dvaya balataḥ niyamavatī anvaye siddhe vyatireka viṣaye pūrvam sthitaḥ api sandehaḥ paścāt parigalati eva na ca vyatireka prasādhakam anyat pramāṇam vaktavyam tatas ca sādhya abhāve sādhanasya ekāntikaḥ vyatirekaḥ sādhane sati sādhyasya avaśyam anvayaḥ vā iti na kaścid artha bhedaḥ 
RKNĀ_70.26–71.1	 tat evam viparyaya bādhaka pramāṇam antareṇa api prasaṅga prasaṅga viparyaya hetu dvaya balāt anvaya rūpa vyāpti siddhau sattva hetoḥ anaikāntika tvasya abhāvāt atas sādhanāt kṣaṇa bhaṅga siddhiḥ anavadyā iti nanu ca sādhanam idam asiddham na hi kāraṇa buddhyā kāryam gṛhyate tasya bhāvi tvāt na ca kārya buddhyā kāraṇam tasya atīta tvāt na ca vartamāna grāhiṇā jñānena atīta anāgatayoḥ grahaṇam atiprasaṅgāt 
RKNĀ_71.3–71.5	 na ca pūrva aparayoḥ kālayoḥ ekaḥ pratisandhātā asti kṣaṇa bhaṅga bhaṅga prasaṅgāt kāraṇa abhāve tu kārya abhāva pratītiḥ sva saṃvedana vādinaḥ manorathasya api aviṣayaḥ nanu ca pūrva uttara kālayoḥ saṃvittī tābhyām vāsanā tayā ca hetu phala avasāyī vikalpaḥ iti ced tat ayuktam sa hi vikalpaḥ gṛhīta anusandhāyakaḥ atad rūpa samāropakaḥ vā 
RKNĀ_71.7–71.11	 na prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ ekasya pratisandhātuḥ abhāve pūrva apara grahaṇayoḥ ayogāt vikalpa vāsanāyāḥ eva abhāvāt na api dvitīyaḥ marīcikāyām api jala vijñānasya prāmāṇya prasaṅgāt tat evam anvaya vyatirekayoḥ apratipatteḥ artha kriyā lakṣaṇam sattvam asiddham iti kim ca prakāra antarāt api idam sādhanam asiddham tathā hi bīja ādīnām sāmarthyam bīja ādi jñānāt tad kāryāt aṅkura ādeḥ vā niścetavyam 
RKNĀ_71.12–71.17	 kārya tvam ca vastu tva siddhau sidhyati vastu tvam ca kārya antarāt kārya antarasya api kāryatvam vastu tva siddhau tat vastu tvam ca tad apara kārya antarāt iti anavasthā atha anavasthā bhayāt paryante kārya antaram na apekṣate tadā tena eva pūrveṣām asattva prasaṅgāt na ekasya api artha kriyā sāmarthyam sidhyati nanu kāryatva sattvayoḥ bhinna vyāvṛttika tvāt sattva asiddhau api kāryatva siddhau kā kṣatiḥ iti ced 
RKNĀ_71.18–71.21	 tat asaṅgatam sati api kāryatva sattvayoḥ vyāvṛtti bhede sattva asiddhāu kutas kāryatva siddhiḥ kāryatvam hi abhūtvā abhāvi tvam bhavanam ca sattā sattā ca saugatānām sāmarthyam eva tatas ca sāmarthya sandehe bhavati iti eva vaktum aśakyam katham abhūtvā abhāvi tvam kārya tvam setsyati apekṣita para vyāpāra tvam kāryatvam iti api na asataḥ dharmaḥ sattvam ca sāmarthyam tat ca sandigdham iti kutas kāryatva siddhiḥ tad asiddhau pūrvasya sāmarthyam na sidhyati iti sandigdha asiddhaḥ hetuḥ 
RKNĀ_71.24–71.27	 tathā viruddhaḥ api ayam tathā hi kṣaṇika tve sati na tāvat ajātasya ananvaya niruddhasya vā kārya ārambhaka tvam sambhavati na ca niṣpannasya tāvān kṣaṇaḥ asti yam upādāya kasmaicid kāryāya vyāpāryeta atas kṣaṇika pakṣaḥ eva artha kriyā anupapatteḥ viruddha tā athavā vikalpena yat upanīyate tat sarvam avastu tatas ca vastu ātmake kṣaṇika tve sādhye avastu upasthāpayan anumāna vikalpaḥ viruddhaḥ 
RKNĀ_71.28–72.2	 yat vā sarvasya eva hetoḥ kṣaṇika tve sādhye viruddha tvam deśa kāla antara an anugame sādhya sādhana bhāva abhāvāt anugame ca nānā kālam ekam akṣaṇikam kṣaṇika tvena virudhyate iti anaikāntikaḥ api ayam sattva sthairyayoḥ virodha abhāvāt iti atra ucyate yat tāvat uktam sāmarthyam na pratīyate iti tat kim sarvathā eva na pratīyate kṣaṇa bhaṅga pakṣe vā 
RKNĀ_72.4–72.9	 prathama pakṣe sakala kāraka jñāpaka hetu cakra ucchedāt mukha spandana mātrasya api akaraṇa prasaṅgaḥ anyathā yena eva vacanena sāmarthyam na asti iti pratipādyate tasya eva tad pratipādana sāmarthyam avyāhatam āyātam tasmāt parama puruṣa artha samīhayā vastu tattva nirūpaṇa pravṛttasya śakti svīkāra pūrvakā eva pravṛttiḥ tat asvīkāre tu na kaścid kvacid pravarteta iti nirīham jagat jāyeta atha dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā asti tāvat sāmarthya pratītiḥ sā ca kṣaṇika tve yadi na upapadyate tadā viruddham vaktum ucitam asiddham iti tu nyāya bhūṣaṇīyaḥ prāyas vilāpaḥ 
RKNĀ_72.11	 na ca sati api kṣaṇika tve sāmarthya pratīti vyāghātaḥ tathā hi kāraṇa grāhi jñāna upādeya bhūtena kārya grāhiṇā jñānena tad arpita saṃskāra garbheṇa asya bhāve asya bhāvaḥ iti anvaya niścayaḥ janyate tathā kāraṇa apekṣayā bhū tala kaivalya grāhi jñāna upādeya bhūtena kārya apekṣayā bhū tala kaivalya grāhiṇā jñānena tad arpita saṃskāra garbheṇa asya abhāve asya abhāvaḥ iti vyatireka niścayaḥ janyate 
RKNĀ_72.15–72.21	 yat āhuḥ guravaḥ ekāvasāya samanantara jātam anya vijñānam anvaya vimarśam upādadhāti evam tad eka viraha anubhava udbhavāni avyāvṛtti dhīḥ prathayati vyatireka buddhim evam sati gṛhīta anusandhāyakaḥ eva ayam vikalpaḥ upādāna upādeya bhūta krami pratyakṣa dvaya gṛhīta anusandhānāt yat āha alaṅkāraḥ yadi nāma ekam adhyakṣam na pūrva apara vittimat adhyakṣa dvaya sadbhāve prāc parāvedanam katham iti 
RKNĀ_72.24–72.26	 na api dvitīyaḥ asiddha prabhedaḥ sāmarthyam hi sattvam iti saugatānām sthitiḥ eṣā na ca etat prasādhana artham asmākam idānīm eva prārambhaḥ kim tu yatra pramāṇa pratīte bīja ādau vastu bhūte dharmiṇi pramāṇa pratītam sāmarthyam tatra kṣaṇa bhaṅga prasādhanāya tatas ca aṅkura ādīnām kārya adarśanāt āhatya sāmarthya sandehe api paṭu pratyakṣa prasiddham sat mātra tvam avadhāryam eva anyathā na kvacid api vastu mātrasya api pratipattiḥ syāt 
RKNĀ_72.29–73.3	 tasmāt śāstrīya sattva lakṣaṇa sandehe api paṭu pratyakṣa bala avalambita vastu bhāve aṅkura ādau kāryatvam upalabhyamānam bīja ādeḥ sāmarthyam upasthāpayati iti na asiddhi doṣa avakāśaḥ na api kṣaṇika tve sāmarthya kṣatiḥ yatas viruddha tā syāt kṣaṇika tva niyata prāc bhāvi tva lakṣaṇa kāraṇa tvayoḥ virodha abhāvāt kṣaṇa mātra sthāyini api sāmarthya sambhavāt iti na ādimaḥ virodhaḥ 
RKNĀ_73.5–73.9	 na api dvitīyaḥ virodha prabhedaḥ avastunaḥ vastunaḥ vā su a ākārasya grāhya tve api adhyavaseya vastu apekṣayā eva sarvatra prāmāṇya pratipādanāt vastu svabhāvasya eva kṣaṇika tvasya siddhiḥ iti kva virodhaḥ yat ca gṛhyate yat ca adhyavasīyate te dve api anya nivṛttī na vastunī sva lakṣaṇa avagāhi tve abhilāpa saṃsarga anupapatteḥ iti ced na adhyavasāya svarūpa aparijñānāt agṛhīte api vastuni mānasa ādi pravṛtti kāraka tvam vikalpasya adhyavasāyi tvam apratibhāse api pravṛtti viṣayīkṛta tvam adhyavaseya tvam etat ca adhyavaseya tvam sva lakṣaṇasya eva yujyate na anyasya artha kriyā arthi tvāt arthi pravṛtteḥ 
RKNĀ_73.12	 evam ca adhyavasāye sva lakṣaṇasya asphuraṇam eva na ca tasya asphuraṇe api sarvatra aviśeṣeṇa pravṛtti ākṣepa prasaṅgaḥ pratiniyata sāmagrī prasūtāt pratiniyatasu a ākārāt pratiniyata śakti yogāt pratiniyataḥ eva atad rūpa parāvṛtte apratīte api pravṛtti sāmarthya darśanāt yathā sarvasya asattve api bījāt aṅkurasya eva utpattiḥ dṛṣṭasya niyata hetu phala bhāvasya pratikṣeptum aśakya tvāt param bāhyena arthena sati pratibandhe prāmāṇyam anyathā tu aprāmāṇyam iti viśeṣaḥ 
RKNĀ_73.18–73.20	 tathā tṛtīyaḥ api pakṣaḥ prayāsa phalaḥ nānā kālasya ekasya vastunaḥ vastutas asambhave api sarva deśa kāla vartinoḥ atad rūpa parāvṛttayoḥ eva sādhya sādhanayoḥ pratyakṣeṇa vyāpti grahaṇāt dvividhaḥ hi pratyakṣasya viṣayaḥ grāhyaḥ adhyavaseyaḥ ca sakalā tad rūpa parāvṛttam vastu mātram sākṣāt asphuraṇāt pratyakṣasya grāhyaḥ viṣayaḥ mā bhūt tad eka deśa grahaṇe tu tanmātrayoḥ vyāpti niścāyaka vikalpa jananāt adhyavaseyaḥ viṣayaḥ bhavati eva kṣaṇa grahaṇe santāna niścaya vat rūpa mātra grahaṇe rūpa rasa gandha sparśa ātmaka ghaṭa niścaya vat ca anyathā sarva anumāna uccheda prasaṅgāt 
RKNĀ_73.25–73.27	 tathā hi vyāpti grahaḥ sāmānyayoḥ viśeṣayoḥ sāmānya viśiṣṭa viśeṣayoḥ viśeṣa viśiṣṭa sāmānyayoḥ vā iti vikalpāḥ na ādyaḥ vikalpaḥ sāmānyasya bādhya tvāt abādhya tve api adṛśya tvāt dṛśya tve api puruṣa artha anupayogi tayā tasya anumeya tva ayogāt na api anumitāt sāmānyāt viśeṣa anumānam sāmānya sarva viśeṣayoḥ vakṣyamāṇa nyāyena pratibandha pratipatteḥ ayogāt 
RKNĀ_74.1–74.5	 na api dvitīyaḥ viśeṣasya ananugāmi tvāt antime tu vikalpa dvaye sāmānya ādhāra tayā dṛṣṭaḥ eva viśeṣaḥ sāmānyasya viśeṣyaḥ viśeṣaṇam vā kartavyaḥ adṛṣṭaḥ eva vā deśa kāla antara vartī yat vā dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa ātmakaḥ atad rūpa parāvṛttaḥ sarvaḥ viśeṣaḥ na prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ ananugāmi tvāt na api dvitīyaḥ adṛṣṭa tvāt na ca tṛtīyaḥ prastuta eka viśeṣa darśane api deśa kāla antara vartinām viśeṣāṇām adarśanāt 
RKNĀ_74.7–74.9	 atha teṣām sarveṣām eva viśeṣāṇām sadṛśa tvāt sadṛśa sāmagrī prasūta tvāt sadṛśa kārya kāri tvāt iti pratyāsattyā eka viśeṣa grāhakam pratyakṣam atad rūpa parāvṛtta mātre niścayam janayat atad rūpa parāvṛtta viśeṣa mātrasya vyavasthāpakam yathā eka sāmagrī pratibaddha rūpa mātra grāhakam pratyakṣam ghaṭe niścayam janayat ghaṭa grāhakam vyavasthāpyate anyathā ghaṭaḥ api ghaṭa santānaḥ api pratyakṣataḥ na sidhyet sarva ātmanā grahaṇa abhāvāt 
RKNĀ_74.12–74.16	 tad eka deśa grahaṇam tu atad rūpa parāvṛtte api aviśiṣṭam yadi evam anena eva krameṇa sarvasya viśeṣasya viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāva vat vyāpti pratipattiḥ api astu tat kim artham nānā kālam ekam akṣaṇikam abhyupagantavyam yena kṣaṇika tva sādhanasya viruddha tvam syāt iti na kaścid virodha prabheda prasaṅgaḥ na ca ayam anaikāntikaḥ api hetuḥ pūrva ukta krameṇa sādharmya dṛṣṭānte prasaṅga viparyaya hetubhyām anvaya rūpa vyāpteḥ prasādhanāt 
RKNĀ_74.17–74.21	 nanu yadi prasaṅga viparyaya hetu dvaya balataḥ ghaṭe dṛṣṭānte kṣaṇa bhaṅgaḥ sidhyet tadā sattvasya niyamena kṣaṇika tvena vyāpti siddheḥ anaikāntika tvam na syāt iti yuktam kevalam idam eva asambhavi tathā hi śaktaḥ api ghaṭaḥ krami sahakāri apekṣayā krami kāryam kariṣyati na ca etat vaktavyam samarthaḥ arthaḥ sva rūpeṇa karoti svarūpam ca sarvadā asti iti anupakāriṇi sahakāriṇī apekṣā na yujyate iti sati api svarūpeṇa kāraka tve sāmarthya abhāvāt katham karotu sahakāri sākalyam hi sāmarthyam tad vaikalyam ca asāmarthyam na ca tayoḥ āvirbhāva tirobhāvābhyām tadvataḥ kācid kṣatiḥ tasya tābhyām anya tvāt tasmāt arthaḥ samarthaḥ api syāt na ca karoti iti sandigdha vyatirekaḥ prasaṅga hetuḥ 
RKNĀ_74.27–74.29	 atra ucyate bhavatu tāvat sahakāri sākalyam eva sāmarthyam tathā api saḥ api tāvat bhāvaḥ sva rūpeṇa kārakaḥ tasya ca yādṛśaḥ cara makṣaṇe akṣepa kriyā dharmā svabhāvaḥ tādṛśaḥ eva ced prathama kṣaṇe tadā tadā api prasahya kurvāṇaḥ brahmaṇā api anivāryaḥ na ca saḥ api akṣepa kriyā dharmā svabhāvaḥ sākalye sati jātaḥ bhāvāt bhinnaḥ eva abhidhātum śakyaḥ bhāvasya akartṛ tva prasaṅgāt evam yāvat yāvat dharma antara parikalpaḥ tāvat tāvat udāsīnaḥ bhāvaḥ 
RKNĀ_75.2–75.5	 tasmāt yat rūpam ādāya svarūpeṇa api janayati iti ucyate tasya prāk api bhāve katham ajaniḥ kadācid akṣepa kriyā pratyanīka svabhāvasya vā prācyasya paścāt anuvṛttau katham kadācid api kārya sambhavaḥ nanu yadi saḥ eva ekaḥ kartā syāt yuktam etat kiṃtu sāmagrī janikā tatas saha kāri antara viraha velāyām balīyasaḥ api na kārya prasavaḥ iti kim atra viruddham na hi bhāvaḥ sva rūpeṇa karoti iti sva rūpeṇa eva karoti sahakāri sahitāt eva tatas kārya utpatti darśanāt tasmāt vyāpti vat kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ api ekatra anya yoga vyavacchedena anyatra ayoga vyavacchedena avaboddhavyaḥ tathā eva laukika parīkṣakāṇām saṃpratipatteḥ iti 
RKNĀ_75.10	 atra ucyate yadā militāḥ santaḥ kāryam kurvate tadā eka artha karaṇa lakṣaṇam sahakāri tvam eṣām astu kaḥ niṣeddhāḥ militaiḥ eva tu tat kāryam kartavyam iti kutas labhyate pūrva aparayoḥ eka svabhāva tvāt bhāvasya sarvadā jananā jananayoḥ anyatara niyama prasaṅgasya durvāra tvāt tasmāt sāmagrī janikā na ekam janakam iti sthira vādinām manorathasya api aviṣayaḥ 
RKNĀ_75.15	 dṛśyate tāvat evam iti ced dṛśyatām kim tu pūrva sthitāt eva sāmagrī madhya praviṣṭāt bhāvāt kārya utpattiḥ anyasmāt eva vā viśiṣṭāt bhāvāt utpannāt iti vivāda padam tatra prāk api sambhave sarvadā eva kārya utpattiḥ na vā kadācid api iti virodham asamādhāya cakṣuṣī nimīlya tatas eva kārya utpatti darśanāt iti sādhya anuvāda mātra pravṛttaḥ kṛpām arhati iti 
RKNĀ_75.20–75.22	 na ca pratyabhijñā balāt ekatva siddhiḥ tad pauruṣasya lūna punar jāta keśa nakha ādau api upalambhataḥ nirdalanāt lakṣaṇa bhedasya ca darśayitum aśakya tvāt sthira siddhi dūṣaṇe ca asmābhiḥ prapañcataḥ nirasta tvāt tasmāt sākṣāt kārya kāraṇa bhāva apekṣayaḥ bhayatra api anya yoga vyavacchedaḥ vyāptau tu sākṣāt paramparayā kāraṇa mātra apekṣayā kāraṇe vyāpake ayoga vyavacchedaḥ kārye vyāpye anya yoga vyavacchedaḥ tathā tat atad svabhāve vyāpake ayoga vyavacchedaḥ tad svabhāve ca vyāpye anya yoga vyavacchedaḥ vikalpa ārūḍha rūpa apekṣayā vyāptau dvividham avadhāraṇam 
RKNĀ_75.27–76.1	 nanu yadi pūrva apara kālayoḥ eka svabhāvaḥ bhāvaḥ sarvadā janaka tvena ajanaka tvena vā vyāptaḥ upalabdhaḥ syāt tadā ayam prasaṅgaḥ saṅgacchate na ca kṣaṇa bhaṅga vādinā pūrva apara kālayoḥ ekaḥ kaścid upalabdhaḥ iti ced tat etat atigrāmyam tathā hi pūrva apara kālayoḥ eka svabhāva tve sati iti asya ayam arthaḥ para kāla bhāvī janakaḥ yaḥ svabhāvaḥ bhāvasya saḥ eva yadi pūrva kāla bhāvī pūrva kāla bhāvī vā yaḥ ajanakaḥ svabhāvaḥ saḥ eva yadi para kāla bhāvī tadā upalabdham eva jananam ajananam vā syāt tathā ca sati siddhayoḥ eva svabhāvayoḥ ekatva ārope siddham eva jananam ajananam vāsajyate iti 
RKNĀ_76.6–76.9	 nanu kāryam eva sahakāriṇam apekṣate na tu kārya utpatti hetuḥ yasmāt dvividham sāmarthyam nijam āgantukam ca sahakāri antaram tatas akṣaṇikasya api krama vat sahakāri nānā tvāt api kramavat kārya nānā tva upapatteḥ aśakyam bhāvānām pratikṣaṇam anya tvam upapādayitum iti ced ucyate bhavatu tāvat nija āgantuka bhedena dvividham sāmarthyam tathā api tat prātisvikam vastu sva lakṣaṇam artha kriyā dharmakam avaśyam abhyupagantavyam tat kim prāk api paścāt eva vā iti vikalpya yat dūṣaṇam udīritam tatra kim uktam anena iti na pratīmaḥ 
RKNĀ_76.12	 yat tu kāryeṇa eva sahakāriṇaḥ apekṣyante iti upaskṛtam tat api nirupayogam yadi hi kāryam eva sva janmani svatantram syāt yuktam etat kevalam evam sati sahakāri sākalya sāmarthya kalpanam aphalam svātantryāt eva hi kāryam kādācid kam bhaviṣyati tathā ca sati santaḥ hetavaḥ sarvathā asamarthāḥ asat tu kāryam svatantram iti viśuddhā buddhiḥ 
RKNĀ_76.17–76.21	 atha kāryasya eva ayam aparādhaḥ yat idam samarthe kāraṇe sati api kadācid na upapadyate iti ced na tat tarhi tat kāryam svātantryāt yat bhāṣyam sarva avasthā samāne api kāraṇe yadi akārya tā svatantram kāryam evam syāt na tat kāryam tathā sati atha na tad bhāve bhavati iti tat kāryam ucyate kiṃtu tad abhāve na bhavati eva iti vyatireka prādhānyāt iti ced 
RKNĀ_76.22–76.25	 na yadi hi svayam bhavan bhāvayet eva hetuḥ sva kāryam tadā tad abhāva prayuktaḥ asya abhāvaḥ iti pratītiḥ syāt no ced yathā kāraṇe sati api kāryam svātantryāt na bhavati tathā tad abhāve api svātantryāt eva na bhūtam iti śaṅkā kena nivāryeta yat bhāṣyam tad bhāve api na bhāvaḥ ced abhāve abhāvitā kutas tad abhāva prayuktaḥ asya saḥ abhāvaḥ iti tat kutas 
RKNĀ_76.28–77.1	 tasmāt yathā eva tad abhāve niyamena na bhavati tathā eva tad bhāve niyamena bhavet eva abhavat ca na tad kāraṇa tām ātmanaḥ kṣamate yat ca uktam prathama kārya utpādana kāle hi uttara kārya utpādana svabhāvaḥ atas prathama kāle eva aśeṣāṇi kāryāṇi kuryāt iti tat idam mātā me bandhyā ityādi vat sva vacana virodhāt ayuktam yaḥ hi uttara kārya janana svabhāvaḥ sa katham ādau kāryam kuryāt na tarhi tad kārya karaṇa svabhāvaḥ na hi nīla utpādana svabhāvaḥ pīta ādikam api karoti iti 
RKNĀ_77.6–77.10	 artā ucyate sthira svabhāva tve hi bhāvasya uttarakālam eva idam kāryam na pūrva kālam iti kutas etat tad abhāvāt ca kāraṇam api uttara kārya karaṇa svabhāvam iti api kutas kim kurmaḥ uttarakālam eva tasya janma iti ced astu sthira tve tat anupapadyamānam asthira tām ādiśatu sthira tve api eṣaḥ eva svabhāvaḥ tasya yat uttarakṣaṇaḥ eva karoti iti ced hata idānīm pramāṇa pratyāśā dhūmāt atra agniḥ iti atra api svabhāvaḥ eva asya yat idānīm atra niragniḥ api dhūmaḥ iti vaktum śakya tvāt tasmāt pramāṇa siddhe svabhāva avalambanam na tu svabhāva avalambanena pramāṇa vyālopaḥ 
RKNĀ_77.12	 tasmāt yadi kāraṇasya uttara kārya kāraka tvam abhyupagamya kāryasya prathama kṣaṇa bhāvi tvam āsajyate syāt sva vacana virodhaḥ yadā tu kāraṇasya sthira tve kāryasya uttara kāla tvam eva asaṅgatam atas kāraṇasya api uttara kārya janaka tvam vastutas asambhavi tadā prasaṅga sādhanam idam janana vyavahāra gocara tvam hi jananena vyāptam iti prasādhitam uttara kārya janana vyavahāra gocara tvam ca tvat abhyupagamāt prathama kārya karaṇa kāle eva ghaṭe dharmiṇi siddham atas tanmātra anubandhinaḥ uttara abhimatasya kāryasya prathame kṣaṇe asambhavāt eva prasaṅgaḥ kriyate 
RKNĀ_77.20–77.23	 na hi nīlakārake api pīta kāraka tva ārope pīta sambhava prasaṅgaḥ svavacanavirodhaḥ nāma tat evam śaktaḥ sahakāri anapekṣita tvāt jananena vyāptaḥ ajanayan ca śakta aśakta tva viruddha dharma adhyāsāt bhinnaḥ eva nanu bhavatu prasaṅga viparyaya balāt eka kāryam prati śakta aśaktatva lakṣaṇa viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ tathā api na tatas bhedaḥ sidhyati 
RKNĀ_77.24–77.28	 tathā hi bījam aṅkura ādikam kurvat yadi yena eva svabhāvena aṅkuram karoti tena eva kṣiti ādikam tadā kṣiti ādīnām api aṅkura svābhāvya āpattiḥ nānā svabhāva tvena tu kāraka tve svabhāvānām anyonya abhāva avyabhicāri tvāt ekatra bhāva abhāvau paraspara viruddhau syātām iti ekam api bījam bhidyeta evam pradīpaḥ api taila kṣaya varti dāha ādikam 
RKNĀ_77.28a–78.3	 tathā pūrva rūpam api uttara rūpa rasa gandha ādikam anekaiḥ svabhāvaiḥ parikaritam karoti teṣām ca svabhāvānām anyonya abhāva avyabhicārāt viruddhānām yoge pradīpa ādikam bhidyeta na ca bhidyate tat na viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ bhedakaḥ tathā bījasya aṅkuram prati kāraka tvam gardabha ādikam prati akāraka tvam iti kāraka tva ākāraka tve api viruddhau dharmau na ca tad yoge api bīja bhedaḥ tat evam ekatra bīje pradīpe rūpe ca vipakṣe paridṛśyamānaḥ śakta aśakta tva ādiḥ viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ na ghaṭa ādeḥ bhedakaḥ iti 
RKNĀ_78.5	 atra brūmaḥ bhavatu tāvat bīja ādīnām aneka kārya kāri tvāt dharma bhūta aneka svabhāva bhedaḥ tathā api kaḥ prastāvaḥ viruddha dharma adhyāsasya svabhāvānām hi anyonya abhāva avyabhicāre bhedaḥ prāpta avasaraḥ na virodhaḥ virodhaḥ tu yat vidhāne yat niṣedhaḥ yat niṣedhe ca yat vidhānam tayoḥ ekatra dharmiṇi paraspara parihāra sthita tayā syāt tat atra ekaḥ svabhāvaḥ svābhāvena viruddhaḥ yuktaḥ bhāva abhāva vat na tu svabhāva antareṇa ghaṭa tva vastutva vat 
RKNĀ_78.10–78.12	 evam aṅkura ādi kāri tvam tat akāri tvena viruddham na punar vastu antara kāri tvena pratyakṣa vyāpāraḥ ca atra yathā nānā dharmaiḥ adhyāsitam bhāvam abhinnam vyavasthāpayati tathā tad kārya kāriṇam kārya antara akāriṇam ca tat yadi pratiyogi tva abhāvāt anyonya abhāva avyabhicāriṇau api svabhāvau aviruddhau tad kāraka tvāni ākāraka tve vā viṣaya bhedāt aviruddhe tat kim āyātam eka kāryam prati śakta aśakta tvayoḥ paraspara pratiyoginoḥ viruddhayoḥ dharmayoḥ etayoḥ api punar avirodhe virodhaḥ nāma datta jala añjaliḥ 
RKNĀ_78.16–78.19	 bhavatu tarhi eka kārya apekṣayā eva sāmarthya asāmarthyayoḥ virodhaḥ kevalam yathā tat eva kāryam prati kvacid deśe śaktiḥ deśa antare ca aśaktiḥ iti deśa bhedāt aviruddhe śakti aśaktī tathā ekatra eva kārye kāla bhedāt api aviruddhe yathā pūrvam niṣkriyaḥ sphaṭikaḥ saḥ eva paścāt sa kriyaḥ iti ced ucyate na hi vayam paribhāṣā mātrāt ekatra kārye deśa bhedāt aviruddhe śakti aśaktī brūmaḥ kim tu virodha abhāvāt tad deśa kārya kāri tvam hi tad deśa kārya akāri tvena viruddham na punar deśa antare tad kārya akāri tvena anya kārya kāri tvena vā 
RKNĀ_78.23–78.25	 yadi evam tad kāla kārya kāri tvam tad kāla kārya akāri tvena viruddham na punar kāla antare tad kārya akāri tvena anya kārya kāri tvena vā tat katham kāla bhede api virodhaḥ iti ced ucyate dvayoḥ hi dharmayoḥ ekatra dharmiṇi anavasthiti niyamaḥ paraspara parihāra sthiti lakṣaṇaḥ virodhaḥ sa ca sākṣāt paraspara pratyanīka tayā bhāva abhāva vat vā bhavet ekasya vā niyamena pramāṇa antareṇa bādhanāt nitya tva sattva vat vā bhavet iti na kaścid artha bhedaḥ tat atra eka dharmiṇi tad kāla kārya kāri tva ādhāre kāla antare tad kārya akāri tvasya a nyakārya kāri tvasya vā niyamena pramāṇa antareṇa bādhanāt virodhaḥ 
RKNĀ_78.30–79.3	 tathā hi yatra eva dharmiṇi tad kāla kārya kāri tvam upalabdham na tatra eva kāla antare tad kārya akāri tvam anya kārya kāri tvam vā brahmaṇā api upasaṃhartum śakyate yena anayoḥ avirodhaḥ syāt kṣaṇa antare kathita prasaṅga viparyaya hetubhyām avaśyambhāvena dharmi bheda prasādhanāt na ca pratyabhijñānāt ekatva siddhiḥ tad pauruṣasya nirmūlita tvāt atas eva vajraḥ api pakṣa kukṣau nikṣiptaḥ katham asau sphaṭikaḥ varākaḥ kāla bhedena abheda prasādhanāya dṛṣṭāntī bhavitum arhati 
RKNĀ_79.5–79.9	 na ca evam samāna kāla kāryāṇām deśa bhede api dharmi bhedaḥ yuktaḥ bheda prasādhaka pramāṇa abhāvāt indriya pratyakṣeṇa nirasta vibhrama āśaṅkena abheda prasādhanāt ca iti na kāla bhede api śakti aśaktyoḥ virodhaḥ sva samaya mātrāt apahastayitum śakyaḥ samaya pramāṇayoḥ apravṛtteḥ iti tasmāt sarvatra viruddha dharma adhyāsa siddhiḥ eva bheda siddhiḥ vipratipannam prati tu viruddha dharma adhyāsāt bheda vyavahāraḥ sādhyate 
RKNĀ_79.11–79.13	 nanu tathā api sattvam idam anaikāntikam eva asādhāraṇa tvāt sandigdha vyatireki tvāt vā yathā hi idam krama ākrama nivṛttau akṣaṇikān nivṛttam tathā sa apekṣa tva anapekṣa tvayoḥ ekatva aneka tvayoḥ api vyāpakayoḥ nivṛttau kṣaṇikāt api tathā hi upasarpaṇa pratyayena deva datta kara pallava ādinā sahacaraḥ bīja kṣaṇaḥ pūrvasmāt eva puñjāt samarthaḥ jātaḥ anapekṣaḥ ādya atiśayasya janakaḥ iṣyate 
RKNĀ_79.15–79.18	 tatra ca samāna kuśūla janmasu bahuṣu bīja santāneṣu kasmāt kiñcid eva bījam paramparayā aṅkura utpāda anuguṇam upajanayati bīja kṣaṇam na anye bīja kṣaṇāḥ bhinna santāna antaḥpātinaḥ na hi upasarpaṇa pratyayāt prāk eva teṣām samāna asamāna santāna vartinām bīja kṣaṇānām kaścid paramparā atiśayaḥ atha upasarpaṇa pratyayāt prāk na tad santāna vartinaḥ api janayanti paramparayā api aṅkura utpāda anuguṇam bīja kṣaṇam bīja mātra jananāt teṣām kasyacid eva bīja kṣaṇasya upasarpaṇa pratyaya sahabhuvaḥ ādya atiśaya utpādaḥ hanta tarhi tad abhāve sati utpannaḥ api janayet eva 
RKNĀ_79.21–79.25	 tathā kevalānām vyabhicāra sambhavāt ādya atiśaya utpādakam aṅkuram vā prati kṣiti ādīnām paraspara apekṣāṇām eva utpādaka tvam akāmena api svīkartavyam atas na tāvat anapekṣā kṣaṇikasya sambhavinī na api apekṣā yujyate sama sama ya kṣaṇayoḥ savya itara go biṣāṇayoḥ iva upakārya upakāraka bhāvā yogāt iti na asiddhaḥ prathamaḥ vyāpaka abhāvaḥ api ca antyaḥ bīja kṣaṇaḥ anapekṣaḥ aṅkura ādikam kurvan yadi yena eva rūpeṇa aṅkuram karoti tena eva kṣiti ādikam tadā kṣiti ādīnām api aṅkura svābhāvya āpattiḥ abhinna kāraṇa tvāt iti na tāvat ekatva sambhavaḥ 
RKNĀ_79.28	 nanu rūpa antareṇa karoti tathā hi bījasya aṅkuram prati upādāna tvam kṣiti ādikam tu prati sahakāri tvam yadi evam sahakāri tva upādāna tve kim ekam tattvam nānā vā ekam ced katham rūpa antareṇa janakam nānātve tu anayoḥ bījāt bhedaḥ abhedaḥ vā bhede katham bījasya janaka tvam tābhyām eva aṅkura ādīnām utpatteḥ abhede vā katham bījasya na nānātvam bhinna tādātmyāt etayoḥ vā eka tvam eka tādātmyāt 
RKNĀ_80.4	 yadi ucyeta kṣiti ādau janayitavye tad upādānam pūrvam eva kṣiti ādi bījasya rūpa antaram iti na tarhi bījam tad anapekṣam kṣiti ādīnām janakam tad anapekṣa tve teṣām aṅkurāt bheda anupapatteḥ na ca anupakārakāṇi apekṣante iti tvayā eva utkam na ca kṣaṇasya upakāra sambhavaḥ anyatra jananāt tasya abhedya tvāt iti aneka tvam api na asti iti dvitīyaḥ api vyāpaka abhāvaḥ na asiddhaḥ tasmāt asādhāraṇa anaikāntika tvam gandhavat tva vat iti 
RKNĀ_80.9–80.11	 yadi manyetān upakārakāḥ api bhavanti sahakāriṇaḥ apekṣaṇīyāḥ ca kāryeṇa anuvihita bhāva abhāvāt ca saha kārya karaṇāt ca nanu anena krameṇa akṣaṇikaḥ api bhāvaḥ anupakārakān api sahakāriṇaḥ kramavataḥ krama vat kāryeṇa anukṛta anvaya vyatirekān apekṣiṣyate kariṣyate ca krama vat sahakāri vaśaḥ krameṇa kāryāṇi iti vyāpaka anupalabdheḥ asiddheḥ sandigdha vyatirekam anaikāntikam sattvam kṣaṇika tva siddhau iti 
RKNĀ_80.15	 atra brūmaḥ kīdṛśam punar apekṣā artham ādāya kṣaṇike sa apekṣā anapekṣa tva nivṛttiḥ ucyate kim sahakāriṇam apekṣate iti sahakāriṇā asya upakāraḥ karttavyaḥ atha pūrva avasthitasya eva bīja ādeḥ sahakāriṇā saha sambhūya karaṇam yat vā pūrva avasthitasya iti anapekṣya milita avasthasya karaṇa mātram apekṣā arthaḥ atra prathama pakṣasya asambhavāt anapekṣā eva kṣaṇikasya katham ubhaya vyāvṛttiḥ 
RKNĀ_80.19–80.23	 yadi anapekṣaḥ kṣaṇikaḥ kim iti upasarpaṇa pratyaya abhāve api na karoti karoti eva yadi syāt svayam asambhavī tu katham karotu atha tat vā tādṛś vā āsīt iti na kaścid viśeṣaḥ tatas tādṛś svabhāva sambhave api akaraṇam sahakāriṇi nirapekṣāt na kṣamate iti ced asambaddham etat varṇa saṃsthāna sāmye api akartuḥ tad svabhāvatāyāḥ virahāt sa ca adya atiśaya janakatva lakṣaṇaḥ svabhāva viśeṣaḥ na samāna asamāna santāna vartiṣu bīja kṣaṇeṣu sarveṣu eva sambhavī kim tu keṣucid eva karmakara kara pallava sahacareṣu 
RKNĀ_80.26–80.28	 nanu ekatra kṣetre niṣpattila vana ādi pūrvakam ānīya ekatra kuśūle kṣiptāni sarvāṇi eva bījāni sādhāraṇa rūpāṇi eva pratīyante tat kutastyaḥ ayam eka bīja sambhavī viśeṣaḥ anyeṣām iti ced ucyate kāraṇam khalu sarvatra kārye dvividham dṛṣṭam adṛṣṭam ca iti sarva āstika prasiddham etat tatas pratyakṣa parokṣa sahakāri pratyaya sākalyam asarva vidā pratyakṣataḥ na śakyam pratipattum tatas bhavet api kāraṇa sāmagrī śakti bhedāt tādṛśaḥ svabhāva bhedaḥ keṣāñcid eva bīja kṣaṇānām yena te eva bīja kṣaṇāḥ ādya atiśayam aṅkuram vā paramparayā janayeyuḥ na anye ca bīja kṣaṇāḥ 
RKNĀ_81.5–81.6	 nanu yeṣu upasarpaṇa pratyaya sahacareṣu sva kāraṇa śakti bhedāt ādya atiśaya janakatva lakṣaṇaḥ viśeṣaḥ sambhāvyate sa tatra avaśyam asti iti kutas labhyam iti ced aṅkura utpādāt anumitāt ādya atiśaya lakṣaṇāt kāryāt iti brūmaḥ kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ tarhi tad abhāvaḥ eva bhaviṣyati iti ced na dṛśya adṛśya samudāyasya kāraṇasya adarśane api abhāva asiddheḥ kāraṇa anupalabdheḥ sandigdha asiddha tvāt 
RKNĀ_81.9–81.14	 tat ayam arthaḥ pāṇi sparśavataḥ kṣaṇasya na bhidā bhinnānyakāla kṣaṇāt bhedaḥ vā iti mata dvaye miti balam yasya asti asau jitvaraḥ tatra ekasya balam nimitta virahaḥ kārya aṅgam anyasya vā sāmagrī tu na sarvathā īkṣaṇa sahā kāryam tu māna anugam iti tat evam na upakāraḥ apekṣā arthaḥ iti anapekṣā eva kṣaṇikasya sahakāriṣu na ubhaya vyāvṛttiḥ 
RKNĀ_81.15–81.19	 atha sambhūya karaṇam apekṣā arthaḥ tadā yadi pūrva sthitasya iti viśeṣaṇa apekṣā tadā kṣaṇikasya na evam kadācid iti anapekṣā eva akṣīṇā atha pūrva sthitasya iti anapekṣya milita avasthitasya eva karaṇam apekṣā arthaḥ tadā sa apekṣatā eva na anapekṣā tathā ca na ubhaya vyāvṛttiḥ iti asiddhaḥ prathamaḥ vyāpaka anupalambhaḥ tathā ekatva aneka tvayoḥ api vyāpakayoḥ kṣaṇikāt vyāvṛttiḥ asiddhāḥ tad tad vyāvṛtti bhedam āśritya upādāna tva ādi kālpanika svabhāva bhede api paramārthataḥ ekena eva sva rūpeṇa aneka kārya niṣpādanāt ubhaya vyāvṛtteḥ abhāvāt 
RKNĀ_81.22	 yat ca bījasya ekena eva svabhāvena kāraka tve kṣiti ādīnām aṅkura svābhāvya āpattiḥ anyathā kāraṇa abhede api kārya bhede api kāryasya ahetuka tva prasaṅgāt iti uktam tat asaṅgatam kāraṇa eka tvasya kārya bhedasya ca paṭunā indriya pratyakṣeṇa prasādhanāt eka kāraṇa janya tva eka tvayoḥ vyāpteḥ pratihata tvāt prasaṅgasya anupada tvāt 
RKNĀ_81.26	 yat ca kāraṇa abhede kārya abhedaḥ iti uktam tatra sāmagrī svarūpam kāraṇam abhipretam sāmagrī sa jātīya tve na kārya vijātīyatā iti arthaḥ na punar sāmagrī madhya gatena ekena anekam kāryam na kartavyam nāma ekasmāt aneka utpatteḥ pratyakṣa siddha tvāt na ca evam pratyabhijñānāt kāla bhede api abheda siddhiḥ iti ukta prāyam na ca indriya pratyakṣam bhinna deśam sa pratigham dṛśyam artha dvayam ekam eva upalambhayati iti kvacid upalabdham yena tatra api bheda śaṅkā syāt śaṅkāyām vā paṭu pratyakṣasya api apalāpe sarva pramāṇa uccheda prasaṅgāt 
RKNĀ_82.3–82.12	 na api sattva hetoḥ sandigdha vyatireki tvam kṣiti ādeḥ dravya antarasya bīja svabhāva tvena asmābhiḥ asvīkṛta tvāt anupakāriṇī apekṣāyāḥ pratyākhyāta tvāt vyāpaka anupalambhasya asiddha tva ayogāt tat etau dvau api vyāpaka anupalambhau asiddhau na kṣaṇikāt sattvam nivartayate iti na ayam asādhāraṇaḥ hetuḥ api ca vidyamānaḥ bhāvaḥ sādhya itarayoḥ aniścita anvaya vyatirekaḥ gandhavat tā ādi vat asādhāraṇaḥ yuktaḥ prakṛta vyāpaka anupalambhāt ca sarvathā artha kriyā eva asatī ubhābhyām vādibhyām ubhayasmāt vinivartita tvena nirāśraya tvāt tat katham asādhāraṇa anaikāntikaḥ bhaviṣyati iti alam pralāpini nirbandhena tat evam śaktasya kṣepā yogāt samartha vyavahāra gocara tvam jananena vyāptam iti prasaṅga viparyayayoḥ sattve hetoḥ api na anaikāntika tvam atas kṣaṇa bhaṅga siddhiḥ iti sthitam 
RKNĀ_83.5–83.13	 namaḥ tārāyai vyatireka ātmikā vyāptiḥ ākṣipta anvaya rūpiṇī vaidharmyavati dṛṣṭānte sattva hetoḥ iha ucyate yat sat tat kṣaṇikam yathā ghaṭaḥ santaḥ ca amī vivāda āspadībhūtāḥ padārthāḥ iti svabhāva hetuḥ na tāvat asya asiddhiḥ sambhavati yathāyogam pratyakṣa anumāna pramāṇa pratīte dharmiṇi sattva śabdena abhipretasya artha kriyā kāri tva lakṣaṇasya sādhanasya pramāṇa samadhigata tvāt na ca viruddha anaikāntikate vyāpaka anupalambha ātmanā viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇena vyāpteḥ prasādhanāt yasya kramākramau na vidyete na tasya artha kriyā sāmarthyam yathā śaśa viṣāṇasya na vidyete ca akṣaṇikasya kramākramau iti vyāpaka anupalambhaḥ 
RKNĀ_83.14	 na tāvat ayam asiddhaḥ hetuḥ akṣaṇike dharmiṇi krama ākrama sadbhāva ayogāt tathā hi prāpta apara kālayoḥ eka tve nitya tvam tasya krama ākrama yoge kṣaṇa dvaye api avaśyam bhedaḥ bheda abhedayoḥ ca paraspara virodhāt kutas akṣaṇike kramākrama sambhavaḥ kṣaṇa dvaye api bhede krama akrama yogaḥ abhede hi prathamaḥ eva kṣaṇe śakta tvāt bhāvinaḥ api kāryasya karaṇa prasaṅge katham kārya antara karaṇe krama antara avakāśaḥ na ca akṣaṇikasya ākrameṇa eva sakala sva kāryam kṛtvā svāsthyam kṣaṇa antare api śakta tvāt punar tad kārya karaṇa prasaṅgāt 
RKNĀ_83.21–84.2	 tasmāt akṣaṇikam iti pūrva apara kālayoḥ abhedaḥ kramākrama yogaḥ iti pūrva apara kālayoḥ bhedaḥ anayoḥ ca paraspara parihāra sthiti lakṣaṇaḥ virodhaḥ tat ayam akṣaṇike dharmiṇi krama akrama abhāva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ na asiddhaḥ vaktavyaḥ krama ākrama yogi tva akṣaṇika tvayoḥ virodhāt eva na api viruddhaḥ sa pakṣe bhāvāt na ca anaikāntikaḥ krama akrama abhāvasya artha kriyā sāmarthya abhāvena vyāpta tvāt 
RKNĀ_84.3	 yena eva hi pratyakṣa ātmanā pramāṇena apara prakāra abhāvāt vidhi bhūtābhyām krama ākramābhyām vidhi bhūtasya artha kriyā sāmarthyasya vyāptiḥ prasādhitā tena eva artha kriyā sāmarthya abhāvena krama akrama abhāvasya vyāptiḥ prasādhitā iti svīkartavyam na hi dahana ādinā dhūma ādeḥ vyāpti sādhaka pramāṇāt aparam dhūma ādi a bhāvena dahana ādi abhāvasya vyāpti sādhakam kiñcid pramāṇam śaraṇa bhūtam asti tasmāt vidhyoḥ eva vyāpti sādhakam pramāṇam abhāvayoḥ api vyāpti sādhakam iti nyāyasya duratikrama tvāt sattva abhāvena krama akrama abhāvaḥ vyāptaḥ eva iti na anaikāntikaḥ iti anavadyaḥ vyāpaka anupalambhaḥ tat ayam akṣaṇikāt vinivartamāṇaḥ sva vyāpyam sattvam nivartya kṣaṇike viśrāmayati iti sattva hetoḥ kṣaṇa bhaṅga siddhiḥ api anavadyāḥ 
RKNĀ_85.1	 nanu vyāpaka anupalambhataḥ sattvasya katham sva sādhya pratibandha siddhiḥ asya api aneka doṣa duṣṭa tvāt tathā hi na tāvat ayam prasaṅga hetuḥ sādhya dharmiṇi pramāṇa siddha tvāt para abhyupagama siddha tva abhāvāt viparyaya paryavasāna abhāvāt ca atha svatantraḥ tad āśraya asiddhaḥ akṣaṇikasya āśrayasya asambhavāt apratīta tvāt vā pratītiḥ hi pratyakṣeṇa anumānena vikalpa mātreṇa vā syāt 
RKNĀ_85.6–85.10	 prathama pakṣa dvaye sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa vā sva pratīti lakṣaṇa artha kāri tve maulaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ hetuḥ vyāpaka anupalambhaḥ ca svarūpa asiddhaḥ syāt artha kriyā kāritve kramākramayoḥ anyatarasya avaśyambhāvāt antima pakṣe tu na kaścid dhetuḥ anāśrayaḥ syāt vikalpa mātra siddhasya dharmiṇaḥ sarvatra sulabha tvāt api ca tat kalpanā jñānam pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvi vā syāt liṅga janma vā saṃskāra jam vā sandigdha vastukam vā avastukam vā 
RKNĀ_85.12–85.14	 tatra ādya pakṣa dvaye akṣaṇikasya sattā eva avyāhatā katham bādhaka avatāraḥ tṛtīye tu na sarva dākṣaṇika sattā niṣedhaḥ tad arpita saṃskāra abhāve tad smaraṇā yogāt caturthe tu sandigdha āśraya tvam hetu doṣaḥ pañcame ca tad viṣayasya abhāvaḥ na tāvat pratyakṣataḥ sidhyati akṣaṇikā ātmanaḥ sarvadā eva tvad mate apratyakṣa tvāt na ca anumānataḥ tad abhāvaḥ tad pratibaddha liṅga anupalambhāt iti āśraya asiddhiḥ tāvat uddhatā evam dṛṣṭāntaḥ api pratihantavyaḥ 
RKNĀ_85.18–85.21	 svarūpa asiddhaḥ api ayam hetuḥ sthirasya api krama ākrami sahakārī apekṣayā krama ākramābhyām artha kriyā upapatteḥ na api krama yaugapadya pakṣa ukta doṣa prasaṅgaḥ tathā hi krami sahakārī apekṣayā krami kārya kāri tvam tāvat aviruddham tathā ca śaṅkarasya saṃkṣiptaḥ ayam abhiprāyaḥ sahakāri sākalyam hi sāmarthyam tad vaikalyam ca asāmarthyam na ca tayoḥ āvirbhāva tirobhāvābhyām tadvataḥ kācid kṣatiḥ tasya tābhyām anya tvāt tat katham sahakāriṇaḥ anapekṣya kārya karaṇa prasaṅgaḥ iti 
RKNĀ_85.25–85.29	 trilocanasya api ayam saṃkṣipta arthaḥ kāryam eva hi sahakāriṇam apekṣate na kārya utpatti hetuḥ yasmāt dvividham sāmarthyam nijam āgantukam ca sahakāri antaram tatas akṣaṇikasya api krama vat sahakāri nānā tvāt api kramavat kārya nānā tva upapatteḥ aśakyam bhāvānām pratikṣaṇam anya anya tvam upapādayitum iti nyāya bhūṣaṇaḥ api lapati prathama kārya utpādana kāle hi uttara kārya utpādana svabhāvaḥ atas prathama kāle eva aśeṣāṇi kāryāṇi kuryāt iti ced 
RKNĀ_85.30–86.3	 tat idam mātā me bandhyā ityādi vat sva vacana virodhāt ayuktam yaḥ hi uttara kārya janana svabhāvaḥ sa katham ādau tat kāryam kuryāt atha kuryāt na tarhi tad kārya karaṇa svabhāvaḥ na hi nīla utpādana svabhāvaḥ pīta ādikam api karoti iti vācaspatiḥ api paṭhati nanu ayam akṣaṇikaḥ svarūpeṇa kāryam janayati tat ca asya svarūpam tṛtīya ādiṣu iva kṣaṇeṣu dvitīye api kṣaṇe sat iti tadā api janayet akurvan vā tṛtīya ādiṣu api na kurvīta tasya tādavasthyāt atādavasthye vā tat eva asya kṣaṇika tvam 
RKNĀ_86.7	 atra ucyate satyam svarūpeṇa kāryam janayati na tu tena eva sahakāri sahitāt eva tatas kārya utpatti darśanāt tasmāt vyāpti vat kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ api ekatra anya yoga vyavacchedena anyatra ayoga vyavacchedena avaboddhavyaḥ tathā eva laukika parīkṣakāṇām saṃpratipatteḥ iti na krami kārya kāri tva pakṣa ukta doṣa avasaraḥ 
RKNĀ_86.11	 na api akṣaṇike yaugapadya pakṣa ukta doṣa avakāśaḥ ye hi kāryam utpāditavantaḥ dravya viśeṣāḥ teṣām vyāpārasya niyata kārya utpādana samarthasya niṣpādite kārye anuvartamāneṣu api teṣu dravyeṣu nivṛtta arthāt ūnā sāmagrī jāyate tat katham niṣpāditam niṣpādayiṣyati na hi daṇḍa ādayaḥ svabhāvena eva kartāraḥ yena amī niṣpatteḥ ārabhya kāryam vidadhyuḥ kim tarhi vyāpāra āveśinaḥ na ceyatā svarūpeṇa na kartāraḥ sva rūpa kāraka tva nirvāha para tayā vyāpāra samāveśāt iti 
RKNĀ_86.17–86.20	 kim ca krama akrama abhāvaḥ ca bhaviṣyati na ca sattva abhāvaḥ iti sandigdha vyatirekaḥ api ayam vyāpaka anupalambhaḥ na hi krama ākramābhyām anyasya prakārasya abhāvaḥ siddhaḥ viśeṣa niṣedhasya śeṣa abhyanujñā viṣaya tvāt kim ca prakāra antarasya dṛśya tve na atyanta niṣedhaḥ adṛśya tve tu na asattā niścayaḥ vipra karṣiṇām iti na krama ākramābhyām artha kriyā sāmarthyasya vyāpti sidhiḥ atas sandigdha vyatirekaḥ api vyāpaka anupalambhaḥ 
RKNĀ_86.23–86.26	 kim ca dṛśya adṛśya sahakāri pratyaya sākalyavataḥ krama yaugapadyasya atyanta parokṣa tvāt tena vyāptam sattvam api parokṣam eva iti na tāvat pratibandhaḥ pratyakṣataḥ sidhyati na api anumānataḥ tad pratibaddha liṅga abhāvāt iti api ca krama ākramābhyām artha kriyā kāritvam vyāptam iti ati subhāṣitam yadi krameṇa vyāptam katham akrameṇa atha akrameṇa na tarhi krameṇa krama akramābhyām vyāptam iti tu bruvatā vyāpteḥ eva abhāvaḥ pradarśitaḥ bhavati na hi bhavati dhūmaḥ vahni bhāva abhāvābhyām vyāptaḥ iti atas vyāpteḥ anaikāntika tvam 
RKNĀ_86.30–87.1	 capi ca kim idam bādhakam akṣaṇikānām asattām sādhayati uta svid akṣaṇikāt sattvasya vyatirekam atha sattva kṣaṇika tvayoḥ pratibandham na pūrvaḥ vikalpaḥ ukta krameṇa hetoḥ āśraya asiddha tvāt na ca dvitīyaḥ yatas vyāpaka nivṛtti sahitā vyāpya nivṛttiḥ vyatireka śabdasya arthaḥ sā ca yadi pratyakṣeṇa pratīyate tadā tad hetuḥ syāt iti sattvam anaikāntikam vyāpaka anupalambhaḥ svarūpa asiddhaḥ atha sā vikalpyate tadā pūrva ukta krameṇa pañcadhā vikalpya vikalpaḥ dūṣaṇīyaḥ 
RKNĀ_87.4–87.9	 atas eva na tṛtīyaḥ api vikalpaḥ vyatireka asiddhau sambandha asiddheḥ kim ca na bhū tala vat atra akṣaṇikaḥ dharmī dṛśyate na ca svabhāva anupalambhe vyāpaka anupalambhaḥ kasyacid dṛśyasya pratipattim antareṇa antar bhāvayitum śakyate iti kim ca asya abhāva dharma tve āśraya asiddha tvam itaretara āśraya tvam ca bhāva dharma tve viruddha tvam ca ubhaya dharma tve ca anaikāntika tvam iti na trayīm doṣa jātim atipatati 
RKNĀ_87.11–87.13	 yat punar uktam akṣaṇika tve krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā virodhāt iti dtatra virodha siddhim anusaratā virodhi api pratipattavyaḥ tad pratītinā antarīyaka tvāt virodha siddheḥ yathā tuhina dahanayoḥ sa apekṣadhruva bhāvayoḥ ca pratiyogī ca akṣaṇikaḥ pratīyamānaḥ pratīti kāri tvāt san eva syāt ajanakasya aprameya tvāt 
RKNĀ_87.15–87.19	 saṃvṛti siddhena akṣaṇika tvena virodha siddhiḥ iti ced saṃvṛti siddham api vāstavam kālpanikam vā syāt yadi vāstavam katham tasya asattvam katham ca artha kriyā kāritva virodhaḥ artha kriyām kurvat dhi vāstavam ucyate atha kālpanikam tatra kim virodhaḥ vāstavaḥ kālpanikaḥ vā na tāvat vāstavaḥ kalpita virodhi virodha tvāt bandhyā putra virodha vat atha virodhaḥ api kālpanikaḥ na tarhi sattvasya vyatirekaḥ pāramārthikaḥ iti kṣaṇa bhaṅgaḥ datta jala añjaliḥ iti 
RKNĀ_87.23–87.28	 ayam eva codya prabandhaḥ asmad gurubhiḥ saṅgṛhītaḥ enityam na asti na vā pratīti viṣayam tena āśraya asiddha tā hetoḥ sva anubhavasya ca kṣatiḥ atas kṣiptaḥ sa pakṣaḥ api ca śūnyaḥ ca dvitayena sidhyati na ca asattā api sattā yathā naḥ nityena virodha siddhiḥ asatā śakyā krama ādeḥ api iti atra ucyate iha vastuni api dharmi dharma vyavahāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā gavi go tvam paṭe śukla tvam turage gamanam ityādi avastuni api dharmi dharma vyavahāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yathā śaśa viṣāṇe tīkṣṇa tva abhāvaḥ bandhyā putre vaktṛ tva abhāvaḥ gagana aravinde gandha abhāvaḥ ityādi tatra avastuni dharmi tvam na asti iti kim vastu dharmeṇa dharmi tvam na asti āhosvit avastu dharmeṇa api 
RKNĀ_88.3–88.8	 prathama pakṣe siddha sādhanam dvitīya pakṣe tu sva vacana virodhaḥ yat āhuḥ guravaḥ dharmasya kasyacid avastuni māna siddhā bādhā vidhi vyavahṛtiḥ kim iha asti naḥ vā kvāpi asti ced katham iyanti na dūṣaṇāni na asti eva ced sva vacana pratirodha siddhiḥ avastunaḥ dharmi tva svīkāra pūrvaka tvasya vyāpakasya abhāvāt āśraya asiddhi dūṣaṇasya anupanyāsa prasaṅgaḥ iti arthaḥ yena eva hi vacanena avastunaḥ dharmi tvam pratiṣidhyate tena eva avastunaḥ dharmi tva abhāvena dharmeṇa dharmi tvam abhyupagatam paran tu pratiṣidhyate iti vyaktam idam īśvara ceṣṭitam tathā hi avastunaḥ dharmi tvam na asti iti vacanena dharmi tva abhāvaḥ kim avastuni vidhīyate anyatra vā na vā kvacid api iti trayaḥ pakṣāḥ 
RKNĀ_88.13–88.15	 prathama pakṣe avastunaḥ na dharmi tva niṣedhaḥ dharmitva abhāvasya dharmasya tatra eva vidhānāt dvitīye avastuni kim āyātam anyatra dharmi tva abhāva vidhānāt tṛtīyaḥ tu pakṣaḥ vyarthaḥ eva nirāśraya tvāt iti katham avastunaḥ dharmi tva niṣedhaḥ tasmāt yathā pramāṇa upanyāsaḥ prameya svīkāra pūrvaka tvena vyāptaḥ vācaka śabda upanyāsaḥ vā vācya svīkāra pūrvaka tvena vyāptaḥ tathā avastunaḥ dharmi tvam na asti iti vacana upanyāsaḥ avastunaḥ dharmi tva svīkāra pūrvaka tvena vyāptaḥ anyathā tad vacana upanyāsasya vyartha tvāt 
RKNĀ_88.19–88.22	 tat yadi vacana upanyāsaḥ vyāpya dharmaḥ tadā avastunaḥ dharmi tva svīkāraḥ api vyāpaka dharmaḥ durvāraḥ atha na vyāpaka dharmaḥ tadā vyāpyasya api vacana upanyāsasya asambhavaḥ iti mūka tā eva atra balāt āyāta iti katham na sva vacana pratirodha siddhiḥ yat āha ācāryaḥ na hi abruvan param bodhayitum īśaḥ bruvan vā doṣam imam parihartum iti mahati saṃkaṭe praveśaḥ 
RKNĀ_88.24	 avastu prastāve sahṛdayānām mūka tā eva yujyate iti ced aho mahat vaidagdhyam avastu prastāve svayam eva yathāśakti valgitvā bhagnaḥ mūka tā eva nyāya prāptā iti paribhāṣayā niḥsartum icchati na ca avastu prastāvaḥ rāja daṇḍena vinā caraṇa mardana ādinā aniṣṭi mātreṇa vā pratiṣeddham śakyate tatas ca atra api kramākrama bhāvasya sādhana tve sattva abhāvasya ca sādhya tve sandigdha vastu bhāvasya avastu ātmanaḥ vā kṣaṇikasya dharmi tvam kena pratiṣidhyate 
RKNĀ_89.1	 trividhaḥ hi dharmaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ kaścid vastu niyataḥ nīla ādiḥ kaścid avastu niyataḥ yathā sarva upākhyā virahaḥ kaścid ubhaya sādhāraṇaḥ yathā anupalabdhi mātram tatra vastu dharmeṇa avastunaḥ dharmi tva niṣedhaḥ iti yuktam na tu avastu dharmeṇa vastu avastu dharmeṇa vā sva vacanasya anupanyāsa prasaṅgāt iti akṣaṇikasya abhāve sandehe api vā vastu dharmeṇa dharmi tvam avyāhatam iti na ayam āśraya asiddhaḥ vyāpaka anupalambhaḥ 
RKNĀ_89.6	 akṣaṇikā pratītau āśraya asiddhaḥ hetuḥ iti yuktam uktam tat apratītau tad vyavahārā yogāt kevalam asau vyavahāra aṅga bhūtā pratītiḥ vastu avastunoḥ eka rūpā na bhavati sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa vastu sāmarthya bhāvinī hi vastu pratītiḥ yathā pratyakṣam anumānam pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvī ca vikalpaḥ avastunaḥ tu sāmarthya abhāvāt vikalpa mātram eva pratītiḥ vastunaḥ hi vastu bala bhāvinī pratītiḥ yathā sākṣāt pratyakṣam paramparayā tad pṛṣṭha bhāvī vikalpaḥ anumānam ca avastunaḥ tu na vastu bala bhāvinī pratītiḥ tad kāraka tvena avastu tva hāni prasaṅgāt tasmāt vikalpa mātram eva avastunaḥ pratītiḥ 
RKNĀ_89.12	 na hi abhāvaḥ kaścid vigrahavān yaḥ sākṣāt kartavyaḥ api tu vyavahartavyaḥ sa ca vyavahāraḥ vikalpāt api sidhyati eva anyathā sarva jana prasiddhaḥ avastu vyavahāraḥ na syāt iṣyate ca tad dharmitva pratiṣedha anubandhāt iti akāmakena api vikalpa mātra siddhaḥ a kṣaṇikaḥ svīkartavyaḥ iti na ayam apratīta tvāt api āśraya asiddhaḥ hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ tatas ca akṣaṇikasya vikalpa mātra siddha tve yat uktam 
RKNĀ_89.17–89.20	 na kaścid dhetuḥ anāśrayaḥ vikalpa mātra siddhasya dharmiṇaḥ sarvatra sulabha tvāt iti tat asaṅgatam vikalpa mātra siddhasya dharmiṇaḥ sarvatra sambhave api vastu dharmeṇa dharmi tva ayogāt vastu dharma hetutva apekṣayā āśraya asiddhasya api hetoḥ sambhavāt yathā ātmanaḥ vibhu tva sādhana artham upanyastam sarvatra upalabhyamāna guṇa tvāt iti sādhanam vikalpaḥ ca ayam hetu upanyāsāt pūrvam sandigdha vastukaḥ samarthite tu hetau avastukaḥ iti brūmaḥ 
RKNĀ_89.23	 na ca atra sandigdha āśraya tvam nāma hetu dośaḥ āstām tāvat sandigdhasya avastunaḥ api vikalpa mātra siddhasya avastu dharma apekṣayā dharmi tva prasādhanāt vastu dharma hetu apekṣayā eva sandigdha āśrayasya hetvābhāsasya vyavasthāpanāt yathā iha nikuñje mayūraḥ kekāyitāt iti avastuka vikalpa viṣayasya asattvam tu vyāpaka anupalambhāt eva prasādhitam evam dṛṣṭāntasya api vyoma utpala ādeḥ dharmi tvam vikalpa mātreṇa pratītiḥ ca avagantavyā tat evam avastu dharma apekṣāya avastunaḥ dharmi tvasya vikalpa mātreṇa pratīteḥ ca apahnotum aśakya tvāt na ayam āśraya asiddhaḥ hetuḥ na ca dṛṣṭānta kṣatiḥ 
RKNĀ_89.30–90.2	 na ca eṣa svarūpa asiddhaḥ akṣaṇike dharmiṇi kramākramayoḥ vyāpakayoḥ ayogāt tathā hi yadi tasya prathame kṣaṇe dvitīya ādi kṣaṇa bhāvi kārya karaṇa sāmarthyam asti tadā prathama kṣaṇa bhāvi kārya vat dvitīya ādi kṣaṇa bhāvi api kāryam kuryāt samarthasya kṣepā yogāt atha tadā sahakāri sākalya lakṣaṇa sāmarthyam na asti tad vaikalya lakṣaṇasya asāmarthyasya sambhavāt na hi bhāvaḥ sva rūpeṇa karoti iti sva rūpeṇa eva karoti sahakāri sahitāt eva tatas kārya utpatti darśanāt iti ced 
RKNĀ_90.4	 yadā tāvat amī militāḥ santaḥ kāryam kurvate tadā eka artha karaṇa lakṣaṇam sahakāri tvam eṣām astu kaḥ niṣeddhāḥ militaiḥ eva tu tat kāryam kartavyam iti kutas labhyate pūrva apara kālayoḥ eka svabhāva tvāt bhāvasya sarvadā jananā jananayoḥ anyatara niyama prasaṅgasya durvāra tvāt tasmāt sāmagrī janikā na ekam janakam iti sthira vādinām manaḥ rajyasya api aviṣayaḥ 
RKNĀ_90.9	 kim kurmaḥ dṛśyate tāvat evam iti ced dṛśyatām kim tu pūrva sthitāt eva paścāt sāmagrī madhya praviṣṭāt bhāvāt kārya utpattiḥ anyasmāt eva viśiṣṭa sāmagrī samutpannāt kṣaṇāt iti vivāda padam etat tatra prāk api sambhave sarvadā eva kārya utpattiḥ na vā kadācid api iti virodham asamādhāya tatas eva kārya utpattiḥ iti sādhya anuvāda mātra pravṛttaḥ kṛpām arhati 
RKNĀ_90.14–90.17	 na ca pratyabhijñānāt eva eka tva siddhiḥ tad pauruṣasya lūna punar jāta keśa kuśa kadalī stamba ādau nirdalanāt vistareṇa ca pratyabhijñā t ūṣaṇam asmābhiḥ sthira siddhi dūṣaṇe pratipāditam iti tatas eva avadhāryam nanu kāryam eva sahakāriṇam apekṣate na tu kārya utpatti hetuḥ yasmāt dvividham sāmarthyam nijam āgantukam ca sahakāri antaram tatas akṣaṇikasya api krama vat sahakāri nānā tvāt api kramavat kārya nānā tvam iti ced 
RKNĀ_90.19–90.23	 bhavatu tāvat nija āgantuka bhedena dvividham sāmarthyam tathā api tat prātisvikam vastu sva lakṣaṇam sadyas kriyā dharmakam avaśya abhyupagantavyam tat yadi prāk api prāk api kārya prasaṅgaḥ atha paścāt eva na tadā sthiraḥ bhāvaḥ na ca kāryam saha kariṇaḥ apekṣate iti yuktam tasya asattvāt hetuḥ ca san api yadi sva kāryam na karoti tadā tad kāryam eva tat na syāt svātantryāt 
RKNĀ_90.25	 yat ca uktam yaḥ hi uttara kārya janana svabhāvaḥ sa katham ādau kāryam kuryāt atha kuryāt na tarhi tad kārya karaṇa svabhāvaḥ na hi nīla utpādana svabhāvaḥ pīta ādikam api karoti iti tat asaṅgatam sthira svabhāva tve bhāvasya uttarakālam eva idam na pūrva kālam iti kutas etat tad abhāvāt ca kāraṇam api uttara kārya svabhāvam iti api kutas 
RKNĀ_90.29–91.4	 kim kurmaḥ uttarakālam eva tasya janma iti ced sthira tve tat anupapadyamānam asthira tām ādiśatu sthira tve api eṣaḥ eva svabhāvaḥ tasya yat uttarakṣaṇaḥ eva kāryam karoti iti ced na pramāṇa bādhite svabhāva abhyupagamā yogāt iti na tāvat akṣaṇikasya krami kārya kāri tvam asti na api akramikārya kāri tva sambhavaḥ dvitīye api kṣaṇe kāraka svarūpa sadbhāve punar api kārya karaṇa prasaṅgāt kārye niṣpanne tad viṣaya vyāpāra abhāvāt ūnā sāmagrī na niṣpāditam niṣpādayet iti ced na sāmagrī sambhava asambhavayoḥ api sadyas kriyā kāraka svarūpa sambhave janaka tvam avāryam iti prāk eva pratipādanāt kāryasya hi niṣpādita tvāt punar kartum aśakya tvam eva kāraṇam asamartham āvedayati 
RKNĀ_91.7	 tat ayam akṣaṇike krama ākrami kārya kāritva abhāvaḥ na siddhaḥ na ca kramākramābhyām apara prakāra sambhavaḥ yena tābhyām avyāptau sandigdha vyatirekaḥ hetuḥ syāt prakāra antara śaṅkāyām tasya api dṛśya tvādṛśya tva prakāra dvaya dūṣaṇe api sva pakṣe api anāśvāsa prasaṅgāt tasmāt anyonya vyavaccheda sthitayoḥ na aparaḥ prakāraḥ sambhavati svarūpa apraviṣṭasya vastunaḥ avastunaḥ vātatsvabhāva tvāt prakāra antarasya api krama svarūpa apraviṣṭa tvāt tathā atīndriyasya sahakāriṇaḥ adṛśya tve api ayoga vyavacchedena dṛśya sahakāri sahitasya dṛśyasya eva sattvasya dṛśya krama ākramābhyām vyāptiḥ pratyakṣāt eva sidhyati evam krama ākramābhyām artha kriyā kāritvam vyāptam iti kramākramayoḥ anyonya vyavacchedena sthita tvāt etad prakāra dvaya parihāreṇa artha kriyā kāri tvam anyatra na gatam iti arthaḥ atas eva etayoḥ vinivṛttau nivartate 
RKNĀ_91.17–91.18	 trilocanasya api vikalpa traye prathama dūṣaṇam āśraya asiddhi doṣa parihārataḥ nirastam dvitīyam ca asaṅgatam vikalpa jñānena vyatirekasya pratīta tvāt na hi abhāvaḥ kaścid vigrahavān yaḥ sākṣāt kartavyaḥ api tu vikalpāt eva vyavahartavyaḥ na hi abhāvasya vikalpāt anyā pratipattiḥ apratipattiḥ vā sarvathā ubhayathā api tad vyavahāra hāni prasaṅgāt evam vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntasya hetu vyatirekasya ca vikalpāt eva pratipattiḥ 
RKNĀ_91.22–91.25	 tṛtīyam api dūṣaṇam asaṅgatam vyāpaka anupalambhena nirdoṣeṇa sattvasya kṣaṇika tvena vyāpteḥ avyāhata tvāt tat ayam vyāpaka anupalambhaḥ akṣaṇikasya asattvam sattvasya tatas vyatirekam kṣaṇika tvena vyāptim ca sādhayati eka vyāpāra ātmaka tvāt iti sthitam nanu vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ iti yadi anupalabdhi mātram tadā na tasya sādhya buddhi janaka tvam avastu tvāt na ca anya upalabdhiḥ vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ abhidhātum śakyā bhū tala ādi vat anyasya kasyacid anupalabdheḥ iti ced 
RKNĀ_91.27	 tat asaṅgatam dharmī upalabdheḥ eva anyatra anupalbdhi tayā vyavasthāpanāt yathā hi na iha śiṃśapā vṛkṣa abhāvāt iti atra vṛkṣa apekṣayā kevala pradeśasya dharmiṇaḥ upalabdhiḥ vṛkṣa anupalabdhiḥ śiśapa apekṣayā ca kevala pradeśasya dharmiṇaḥ upalabdhiḥ eva śiṃśapāyā abhāva upalabdhiḥ iti svabhāva hetu paryavasāyi vyāpāraḥ vyāpaka anupalambhaḥ tathā nityasya dharmiṇaḥ vikalpa buddhi avasitasya kramikāri tvā krami kāritva apekṣayā kevala grahaṇāt eva kramikāri tvā krami kāritvā anupalambhaḥ artha kriyā apekṣayā ca kevala pratītiḥ eva artha kriyā yoga pratītiḥ iti vyāpaka anupalambha antarāt asya na kaścid viśeṣaḥ 
RKNĀ_92.5	 adhyavasāya apekṣayā ca bāhye akṣaṇike vastuni vyāpaka abhāvāt vyāpya abhāva siddhi vyavahāraḥ adhyavasāyaḥ ca samanantara pratyaya bala āyāta ākāra viśeṣa yogāt agṛhīte api pravartana śaktiḥ boddhavyaḥ īdṛśaḥ ca adhyavasāyaḥ asmad citrā dvaita siddhau nirvāhitaḥ sa ca avisaṃvādī vyavahāraḥ parihartum aśakyaḥ yat vyāpaka śūnyam tat vyāpya śūnyam iti etasya eva arthasya anena api krameṇa pratipādanāt ayam ca nyāyaḥ yathā vastu bhūte dharmiṇi tathā avastu bhūte api iti kaḥ viśeṣaḥ 
RKNĀ_92.10	 tathā hi eka jñāna saṃsargi atra vikalpya eva yathā ca hariṇa śirasi tena eka jñāna saṃsargi śṛṅgam upalabdham śaśaśirasi api tena saha eka jñāna saṃsargi tva sambhā vanayā eva śṛṅgam niṣidhyate tathā nīla ādau apariniṣṭhita nitya aniti abhāve kramākramau svadharmiṇā sārdham eka jñāna saṃsargiṇau dṛṣṭau yadi nitye bhavataḥ nitya grāhi jñāne sva dharmiṇā nityena saha eva gṛhye yātām iti sambhā vanayā eka jñāna saṃsarga dvārakam eva pratiṣidhyate katham punar etasmin iti ajñāne kramākramayoḥ asphuraṇam iti yāvatā kramākrama kroḍīkṛtam eva nityam vikalpayām iti ced atas eva bādhaka avatāraḥ viparīta āropam antareṇa tasya vaiyarthyāt 
RKNĀ_92.17	 kāla antare api eka rūpa tayā nitya tvam krama ākramau ca kṣaṇa dvaye bhinna rūpa tayā tatas nitya tvasya krama ākrami kārya śakteḥ ca paraspara parihāra sthiti lakṣaṇa tayā durvāraḥ virodhaḥ iti katham nitye kramākramayoḥ antarbhāvaḥ anantarbhāvāt ca śuddha nitya vikalpena dūrīkṛta krama ākrama samāropeṇa katham ullekhaḥ tatas ca pratiyogini nitye api vikalpyamānaḥ eka jñāna saṃsargi lakṣaṇa prāpte nitya upalabdhiḥ eva nitya viruddhasya anupalabhyamānasya kramākramasya anupalabdhiḥ tatas eva ca artha kriyā śakteḥ anupalabdhiḥ tasmāt vyāpaka viveki dharmī upalabdhi tayā na vyāpaka anupalambha antarāt asya viśeṣaḥ 
RKNĀ_92.25–93.1	 na tu etat avastu dharmi tva upayogivaḥ tu adhiṣṭhāna tvāt pramāṇa vyavasthāyāḥ iti ced kim idam vastu adhiṣṭhāna tvam nāma kim pamparayā api vastunaḥ sakāśāt āgata tvam atha vastuni kenacid ākāreṇa vyavahāra kāraṇa tvam vastu bhūta dharmi pratibaddha tvam vā yadi ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā krama ākramasya artha kriyāyāḥ ca vyāpti grahaṇa gocara vastu pratibaddha tvam asya api na kṣīṇam 
RKNĀ_93.2–93.10	 na dvitīye api pakṣe doṣaḥ sambhavati kṣaṇa bhaṅgi vastu sādhana upāya tvāt asya na ca antimaḥ api vikalpaḥ kalpyate tasya eva nitya vikalpasya vastunaḥ dharmi bhūtasya kramākrama vat bāhya nitya upādāna śūnya tvena artha kriyāvat bāhya nitya upādāna śūnya tve prasādhanāt paryudāsa vṛttyā buddhi svabhāva bhūta akṣaṇikā ākāre vastu bhūte dharmiṇi pratibaddha tva sambhavāt ayam eva nyāyaḥ na vaktā bandhyā sutaḥ caitanya abhāvāt ityādau yojyaḥ etena yathā vṛkṣa abhāva ādiḥ antar bhāvayitum śakyate na tathā ayam iti trilocanaḥ api nirastaḥ na ca krama āt yabhāvaḥ trayīm doṣa jātim na atikrāmati abhāva dharma tve api āśraya asiddhi doṣa parihārāt 
RKNĀ_93.11	 yat tu anena pramāṇa antarāt nityānām asattva siddhau krama ādi virahasya abhāva dharmatā sidhyati iti uktam tat bālasya api durabhidhānam nityaḥ hi dharmī asattvam sādhyam krami kārya kāri tva ākrami kārya kāri tva virahaḥ hetuḥ asya ca abhāva dharma tvam nāma asattva lakṣaṇa svasādhya avinābhāvi tvam ucyate tat ca kramākrameṇa sattvasya vyāpti siddhau sattvasya vyāpyasya abhāvena kramākramasya vyāpakasya virahaḥ vyāptaḥ sidhyati iti abhāva dharma tvam prāk eva vidhyoḥ vyāpti sādhanāt pratyakṣāt anumānāt ekasmāt vā pramāṇa antarāt siddham iti na itaretara āśraya doṣaḥ 
RKNĀ_93.18–93.19	 na ca sattāyām iva asattāyām api tulyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ bhinna nyāya tvāt vastu bhūtam hi tatra sādhyam sādhanam ca tayoḥ dharmī api vastu eva yujyate vastunaḥ tu pratyakṣa anumānābhyām eva siddhiḥ tayoḥ abhāve niyamena āśraya asiddhiḥ iti yuktam asattā sādhane tu avastu dharmaḥ hetuḥ avastu vikalpa mātra siddhe dharmiṇi na āśraya asiddhi doṣeṇa dūṣayitum śakyaḥ tathā akṣaṇikasya krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā virodhaḥ sidhyati eva 
RKNĀ_93.22	 tathā vikalpāt eva akṣaṇikaḥ virodhī siddhaḥ vikalpa ullikhitaḥ ca asya svabhāvaḥ na aparaḥ iti api vyavahartavyam anyathā tad anuvādena krama ākrama ādi rahita tva ādi niṣedha ādikam ayuktam tad svarūpasya anullekhāt anyasya ullekhāt iti akṣaṇika śaśa viṣāṇa ādi śabdān uccāraṇa prasaṅgaḥ asti ca atas yathā pramāṇa abhāve api vikalpa siddhasya bandhyā suta ādeḥ saundarya ādi niṣedhaḥ anurūpaḥ tathā vikalpa upanītasya eva akṣaṇika rūpasya tatas eva pratyanīka ākāreṇa saha virodha vyavasthāyām kīdṛśaḥ doṣaḥ syāt yadi ca akṣaṇikā anubhava abhāvāt virodha pratiṣedhaḥ tarhi bandhyā putra ādi anubhava abhāvāt eva saundarya ādi niṣedhaḥ api mā bhūt 
RKNĀ_94.5–94.6	 nanu evam virodhasya apāram ārthika tvam tad dvāreṇa kṣaṇa bhaṅga siddhiḥ api apāramārthikī syāt iti ced na hi virodhaḥ nāma vastu antaram kiñcid ubhaya koṭi datta pāda sambandha abhidhānam iṣyate asmābhiḥ upapadyate vā yena eka sambandhinaḥ vastu tva abhāve apāramārthikam syāt yathā tu iṣyate tathā pāramārthikaḥ eva viruddha abhimatayoḥ anyonya svarūpa parihāra mātram virodha arthaḥ sa ca bhāva abhāvayoḥ pāramārthikaḥ eva na bhāvaḥ abhāva rūpam āviśati na api abhāvaḥ bhāva rūpam praviśati iti yaḥ ayam anayoḥ asaṃkara niyamaḥ saḥ eva pāramārthikaḥ virodhaḥ kāla antara eka rūpa tayā hi nitya tvam kramākramau kṣaṇa dvaye api bhinna rūpa tayā tatas nitya tvakrama ākrami kārya kāri tvayoḥ bhāva abhāva vat virodhaḥ asti eva 
RKNĀ_94.14–94.15	 nanu nitya tvam krama yaugapadyavat tvam ca viruddhau dharmau vidhūya na aparaḥ virodhaḥ nāma kasya vāstava tvam iti ced na na hi dharma antarasya sambhavena virodhasya pāramārthika tvam brūmaḥ kim tu viruddhayoḥ dharmayoḥ sadbhāve anyathā virodha nāma dharma antara sambhave api yadi na viruddhau dharmau kva pāramārthika virodha sambhavaḥ viruddhau ced dharmau tāvatā eva tāttvikaḥ virodha vyavahāraḥ kim apareṇa pratijñā mātra siddhena virodha nāmnā vastu antareṇa 
RKNĀ_94.20–94.25	 tat ayam pūrva pakṣa saṃkṣepaḥ gnityam na asti na vā pratīti viṣaya s tena āśraya asiddha tā hetoḥ sva anubhavasya ca kṣatiḥ atas kṣiptaḥ sa pakṣaḥ api ca śūnyaḥ ca dvitayena sidhyati na ca asattā api sattā yathā naḥ nityena virodha siddhiḥ asatā śakyā krama ādeḥ api iti atra siddhānta saṃkṣepaḥ hdharmasya kasyacid avastuni māna siddhā bādhā vidhi vyavahṛtiḥ kim iha asti naḥ vā kvāpi asti ced katham iyanti na dūṣaṇāni na asti eva ced sva vacana pratirodha siddhiḥ 
RKNĀ_95.1	 tat evam nityam na krami kārya kāri tva ākrami kārya kāri tva yogī iti parama arthaḥ tatas ca sattā yuktam api na eva iti parama arthaḥ tatas ca kṣaṇikā kṣaṇika parihāreṇa rāśi antara abhāvāt akṣaṇikān nivartamānam idam sattvam kṣaṇikaḥ eva viśrāmyat tena vyāptam sidhyati iti sattvāt kṣaṇika tva siddhiḥ avirodhinī prakṛtiḥ sarva dharmāṇām yat bodhāt muktiḥ iṣyate saḥ eva tīrthya nirmāthī kṣaṇa bhaṅgaḥ prasādhitaḥ 
RKNĀ_96.4–96.6^1	 pramāṇa dvitayāt anya pramāṇa gaṇa dūṣaṇam na apūrvam ucyate tat tu prayogeṇa atra mudryate iha khalu pramāṇa mātre na kecid vipratipadyante antatas cārvākasya api saṃpratipatteḥ pramāṇa mātra uccheda vādī ca tat tadā aṅśakya pratividhānāt asmad gurubhiḥ avajñātaḥ pramāṇam apramāṇam ced vicāra avasaraḥ hataḥ bruvatā niyatam kiñcid sādhyam vā bādhyam eva vā tatra ayuktim bruvāṇasya ślāghā sadasi kīdṛśī na anumāyāḥ parā yuktiḥ kim siddham tad anādare svīkṛtā tena sā iti asmāt tad matyā bādhanam yadi abādhane asyāḥ svīkārāt tad bhiyā bādhanam katham 
RKNĀ_96.4–96.6^2	 sādhyam na kiñcid iti ced bādhāyāḥ api sādhya tā sā api na iti vacaḥ vyartham praśna mātre api kim phalam phalam yadi giraḥ kvāpi na anyat tat ca avabodhanāt vācaḥ pratyāyane śaktāḥ na akṣa dhūma ādi sundaram saṃvṛtau mānam iṣṭam ced vicāraḥ api eṣa saṃvṛtiḥ saṃvṛtau api na iṣṭam ced vadan jetā yathā tathā saṃvṛtiḥ ca vinā mānam vāc mātreṇa na sidhyati mānataḥ yadi durvāraḥ pramāṇasya parigrahaḥ ācāryaḥ api āha aniṣṭeḥ ced pramāṇam hi sarva iṣṭīnām nibandhanam bhāva abhāva vyavasthām kaḥ kartum tena vinā prabhuḥ iti 
RKNĀ_96.26–97.1	 tat evam pramāṇa mātrā pratikṣepe pratyakṣam tāvat ādau gaṇanīyam tad mūla tvāt apara pramāṇa upapatteḥ na ca cārvākaḥ api anumānam anavasthāpya sthātum prabhavati vyāpāra traya karaṇāt tat śāstre hi pratyakṣa itara sāmānyayoḥ pramāṇa itara vidhānam lakṣaṇa praṇaya nataḥ vidhātavyam tat ca lakṣaṇam pratyakṣe dharmiṇi lakṣye prāmāṇye pratyetavye svabhāvaḥ hetuḥ para buddhi pratipattau ca kārya adi vyāpāraḥ kārya hetuḥ para loka pratiṣedhe ca dṛśya anupalambhaḥ aṅgīkartavyaḥ iti katham anumāna apalāpaḥ yat ācāryaḥ pramāṇa itara sāmānya sthiteḥ anyadhiyaḥ gateḥ pramāṇa antara sadbhāva pratiṣedhāt ca kasyacid api ca arthasya asambhave abhāvāt pratyakṣe api pramāṇa tā pratibaddha svabhāvasya tad hetu tve samam dvayam iti anumānam api pramāṇam prāmāṇyam ca pramāṇa antara agṛhīta niścita pravṛtti viṣaya artha tayā tad prāpaṇe śaktiḥ 
RKNĀ_97.13	 nanu astu prāpaṇe śaktiḥ prāmāṇyam parama sauna arthāt utpatteḥ api tu artha darśanāt iti ced kim idam artha darśanam arthasya dharmaḥ dṛśya tvam jñānasya dharmaḥ draṣṭṛ tvam prathama pakṣe nīlatva vat dṛśya tvasya api sādhāraṇa tvāt eka gocaraḥ arthaḥ sarva gocaraḥ syāt na hi prati puruṣam arthānām bhedaḥ nairātmya prasaṅgāt dvitīya pakṣe tu katham anyasmin jñāna svabhāve draṣṭṛ tve sati anyasya asambaddhasya arthasya pratyāśā syāt draṣṭṛa tvam dṛśya tvam antareṇa anupapadyamānam tadā ākṣipati iti ced nanu jñāna arthayoḥ utpatti sārūpya balataḥ draṣṭḥ dṛśya tva vyavasthāpanam etat anabhyupagame draṣṭṛ tvam dṛśya tvam ca na sambhavati iti kim kena ākṣipyatām bhavatu vā prakāra antareṇa api draṣṭṛ dṛśya bhāvaḥ tathā api bhede sati avyabhicāra dutpattiḥ eva prāpti nimittam sā ca prāpaṇa śaktiḥ pratyakṣa anumānayoḥ aviśiṣṭa iti pramāṇe eva 
RKNĀ_97.23–97.27	 nanu anyat api śābda upamāna ādikam pramāṇam asti tathā hi śabdāt codanā rūpāt asannikṛṣṭe arthe svarga ādau yat jñānam utpadyate tat api śābdam jñānam pramāṇam eva pratyayita udita vākya prasūtam ca jñānam pramāṇam yat āha kumārilaḥ tat ca akartṛkatas vākyāt anyāt vā pratyayitaḥ ditāt iti tatra yadā śabda samuttham jñānam pramāṇam tadā upādāna ādi buddhiḥ phalam yadā tu śabdaḥ tadā tad ālambanam jñānam phalam iti naiyāyikasya punar āpta upadeśaḥ śabdaḥ iti śabda pramāṇa lakṣaṇa sūtram tatra śabdaḥ iti lakṣya padam āpta upadeśaḥ iti lakṣaṇa padam asya ayam saṃkṣepa arthaḥ āpta upadiṣṭaḥ śabdaḥ pramāṇam iti āptaḥ ca sākṣātkṛta heya upādeya tattvaḥ yathādṛṣṭasya ca arthasya acikhyāsayā prayuktaḥ upadeṣṭā abhidhīyate pramāṇa phala vyavasthā ca pūrvavat draṣṭavyā iti 
RKNĀ_98.3–98.5	 tathā mīmāṃsakānām upamānam pramāṇam yat uktam śabara svāminā upamānam api sādṛśyam asat nikṛṣṭe arthe arthe buddhim utpādayati yathā gavaya darśanam goḥ smaraṇasya iti asya ayam arthaḥ ekatra dṛśyamānam sādṛśyam kartṛ pratiyogi antare dṛśyamāna pratiyogi sādṛśya viśiṣṭa tayā etat sādṛśya viśiṣṭaḥ asau iti asat nikṛṣṭe arthe yām buddhim utpādayati tad upamānam pramāṇam iti yat tadoradhyāhāraḥ iti tasmāt samarati iti smaraṇam puruṣaḥ tena ayam arthaḥ yathā gavaye dṛśyamānam sādṛśyam gām smarataḥ manuṣyasya etat sādṛśya viśiṣṭaḥ asau gauḥ iti buddhim utpādayati iti 
RKNĀ_98.10–98.17	 na ca idam upamānam smaraṇam kartavyam gavaya sādṛśya viśiṣṭasya goḥ go viśiṣṭasya ca sādṛśyasya prameya tvāt go sādṛśyayoḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvasya upamāna pramāṇa viṣayasya go grāhiṇā gavaya grāhiṇā vā pratyakṣeṇa kenacid agrahaṇāt yat āha bhaṭṭaḥ pratyakṣe api yathā deśe smaryamāṇe ca pāvake viśiṣṭasya anyatas siddheḥ anumāna pramāṇa tā pratyakṣeṇa avabuddhe ca sādṛśye gavi ca smṛte viśiṣṭasya anyatas asiddheḥ upamāna pramāṇa tā na ca grahaṇam antareṇa smaraṇam asti tasmāt na upamānam smaraṇam atas pramaṇam iti naiyāyika ādīnām tu upamāna sūtram prasiddha sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam upamānam iti 
RKNĀ_98.20	 asya ayam arthaḥ prasiddham sādharmyam yasya tasmāt gavaya ādeḥ sādhyasya saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandhasya sādhanam siddhiḥ tad upamāna phalam samākhyā sambandha pratipatti hetuḥ upamānam iti arthaḥ ayam asya prapañcaḥ yaḥ pratipattāḥ gām jānāti na gavayam ādiṣṭaḥ ca svāminā gaccha araṇyam gavayamānayā asmāt iti gavaya śabda vācyam artham ajānānaḥ vanecaram anyam vā tad jñam pṛṣṭavān bhrātar kīdṛśaḥ gavayaḥ iti tena ca ādiṣṭam yathā gauḥ tathā gavayaḥ iti tasya śruta atideśa vākyasya kasyāñcid araṇyānyām upagatasya atideśa vākya arthsmaraṇa sahakāri yat gavaya sārūpya jñānam tat prathamatas eva asau gavaya śabda vācyaḥ arthaḥ iti pratipattim prastuvānam upamānam pramāṇam iti 
RKNĀ_99.1	 tathā arthāpatti saṃjñam pramāṇam mīmāṃsakasya arthāpattiḥ api dṛṣṭaḥ śrutaḥ vā arthaḥ anyathā na upadyamānaḥ yat artha antaram parikalpayati sārtha āpattiḥ yathā jīvati devadatte gṛha abhāva darśanena bahirbhāvasya arthasya parikalpanā asya ayam arthaḥ pratyakṣa ādibhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ pramāṇaiḥ prasiddhaḥ yaḥ arthaḥ sa yena vinā na yujyate tasya arthasya kalpanam arthāpattiḥ iti sā ca ṣaṣ pramāṇa pūrvikā ṣaṣ prakāra eva iti 
RKNĀ_99.6	 pratyakṣa anumāna ādi pramāṇa pañcaka abhāva svabhāvam abhāva ākhyam pramāṇam prameyam ghaṭa ādi abhāvaḥ na asti iha ghaṭa ādi iti jñānam ghaṭa ādi abhāva ālambanam phalam yat āha kumārilaḥ pratyakṣa ādeḥ anupattiḥ pramāṇa abhāvaḥ ucyate sa ātmanaḥ apariṇāmaḥ vā vijñānam vā anya vastuni pramāṇa pañcakam yatra vastu rūpe na jāyate vastu sattā avabodha artham tatra abhāva pramāṇa tā iti etāni ṣaḍ pramāṇāni pratyakṣa ādīni asaṃkīrṇa sva sva lakṣaṇa yogi tvāt anya apraviṣṭa svabhāvāni pratyetavyāni iti 
RKNĀ_99.15	 atra ucyate codanāyāḥ tāvat bāhye arthe pratibandha abhāvāt na prāmāṇyam prayogaḥ yasya yatra pratibandhaḥ na asti na tasya tatra prāmāṇyam yathā dahane apratibaddhasya rāsabhasya apratibaddhāḥ ca bahis arthe vaidikāḥ śabdāḥ iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ na tāvat ayam asiddhaḥ hetuḥ śabdānām vastutas pratibandha abhāvāt pratibaddha svabhāva tā hi pratibandhaḥ na ca sā nirnibandhanā sarveṣām sarvatra pratibaddha svabhāvatā prasaṅgāt nibandhanam ca asyāḥ tādātmya tad utpattibhyām anyat na upalabhyate atad svabhāvasya ātad utpatteḥ ca tatra apratibaddha svabhāva tvāt na hi śabdānām bahis artha svabhāvatā asti bhinna pratibhāsā avabodha viṣaya tvāt na api śabdāḥ bahis arthāt upajāyante artham antareṇa api puruṣasya icchā pratibaddha vṛtteḥ śabdasya utpāda darśanāt 
RKNĀ_99.24^1	 nanu yogya tayā eva kiñcid pratibaddha svabhāvam upalabhyate yathā cakṣuḥ indriyam rūpe cakṣuḥ khalu vyāpāryamāṇam rūpam eva upalabhyati tathā eva ete vaidikāḥ śabdāḥ tādātmya tad utpatti viyuktāḥ api yogyatā mātreṇa atīndriyam artham bodhayiṣyanti tat katham tādātmya tad utpatti viraha mātreṇa apratibandhaḥ yena evam vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ sidhyati iti na eṣa doṣaḥ yatas cakṣuḥ indriyam api rasa ādi parihāreṇa rūpaḥ eva prakāśaka tvena pratiniyatam tad kārya tvāt rūpam hi cakṣuḥ upakaroti na sattā mātreṇa cakṣuḥ rūpam prakāśayati vyavahitasya api rūpa upalabdhi prasaṅgāt 
RKNĀ_99.24^2	 tasmāt rūpāt yogya deśa sannihitāt tad jñāna janana yogya tām āsādya cakṣuḥ rūpa jñānam utpādayat tat kāryam iti vyaktam avasīyate anyathā tad upakāra anapekṣasya tasya api tad prakāśana niyamaḥ na upapadyate na hi anupakārya tva aviśeṣe cakṣuḥ rūpasya eva prakāśakam na rasa ādeḥ iti ghaṭām upaiti niyamaḥ ayam eva tarhi niyamaḥ kutas yat rūpeṇa eva cakṣuḥ upakartavyam na rasa ādinā iti yadi vastu vaśāt eva rūpam upakaroti na rasa ādikam hanta tarhi yathā upakārya tvam prati niyamaḥ cakṣuṣaḥ rūpeṇa tathā śabdānām api svābhāvikaḥ eva astu bahis artha pratyāyana niyamaḥ iti 
RKNĀ_100.6	 atra ucyate na cakṣuṣaḥ svābhāvikaḥ rūpa upakārya tā niyamaḥ kasyacid vastunaḥ svābhāvika tva anupapatteḥ tathā hi svābhāvika tvam vastu dharmasya anujānānaḥ praṣṭavyaḥ kim svābhāvikaḥ iti svatas bhavati āhosvit paratas atha ahetutaḥ yadi svatas bhavati tat asaṅgatam sva ātmani kriyā virodhāt atha ahetutaḥ tat ayuktam ahetoḥ deśa ādi niyama ayogāt tasmāt na svābhāvikaḥ rūpa upakārya tā pratiniyamaḥ cakṣuṣaḥ kiṃnibandhanaḥ tarhi sva hetu pratibaddhaḥ iti brūmaḥ cakṣuḥ khalu sva hetunā janyamānam tādṛśam eva janitam yat rūpa upakartavyam eva bhavati rūpam api tādṛśam eva sva hetunā janitam yat tat upakāraka svabhāvam 
RKNĀ_100.14	 śabdānām api sa svabhāvaḥ sva hetu pratibaddhaḥ yena ete bāhya artha avyabhicāriṇaḥ iti ced na śakyam evam abhidhātum nitya tva abhyupagamāt veda vākyānām atha anitya tvam abhyupagamya ayam ākṣepaḥ parihartum iṣyate tat api duṣkaram doṣa antara prasaṅgāt yadi sva hetunā eva te niyama artha upadarśana śaktimantaḥ janitāḥ tadā avyutpanna samayasya api sva artham avabodhayeyuḥ yathā cakṣuḥ sva hetaḥ rūpa prakāśakam utpannam sat prakāśayati eva rūpam asaṅketa vidaḥ api na ca śabdāt uccaritāt prāk apratīta samayasya api viśeṣa avagamaḥ samasti tasmāt na sva hetu pratibaddhaḥ cakṣuḥ ādeḥ iva śabdānām artha pratipādana niyamaḥ iti niścayaḥ 
RKNĀ_100.22	 atha sva hetubhiḥ eva ayam īdṛśaḥ teṣām svabhāvaḥ dattaḥ yena te saṃketa viśeṣa sahāyāḥ eva kam api artham avabodhayanti na tarhi saṅketa parāvṛttau padārtha antara vṛttayaḥ bhaveyuḥ yadi hi ayam agnihotra śabdaḥ saṃketa apekṣaḥ yāga viśeṣa pratipādakaḥ katham saṅketa anya tvena artha antaram pratipādayati na hi kṣiti ādi apekṣeṇa bījena sva hetoḥ aṅkura janana svabhāvena utpannena rāsabhaḥ śakyaḥ janayitum tathā śabdaḥ api yat artha pratipādana niyataḥ tam eva prakāśayet 
RKNĀ_100.27	 atha tad tad saṅketa apekṣaḥ tad tad artha pratyāyana yogyaḥ eva ayam jātaḥ iti ucyate tat api na prasuta upayogi na hi evam asya prāmāṇyam avatiṣṭhate yadā hi saṅketena apuruṣa artha pratipādanam api sambhāvyatas eva tadā na śakyam upakalpayitum kim ayam abhimatasya eva arthasya dyotakaḥ na vā iti tarhi vācya vācaka lakṣaṇaḥ śabda arthayoḥ sambandhaḥ bhaviṣyati tathā ca āha vācya vācaka sambandhāḥ santi yadi api vāstavāḥ saṅketaiḥ anabhivyaktāḥ na te artha vyakti hetavaḥ iti ced nanu tasya vāstava tve asaṅketa vidaḥ api artha pratipattiḥ bhavet iti uktam saṅketa apekṣāyām ca artha antare na pravarteta ityādi abhihitam atas pūrvam eva ayam pratyākhyātaḥ vācya vācaka lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ tasmāt na bahis arthe pratibandhaḥ śabdānām iti nirṇayaḥ tatas ca na asiddhaḥ hetuḥ 
RKNĀ_101.6–101.9	 na api viruddhaḥ viparyaya vyāpti abhāvāt tad abhāvaḥ ca sa pakṣe vṛtti upadarśanāt na hi viruddhasya sādharmyavati dharmiṇi sadbhāvaḥ yuktaḥ sādhya viparyayasya tatra abhāvāt na ca vyāpakam antareṇa vyāpyasya sambhavaḥ tad pracyuti prasaṅgāt na api anaikāntikaḥ hetuh viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa sambhavāt prāmāṇya pratiṣedhe hi sādhye prāmāṇyam eva vipakṣaḥ na ca tasmin pratibandha abhāva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ asti sva viruddhena pratibandhena vyāpta tvāt na khalu ayam prādeśikaḥ pramāṇa śabdaḥ jñāneṣu nirnibandhanaḥ eva sarva jñāneṣu prāmāṇya vyapadeśa prasaṅgāt nibandhanam ca sva viṣaya pratibandhāt anyat na upapadyate tasmāt pramāṇasya pramāṇa vyapadeśa viṣaya tvam sva viṣaya pratibandhena vyāptam atas pramāṇe dharmiṇi vipakṣe prāmāṇyasya viruddha vyāptasya upalambhena vipakṣe vyavaccheda siddheḥ na anaikāntikaḥ hetuḥ 
RKNĀ_101.16–101.18	 na ca anyaḥ doṣaḥ sambhavī tasmāt nirasta aśeṣa doṣeṇa hetunā yat prasiddham tat upādeyam eva satām iti paṇḍita śrī jita ari pādaiḥ eva veda aprāmāṇye darśitam evam ca vaidika śabdānām prāmāṇye niraste tad uttham jñānam api apramāṇam eva āpta praṇītasya punar vacanasya artha avi abhicāre tad janmanaḥ jñānasya avyabhicāra sambhave api na prāmāṇyam upagantum śakyate para citta vṛttīnām aśakya niścaya tvena āpta tva aparijñānāt vacanasya api tad praṇīta tva apratipatteḥ prayogaḥ ca atra 
RKNĀ_101.22–101.24	 yat yena rūpeṇa na niścitam na tat tena rūpeṇa vyavahriyate yathā rathyā puruṣaḥ sarvajña tvena na pratīyate ca abhimata puruṣaḥ āpta tvena iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ na ayam asiddhiḥ āpta abhimatasya tathā tva aniścayāt tathā hi para citta vṛttayaḥ atīndriya tvāt na pratyakṣa samadhigamyāḥ iti kāya vāc vyavahārataḥ anumātavyāḥ tau ca kāya vāc vyavahārau buddhiḥ pūrvam anyathā api kartum śakyate tatas tad pratibaddha tvena aniścayāt katham kāya vāc vyavahārataḥ viśiṣṭa para citta vṛtti anumānam 
RKNĀ_101.28–101.29	 na api viruddhaḥ sa pakṣe sadbhāva sambhavāt na api anaikāntikaḥ prāmāṇika tad rūpa vyavahartavya tva niścita tvayoḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhūtayoḥ vidhi bhūtayoḥ vṛkṣa tva śiṃśapā tvayoḥ iva pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām sarva upasaṃhāreṇa vyāpteḥ siddha tvāt tat atas sādhanāt doṣatraya rahitāt sādhyam siddhyat avācyam eva tat evam āpta tvasya durbodha tvena tad praṇīta tva aniścayāt eka prahāra nihatam āpta vacasaḥ prāmāṇyam 
RKNĀ_102.4–102.11	 atas yat etasya prāmāṇya prasiddhi artham vācaspati prabhṛtīnām valgitam tad aprāpta avasaram eva evam pratyaya uditam api bhaṭṭa abhimatam śābdam prāmāṇyam vyastam iti boddhavyam tasmāt sthitam etat na śābdam bahis arthe pramāṇam asti iti buddhi ākāre tu tad kārya prasūta tvāt tad anumānam eva iti mīmāṃsaka uktam tāvat upamānam mānam eva na bhavati nirviṣaya tvāt asya iha api prayogaḥ yasya na viṣayavat tvam na tasya prāmāṇyam yathā keśoṇḍuka jñānasya na siddham ca viṣayavat tvam upamāna jñānasya iti vyāpaka anupalambhaḥ na ayam asiddhaḥ hetuḥ nirviṣaya tvāt upamānasya tathā hi sādṛśya viśiṣṭaḥ piṇḍaḥ piṇḍa viśiṣṭam vā sādṛśyam upamānasya viṣayaḥ varṇyate na sadṛśa vastu vyatiriktam sādṛśyam vyavasthāpayitum śakyate pramāṇena apratīta tvāt 
RKNĀ_102.14	 nanu sādṛśyam vastu durvāram eva yat āha sādṛśyasya ca vastu tvam na śakyam apabādhitum bhūyas avayava sāmānya yogaḥ jāti antarasya tat iti atra ucyate yadi sadṛśa atiriktam sādṛśyam vastu dṛśyam syāt tadā dṛśya anupalambha grastam eva śāstra anāhita saṃskāreṇa api kenacid tasya adarśanāt tasya ca astitve sarvam sarvatra asti iti apravṛtti nivṛttikam jagat āpadyeta atha adṛśyam tad sādṛśyam upeyate tathā api tatra prasiddha liṅga abhāvāt asiddham eva siddhena ca tena viṣaya vat tā upamānasya sidhyeta sādṛśya pratyayaḥ tu sva hetoḥ tathā utpannena sadṛśa vastunā api kriyamāṇaḥ ghaṭataḥ eva iti na sādṛśyam upsthāpayitum prabhavati upamāna pramāṇa balāt eva sādṛśya siddhiḥ iti ced na pramāṇa antara siddhayoḥ eva sādṛśya piṇḍayoḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvasya upamāna viṣaya tvāt katham sādṛśya mātrasya upamānāt siddhiḥ tatas ca sādṛśyasya asiddheḥ na tad viśiṣṭaḥ piṇḍaḥ piṇḍa viśiṣṭam vā sādṛśyam upamānasya viṣayaḥ tat evam upamānasya nirviṣaya tvam siddham iti na asiddhaḥ hetuḥ na api viruddhaḥ sa pakṣe bhāvāt 
RKNĀ_102.28	 na ca anaikāntikaḥ tathā hi prāmāṇyān bhāve sādhye prāmāṇyam eva vipakṣaḥ tat ca viṣayavat tayā vyāptam nirnimitta tve sarva jñāna prāmāṇya prasaṅgāt tat yam viruddha vyāpta upalabdhyā vipakṣān nivartamānaḥ viṣaya vat tva abhāva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ prāmāṇya abhāva lakṣaṇaḥ eva viśrāmyati iti vyāpti siddhiḥ atas na upamānam pramāṇam iti 
RKNĀ_103.1^1	 naiyāyika parikalpita upamāna nirākaraṇa artham api ayam eva prayogaḥ draṣṭavyaḥ tasya api nirviṣaya tvāt tathā hi samākhyā sambandhaḥ tasya viṣayaḥ varṇyate sa ca paramārthataḥ na asti sa hi sambandhaḥ sambandhibhyām bhinnaḥ abhinnaḥ vā yadi bhinnaḥ tadā tayoḥ iti kutas na ca sambandha antarāt iti vaktavyam tat api katham teṣām iti cintāyām anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ na ca yathā pradīpaḥ prakāśa antaram antareṇa prakāśate tathā sambandhaḥ api sambandha antareṇa sambaddhaḥ bhaviṣyati iti vaktum ucitam pramāṇa siddhe hi vastu rūpe ayam asya svabhāvaḥ iti varṇyate yathā pradīpasya eva sambandhaḥ tu na pramāṇa pratītaḥ tat kaḥ evam jānātu ayam asya svabhāvaḥ iti yat vā na asti eva ayam iti 
RKNĀ_103.1^2	 ayam anayoḥ sambandhaḥ sambaddhau etau iti tu buddhiḥ sva hetu balāt sambaddha vastu dvayāt api sambhāvyamānā na sambandham ākṣeptum prabhavati tasmāt na bhinna sambandha siddhiḥ atha abhinnaḥ tadā sambandhinau eva kevalau iti na samākhyā sambandhaḥ nāma yaḥ kaścid upamānasya viṣayaḥ syāt nanu sambandha buddhi janaka tvam sambaddha padārthāt bhinnam abhinnam vā bhede ca saḥ eva sambandhaḥ nāmni param vivādaḥ atha abhinnam tadā yathā sambaddha padārthasya svabhāvaḥ sarva padārtha sādhāraṇaḥ tathā tat api rūpam tat avyatibhinnam sarva padārtha sādhāraṇam iti sa padārthaḥ abhimata padārthena iva paraiḥ api padārthaiḥ saha sambaddhaḥ syāt 
RKNĀ_103.17	 na ca evam tasmāt bhinnam tad sambandha buddhi janaka tvam sambaddha padārthāt eṣṭavyam iti ced nanu etat āśaṅkya rāja kula pādaiḥ parihṛtam eva tathā hi sambaddham svayam eva ced nanu yathā tam tasya sambandhinam pratyātmā jagatīm api prati tathā tat kena yogaḥ asya na sambandhe paratas api tulyam akhilam tena eva ced saṃyamaḥ hetuḥ kim na niyāmakaḥ sa ca katham yogaḥ kvacid na apare iti tasmāt sambandha abhāvāt pūrva uktena nyāyena sārūpya abhāvāt ca asiddham naiyāyikasya api nirviṣayam upamānam pramāṇam atas anantareṇa eva vyāpakān upalambhena nirākṛtam 
RKNĀ_103.25^1	 arthāpattiḥ api yat etat sāmānya lakṣaṇam pratyakṣa ādi pratītaḥ yaḥ arthaḥ sa yena vinā na upapadyate tasya arthasya parikalpanam atha āpattiḥ iti atra vicāryate yasya arthasya darśanāt yaḥ arthaḥ parikalpyate tayoḥ yadi pratibandhaḥ asti tadā artha āpattiḥ anumānam eva atha āpattiḥ iti nāma antara karaṇe na asmākam kācid vipratipattiḥ tathā hi pramāṇa paridṛṣṭaḥ arthaḥ kenacid vinā na upapadyate iti kutas labhyate yadi paridṛśyamāna parikalpyamānayoḥ kaścid sambandhaḥ syāt anyathā tena vinā na upapadyate iti ahrīkāt anyaḥ na brūyāt ghaṭa paṭa vat sa ca sambandhaḥ kvacid pūrvam avaśyam pratyakṣa anupalambhataḥ kvacid adṛśya tve api viparyaya bādhaka pramāṇa balāt vā niścetavyaḥ anyathā tena vinā anupapatti jñānasya eva anupapatteḥ sati ca evam ekam sambadhinam dṛṣṭvā yatrasthena vinā tatrastham na upapadyate tasya dvitīyasya sambandhinaḥ kalpanam anumānam eva 
RKNĀ_103.25^2	 tatra svabhāva pratibandhe svabhāva hetu jā eva sārtha āpattiḥ tad utpatti pratibandhe kārya liṅga jā eva tat uktam anyathā anupapanna tvam anvaya vyatirekiṇī arthe bhavati yat tasmāt na artha āpattiḥ pramāṇa antaram iti tasmāt paridṛśyamāna parikalpyamānayoḥ sati pratibandhe na artha āpattiḥ pramāṇa antaram iti atha tayoḥ na pratibandhaḥ tadā artha āpattiḥ pramāṇam eva na bhavati iti mantavyam sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa ca sambandha abhāvāt yasya yatra pratibandhaḥ na asti na tasya tatra prāmāṇyam ityādiḥ veda nirākaraṇa artham yaḥ pūrvam upanyastaḥ saḥ eva asyāḥ api prāmāṇya nirākaraṇāya draṣṭavyaḥ sāmānyena eva artha āpattau nirākṛtāyām pratyakṣa ādiḥ pūrvakatva lakṣaṇa s tad prapañcaḥ nirastaḥ bhavati eva iti tad artham na prabandhaḥ abhidhīyate gavi nirākṛte śāvaleya nirākṛti vat tasmāt na artha āpattiḥ pramāṇa antaram iti 
RKNĀ_104.14	 tathā abhāva pramāṇasya api prāmāṇyam na upapadyate tasya api nirviṣaya tvāt tatas ca mīmāṃsaka upa valgita upamāna nirākaraṇa artham upanyastaḥ yaḥ viṣaya vat tva abhāva lakṣaṇaḥ anupalambhaḥ saḥ eva asya api nirāsa artham upanyasitavyaḥ nanu ca atra asiddhaḥ hetuḥ tathā hi yadi ghaṭa abhāvaḥ vāstavaḥ prameya bhūtaḥ na syāt tadā na asti iha ghaṭaḥ iti pratyayaḥ katham utpadyate iti ced kevala pradeśa grāhi pratyakṣāt iti brūmaḥ nanu yadi kaivalyam pradeśa svarūpam tat tarhi sa ghaṭe api pradeśe vidyate iti tatra api tasya pratyayasya sadbhāva prasaṅgaḥ atha atiriktaḥ mukha antareṇa abhāvaḥ eva abhyupagataḥ bhavati iti ced na kaivalyam tad vivikta tvam asaṅkīrṇa tvam ityādibhiḥ padaiḥ pradeśasya ghaṭam pratyanāpanna ādhāra bhāvasya sva hetutaḥ utpannasya ghaṭa pradeśāt anyaḥ eva ātmā abhidhīyate saḥ eva ca abhāva pratyayam janayati iti kim apareṇa abhāvena kartavyam 
RKNĀ_104.24	 nanu ghaṭam pratyanāpanna ādhāra bhāvasya pradeśasya iti ghaṭa abhāva yuktasya pradeśasya iti uktam bhavati iti ced tarhi ghaṭa abhāvaḥ api ghaṭam pratyanāpanna ādhāra bhāvaḥ kim abhāva antareṇa sva rūpeṇa eva vā prathama pakṣe anavasthā atha tad abhāva rūpa tvāt abhāva antaram antareṇa eva ghaṭa abhāvaḥ ghaṭam pratyanāpanna ādhāra bhāvaḥ yadi evam asahāyaḥ pradeśa viśeṣaḥ api paryudāsa vṛttyā ghaṭa abhāva rūpa tvāt abhāvam vinā eva ghaṭam pratyanāpanna ādhāra bhāvaḥ yuktaḥ iti kim akāṇḍam āhopuruṣikayā mithyā pralāpena ābodha viklavam śiṣya pudgalam ākulayasi tasmāt bhū tala atiriktasya abhāvasya asiddha tvāt na ayam viṣaya vattā bhāva lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ asiddhaḥ pramāṇa pañcaka abhāvāt eva tu prameya abhāva siddhi pratyāśā api na yujyate vipratipatti viṣaya tvāt asya anena eva prameya abhāva siddheḥ ayogāt 
RKNĀ_104.33–105.1	 viruddha anaikāntika tve ca pūrvam eva hetoḥ parihṛte tat atas siddham abhāva pramāṇa abhimatasya aprāmāṇyam iti atha vā abhāva pramāṇa svarūpam eva nirūpyatām kaḥ punar pramāṇa abhāva ātma abhimataḥ bhavatām kim prasajya vṛttyā pramāṇa an utpatti mātram atha vā paryudāsa vṛttyā bhāva antaram vastu antaram api jaḍa rūpam jñāna rūpam vā jñāna rūpam api jñāna mātrakam eka jñāna saṃsargi vastu jñānam vā iti ṣaṭ vikalpāḥ 
RKNĀ_105.5^1	 tatra na tāvat nivṛtti rūpaḥ abhāvaḥ yujyate sa khalu nikhila śakti vikala tayā na kiñcid yat ca na kiñcid tat katham abhāvam paricchindyāt tad viṣayam vā jñānam janayet pratītam vā tat katham iti sarvam andhakāra nartanam yat āhuḥ na hi abhāvaḥ kasyacid pratipattiḥ pratipatti hetuḥ vā tasya api katham pratipattiḥ iti na api vastu antara tā pakṣe jaḍa rūpaḥ abhāvaḥ saṅgacchate tasya abhāva lakṣaṇa prameya pariccheda abhāvāt paricchedasya jñāna dharma tvāt na api jñāna mātra svabhāvaḥ abhāvaḥ vaktavyaḥ deśa kāla svabhāva viprakṛṣṭasya api tatas abhāva prasaṅgāt tat apekṣayā api jñāna mātra tvāt tasya 
RKNĀ_105.5^2	 atha eka jñāna saṃsargi vastu jñāna svabhāvaḥ anumanyate tadā astam abhāva pramāṇa pratyāśayā pratyakṣa viśeṣasya eva abhāva nāmakaraṇāt tasya ca asmābhiḥ dṛśya anupalambha ākhya sādhana tvena svīkṛta tvāt atas na kācid vipratipattiḥ nāma tasmāt abhāva pramāṇa svarūpam api nirūpyamāṇam viśīryate eva yat api asya lakṣaṇam uktam pratyakṣa ādeḥ anutpattiḥ pramāṇa abhāvaḥ ucyate ityādi tat api yācitakam aṇḍanam tasmāt sthitam etat pramāṇasya sataḥ atra eva antarbhāvāt pramāṇaḥ eva 
RKNĀ_106.4	 iha dahana ādinā dhūma ādeḥ artha antarasya vyāptiḥ tad utpatti lakṣaṇā sā ca viśiṣṭa anvaya vyatireka grahaṇa pravaṇa viśiṣṭa pratyakṣa anupalambha sādhana iti nyāyaḥ atra ca bhaṭṭa prabhṛtayaḥ vipratipadyante tathā hi te agnimati pradeśe dhūmasya bhūyas darśanam tad vyukte ca tathā eva adarśanam iti anvaya vyatireki tvam kalpayām babhūvuḥ
