RKNĀ_106.8	 nanu bhūyasā api pravṛtte darśana adarśane ghaṭa kulaṭa ādau upalabdhaḥ vyabhicāraḥ iti ced kim etāvatā tatra api tatra api anumānam astu tadvat vā dhūma ādau api mā bhūt prathama pakṣaḥ tāvat vyabhicārāt eva nirastaḥ dvitīyaḥ api vyabhicārāt eva na hi anyasya vyabhicāre dhūmasya kiñcid tasmāt agni dhūmayoḥ avyabhicārasya asambhave śaktam api tad upapattayaḥ tad prasādhaka viśiṣṭa pratyakṣa anupalambhāḥ vā na anumāna upayoginaḥ sambhave vā kim tad utpattyā tad upayoginā viśiṣṭa pratyakṣa anupalambhena darśana adarśanābhyām eva avyabhicāra siddheḥ tathā ca kāśika ākāraḥ prācīna aneka darśana janita saṃskāra sahāyena carameṇa cetasā dhūmasya agni niyata tvam gṛhyate iti 
RKNĀ_106.16	 trilocanaḥ tu āha pratyakṣa anupalambhayoḥ viśeṣa viṣaya tvāt katham tābhyām sāmānyayoḥ sambandha pratipattiḥ atha anagni vyāvṛttena adhūma vyāvṛttasya sambandhaḥ pratīyate eva iti nanu saḥ api kasya pramāṇasya viṣayaḥ na tāvat pratyakṣasya sva lakṣaṇa viṣaya tvāt tasya na api anumānasya tasya api tad pūrvaka tvāt na ca vyāvṛttyoḥ kaścid sambandhaḥ atha pratyakṣa pṛṣṭha bhāvī vikalpaḥ dṛṣṭe bhede abhedam adhyavasyati tat eva sāmānyam evam api vikalpānām na vastu eva viṣayaḥ api tu grāhya ākāraḥ sa ca na vastu vastu tu teṣām parokṣam eva iti katham tena api sambandha grahaḥ asmākam tu bhūyas darśana sahāyena manasā tad jātīyānām sambandhaḥ gṛhītaḥ bhavati atas dhūmaḥ na agnim vyabhicarati tad vyabhicāre dhūmaḥ upādhi rahitam sambandham atikrāmet iti hetoḥ vipakṣa śaṅkā nivartakam pramāṇam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta upādhi viraha hetuḥ anupalambha ākhyam pratyakṣam eva tatas siddhaḥ svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ 
RKNĀ_106.27^1	 vācaspateḥ tu prapañcaḥ tathā hi dhūma ādīnām vahni ādibhiḥ svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ na tu vahni ādīnām dhūma ādibhiḥ te hi vinā api dhūma ādibhiḥ upalabhyante vahni ādayaḥ tu yadārdra indhana sambandham anubhavanti tadā dhūma ādibhiḥ sambadhyante vahni ādīnām tu sphuṭam ārdra indhana ādi upādhi kṛtaḥ sambandhaḥ na tu svābhāvikaḥ tatas aniyataḥ svābhāvikaḥ tu dhūma ādīnām vahni ādibhiḥ sambandhaḥ tad upādheḥ anupalabhyamāna tvāt kvacid vyabhicārasya adarśanāt anupalabhyamānasya api kalpanā anupapatteḥ na ca adṛśyamānaḥ api darśanān arha tayā sādhaka bādhaka pramāṇa abhāvena sagdihyamānaḥ upādhiḥ sambandhasya svābhāvika tvam pratibadhnāti iti yuktam 
RKNĀ_106.27^2	 avaśyam śaṅkayā bhāvyam niyāmakam apaśyatām iti tu datta avakāśā laukika maryādā atikrameṇa śaṅkā piśācī labdha prasarāḥ na kvacid na asti iti na ayam kvacid pravarteta sarvatra eva kasyacid anarthasya kathañcid śaṅkā āspada tvāt anartha śaṅkāyāḥ ca prekṣāvatām nivṛtti aṅga tvāt antatas snigdha anna pāna upayoge api maraṇa darśanāt tasmāt prāmāṇika lokayātrām anupālayatā yathādarśanam eva śaṅkanīyam na tu adṛṣṭa pūrvam api viśeṣa smṛti apekṣaḥ eva hi saṃśayaḥ na asmṛteḥ bhavati na ca smṛtiḥ ananubhūta care bhavitum arhati tat uktam mīmāṃsā vārtika kṛtā na āśaṅkā niḥpramāṇikāḥ iti tasmāt upādhim prayatnena anviṣyantaḥ anupalabhamānā na asti iti avagamya svābhāvika tvam sambandhasya niścinumaḥ 
RKNĀ_107.16^1	 syāt etat anyasya anyena saha akāraṇena ced svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ bhavet sarvam sarveṇa svabhāvataḥ sambadhyeta sarvam sarvasmāt gamyeta atha anyasya ced anyat kāryam kasmāt sarvam sarvasmāt na bhavati anya tva aviśeṣāt tatas ca saḥ eva atiprasaṅgaḥ yadi ucyeta na bhāva svabhāvāḥ paryanuyojyāḥ tasmāt anya tva aviśeṣe api kiñcid eva kāraṇam kāryam ca kiñcid iti nanu eṣa svabhāvānām anuyogaḥ bhinnānām akārya kāraṇa bhūtānām api svabhāva pratibandhe tulyaḥ eva tasmāt yat kiñcid etat api kena punar pramāṇena eṣa svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ gṛhyate 
RKNĀ_107.16^2	 pratyakṣa sambandhiṣu pratyakṣeṇa tathā hi abhijāta maṇi bheda tattva vat bhūyas darśana janita saṃskāra sahāyam indriyam eva dhūma ādīnām vahni ādibhiḥ svābhāvika sambandha grāhī iti yuktam utpaśyāmaḥ evam māna antara vidita sambandheṣu māna antarāṇi eva yathāsvam bhūyas darśana sahāyāni svābhāvika sambandha grahaṇe pramāṇāni unnetavyāni svabhāvataḥ ca pratibaddhāḥ hetavaḥ sva sādhyena yadi sādhyam antareṇa bhaveyuḥ svabhāvāt eva pracyaveran iti tarka sahāyāḥ nirasta sādhya vyatir eka vṛtti sandehāḥ yatra dṛṣṭāḥ tatra sva sādhyam upasthāpayanti eva iti 
RKNĀ_108.3	 atra ucyate iha khalu bhede tad utpattiḥ eva vyāptiḥ na ca asau= anyaḥ vā svatas eva avinābhāva lakṣaṇaḥ svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ bhūyas darśana mātrataḥ sidhyati tathā hi kim yatra bhūyas darśana pravṛttiḥ tatra niyata tva vyavasthā yatra vā niyata tvam asti tatra eva bhūyas darśana pravṛttiḥ prathama pakṣe ghaṭāt api kulaṭāḥ pārthiva tvāt api loha lekhya tvam sidhyet bhūyas darśana sambhave api niyata tva sambhavāt 
RKNĀ_108.8	 vyabhicāra darśanāt na evam iti ced kasya punar vyabhicāra darśanam yasya kasyacid śāstra kārasya pratipattuḥ vā prathama pakṣe pratipattuḥ kim āyātam yatas na anumānam ayam kuryāt anyathā anyasya tad viṣaya pratyakṣīkāreṇa eva saḥ api kṛtārthaḥ iti kim avaśyam anumānam anveṣate na ca āpta vacanāt avyabhicāra darśanāt anumānam āptasya niścetum aśakya tvāt iti anyatra prasādhanāt śāstra kāram ca pṛṣṭvā dṛṣṭa sambandhaḥ api dhūmāt agnim anumāsyate iti alaukikam pratipattuḥ tu na avaśyam san api vyabhicāraḥ gocarībhavati na hi yatra vyabhicāraḥ tatra eva tāvati kāle deśe vā avaśyam pratītim avatarati apratīyamānaḥ ca na asti eva iti na niyamaḥ sati api vyabhicāre darśana sāmagrya bhāvāt tasya adarśanāt ati cira kāla vyavadhāne api darśanāt brāhmaṇī ādi vyabhicāra vat 
RKNĀ_108.18	 ghaṭa pārthiva ādau pratipattā eva pravṛttaḥ tadā eva krameṇa vā vyabhicāram paśyet iti ced yadi tāvat asau kathañcid pravartate pravṛttaḥ api vā sāmagrya bhāva avyabhicāram na paśyet vajram vā lohena vyāpārayet vyaktam tasya tāvat tat api amānam āpannam iti mahat pāṇḍityam tasmāt yadi vyabhicāra darśanāt anumānam tadā adṛṣṭa vyabhicārasya pratipattuḥ ghaṭa pārthiva tvāt api asti tathā adarśana mātreṇa vyabhicāra abhāvaḥ na sidhyati yogyā anupalabdheḥ eva sarvatra abhāva sādhane adhikārāt tatas bahulam sahacāra mātreṇa na vyabhicārī na vyāvyabhicārī niścitaḥ iti śaṅkā avakāśaḥ 
RKNĀ_108.25	 yadi evam adṛṣṭa vyabhicārāt api dhūmāt anumānam mā bhūt na īdṛśasya śaṅkā avakāśasya sarvatra tad utpatti rahite sambhavāt iti atha kadācid pratipattā pravṛttaḥ vyabhicāram paśyati na tarhi yatra bhūyas darśanam tatra niyata tva sthitiḥ tatra kutas dhūme pratibandha siddhiḥ bhūyas darśanasya anyatra niyata tva upasthāpaka tva kṣatau malina pauruṣa tvena sarva tra anāśvāsāt 
RKNĀ_108.30	 yadi evam dvi candra ādau cakṣuḥ ādi pratyakṣam malina pauruṣam upalabdham iti ghaṭa ādikam api na upasthāpayet iti ced na indriya viṣaya kāryam hi pratyakṣam na dvi candra ādi jñānam īdṛśam artha kārya tva abhāvāt tatas bhinna lakṣaṇasya pratyakṣa ābhā sattve api ghaṭa jñānam pratyakṣam eva na ca eva dhūma ādau pārthiva tva ādau ca vyāpti grāhakasya bhūyas darśanasya lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ yena ekatra āśvāsaḥ syāt 
RKNĀ_109.4	 ete eva artha kāryatva akārya tve lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ iti ced na ghaṭa ādi jñānasya hi artha kārya tva vivāde pramāṇa antarataḥ artha kriyā lābhataḥ vā niścayaḥ na pratijñā mātreṇa na ca atra dhūmasya agni sahacāraḥ sadātanaḥ ayam atha suhṛd dvayasya iva sātyayaḥ gṛhītaḥ iti saṃśaye sadātana sahacāra prasādhaka pramāṇa antara saṅgatiḥ asti tat kāryam vā kiñcid upalabhyate tarhi bādhyamāna tva abādhyamāna tva lakṣaṇaḥ lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ bhaviṣyati iti api na vaktavyam avyabhicāra grahākasya bhūyas darśanasya bādhita tva asiddheḥ abādha mātram hi prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ apramāṇam pramāṇa antara saṅgatiḥ artha kriyā lābhaḥ vā prayudāsaḥ ca asiddhaḥ iti na tāvat prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ na api dvitīyaḥ niyata tva abhāve api pārthiva tva ādau bhūyas darśana sambhavāt iti na bhūyas darśana gamyā vyāptiḥ 
RKNĀ_109.13^1	 trilocana codye api brūmaḥ yadi pratyakṣam sva lakṣaṇa viṣayam iti ayoga vyavacchedena ucyate tadā siddha sādhanam anya yoga vyavacchedaḥ tu asiddhaḥ pratyakṣa anumāna ādi sarva jñānānām grāhya avaseya bhedena viṣaya dvaividhya anatikramāt yat dhi yatra jñāne pratibhāsate tat grāhyam yatra tu tat pravarte tat adhyavaseyam tatra pratyakṣasya sva lakṣaṇam grāhyam adhyavaseyam tu sāmānyam atad rūpa parāvṛtta sva lakṣaṇa mātra ātmakam anumānasya tu viparyayaḥ tatas ca sāṃvyavahārika pramāṇa apekṣayā rūpa rasa gandha sparśa samudāya ātmakasya ghaṭasya rūpa bheda mātra grahaṇe api pratyakṣatas samudāya siddhi vyavasthā 
RKNĀ_109.13^2	 tathā ekasya atad rūpa parāvṛttasya grahaṇe api sādhya sādhana sāmānyayoḥ atad rūpa parāvṛtta vastu mātra ātmanoḥ ayoga vyavacchedena viṣaya bhūtayoḥ vyāpti grahaḥ yuktaḥ eva atas eva vikalpānām avastu eva viṣayaḥ vastu tu teṣām parokṣam eva iti api durjñānam sarva vikalpānām adhyavaseya apekṣayā vastu viṣaya tvāt śāstre api tathā eva pratipādanāt na ca manasā tad jātīyānām vyāpti grahaḥ śakyaḥ manasaḥ bahis asvātantryāt anyathā andha badhiḥ ādya bhāva prasaṅgāt na ca vahni vyabhicāre dhūmaḥ upādhi rahitam sambandham atikrāmet iti vaktum ucitam sva kapola kalpita svābhāvika sambandhasya yācita kamaṇḍana tvāt iti 
RKNĀ_109.27^1	 yat api vācaspati jalpitam yaḥ yatra upādhinā niyataḥ tatra tasya svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ yathā dahane dhūmasya tad upādheḥ dṛśyasya anupalabhyamāna tvāt kvacid vyabhicārasya adarśanāt iti atra idam vicāryate yasya adarśanataḥ svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ vavasthāpanīyaḥ sa khalu dhūma svarūpāt artha antaram upādhiḥ vaktavyaḥ yathā dahanāt indhanam artha antaram ca kiñcid dṛśyam adṛśyam ca kiñcid na tu sarvam eva dṛśyatā niyatam tatas ca dhūmasya api hutāśane syāt upādhiḥ na ca upalabhyate iti upādhi mātra anupalabdhiḥ anaikāntikī 
RKNĀ_109.27^2	 tat katham adarśana mātrāt na asti eva upādhiḥ yatas svābhāvika sambandha siddhiḥ syāt dṛśya upadhyabhāva sādhane tu siddha sādhanam parama dṛśya upādhi śaṅkā sambhave svābhāvika tva pratirodhaḥ tad au sthaḥ eva kvacid vyabhicāra adarśanāt iti asambaddham eva upādhi vat vyabhicārasya api adarśana mātrāt abhāva asiddheḥ vyabhicārasya sarva deśa kālayoḥ sambhave api sarvadā sarvatra sarveṇa sāmagrya bhāvāt api niścetum aśakya tvāt brāhmaṇī ādi vyabhicāra vat eva āhatyā darśane api deśa kāla antare tad darśanasya niṣeddham aśakya tvāt 
RKNĀ_110.7	 nanu yadi dhūmasya apekṣaṇīyam artha antaram upādhiḥ syāt katham dhūmaḥ iti eva pāvaka sattā niyamaḥ iti ced nanu idam eva cintyate kim dhūme sati avaśyam agniḥ sambhavī na vā iti kadācid artha antaram upādhim apekṣya dhūmaḥ api syāt na agniḥ iti kim atra niṣṭabdham kāraṇam tasmāt pāvaka para adhīna udayaḥ dhūmaḥ pariniṣṭhitaḥ katham tad abhāve bhāvam svīkuryāt iti eva sādhu 
RKNĀ_110.12^1	 atha vyaktau jātau vā vahni vyabhicāraḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ katham tatra śaṅkyate iti ced tat kim sthāṇu vyaktau jātau vā puruṣa tvam dṛṣṭam yena sthāṇau śaṅkyate anyatra ūrdhva tā āliṅgite dṛṣṭam iti ced iha api anyatra bhūyas sahacāriṇi pārthiva tva ādau dṛṣṭaḥ eva vyabhicāraḥ yatra eva tu yat saṃśayate tatra eva tasya darśanam apekṣyate iti alaukikam yadi dhūma vyaktau vyabhicāraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tadā dhūma sāmānyam vyāptau bahis bhūtam eva katham saṃśayaḥ atha jātau dṛṣṭaḥ tadā api vyabhicāra niścayaḥ eva katham saṃśayaḥ atas dhūma jātau adṛśyamānaḥ api vyabhicāraḥ upādhiḥ vā darśana ayogya tayā niṣeddhum aśakyaḥ iti saṃśayaḥ durvāra prasaraḥ 
RKNĀ_110.12^2	 sa ca idānīm upādheḥ vyabhicārasya vā saṃśayaḥ svābhāvika tva saṃśaya svabhāvaḥ svābhāvika tva niścayam tāvat avaśyam pratibadhnāti tasmāt svābhāvika tva niścaya pratibandhaḥ eva arthataḥ niścayam antareṇa gamakasya svayam akiñcitkara tvāt tat evam upādhi anupalabdhiḥ vyabhicārasya anupalabdhiḥ vā anaikāntikī na tayoḥ abhāvam sādhayati yatas sambandhasya svābhāvika tva siddhiḥ syāt asiddhā ca iyam upādhi anupalabdhiḥ yathā dahanaḥ na indhanena vinā dhūmena sambadhyate tathā dhūmaḥ api na vinā agninā sambadhyate iti samānam upādhi tvam indhanasya ubhayatra 
RKNĀ_110.26	 atha siddhasya agneḥ indhana sāhityena dhūma lābhaḥ iti upādhi vyavasthā asiddhasya tu dhūmasya tad nimitta ātma lābha tayā avyabhicārāt svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ iti vyavasthāpyate iti ced evam api sā eva tad utpattiḥ āyātāḥ sā eva svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ na punar pratijñā asiddhaḥ sahacāra mātra ātmakaḥ kim ca svābhāvika tvāt avyabhicāraḥ sarvatra sarvatra avyabhicārāt ca svābhāvika tvam atītaretara āśraya tvam anivāryam yasya tu sakṛt tad utpatti pratītiḥ eva sarvatra avyabhicāra pratītiḥ tasya na ayam prasaṅgaḥ 
RKNĀ_110.32	 yadi evam mama api bhūyas darśanāt avyabhicāra siddhiḥ iti ced na bhūyas iti apariniṣṭhita vāra saṃkhya tvāt kiyatā darśanena lakṣaṇa anusārī nirvṛtim āsādayet asmākam tu pratyakṣa anupalabdhau parigaṇita saṃkhyau eva yat āhuḥ prāk adṛṣṭau kramāt paśyan vā iti hetu phala sthitim dṛṣṭau vā kramaśas apaśyan anyathā tu anavasthitiḥ iti 
RKNĀ_111.4	 yat tu anupalabhyamānasya api kalpanā anupapatteḥ iti vilapitam tat bālasya api asāmpratam anupalabhyamāne arthe ca kalpanā avakāśāt na hi dṛśyamānaḥ ghaṭaḥ kalpitaḥ ucyate na ca sandihyamānaḥ upādhiḥ sambandhasya svābhāvika tvam pratibadhnāti iti yuktam sādhaka bādhaka abhāvaḥ eva saṃśayasya nyāya prāpta tvāt atas eva na sarvatra śaṅkā piśāca avakāśaḥ tat katham na ayam pravarteta 
RKNĀ_111.9	 pramāṇa viṣaye api śaṅkā kartum śakyate iti ced na svīkṛta pramāṇasya hi niścaya phala tvāt pramāṇasya avipratipanna pramāṇa viṣaye niścaya svīkāranā antarīyakaḥ eva tad svīkāraḥ na ca śaṅkā iti eva na pravṛttiḥ artha saṃśayena api pravṛtteḥ anivārya tvāt snigdha anna pāna upayoga vat tad upayoge kadācid maraṇa darśane api koṭiśas jīvita darśanāt na ca prāmāṇika lokayātrā kṣatiḥ prāmāṇikaiḥ eva pramāṇa abhāve saṃśayasya vihita tvāt yathādarśanam āśaṅkanīyam ityādi api siddha sādhanam anyatra dṛṣṭasya eva upādheḥ vyabhicārasya vā śaṅkita tvāt kim ca bādhakā darśane api sādhaka abhāvāt api śaṅkā syāt eva 
RKNĀ_111.17	 yat api syāt etat iti valgitam tat api niḥsāram pramāṇa siddhe hi rūpe sva abhāva avalambanam na tu svabhāva avalambanena eva vastu svarūpa vyavasthā tat yadi niyata viṣaya anvaya vyatireka grāhaka pratyakṣa anupalambha pramāṇa siddhe hetu phala bhāve svabhāva vādaḥ tat kim āyātam svābhāvika sambandhe yatra tad utpatti sāmagrīm hṛdayena dūrīkṛtya anyatas sahacarita dvayāt viśeṣeṇa pratītau pratyupāyaḥ eva davīyān tad sāmagrya pakṣaṇe ca tad utpattiḥ eva sā kim āhopuruṣikayā nāma antara karaṇena kena punar pramāṇena eṣa svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ gṛhyate ityādiḥ tad grahaṇa prakāraḥ pūrvam eva nirākṛtaḥ tathā svābhāvika tva asiddhau svabhāvataḥ ca pratibaddhāḥ hetavaḥ ityādi upasaṃhāraḥ api manorājya mātram tasmāt artha antare gamye kārya hetuḥ tad bhāva siddhiḥ ca pratyakṣa anupalambhāt iti sthitam tat evam svābhāvika vādena hṛdaya anulepanam aśucin eva parihāryam dūratas iti 
RKNĀ_112.3–112.10	 namaḥ tārāyai yad yogāt andha vat viśvam saṃsāre bhramat iṣyate sā kṛpā vaśagaiḥ pāpā sthira siddhiḥ apāsyate iha pare sakala padārtha sthairya prasādhana artham pratyakṣam anumānam arthāpattim  pramāṇāni ācakṣate tathā hi saḥ eva ayam ghaṭa sphaṭika ādiḥ iti pratyabhijñā ākhyam pratyakṣam udīyamānam sthairyam utthāpayati na ca idam apramāṇam abhidhātavyam aprāmāṇyam hi bhavat aprāmāṇya kāraṇa upapattyā vā bhavet prāmāṇya lakṣaṇa virahāt vā yadi ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ kim aprāmāṇya kāraṇam mithyātvam ajñānam saṃśayaḥ vā na tāvat atra mithyātvam mithyātvam hi tad viṣaye bādhaka pratyayāt vā hetu ukta doṣataḥ vā sambhāvyeta 
RKNĀ_112.11	 na tāvat bādha gandhaḥ api sambhavati deśa kāla nara antareṣu api asambhavāt na ca anavagatā api bādhā kadācid api bhaviṣyati iti śaṅkā yuktimatī nirbīja śaṅkā anupapatteḥ avaśayam śaṅkayā bhāvyam niyāmakam apaśyatām iti datta avakāśā saṃśaya piśācī labdha prasarāḥ na kvacid na asti iti na ayam kvacid pravarteta antatas snigdha anna pāna upayoge api maraṇa darśanena sarvatra śaṅkā nivṛtteḥ tasmāt prāmāṇika lokayātrām anupālayatā yathā darśanam eva śaṅkanīyam na adṛṣṭa pūrvam api 
RKNĀ_112.18–112.24	 yat uktam kārikāyām na āśaṅkā niṣpramāṇikāḥ iti bṛhaṭṭīkāyām api utprekṣeta hi yaḥ mohāt ajñātam api bādhakam sa sarva vyavahāreṣu saṃśaya ātmā kṣayam vrajet iti kṣaṇa bhaṅga sādhanam bādhakam asya iti ced na anumānasya paramparayā api pratyakṣa pūrva tvāt pratyakṣam pradhānam prādhānyāt ca anumānasya bādhakam na tu anumānam asya pratyakṣa antaram tu bādhakam bhavati yathā sarpa ādi pratyayasya rajju ādi pratyakṣam tat ca atra na sambhavati 
RKNĀ_112.28–113.3	 nanu pratyakṣe api bādhake kasmāt na bhavati paraspara pratibhandhena dvayoḥ api apratyakṣatā na artha kriyā samartha vastu viṣaya aviṣaya tvena samāna tva abhāvāt ekasya pratyakṣa ābhāsa tvāt iti na sat viṣaya tva bādhaka pratyayāt mithyātvam na api hetu ukta doṣataḥ deśa kāla nara antareṣu avisaṃvādāt na api ajñānam aprāmāṇya kāraṇam atra asti pratyabhijñāna saṃvedana sambhavāt na ca saṃśayaḥ na hi tat eva idam syāt vā na vā iti sphaṭika ādiṣu udayati matiḥ kim tu tat eva idam sphaṭika ādikam iti nirastāḥ vibhrama āśaṅkā tat na aprāmāṇya kāraṇa upapattyā pratyabhijñānasya aprāmāṇyam 
RKNĀ_113.5	 na api lakṣaṇa kṣayāt yat eva hi utpannam asandigdham aduṣṭa kāraṇa janyam deśa kāla nara antareṣu abādhitam ca tat eva pramāṇam iti naḥ siddhāntaḥ tat uktam tasmāt dṛḍham yat utpannam na visaṃvādam ṛcchati jñāna antareṇa vijñānam tat pramāṇam pratīyatām tathā bṛhaṭṭīkā api tatra apūrva artha vijñānam niścitam bādha varjitam aduṣṭa kāraṇa ārabdham pramāṇam loka sammatam iti etat ca lakṣaṇam ukta nyāyena pratyabhijñāne api sambhavati iti pramāṇam eva idam 
RKNĀ_113.14–113.16	 nanu idam ekam eva na bhavati kāraṇa bhedāt viṣaya bhedāt svabhāva virodhāt ca tathā hi saḥ iti saṃskāra kāryam ayam iti ca indriya kāryam na ca kāraṇa bhede api kārya abhedaḥ viśva vaicitryā hetuka tva prasaṅgāt tathā sati api sphaṭikaḥ sphaṭikaḥ iti vyapadeśa abhede pūrva deśa kāla sambandha apara deśa kāla sambandhābhyām viruddha dharmābhyām yogāt sphaṭikaḥ pūrva apara kālayoḥ bhidyate iti viṣaya bhedaḥ vaktavyaḥ 
RKNĀ_113.18–113.20	 tathā saḥ iti parokṣam ayam iti sākṣātkāraḥ na ca anayoḥ svabhāva viruddhayoḥ dahana tu hinayoḥ iva śakyā śakreṇa api ekatā āpādayitum trailokasya aikya prasaṅgāt na ca asya prāmāṇyam vikalpa tvena avastu nirbhāsi tvāt smārtāt aviśeṣāt ca tasmāt pratyabhijñā ekatvam sthāpayati bhāvānām iti manoratha mātram 
RKNĀ_113.23–113.23a	 atra ucyate ekam eva idam pratyabhijñānam samākhyātam yadi api indriyam kevalam asamartham yadi api saṃskāra mātram saṃskāra sadhrīcīnam tu indriyam bhāvayiṣyati pratyabhijñām tad bhāva abhāva anuvidhānāt pratyabhijñā abhāva abhāvayoḥ na hi na ajījanat bīja mātram aṅkuram iti mṛd ādi sahitam api na janayati 
RKNĀ_113.26–113.30	 atha bhavatu deśa kālayoḥ tad saṃsargayoḥ vā paraspara nānā tvam na tad avacchinnasya padmarāgasya tasya tābhyām tad saṃsargābhyām ca anya tvāt tatas anya tve tad saṃsargayoḥ kutas tadīya tvam iti ced svabhāvāt eva iti saṃsarga parīkṣāyām nipuṇataram upapādayiṣyate na ca svabhāva virodhaḥ anumānasya api aneka tva prasaṅgāt tat api hi pratyakṣam apratyakṣam ca avikalpaḥ vikalpaḥ ca asamāropaḥ samāropaḥ ca 
RKNĀ_113.32	 sva anubhava avasthāpita abhedasya svarūpa tad grāhya bheda apekṣayā pratyakṣa ādīnām avirodhaḥ iti ced na iha api sāmyāt na khalu etat api vijñānam tat tedanta adhikaraṇam ekam ābhyām anuraktam sphaṭikam gocarayat abhinnam na anubhūyate na avasīyate vā eka tve api ca vastunaḥ tad anurañjaka tattet antā bheda apekṣayā pratyakṣatā aparokṣate na virotsyete saha sambhavāt vijñāna eka tvasya ca pramāṇa siddha tvāt 
RKNĀ_114.3	 na ca saḥ iti pūrva deśa kāla saṃsargaḥ ayam iti ca sannihita deśa kāla saṃsargaḥ ekasya virudhyate yatas yuktam yat padmarāgasya svarūpe paricchidyamāne tad abhāvaḥ vyavacchidyate iti tat avyavacchede tad svarūpa aparicchedāt sva pracyuti vyavacchedya svabhāva tvāt padmarāga bhāvasya tad anavacchede tad pariccheda anupapatteḥ 
RKNĀ_114.8	 kasmāt punar tad anye puṣparāga ādayaḥ vyavacchidyante tad abhāva avinā bhāvāt iti ced saḥ eva kutas pratyakṣeṇa kadācid api puṣparāga padmarāgayoḥ tādātmya anupalambhāt iti ced yatra tarhi tatas tādātmya pratītiḥ tatra tad avinābhāvaḥ samasti ca saḥ ayam padmarāgaḥ iti deśa kalā avasthā anugatam ekam padmarāgam avabhāsayantī sākṣātkāravatī pratītiḥ 
RKNĀ_114.12–114.15	 na vikalpa rūpa tayā asyāḥ aprāmāṇyam abhilāpa saṃsarga pratibhāsa tva prāmāṇyayoḥ avirodhāt na ca idam smārtam adeśa kāla avasthāvataḥ asya deśa kāla avasthā anugata tvena ādhikyāt iti atha keśa kuśa kadalī stamba ādau sati api bhede pratyabhijñānam utpannam iti ced utpadyatām kaḥ doṣaḥ kim anena pratipāditam bhavati kim pratyabhijñāyāḥ sādhāraṇa anaikāntika tvam atha śabda sāmyāt ubhayoḥ api aprāmāṇyam uta saṃśaya āpādana mātram 
RKNĀ_114.18–114.21	 prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ anabhyupagamāt eva nirastaḥ na hi iyam anumāna tvena upanyastā anumāna tve api abādhita tvāt iti viśeṣaṇe na doṣaḥ iti pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ na api dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ dṛṣṭānta mātrataḥ sādhya siddheḥ ayogāt keśoṇḍuka ādi viṣayasya cakṣuḥ vijñānasya api aprāmāṇye ghaṭa ādi pratyakṣasya aprāmāṇya prasaṅgāt saṃśaya mātram tu vyavahāra ucchedaka tvāt na aśraṇīyam eva iti pratipāditam iti na tṛtīyaḥ api pakṣaḥ 
RKNĀ_114.23	 kim ca keśa ādau yadi pratyabhijñā vyabhicāriṇī kārya kāraṇa pratītiḥ kim na vyabhicāriṇī yā vyavicāriṇī sā kārya kāraṇa pratītiḥ eva na bhavati iti ced yadi evam yā visaṃvādinī sā pratyabhijñā eva na bhavati tad ābhāsa tvāt iti samānam pratyabhijñānasya ca sati prāmāṇye anumāna ādiṣu anantarbhāve pratyakṣā eva saṃskāra sahāya indriya anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāyi tvāt ca sat saṃprayoge sati indriyāṇām bhāvāt ca tat iyam pratyabhijñā aneka deśa kāla avasthā sambaddham ekam sphaṭika ādikam gocarayantī sthairyam vyavasthāpayati 
RKNĀ_114.30	 tathā anumānataḥ api sthira tā siddhiḥ prayogaḥ vivāda adhyāsitaḥ saḥ eva ayam sphaṭikaḥ ityādi pratyabhijñā pratyayaḥ yathārthaḥ abādhita pratyaya tvāt yāvān abādhita pratyayaḥ sa sarvaḥ yathārthaḥ upalabdhaḥ yathā sva saṃvedana pratyayaḥ abādhitaḥ ca ayam tasmāt tathā iti abādhitan ca para udbhāvita kṣaṇika tva sādhana bādhaka uddhārān niśceyam 
RKNĀ_115.1	 atha aparaḥ prayogaḥ vivāda adhyāsitāḥ bhāvāḥ pūrva apara kālayoḥ eka svabhāvāḥ abādhita pratyabhijñayā pratyabhijñāyamāna tvāt yat yat abādhita pratyabhijñayā pratyabhijñāyate tat sarvam abhinnam yathā yaḥ tvayā dṛṣṭaḥ nīlaḥ arthaḥ saḥ eva mayā dṛṣtaḥ iti nīlaḥ arthaḥ pratyabhijñāyate tathā ca ete bhāvāḥ tasmāt tathā iti pūrvam pratyayasya dharmitā adhunā bhāvānām iti viśeṣaḥ 
RKNĀ_115.6–115.9	 kim ca sa hetuka tvāt vināśasya sthairyam siddham prayogaḥ vivāda āspadībhūtāḥ bhāvāḥ yathāsvam vināśa hetu sannidheḥ prāk na vināśinaḥ sa hetuka vināśa tvāt yat yat hetukam tat tad asannidhau na bhavati yathā vahni ādi abhāve dhūma ādiḥ sa hetuka vināśāḥ ca aṃī bhāvāḥ tasmāt tathā iti sa hetuka vināśa tvam ca ghaṭasya agni dhūmayoḥ iva pratyakṣa anupalambhataḥ mudgara vināśayoḥ api kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhau siddham na ca vināśa hetoḥ asāmarthya vaiyarthya abhidhānam ucitam aṅkura ādi hetoḥ api tathā tva prasaṅgāt śakyam hi vaktum arthasya bhaviṣṇu tāyām asamarthaḥ janma hetuḥ bhaviṣṇu tāyām vyarthaḥ iti 
RKNĀ_115.13–115.17	 api ca akṣaṇikāḥ santaḥ kāraṇavat tvāt yat kāraṇa vat tat akṣaṇikam yathā bhāva vināśaḥ kāraṇavantaḥ ca ime santaḥ tasmāt akṣaṇikāḥ iti kāraṇavat tvasya sādhya viparyaye vṛtti śaṅkā vināśasya sa hetuka tvam eva nivartayati iti prasiddha vyāptikāt kāraṇavat tvāt akṣaṇika tva siddhiḥ iti tathā śaṅkaraḥ sthira siddhau prāha na utpatti anantara vināśī bhāvaḥ prameya tvāt vastu vyāvṛtti vat iti 
RKNĀ_115.18–115.22	 avidyamāna vipakṣa tvāt anvayi eva hetuḥ prameya tvasya kṣaṇika tvena virodha abhāvāt sandigdha vyatireki tvam iti ced na khalu kṣaṇika tve kasyacid prameya tvam sidhyati kṣaṇa sthiti dharmaṇaḥ pramāṇa kāle apātāt atītasya ca prameya tve ati prasaṅgāt iti evam eva prayogam upastuvan trilocanaḥ api āha akṣaṇikāḥ sarva bhāvāḥ prameya tvāt yat pramīyate tat akṣaṇikam yathā bhāva vināśaḥ prameyāḥ ca sarva bhāvāḥ tasmāt akṣaṇikāḥ iti 
RKNĀ_115.25–116.1	 asiddhaḥ dṛṣṭānta dharmī iti ced na sva kāraṇa kalāpāt utpattimataḥ bhāvasya antareṇa nivṛtti prasavam sarvadā avasthāna prasaṅgāt tadā eva bhāvaḥ asti na pūrvam na paścāt iti api śabdaḥ kṣaṇika paryāya tvena iṣyamāṇaḥ kṣaṇāt ūrdhvam sattā viccheda upajananam antareṇa na arthavān devaiḥ api śakyaḥ parikalpayitum vināśa kāla apekṣayā hi kṣaṇaḥ alpīyān kālaḥ tena saḥ asya asti iti kṣaṇikaḥ vaktavyaḥ itarathāḥ janma vināśayoḥ ekasmin kāle bhavatoḥ tulya hetuka tvena ekatva prasaṅgaḥ eka tve tu dvayoḥ ekataraḥ prahātavyaḥ tatra janma prahāṇe bhāvāḥ niḥsvabhāvāḥ prasajyeran nivṛtti pratiyāge ca janminaḥ bhāvāḥ nityāḥ iti durnivāraḥ prasaṅgaḥ tat siddhaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ nanu prameya tva kṣaṇika tvayoḥ virodha asiddheḥ sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttikam prameya tvam iti ced 
RKNĀ_116.2	 na etat asti yasmāt artham kiñcid prāpayat pratyakṣam tena pratyāsanna tvāt prāpayati pratyāsattiḥ ca tad utpattiḥ eva avakalpate na tādātmyam sa ākāra nirākāra vādayoḥ aprakṛta tvāt anyatra nirākṛta tvāt ca sā ca niyata vastu pratibhāsā ākṣiptā kārya kāraṇa bhāva lakṣaṇā pratyāsattiḥ tulya kālam pramāṇa prameyayoḥ anupapannāḥ sevya itara viṣāṇayoḥ iva tatas pramāṇam artha sattām bodhayat tad adhīna utpāda tayā bodhayati kāraṇa bhāva mātra anubandhi tvāt ca tasya pūrva kāla sattyā bhavitavyam atas pūrva kāla sattvena vyāptam prameya tvam pūrva kāla sattvam ca kṣaṇika tve anupapannam iti vyāpaka anupalabdhyā vipakṣāt kṣaṇika tvāt vyāvartamānam prameya tvam akṣaṇika tvena vyāpyate iti asandigdhaḥ vyatirekaḥ 
RKNĀ_116.10–116.11	 tat evam anumāna pramāṇa siddhaḥ akṣaṇikaḥ iti evam arthāpattiḥ api asya sādhikā tathā hi kārya kāraṇa bhāva grahaṇam krama yaugapadya grahaṇam smaraṇam abhilāṣaḥ svayaṃnihita pratyanumārgaṇam dṛṣṭa artha kutūhala viramaṇam karma phala sambandhaḥ saṃśaya pūrvaka nirṇayaḥ bandha mokṣaḥ mokṣa prayatnaḥ śubha ādike karmaṇi pravṛttiḥ pratyabhijñā kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ upādāna upādeya bhāva prabhṛtayaḥ sthira sattām antareṇa anupapadyamānāḥ sthairyam sādhayanti pratikṣaṇam bhede sati anubhavituḥ vinaṣṭa tve anyasya kārya kāraṇa bhāva grahaṇa ādi anupapatteḥ iti katham kṣaṇa bhaṅga śaṅkā api 
RKNĀ_116.17–116.18	 atra abhidhīyate apramāṇam eva ayam pratyabhijñā ākhyaḥ vikalpaḥ mithyātvam ca sat viṣaya tva bādhaka pratyayāt nanu asya bādhakam pratyakṣam asambhavi anumānam ca asamartham āveditam iti ced nanu asya pratyabhijñānasya sva artha avinābhāva dārḍhye pratyakṣa sahasreṇa api kim saṃvāda śaithilye tu bādhaka pratyakṣa vat anumānam api prāpta avakāśam pramāṇasya eva siddhi bādhyoḥ adhikārāt tathā hi māyākāraḥ śirasi nimajjitam golakam āsyena niḥsārayati iti pratyabhijñā śirasi cchidra prasaṅga saṅgatena anumānena bādhyamānā pratītā eva bādhyamānā na pratyabhijñā iti prastute api astu 
RKNĀ_116.23–1	 yathā avanata ākāśa pratibhāsaḥ sarva saṃpratipattau api bādhyaḥ eva tadvat eka tā grahaḥ sarva saṃpratipattau api bādhyaḥ astu tasmāt asyāḥ pratyakṣatā kīrtanam yācita ka maṇḍana mātram atrāṇam katham atas sthairya sthitiḥ astu tatas ca anumāna tvam api asyāḥ dhvastam ukta krameṇa ābādhita tva viśeṣaṇa viruddha bādhyamāna tāyāḥ prasādhanāt iti viśeṣaṇa asiddhaḥ hetuḥ yadā api kṣaṇa bhaṅga sādhakam bādhakam na ucyate asyāḥ tadā api iyam apramāṇam eva lūna punar jāta keśa ādau vyabhicāra upalambhāt nanu uktam yā vyabhicāriṇī sā na pratyabhijñā ityādi 
RKNĀ_116.30	 yuktam etat yadi kārya kāraṇa bhāva pratīti vat lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ pratipādayitum śakyeta yathā hi anvaya vyatireka grahaṇa pravaṇa pratyakṣa anupalambhāt upapannaḥ niścayaḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāva pratītiḥ anyaḥ tad ābhāsa pratītiḥ iti anayoḥ lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ tathā yadi pratyabhijñe api lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ darśitaḥ syāt darśayitum vā śakyaḥ vyabhicāra avi abhicāra upayogī tadā bhavatu pratyabhijñā tad ābhāsayoḥ vivekaḥ na tu evam asti sarvatra atyanta sadṛśe vastuni pṛthagjana pratyabhijñāyāḥ eka rasa tvāt 
RKNĀ_117.3–117.6	 saṃvāditvā saṃvādi tve lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ iti ced na aliṅgasya hi vikalpasya saṃvādaḥ nāma pramāṇa antara saṅgatiḥ atha kriyā prāptiḥ vā tatra na tāvat ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ paścāt api saḥ eva ayam iti svatantra eka adhyavasāya mātrāt aparasya pramāṇa gandhasya api abhāvāt na api dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ saṅgacchate na hi pūrva apara kālayoḥ eka vastu pratibaddhā siddhā kācid artha kriyā bhinnena api tad samāna śaktinā tādṛś artha kriyāyāḥ karaṇa avirodhāt tathā hi yathā ekaḥ ghaṭaḥ vāri dhārayati iti tad kāla bhāvinaḥ api anyasya deśa antara vartinaḥ na vāri dhāraṇa vāraṇam tathā dvitīya ādi kṣaṇaḥ api anyaḥ yadi vāri dhārayati kīdṛśaḥ doṣaḥ syāt visadṛśa kriyāyām tu cintā eva na asti tat katham pratyabhijñānasya saṃvāda sambhavaḥ 
RKNĀ_117.12–117.15	 nanu yadi ekam pratyabhijñānam visaṃvādi dṛṣṭam iti sarvam eva pratyabhijñānam visaṃvādi śaṃkyate tadā ekam indriya jñānam keśoṇḍuka dvi candra ādau visaṃvādi upalabdham iti ghaṭa ādiṣu api sarvam eva pratyakṣam visaṃvādi sambhāvyatām indriya janya tvasya eka lakṣaṇasya sarvatra sambhavāt iti ced na tatra api lakṣaṇa bhedasya sadbhāvāt tathā hi bahis artha sthitau indriya artha kārya tayā sākṣāt artha ākāra anukāri tvam pratyakṣa tvam tat ca abhyāsa viśeṣa āsādita paṭimnā pratyakṣeṇa niścīyate kvacid tu artha kriyā prāpti jñānāt iti pratyakṣa tvam anavadyam eva dvi candra ādau tu artha vinākṛtena timira ādi vipluta cakṣuḥ mātreṇa tat jñānam janitam iti pratyakṣa ābhāsam eva dvi candra ādi artha abhāvaḥ tu deśa kāla nara antaraiḥ dvi candra ādeḥ arthasya bādhita tvāt avyāhate iti pratyakṣa ābhāsa pariihāre api pratyakṣeṣu kaḥ āśvāsa virodhaḥ 
RKNĀ_117.21–117.26	 pratyabhijñāne api sarvam idam asti iti na yuktam yathā hi pūrvam pāvaka ādau pāka ādi kriyā pratibaddhā siddhā paścāt anubhūyamānāḥ dahana jñānasya saṃvādam āvedayati anyathā bāhya artha ucchedāt nirīham jagat jāyate na tathā prathama carama kālayoḥ ekībhāva pratibaddhā kācid artha kriyā upalabdhi gocarā pūrva apara kālayoḥ eka tvam antareṇa vā pravṛtti ādi kṣatiḥ yena ekatā avagrahaḥ api saṃvādī syāt tat iyam anumāna bādhita tvāt vyabhicāra śaṅkā kalaṅkita tvāt ca na pratyakṣam anumānam vā iti katham atas sthairya siddhiḥ anumāna pratihatiḥ vā 
RKNĀ_117.28	 yat punar vācaspatiḥ uvāca saṃskāra indriyayoḥ militayoḥ eva pratyabhijñānam prati kāraṇa tvam iti tat ayuktam bhinna sāmagrī prasūta tvāt anayoḥ jñānayoḥ tathā hi nimīlite cakṣuṣi saḥ iti atra indriya vinākṛtasya eva saṃskārasya sāmarthyam upalabdham prathama darśane tu ayam iti atra saṃskāra rahitasya eva indriyasya sāmarthyam dṛṣṭam tasmāt sāmagrī dvaya pratibaddham jñāna dvayam idam avadhāritam katham ubhābhyām militvā ekam eva pratyabhijñānam utpāditam iti udghuṣyate bīja kṣiti ādyoḥ tu pṛthak sāmarthyam na dṛṣṭam iti ekā eva sāmagri iti aṅkuraḥ api ekaḥ eva astu 
RKNĀ_118.3	 tathā pūrva deśa kāla apara deśa kālābhyām tad sambaddhābhyām anya tvāt padmarāgasya abhedaḥ iti api asaṅgatam viruddhayoḥ dharmayoḥ padmarāgāt anya tve api viruddha dharma yogāt padmarāgasya bhedaḥ katham apahnūyate trailoka ekatva prasaṅgasya durvāra tvāt na hi dharma dharmiṇoḥ anya tve api brāhmaṇa tva caṇḍāla tve eka ādhāre bhavitum arhate iti padmarāgasya bhedaḥ duratikramaḥ 
RKNĀ_118.7	 tathā ca na svabhāva virodhaḥ anumānasya api aneka tva prasaṅgāt tat api pratyakṣam apratyakṣam ca avikalpaḥ vikalpaḥ ca asamāropaḥ samāropaḥ ca iti api ayuktam anumānasya hi paramārthataḥ sva saṃvedana pratyakṣa ātmanaḥ avikalpasya asamāropa svabhāvasya aparti akṣa tva vikalpa tva samāropa tva ādeḥ para apekṣayā prajñaptatvāt viruddha dharma adhyāsa abhāvāt katham bheda siddhiḥ saḥ eva ayam iti tu pratyabhijñānasya saḥ iti aspaṣṭa ākāra yogi tvam ayam iti spaṣṭa ākāra yogi tvam iti viruddha dharma dvayam bhedakam 
RKNĀ_118.13	 na ca evam vaktavyam tad tedanta apekṣayā pratyabhijñānasya api ekasya eva pārokṣyā pāra ukṣyam aviruddham iti na hi idam eka ākāratayā vyavasthitam yena anumāna vat asya api pārokṣya apārokṣya vyavasthā mātram syāt yāvat atīta artha ākāra anukāraḥ vartamāna artha anukāraḥ ca svadharmaḥ na bhavati tāvat tad artha gocara tā eva na asti kutas pārokṣyā pārokṣya vyavahāraḥ bhaviṣyati tasmāt spaṣṭa aspaṣṭa ākāra dvaya viruddha dharma adhyāsāt pratyabhijñānam pratyaya dvayam etat iti sthitam 
RKNĀ_118.19	 tathā sa hetuka vināśa tvāt ayam api asiddhaḥ hetuḥ yat punar atra uktam sa hetuka vināśa tvam ghaṭasya agni dhūmayoḥ iva pratyakṣa anupalambhataḥ mudgra ghaṭa vināśayoḥ api kārya kāraṇa bhāva siddhau siddham iti tat asaṅgatam agni dhūmayoḥ api dṛśya tvāt pratyakṣa anupalambhataḥ dhūmasya vahni kārya tā sidhyatu vināśa śabda vācyaḥ tu arthaḥ na kaścid idantayā dṛṣṭaḥ karparam eva ghaṭa mudgarābhyām utpadyamānam upalabdham 
RKNĀ_118.23	 yat āhuḥ guravaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ tāvat ayam ghaṭaḥ atra ca patan dṛṣṭaḥ tathā mudgaraḥ dṛṣṭā karpara saṃhatiḥ paramatas nāśaḥ na dṛṣṭaḥ paraḥ tena abhāvaḥ iti śrutiḥ kva nihitā kim vā atra tad kāraṇam svādhīnā palighasya kevalam iyam dṛṣṭā kapāla āvaliḥ tat ayam abhāvaḥ dṛśya anupalabdhi bādhitaḥ katham pratyakṣatas mudgara ādi kāryam avadhāryaḥ 
RKNĀ_118.29–119.1	 yat punar asmin adṛśyamāne api dṛśyate iti bāgjālam sā bhaṇḍa vidyā tad vacanāt gṛhṇan api paśuḥ eva tatha hi kasyacid pratibhāsena sādhyate apratibhāsi yat pratibhāsaḥ asya na asya iti na upapatteḥ tu gocaraḥ iti atha evam vaktavyam kim anyena dhvaṃsena karparam eva ghaṭa dhvaṃsaḥ astu tathā ca sati mudgara ādi abhāve karpara abhāvāt ghaṭa sthairyam avyāhatam iti 
RKNĀ_119.2	 durāśā khalu eṣā tathā hi yathā nāśa śabdena karparam ucyate tathā yadi abhāva śabdena api karparam eva ucyate tadā ekatra pradeśe ghaṭam ekam apanīya ghaṭa antara nyāse tatra apanīta ghaṭasya abhāva vyavahāraḥ na syāt tad pradhvaṃsa kapālayoḥ tatra anutpādāt tasmāt yathā apanīta ghaṭasya pracyuti mātra apekṣayā nyasta ghaṭe abhāva vyavahāraḥ tathā mudgara ādi kāraṇa abhāvāt pradhvaṃsa karparayoḥ anupāde api pracyuti mātra apekṣayā eva pratikṣaṇam anya anyatva vyavahāraḥ ghaṭasya sidhyati iti kutas sthairya siddhiḥ tasmāt pradhvaṃsa karpara abhāve api pracyuti mātra ātmaka bhāva apekṣayā api asmad matam avyāhatam 
RKNĀ_119.9–119.16	 yat āhuḥ guravaḥ āstām karparapaṃktiḥ eva kalaśa dhvaṃsaḥ na ca iyam purā tena sthairyam api prasidhyatu tatas bhinnena nāśena kim atra uttaram nāsaḥ sā eva yathā ucyate yadi tathā abhāvaḥ api kumbha antara nyāse abhāva vacaḥ katham matam atas sidhyati abhāve api naḥ iti nanu yadi sva hetu janitaḥ nāśaḥ na asti katham kvacid eva deśe kāle ghaṭaḥ naṣṭaḥ iti pratīti niyamaḥ na ca mudgarāt anyaḥ nāśasya hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ prāk api nāśa sambhave naṣṭa ghaṭa buddhi sambhava prasaṅgāt yat āhuḥ nāśaḥ na asti yadi sva hetu niyataḥ kim desa kāle kvacid kumbhaḥ naṣtaḥ iti pratīti niyamaḥ tena asti kāryaḥ ca saḥ na api anayat kila kāraṇam rayavataḥ daṇḍāt purā api anyathā nāśa utthāna kṛtā vinaṣṭa ghaṭa dhīḥ kena uddhurā vāryate iti ced 
RKNĀ_119.23–119.26	 tarhi idānīm arthāpattyā pradhvaṃsam prasādhya mudgara adhīna tvam asya sādhayitum ārabdham tathā ca sati dhūma agni vat pratyakṣatas pradhvaṃsasya mudgara ādi kārya tvam siddham iti utphulla gallam ullapitam vyāluptam na ca arthāpattitaḥ api tad siddhiḥ sampadyate ghaṭaḥ naṣṭaḥ iti pratīteḥ anyathā api upapadyamāna tvāt vināśam vinā api hi ghaṭa darśanavataḥ mudgara kṛta kapāla anubhavaḥ eva naṣṭa ghaṭa āvasāya sādhanaḥ kim apareṇa nāśena kartavyam ghaṭaḥ naṣṭaḥ iti buddheḥ ghaṭa niścaya pūrvaka mudgara kṛta kapāla anubhava mātra anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna darśanāt 
RKNĀ_119.29–119.31	 na ca iyam sāmagrī pūrvam api asti mudgara abhāve karparapaṃkteḥ eva abhāvāt katham prāk api naṣṭa ghaṭa buddhi prasaṅgaḥ saṅgataḥ nāma yat āhuḥ guravaḥ dṛṣte ambhaḥ bhṛti mudgara ādi janitām dṛṣtvā kapāla āvalīm saṅketa anugamāt vinaṣṭa ghaṭa dhīḥ tāvat samutpādyate sāmagryām iha nāśa nāma na kim api aṅgam na ca asyām api syāt eṣā na kadāpi na api ca purā api eṣā samagrā sthitiḥ arthāpattiḥ atas gatā kṣayam iyam na dhvaṃsa siddhau prabhuḥ iti 
RKNĀ_120.4–120.9	 yadi nāśa anubhavaḥ na asti kapāla anubhavāt kapāla kalpanā eva syāt na naṣṭa ghaṭa buddhiḥ iti ced tat etat ati sāhasam ghaṭa niścaya pūrvaka kapāla valaya darśanāt eva naṣṭa ghaṭa buddheḥ sākṣāt eva anubhūyamāna tvāt tad apalāpe dhūma ādīnām api dahana ādi pūrvakatva niścayaḥ na syāt iti atiprasaṅgaḥ nanu ghaṭaḥ naṣṭaḥ iti buddhiḥ viśeṣya buddhiḥ sā ca vināśam viśeṣaṇam ākṣipati iti ced tat asat yatas sva buddhyā rajyate yena viśeṣyam tat viśeṣaṇam ucyate na ca avidyamānam adṛśyam vā sva buddhyā kiñcid rañjyati 
RKNĀ_120.11	 prayogaḥ atra yasya na svarūpa nirbhāsaḥ tat na kasyacid sva anurakta pratīti nimittam yathā karikeśaraḥ na asti ca svarūpa nirbhāsaḥ dhvaṃsasya iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ na asyāḥ asiddhiḥ abhāvasya sva rūpeṇa evedantayā nirbhāsa abhāvāt na ca viruddha tā sa pakṣe bhāvāt na api anaikāntika tvam pratibhāsa abhāve api sva anurakta pratīti hetu tve śaśaviṣāṇa ādeḥ api tathātvam syāt iti atiprasaṅgaḥ 
RKNĀ_120.17–120.22a	 nanu na dhvaṃsena vinā vinaśyati jagat bhāvena sārdham sa ced sat ca asat ca kim astu vastu niyatam bhāva anujaḥ asau tatas bhāvāt tena tu bhinna kāraṇa tayā tad kāraṇā sambhave abhāvāt tena kṛtānyatā api galitāḥ bhaṅgaḥ kotaḥ anukṣaṇam atra ucyate kāraṇa antarāt utpadyamānaḥ dhvaṃsaḥ abhinnaḥ bhinnaḥ vā na ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ bhinna kāraṇa tvāt taiḥ anabhyupagata tvāt ca atha dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā kaḥ punar bhāvasya pradveṣaḥ yena pradhvaṃsa ākhye vastuni sva hetoḥ utpanne nivartate nāma 
RKNĀ_120.25	 yat punar etat ucyate na abhāvasya utpāde bhāvasya parā nivṛttiḥ kim tu abhāva utpattiḥ eva tad nivṛttiḥ iti katham anyasya utpāde anyasya nivṛttiḥ atra svabhāva bhedaiḥ uttaram vācyam ye paraspara parihāra sthitayaḥ sva hetubhyaḥ jāyante na hi svatas anyasya aṅkurasya vahniḥ na kāraṇam iti anya tva aviśeṣāt bhasmanaḥ api na kāraṇam svabhāva bhedena tu kārya kāraṇa bhāva samarthanam paraspara parihāra sthiti niyame api tulyam yathā ca utpādasya purastāt akhila sāmarthya rahitasya aṅkura prāgabhāvasya apakāram kiñcid akurvantaḥ api bīja ādayaḥ aṅkuram ārabhamāṇāḥ prāgabhāvam nivartayanti tad utpādasya eva tad prāgabhāva nivṛtti rūpa tvāt evam tad abhāva hetavaḥ api bhāva rūpe akiñcitkarāḥ api tad abhāvam ādadhānāḥ tat nivartayanti abhāva utpādasya eva bhāva nivṛtti rūpa tvāt tena pūrvavat na artha kriyā karaṇa prasaṅgaḥ iti 
RKNĀ_121.2–121.6	 tat ucitam syāt yadi kārya kāraṇayoḥ eva asya api ātmā pramāṇa pratītaḥ syāt kevalam dṛśya anupalambha graste api etasmin upalabhyate iti pralāpaḥ vyaktam iyam bhaṇḍa vidyā iti uktam arthāpattiḥ api kṣīṇa iti api prāgabhāvasya ca dṛṣṭānta tvena upanyāsaḥ bhaṇḍālekhya nyāyaḥ kiñ ca kaḥ punar atra virodhaḥ saha sthāna abhāvaḥ yadi tava virodhaḥ artha vipadoḥ saha sthāna āsaṅgaḥ kṣaṇam api yathā śīta śikhinoḥ sa ca dhvaṃsaḥ dhvaṃsa antaram upanayan saṃprati bhavet virodhī saḥ api anyam kṣayam iti na nāśaḥ katham api 
RKNĀ_121.11–121.17	 anyathā siddha sattā mātreṇa virodhi tve sarvam sarveṇa viruddham prasajyeta svabhāva ālambhanam api adarśanāt eva nirastam iti atha anyonya abhāva prakṛti katayā arthe sati tadā kṣayasya eva abhāvaḥ saha bhavatu vā hetu balataḥ anena dhvaṃse ca prakṛta hatiḥ asya tu anudaye balīyān eva arthaḥ svayam apacaye anyena kim iha sat ca asat ca kim astu vastu iti tu prasaṅgaḥ trilocana prastāve nirākaraṇīyaḥ atas eva atra prastāve bhuvana eka gurūn bhagavataḥ kīrti pādān avamanyamānaḥ śaṅkaraḥ paśoḥ api paśuḥ iti kṛpā pātram eva eṣa jālmaḥ 
RKNĀ_121.20	 yat api āha trilocanaḥ bhāva vyatiriktām nivṛttim anicchadbhiḥ aśakyā svarūpa nivṛttiḥ avasthāpayitum yā hi tasya prāktanī kācid avasthā bhavadbhiḥ artha kriyā nirvartana yogyā dṛṣṭā sā eva yadi uttara kālam api anuvartate tarhi sva rūpeṇa eva nivṛttaḥ bhāvaḥ katham avasthāpyate tadānīm ayam naṣṭaḥ nāma yadi sva hetu pratilabdha svarūpa vyatirekinī tasya kācid avasthā utpādyata utpattau sā eva tasya ātmā antaram jātam iti atādavasthyam eva asya vināśam brūmaḥ tādavasthya tādātmye ca svarūpeṇa nivṛttaḥ bhāvaḥ iti asya śabdasya satyam artham na vidmaḥ 
RKNĀ_121.26–122.1	 svarūpa nivṛttiḥ khalu iyam bhavantī bhāvaḥ eva syāt bhāvāt anyā vā tattve sva kāraṇebhyaḥ niṣpannasya arthasya anyathā anupapattau utpatteḥ ārabhya sattvāt nitya tvam prasajyeta anya tve ca tat eva nivṛtteḥ anya tva nirvṛtiḥ iti priyam anuṣṭhitam priyeṇa tasmāt utsṛjya vibhramam nāśa utpattiḥ eva naṣṭa tvam abhyupagantavyam iti tat etat ajñāna phalam tathā hi sva kāraṇāt eva yathā anya deśa vicchinna rūpaḥ samudeti bhāvaḥ vicchinna bhinna kṣaṇa vṛttiḥ evam sva kāraṇāt eva na jāyate kim abhāvataḥ artha antara rūpa bādhe tatra api abhāva antaram īkṣaṇīyam pradīpa dṛṣṭānta matam na kāntam svarūpa sandarśana viprayogāt 
RKNĀ_122.6	 yathā hi deśa antara parāvṛttam anīla ādi parāvṛttam ca sva hetoḥ utpannam vastu tathā dvitīya kṣaṇātara parāvṛttam api yathā ca anya deśān avasthāyi tvam tad deśa avasthāyi tvena aviruddham viruddham ca deśa antara avasthāyi tvena eva tathā dvitīya kṣaṇān avasthāyi tvam prathama kṣaṇa avasthāyi tvena aviruddham viruddham punar dvitīya kṣaṇa avasthāyi tvena eva kevalam deśa antara dvitī ya kṣaṇayoḥ tad pracyuti mātram vyavahriyate tat anyonya abhāva pradhvaṃsa abhāvayoḥ padārthayoḥ sadbhāve api avāryam abhāva antara asvīkāre api bhāva abhāvayoḥ api amiśratvā asu īkāre tādātmya prasaṅgāt tasmāt abhāva abhāvayoḥ tādātmyam iti 
RKNĀ_122.16	 yathā artha kriyā kāri tvasya tad deśa varti tva nīla tva ādi bhinna virodhaḥ tathā dvitīya kṣaṇān avasthāyi tvena api iti vivakṣitam paramārthataḥ tu dharmi dharmayoḥ tādātmyam vyāvṛtti kṛtaḥ bheda vyavahāraḥ iti apoha siddhau prasādhitam etat ca ukta krameṇa aviruddham āpāditam eva avati tu tattve vāc chala mātra pravṛttāḥ dveṣa viṣa jvalita ātmānaḥ kṣudrāḥ pralapanti iti kim atra brūmaḥ 
RKNĀ_122.21–122.24	 tatas ca vyatirikta nivṛtti utpattim antareṇa svarūpa nivṛtteḥ upapatteḥ katham kṣaṇāt ūrdhvam prāktana satta avasthitiḥ tasmāt utsṛṣṭa vibhramam naṣṭa vyavahāra mātram astu na tu asya anyat kiñcid jāyeta bhāvasya tādavarthya prasaṅgāt abhāvaḥ katham niṣidhyate iti ced na tad anutpatti mātra viṣayasya vācā niścayena ca paścāt abhāva vyavahāra mātra pravartanasya iṣṭa tvāt vastu utpatteḥ eva niṣiddha tvāt 
RKNĀ_122.26–122.29	 nanu kā iyam vācoyuktiḥ abhāva vyavahāra mātram iṣyate paścāt na abhāvaḥ iti evam sati visaṃvāditā prasaṅgaḥ abhāva vyavahārasya abhāvaḥ ca mithyā iti bhāvaḥ eva pratiṣeddhavyaḥ syāt sa ca abhāvaḥ paścāt bhavati iti sphuṭataram asya kādācid ka tvam ātma hetuka tvam vastu tvam ca iti asat etat abhāva ākhya vastu antara asvīkāre api pracyuti mātra apekṣayā api vyavahārasya caritārtha tva pratipādanāt yat tu tad vivikta bhū tala ādeḥ viṣaya tvam āśaṅkya uktam na bhū tala ādeḥ vastu antara tvāt na ca vastu antare pratipādite pratīte vā ghaṭa ādi vastu bhūtam iti pratipāditam vā bhavati 
RKNĀ_123.1	 evam vastu antaram eva nāśaḥ iti asmin mate yat dūṣaṇam uktam tat svayam eva parihṛtam syāt iti tat api asambaddham kevalam hi bhū talam asya viṣayaḥ iti katham na ghaṭa ādeḥ abhūta tva bodhaḥ yā eva hi ghaṭa ādi apekṣayā kaivalya avasthā pradeśasya saḥ eva ghaṭa virahaḥ vacana āt inā api evam kevala pradeśa pratipādane katham iva na prakṛta ghaṭa ādi abhāva pratipādanam kaivalyam ca asahāya praseśāt avyatibhinnam eva 
RKNĀ_123.6–123.13	 na ca iha ghaṭaḥ na asti iti pratyayasya ghaṭavatī api pradeśe prasaṅgaḥ sva hetoḥ tathā utpannasya sa ghaṭa pradeśasya kevala pradeśāt anya tvāt na ca pratyabhijñānataḥ sa ghaṭā ghaṭa pradeśayoḥ eka tvam pūrvam asya nirākaraṇāt na ca vināśa hetoḥ asāmarthya vaiyarthya abhidhāne aṅkura ādi hetoḥ api tathā abhidhātum ucitam asiddhe hi kārye hetoḥ āśrayaṇam avāryam siddhe ca iyam cintā yadi hetoḥ nityaḥ anityaḥ vā arthaḥ jātaḥ kim nāśa kāraṇena iti hetu puraskāreṇa eva pravṛtteḥ na ca evam asiddhe aṅkura ādau kārye śakyam abhidhātum svarūpasya eva abhāvāt tad dharmaka tvā dharmaka tva ādi paryanuyogasya nirviṣaya tvāt nanu tvayā api bhāva abhāvayoḥ lakṣaṇa bhedaḥ abhihitaḥ tat katham eka tvam sarva arthānām lakṣaṇa bhedāt eva bheda vyavasthā tatas api ced na bheda vyavasthitiḥ na kasyacid kutaścid bheda vyavasthitiḥ iti advaita prasaṅgaḥ iti ced 
RKNĀ_123.15	 na yaḥ hi naśvara svabhāvaḥ saḥ eva nāśaḥ naśyati iti bahula adhikārāt kartari ghañaḥ prasādhanāt tam nāśam bhāva svabhāvam icchāmaḥ naśanam nāśaḥ iti prasajya ātmā dvidhā kartavyaḥ tattvataḥ tāvat vastu tva virahāt tattva anya tva virahitaḥ eva asau bhāvaḥ na bhavati iti tad bhāva niṣedha mātram āyātam tu bhavati kharaśṛṅga ādi vat saṃvṛtau tu yathā kāla bhedena vikalpyamānaḥ kādācid kaḥ iva pratibhāti tathā sarva upākhyā viraha rūpa tayā bhāvāt bhinnaḥ iva pratibhāti iti na avastu tva upalakṣaṇa bheda ākhyāna virodhaḥ evam ca sati saṃvṛttyā lakṣaṇa bhede bhāva abhāvayoḥ bhedasya iṣṭa tvāt tattvena ca lakṣaṇa eka tā virahe bhāvasya tena aikya niṣedhāt katham advaita prasaṅga upālambhaḥ 
RKNĀ_123.24–123.25	 syāt etat na ca viveka apratītau tad vivikta grahaṇam bhavati tad vivekaḥ ca na bhū tala ādi svarūpam eva viśeṣaṇa tvāt iti tat etat nyāya bahiṣkṛtam viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ hi saṅkalpa ārūḍhe rūpe bāhya artha sparśe vikalpa śabda liṅga antarāṇām vaiyarthya prasaṅgāt iti śāstre vistareṇa pratipādanāt sa ca saṅkalpaḥ abhinnam api bhāvam bhinnam iva akalayati yathā śilāputrakasya śarīram śarīre karaṇa ādayaḥ lamba karṇaḥ devadattaḥ ityādi tasmāt kalpanā adhīnaḥ viśeṣaṇa viśeṣya bhāvaḥ abhinne api bhāve bheda vivakṣa apekṣaḥ bheda vyavahāraḥ katham bheda niyatam ātmānam ātanotu 
RKNĀ_123.31–123.31a	 skhalat gatiḥ ayam rāhoḥ śiraḥ iti ādinirdeśaḥ itit ced yadi satyam etat tadā śiraḥ atiriktasya rāhoḥ iva kṣmā tala ādeḥ atiriktasya vivektasya dṛśya anupalambha bādhita tvāt ayam api nirdeśaḥ skhalat gatiḥ eva tathā api na iti koṣa pānam pramāṇam tasmāt sa ghaṭāt pradeśa antarāt pradeśaḥ eva ayam anyaḥ ghaṭa viviktaḥ sva hetoḥ utpannaḥ na tu ghaṭa vivekena viśeṣitaḥ sva hetoḥ utpannasya viviktasya abhāve vivekasya abhāvāt 
RKNĀ_124.3–124.10	 kim ca vyāptam bhidā yadi viśeṣya viśeṣaṇa tvam bheda atyayāt nanu tadā tad abhāvaḥ eva deśaḥ viśiṣṭaḥ iti na asti yathā tathā idam api asti dṛśya mata bheda dṛś asti na iti tasmāt na abhāvaḥ nāma kaścid yatra kāraṇa vyāpāraḥ tat evam sa hetuka vināśa tvāt iti hetuḥ svarūpa asiddhaḥ iti sthitam satām akṣaṇika tvam kāraṇavat tvāt iti api asambaddham eva kṣaṇika tva kāraṇavat tvayoḥ virodha abhāvāt akṣaṇika tvena kāraṇavat tvasya vyāpteḥ asiddheḥ sandigdha vyatireka tvāt na ca asya viparyaye vṛtti śaṅkā nāśasya sa hetuka tvam eva nivartayati ukta krameṇa nāśasya eva abhāvāt iti 
RKNĀ_124.14	 tathā prameya tvāt api sthira siddhiḥ manoratha mātram sa ākāra vedanā udaya pakṣa sthitau hi dvitīya kṣaṇa anuvṛttau api arthasya vyavahita tvāt prakāśa anupapatteḥ viṣaya svarūpa vedanam eva jñānasya viṣaya vedanam evam ca vartamāna anurodhaḥ atīte api tad pratyāsatteḥ apracyuteḥ na ca atiprasaṅgaḥ anantara atītāt anyena kṣaṇena sārūpya asamarpaṇāt tatas ca kāraṇa tvāt yadi nāma prameya tvasya pūrva kāla sattvena vyāptiḥ tathā api prameya tva vat pūrva kāla sattvam api kṣaṇike aviruddham iti prameya tva akṣaṇika tvayoḥ vyāpti sādhanaḥ vyāpaka anupalambhaḥ asiddhaḥ jñāna ākāra arpaka tvam hi hetu tvam prameya tvam prāmāṇika pratītam tat ca anantarā atītaḥ eva kṣaṇe samupapadyate 
RKNĀ_124.22–124.22a	 jñāna sattā samaye artha anuvṛtteḥ abhāvāt nirviṣayata iti ced nanu ananuvṛttau api tad arpita ākāra svarūpa saṃvedanam eva tad vedanam tat eva ca sa viṣaya tvam iyam ca pratyāsattiḥ anantara atīte api kṣaṇe akṣīna iti na dvitīya kṣaṇa anuvṛtteḥ anurodhaḥ iti uktam atas sandigdha vyatireki tvāt anaikāntikam eva prameya tvam 
RKNĀ_124.26–124.29	 atha sa ākāra vāda vidveṣāt anākāra jñāna grāhya tvam prameya tvam abhipretam tadā asiddha tā asya hetoḥ indriya artha sannikarṣa ādeḥ jñānam utpadyatām nāma tat ca anubhava eka rasa tvena sarvatra arthe sadṛśa ākāra tvāt kasya grāhakam astu yena abhisambaddham iti ced ātama manaḥ saṃyoga ādīnām api grahaṇam syāt janakasya grahaṇam iti ced 
RKNĀ_124.29a–124.31	 tathā api ātma ādīnām grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ viṣaya tvena janakasya grahaṇam iti api asādhu viṣaya tvasya adya api aniścayāt idam dṛṣṭam śrutam vedam iti adhyavasāyaḥ yatra arthe sa viṣayaḥ iti ced nanu asti eva pratiniyataḥ vyavahāraḥ kaḥ punar atra pratyāsatti niyamaḥ iti pṛcchāmaḥ sa ced upavarṇayitum na śakyate vyavahāraḥ api tvad mate niyataḥ na syāt iti brūmaḥ 
RKNĀ_124.33–125.1	 asti tāvat iti ced atas eva artha sārūpyam asādhāraṇam pratyāsatti nimittam astu nirnimitte niyama ayogāt nanu sārūpyam api artha adarśane katham avadhāryate tat ca kim eka deśena sarva ātmanā vā ādye pakṣe sarvam sarvasya vedanam syāt dvitīye tu jñānam ajñāna tām vrajet kim ca sārūpyāt artha vedane anantaram jñānam tulya viṣayam viśayaḥ syāt iti ced 
RKNĀ_125.4–125.7	 mā bhūt arthasya darśanam ākāra viśeṣa balāt adhyavasita arthasya artha kriyā prāpteḥ eva arthaḥ api īdṛśaḥ iti sārūpya vyavahāraḥ aviruddhaḥ atas eva sthūla gatam paramāṇu gatam vā sārūpyam na cintyate jñāna ākārasya sthūla tve api eka sāmagrī pratibaddha puñja viśeṣāt api abhīṣṭa kriyā karaṇāt puruṣa artha siddheḥ sārūpyam ca eka deśena eva na ca atra sarva vedana prasaṅgaḥ sarveṣām jñānam prati ajanaka tvāt janakānām ca sva vyapadeśa nimitta asādhāraṇa eka deśa arpaka tvena grāhya tvāt 
RKNĀ_125.9–125.14	 na api tulya viṣaya anantara jñāna grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ tasya sva saṃvedanāt eva pramāṇāt siddha tvāt pramāṇa antarasya tatra vaiyarthyāt jaḍa tve sati ākāra arpakasya vastunaḥ grāhya tvāt iti asya arthasya abhīṣṭa tvāt ca bāhya artha sthitau ca iyam cintā iti sarvam anavadyam tat evam ayam prameya tvāt iti hetuḥ sa ākāra vāda pakṣe sandigdha vyatirekaḥ nirākāra pakṣe ca asiddhaḥ iti sthitam na ca arthāpattiḥ api sthira ātma sādhanī kārya kāraṇa bhāva grahaṇa ādīnām anyathā upapatteḥ 
RKNĀ_125.15	 tathā hi upādāna upādheya bhāva sthita citta santatim api āśritya iyam vyavasthā susthā iti katham ātmānam pratyujjīvayatu tatra kārya kāraṇa bhāva pratītiḥ tāvat anākulāḥ tathā api prāc bhāvi vastu niścaya jñānasya upādeya bhūtena tad arpita saṃskāra garbheṇa paścāt bhāvivaḥ tu jñānena asmin sati idam bhavati iti niścayaḥ janyate tathā prāk bhāvivastu apekṣayā kevala bhū tala niścayaka jñāna upādeya bhūtena tad arpita saṃskāra garbheṇa paścāt bhāvivaḥ tu apekṣayā kevala bhū tala niścāyaka jñānena asmin asatī idam na bhavati iti vyatireka niścayaḥ janyate yathā uktam eka avasāya samantara jātam anya vijñānam anvaya vimarśam upādadhāti evam tad eka viraha anubhava udbhavāni avyāvṛtti dhīḥ prathayati vyatireka buddhim 
RKNĀ_125.26	 atas eva devadattena agnau pratīte yajñadattena ca dhūme pratīte na kārya kāraṇa bhāva grahaṇam tad jñānayoḥ upādāna upādeya bhāva abhāvāt yatra tu eka santāne jñāna kṣaṇayoḥ upādāna upādeya bhāvaḥ tatra kārya ādi grahaḥ sugrahaḥ anyathā sati api nitya ātmani pratisandhātari kārya kāraṇa bhāva ādīnām apratītiḥ eva syāt 
RKNĀ_125.30–126.2	 tathā hi ātmanaḥ sakāśāt pratisandheya buddhīnām abhedaḥ bhedaḥ vā bheda abhedaḥ vā prathama pakṣe ātmā eva syāt pratisandhātā buddhayaḥ eva vā syuḥ pratisandheyāḥ iti kaḥ pratisandha arthaḥ bheda pakṣe api buddhibhyaḥ bhidyamānasya jaḍasya ātmanaḥ kaḥ pratisandhāna arthaḥ iti na vidmaḥ buddhi yogāt draṣṭṛ tva vat pratisandhātṛ tvam iti ced buddhiḥ eva tarhi draṣṭrī pratisandhātrī ca iti niyama svīkāre tad yogāt asya tathātvam iti kim anena yācita kamaṇḍanena buddhīnām kartṛ tva abhāvāt iti ced 
RKNĀ_126.2a	 tad dvāreṇa api tarhi tasya ātmanaḥ draṣṭṛ tva ādi vyavahāra anupapattiḥ yadi hi buddhiḥ hetoḥ phalasya vā draṣṭṛī syāt tad ānantarya pratiniyamasya ca anusandhātrī kalpitā tad yogāt draṣṭṛ tvam pratisandhātṛ tvam ca ucyate iti syāt api prativiṣayam alabdha viśeṣāyām ca buddhau sambandhaḥ api na viśeṣam vyavahārayitum īśaḥ adhunā nibandhana adhigantā adhunā phalasya idānīm pratisandhātā iti tathā api ca buddhi yuta viśeṣa svīkāre tu kim apareṇa ātmanā kartavyam tāvatā eva paryāpta tvāt vyavahārasya 
RKNĀ_126.9–126.9a	 sthira ātmānam antareṇa sā eva buddhiḥ na syāt iti ced kena evam pratāritaḥ asi aho moha māhātmyam yat īdṛśān api para vaśīkaroti tathā hi na idam idam antareṇa yat ucyate tat khalu anyatra pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām sāmarthya avadhāraṇe sati yujyate vahneḥ iva dhūme cakṣuḥ ādi vat vā dṛṣṭa kāraṇa antara sāmagyā kārya adarśane paścāt darśane ca kiñcid anyat apekṣaṇīyam asti iti sāmānya ākāreṇa 
RKNĀ_126.14	 ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ tāvat na asti iti vyaktam dvitīyaḥ api na sambhavī na hi kāraṇa buddhi samanantaram kārya buddhau satyām niścaya pravṛttasya idam asya anantaram dṛṣṭam mayā iti pratisandhānam adṛṣṭa pūrvam kadācid yatas anyasya sāmarthya parikalpanam syāt iti udasya vyāmoham ukta krameṇa eva kārykāraṇa grahaṇa vyavasthā svīkartavyā 
RKNĀ_126.18–126.20	 bheda abheda pakṣaḥ tu dhakkāraḥ eva tasya eva tad apekṣayā bheda abheda viruddha dharma adhyāsāt ekatva anupapatteḥ tatas ca yat bhinnam bhinnam eva abhinnm ca abhinnam iti na ekasya bheda abhedau tathapi abheda viśvam ekam iti yugapad utpāda sthiti pralaya prasaṅgaḥ evam krami vaḥ tu grāhakaiḥ krami jñānaiḥ upādāna upādeya bhūtaiḥ sākṣāt pāramparyeṇa krameṇa amī jāyante iti niścayaḥ janyate eka kālika aneka vastu grāhakaiḥ eva tad jñānaiḥ eka upādāna tvāt sakṛt imāni jātāni iti vikalpaḥ kriyate iti krama ākrama grahaṇam api anavadyam 
RKNĀ_126.24–126.29	 katham aneka jñānāt eka vikalpaḥ iti ced kaḥ doṣaḥ bhavantu bhinnāḥ matayaḥ tathā api tāḥ dadhati upādāna tayā eka kalpanam na bhinna saṃkhyā phala hetu bādhanī na ca anya santāna bhavāḥ iva akṣamāḥ yat api uktam śaṅkareṇa atha pūrva uttara kṣaṇayoḥ saṃvittī tābhyām vāsanā tayā hetu phala bhāva adhyavasāyī vikalpaḥ iti ced 
RKNĀ_126.30–126.32	 tat kim idānīm yat kiñcid āśaṅkitena vaktavyam iti evam vidhiḥ anuṣṭhīyate bhavatā vikalpaḥ hi agṛhīta anusandhānam atad rūpa samāropaḥ vā syāt na tāvat pūrvaḥ pakṣaḥ adṛṣṭa anvaya vyatirekasya puruṣasya hetu phala bhāva agrahe anusandhāna pratyaya hetoḥ vāsanā viśeṣasya eva anupapatteḥ agṛhītasya ca anusandhāne ati prasaṅgāt iti 
RKNĀ_127.1	 tat etat na samyak ālocitam yatas hetu phala bhūtayoḥ pūrva uttara kṣaṇayoḥ ekaikena jñānena ananubhave a pi upādāna upādheya bhūtābhyām krami jñānābhyām hetu phala tve gṛhīte eva kevalam hetu kāle phala abhāvāt tad viṣaya sāmarthya grahaṇe api phala adarśanāt tad avasāyaḥ eva apravṛttaḥ kārya darśanena pravartyate tathā phala avalokane api tad kāryatā gṛhītā eva vikalpena anusandhīyate iti gṛhīta anusandhāna rūpaḥ eva ayam vikalpaḥ iti yat kiñcid etat 
RKNĀ_127.7–127.10	 yat āha mahābhāṣya alaṅkāraḥ yadi nāma ekam adhyakṣam na pūrva apara vittimat adhyakṣa dvaya sadbhāve prāc parāvedanam katham iti tathā smaraṇam abhilāṣaḥ svayaṃnihita pratyanumārgaṇam dṛṣṭa artha kutūhala viramaṇam karma phala sambandhaḥ saṃśaya pūrvaka nirṇayaḥ ca pūrva pūrva artha anubhavaiḥ upādāna kāraṇaiḥ samarpita saṃskāra garbhaiḥ uttara uttara artha anubhavaiḥ eva upādeya bhūtaiḥ janyamānaḥ yujyate iti kim adhikena ātmānā parikalpitena 
RKNĀ_127.13–127.17	 upādāna upādeya bhāva niyamāt eva ca na santāna antare smaraṇa ādi prasaṅgaḥ saṅgataḥ kim idam upādānam iti ced ucyate yat santāna nivṛttyā yat utpadyate tat tasya upādāna kāraṇam yathā mṛd santāna nivṛttya utpadyamānasya kumbhasya mṛd upādānam iti śāstre prapañcitam na ca atra para loka kṣatiḥ yat api uktam citta śarīrayoḥ kiyat kāla sthiti nibandhanasya dṛṣṭasya nivṛttau cittasya api nivṛtti prasaṅgaḥ maraṇa vedanayā hi cittam vikalam tatas avikalā citta antara janana avasthā na sambhavati tasmāt upasthite maraṇa duḥkhe sarva saṃskāra virodhini cittam api ucchidyeta iti nāstikyam āyātam iti 
RKNĀ_127.20–127.23	 tat ayuktam yatas maraṇa duḥkham citta viśeṣaḥ eva tasya citta antara janana sāmarthya svabhāvasya svabhāvāt avārya eva jñāna utpattiḥ iti bandhāt mokṣaḥ api saṃsāri citta prabandhāt anāśrava citta prabandhaḥ yaḥ śubha ādi mokṣayoḥ api pravṛttiḥ avāryāḥ yatas sati api ātmani aham eva muktaḥ bhaviṣyāmi sukhī ca iti ātma graha lakṣaṇāt adhyavasāyāt pravartate na punar ātmanā gala hastitaḥ sa ca anādya vidyā paramparā āyātaḥ pūrva aparayoḥ ekatva āropakaḥ mithyā saṅkalpaḥ bādhite api ātmani avyāhata prasaraḥ iti katham apravṛttiḥ 
RKNĀ_127.26–na	 nanu nairātmya vāda pakṣe  pūrvam eva avabudhyate mad vināśāt phalam na syāt mattaḥ anyasya athavā bhavet iti apravṛttiḥ eva astu iti ced astu kaḥ doṣaḥ yadi ayam ātma grahaḥ nirviṣayaḥ api pravṛttim anākṣipya kṣaṇam api sthātum  prabhavati yathā hi jātasya avaśyam mṛtyuḥ iti jātavataḥ api apratikriya putra ādi maraṇe sa uraḥ tāḍam ākrandaḥ maraṇa ādau ca yatnaḥ śoka udrekāt evam avidyā udrekāt eva nairātmyam jānan api pravartate na sukham āste iti kim atra kriyatām avidyāyāḥ pravartana śakteḥ avārya tvāt 
RKNĀ_128.3–121.8	 pratyabhijñā ca pūrvam eva dhvastā kārya kāraṇa bhāva niyatā paścāt bhā vi pūrva bhāvitāḥ sā ca kṣaṇike api aviruddhāḥ upādāna upādeya tā ca krami sva saṃvedana jñāna dvayena sākṣātkṛta tad pṛṣṭha bhāvinā niścīyate iti asati api ātmani pratisandhātari kārya kāraṇa grahaṇa ādayaḥ upapadyamānāḥ na ātmānam upasthāpayitum prabhavanti atas arthāpattiḥ api na kṣamā iti bhāgya hīna manaḥ rājyam iva sthira siddhiḥ viśīryate eva tathā ca kṣaṇa bhaṅga sandehe sattva ādi anumānam prāpta avasaram 
RKNĀ_129.4–129.7	 namaḥ tārāyai diś eṣā sva para aśeṣa prativādi prasādhanī citrā dvaita matā bodha dhvānta stoma kadarthinī iha khalu sakala jaḍa padārtha rāśau pratyākhyāte nirākṛte ca nirākāra vijñāna vāde pratihate ca alīka ākāra yogini pāramārthika prakāśa mātre samyak unmūlite ca sa ākāra vijñāna alīka tva samārope pratisantānam ca svapna vat abādhita deha bhoga pratiṣṭhā ādi ākāra prakāśa mātra ātmake jagati vyavasthite yasya yadā yāvat ākāra cakra pratibhāsam yat vijñānam parisphurati tasya tadā tāvat ākāra cakra parikaritam tat vijñānam citrā dvaitam iti sthitiḥ tat evam citram advaitam vijñānam iti pada trayam iha pratyupasthitam 
RKNĀ_129.13–129.22	 atra ca vipratipattiḥ nāma kim citra tāyām advaite vijñāna tve sarvatra eva iti vikalpāḥ na tāvat asau citra svarūpa anusāriṇī bhavitum arhati tanmātrasya sarva jana anubhava siddha tvāt anyathā śaśa viṣāṇa ādau iva jaḍam idam alīkam vijñānam vā iti vipratipattīnām anavakāśa prasaṅgāt na api vijñāna tve vivādaḥ kartum ucitaḥ saha upalambha niyamāt ityādinā pūrvam eva nīla ādīnām sa ākāra vijñāna tva prasādhanāt atas eva sarvatra api vimatiḥ asaṅga tā sa ākāra vijñāna siddhau eva citrā dvaitavāda avatārāt tasmāt citratā iyam advaita virodhinī iti vyāmohāt ekatvaḥ eva vipratipatiḥ iti tatra prasādhanam sādhanam idam ucyate yat prakāśate tat ekam yathā citra ākāra cakra madhya vartī nīla ākāraḥ prakāśate ca idam gaura gāndhāra madhura surabhi sukumāra sātā itara ādi vicitra ākāra kadambakam iti svabhāva hetuḥ 
RKNĀ_129.25	 na tāvat asya asiddhiḥ abhidhātum śakyate pratyakṣa pramāṇa prasiddha sadbhāve vijñāna ātmaka nīla ādi ākāra cakre dharmiṇi prakāśam ānatāyāḥ pratyakṣa siddha tvāt na ca asya hetoḥ viruddha tā sambhavati vicitra ākāra madhya vartini nīla ākāre dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi prakāśam ānatā lakṣaṇasya sādhanasya dṛṣṭa tvāt nanu ca eka tve sādhye yat aparam eka tva adhikaraṇam tat iha dṛṣṭāntīkartum ucitam na ca asya nīla ākārasya ekatā vidyate viruddha dharma adhyāsa prasiddhasya aneka tvasya sambhavāt deśa kāla ākāra bhedaḥ hi viruddha dharma adhyāsaḥ tatas ca yathā citra tā ākāra cakrasya ākāra bhedataḥ bhedaḥ tathā nīla ākārasya api deśa bhedataḥ bhedaḥ tat ayam sādhya śūnyaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ hetuḥ ca vipakṣe paridṛśyamānaḥ yadi tatra eva niyataḥ tadā viruddhaḥ 
RKNĀ_130.8	 tatra api sambhave anaikāntaḥ iti ced atra ucyate yadi deśa bhedataḥ vijñāna ātmaka sthūla nīla ākārasya bhedaḥ tadā asya pratiparamāṇu deśa bhede bheda sambhavāt paramāṇu pracaya mātra ātmakaḥ vijñāna ātmaka sthūla nīla ākāraḥ syāt tathā ca sati sarveṣām vijñāna ātmaka nīla paramāṇūnām sva svarūpa nimagna tvena saṃtamasa nimagna aneka puruṣa vat vyativedana abhāvāt sthūla nīlā khaṇḍalaka pratibhāsā bhāva prasaṅgaḥ na ca sva svarūpa nimagna tvena api anyena anyasya vedanam yujyate yena sthūla pratibhāsaḥ saṅgataḥ syāt grāhya grāhaka lakṣaṇayoḥ purastāt apakartavya tvāt na ca evam vaktavyam paramāṇūnām sva svarūpa nimagna tve api eka upādāna tayā puñja ātmā eva sthūlaḥ sthūlam ātmanam jñāsyati iti sati api eka upādāna tve sva svarūpa nimagna tvāt eva sthūla vyavasthāpakasya bhinnasya ātmanaḥ anyonyam vā grāhyāgrāhaka bhāvasya ayogāt tādātmyena vyativedanasya ca anabhyupagamāt vargaḥ vargam vā iti 
RKNĀ_130.19–nne^1	 iti asya anupada tvāt na ca yathā bāhya artha vāde sthūla eka ākāra jñāna pratibhāsaḥ eva bāhya paramāṇu pracaya pratibhāsa vyavasthā gati antara abhāvāt tathā jñāna paramāṇu vyavasthā sthūla eka ākāra yogi vijñāna antarasya anabhyupagamāt abhyupagame vā tasya eva dṛṣṭānta tvāt tasmāt yāvat yāvat pratibhāsaḥ tāvat tāvat sthūla tayā eva vyāptaḥ asthūle paramāṇau sthūla nivṛtti mātre ca pratibhāsasya dṛśya anupalambha bādhita tvāt yathā prasiddha anumāne sattvam kṣaṇika tvena vyāptam krama ākramkāri tvena api kṣaṇika tva abhāvāt ca krama ākrama nivṛttau nivartamānam kṣaṇika tve niyatam sidhyati tathā atra api prakāśamāna tvam sādhanam eka tvena api sthaulyena api ekatva abhāvāt ca vipakṣāt paramāṇu puñja ātmanaḥ eka tva nivṛtti mātra ātmanaḥ ca sva viruddha upalambhāt sthaulyasya vyāpakasya nivṛttau nivartamānam eka tve niyatam sidhyati 
RKNĀ_nne^2	 tatas ca yathā bahis vyāpti pakṣe ghaṭe dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi viparyaya bādhaka pramāṇa balāt sattvam kṣaṇika tva niyatam avadhārya dhārya sattvāt pakṣe kṣaṇika bhaṅga siddhiḥ tathā atra api nīla ākāre dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇi viparyaya bādhaka pramāṇa balāt eva prakāśamāna tvam ekatva niyatam avagamya prakāśamāna tvāt vicitra ākāra cakra sādhya dharmiṇī ekatva siddhiḥ iti na dṛṣṭāntasya sādhya śūnya tvam na api hetoḥ viruddha tā na ca anaikāntika tā 
RKNĀ_130.33	 nanu eka tve sādhye tad pracyutiḥ dvi tvam ca vipakṣaḥ tasmāt ca vipakṣāt dhetu vyatireka pratipatti avasare kim vipakṣa ātmā prakāśate na vā pratibhāsa pakṣe prakāśamāna tvasya hetoḥ sādhāraṇa anaikāntika tā vipakṣe api dṛṣṭa tvāt atha na prakāśate tadā sandigdha vyatireki tvam kutas vyatirekaḥ iti avadheḥ eva aprakāśa māna śarīra tvāt katham atas sādhya siddhi pratyāśā 
RKNĀ_131.4	 atra ucyate iha dvividhaḥ vijñānānām viṣayaḥ grāhyaḥ adhyavaseyaḥ ca pratibhāsamānaḥ grāhyaḥ agṛhītaḥ api pravṛtti viṣayaḥ adhyavaseyaḥ tatra asarva jñe anumātari sakala vipakṣa pratibhāsā bhāvāt na grāhya tayā vipakṣaḥ viṣayaḥ vaktavyaḥ sarva anumāna uccheda prasaṅgāt sarvatra sakala vipakṣa pratibhāsā bhāvāt tatas vyatireka asiddheḥ pratibhāse ca deśa kāla svabhāva antarita sakala vipakṣa sākṣātkāre sa adhyātmā api virākaḥ sutarām pratīyate iti anumāna vaiyarthyam tasmāt apratibhāse api adhyavasāya siddhāt eva vipakṣāt dhūma ādeḥ vyatirekaḥ niścitaḥ tat kim artham atra vipakṣa pratibhāsaḥ prārthyate yadi punar asya adhyavasāyaḥ api na syāt tadā vyatirekaḥ na niścīyate iti yuktam pratiniyata viṣaya vyavahāra abhāvāt 
RKNĀ_131.13	 nanu asmin mate vastu avastu ātmaka sakala vipakṣa pratipatti sambhavāt tatas hetu vyatirekaḥ saṃpratyetum śakyataḥ eva na ca pratibhāsa mātreṇa sattva prasaṅgaḥ artha kriyā kāritva lakṣaṇa tvāt sattvasya tvad mate tu prakāśaḥ eva vastu tvam atas vipakṣayoḥ ekatva pracyuti dvi tvayoḥ pratibhāse prakāśamāna tva sādhanasya vipakṣa sādhāraṇa tā apratibhāse ca sandigdha vyatireki tvam iti ca udyam duruddharam eva iti ced tat etat asaṅgatam tathā hi dhūma ādiḥ avahni ādeḥ vipakṣāt vyāvṛttaḥ vahni ādi niyataḥ sidhyati tasya ca vastu avastu ātmaka sakala vipakṣa padārtha rāśeḥ svarūpa nirbhāsaḥ iti kim nirvikalpa jñāne kalpanāyām vā nirvikalpe ced pratibhāsaḥ iti ca kaḥ arthaḥ kim nirākāre jñāne sakala vipakṣa ādi svarūpasya sākṣāt sphuraṇam yadi vā tad arpita buddhi svabhāva bhūta sadṛśa ākāra prakāśaḥ atha samanantara pratyaya bala āyāta buddhi gata bāhya sadṛśa ākāra pratibhāsaḥ āhosvit buddheḥ ātma bhūta vipakṣa sadṛśa alīka ākāra parisphūrtiḥ 
RKNĀ_131.24–131.29	 na tāvat ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ yuktaḥ deśa kāla svabhāva viprakṛṣṭānām padārthānām arvācīne jane nirākāre ca jñāne sphuraṇa ayogāt iti asya arthasya śāstre eva vistareṇa prasādhānāt sphuraṇe vā asādhyasya api prakāśana prasaṅge anumāna vaiyarthyasya pratipādanāt na api dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ deśa ādi viprakṛṣṭa tvāt eva sākṣāt su a ākāra samarpaṇa sāmarthya abhāvāt na ca tṛtīyaḥ saṅgataḥ sādṛśya sambhave api samanantara balāt eva āyātasya bāhyena saha pratyāsatteḥ abhāvāt 
RKNĀ_131.31	 na caturthaḥ api prakāraḥ sambhavati asat prakāśayoḥ virodhāt sphurataḥ alīka tva ayogāt tathā hi asat prakāśaḥ iti kim asat īśvara ādeḥ khyātiḥ bhāsamānaḥ vā ākāraḥ asan san vā na kaścid khyāti iti vivakṣitam tatra yasya padārthasya sva rūpa parinirbhāsaḥ sa katham asan iti prāṇa dhāribhiḥ abhidhātavyaḥ sphurataḥ keśoṇḍuka ākārasya bāhya rūpa tayā bādhya tve api jñāna rūpa tayā artha tvasya ācāryeṇa pratipādita tvāt grāhaka abhimata nirākāra prakāśasya api asattva abhidhāna prasaṅgāt 
RKNĀ_132.3–132.19^1	 pratibhāse api bādhanāt asatya tvam iti ced kim tat bādhakam pratyakṣam anumānam vā yadi ekatra svarūpa sākṣāt kāriṇi pratyakṣe aviśvāsaḥ katham anyatra bādhake svarūpa antara prakāśa eva nirvṛttiḥ tad pūrvakam anumānam ca sutarām aviśvāsa bhājanam iti na bādhaka vārtā api yat āhuḥ guravaḥ yasya svarūpa nirbhāsaḥ tat eva āsāt katham bhavet bādhātas yadi sā api ekā pratyakṣa anumayoḥ nanu pratyakṣe yadi aviśvāsaḥ ekatra anyatra kā gatiḥ tat pūrvam anumānam ca katham āśvāsa gocaraḥ iti 
RKNĀ_132.3–132.19^2	 nanu dṛṣṭam eva dvi candra ādi pratibhāse api bādhitam na dṛṣṭe anupapanna tvam tat jñātam api bādhyate iti ced na bādhyasya apratibhāsanāt pratibhāsinaḥ ca abādhya tvāt tathā hi buddhi ākārasya nirbhāsaḥ bādhā bāhyasya vastunaḥ sphūrtau api aviśvāse kva viśvāsaḥ iti kīrtitam etena bhāsamānaḥ vā ākāraḥ asan iti dvitīyaḥ api pakṣaḥ pratikṣiptaḥ pratibhāsāt eva sattā siddheḥ bādhaka avakāśa abhāvāt tathā san vā kaścid na khyāti iti tṛtīya saṅkalpaḥ api vyākulaḥ prakāśa vyāpta tvāt sattāyāḥ aprakāśasya asat tayā grasta tvāt 
RKNĀ_132.21	 nanu prakāśaḥ nāma vastunaḥ sattā sādhakam pramāṇam na ca pramāṇa nivṛttau artha abhāvaḥ artha kriyāśaktiḥ tu sattvam tat ca aprakāśasya api na virudhyate iti ced satyam etat bahis artha vāde aprakāśasya api sāmarthya abhyupagamāt keśoṇḍuka ādi pratibhāse adhyavasitasya artha kriyā śakti viyogāt eva abhāva siddheḥ sarvathā bahis abhāve tu jñānasya prakāśa avyabhicārāt tāvatā eva sattve kim artha kriyayā katham anya hṛdaḥ sattvam prakāśāt eva na asya ced na artha kriyā api sarvasmai kvacid ced bhāsanam na kim iti nirvikalpe tāvat sva saṃvedana siddha su a ākāram antareṇa vipakṣa ādayaḥ na parisphuranti atha amī vikalpe pratibhāsantaḥ iti dvitīyaḥ saṅkalpaḥ abhyupagamyate asmin api pakṣe pratibhāsamānaḥ ākāraḥ asādhāraṇaḥ aśabda saṃsṛṣṭa tayā sva saṃvedana tādātmye praviṣṭa tvāt vastu san eva 
RKNĀ_132.32	 adhyavseya tā vipakṣa ādayaḥ gṛhyante iti ced tadā api teṣām svarūpasya nirbhāsaḥ asti na vā nirbhāse pratyakṣa siddha tā eva na asat khyātiḥ śāstre api svarūpa sākṣātkāri tvam eva pratyakṣa tvam uktam tasya ca itara pratyakṣeṣu iva vikalpe api svīkāre viruddha vyāpta upalambhena vikalpa bhrānta tvayoḥ dūram apāsta tvāt vikalpe api tvad mate pratyakṣa tvam akṣatam tat katham tat siddhasya pratyakṣa antara anumānābhyām bādha abhidhānam tayoḥ api svarūpa antara prakāśa pauruṣa tvāt 
RKNĀ_133.5^1	 atha vikalpa bhrānta tvayoḥ vyāpaka viruddhayoḥ sambhavāt vikalpe pratyakṣa tvam eva asambhavi nanu asya pratyakṣa tvam asambhavi iti svarūpa sākṣātkāri tvam asambhavi iti uktam atha vipakṣa ādiḥ arthaḥ asmin prakāśate iti vācā svarūpa sākṣātkāri tvam kathitam iti mātā me bandhyā iti vṛttāntaḥ iṣyate ca tvayā vipakṣa ādi svarūpa sākṣātkāri tvam vikalpasya iti pratyakṣatā anatikramaḥ apratyakṣa tve vastu svarūpa sphuraṇa ayogāt tatas ca tad pratibhāsinaḥ api rūpasya sataḥ eva khyātiḥ na asat khyātiḥ 
RKNĀ_133.5^2	 na ca tat eva vikalpe parisphurat rūpam asatām īśvara ādīnām sva rūpam asattvasya eva abhāva prasaṅgāt sva rūpa sphuraṇe api asattve anyatra api prakāśinī anāśvāsāt tatas yat sa ākāra vāde jalpitam nitya ādayaḥ santaḥ eva syuḥ iti tad ātmanaḥ eva patitam yat āhuḥ guruvaḥ svarūpa sākṣātkaraṇāt adhyakṣa tvam na ca aparam vikalpa bhrama bhūmi tvam atas eva hi bādhitam yadi na adhyakṣatā tasya rūpa nirbhāsaḥ eva na tatas tad asat īśā ādi pratibhāti iti asaṅgatam yadi tu pratibhāseta rūpam asya sat eva tat tat asat pratibhāti iti tat ca bhāti asat eva vaḥ 
RKNĀ_133.22	 atha adhyavasāye adhyavaseya svarūpasya pratibhāsaḥ na asti iti ucyate na tadā kasyacid adhyavasāyaḥ katham atas pratiniyata vastu vyavasthā siddhiḥ kim ca kaḥ ayam adhyavasāyaḥ nāma kim vyāvṛtti bheda parikalpitasya prakāśa aṃśasya su a ākāra aṃśasya alīka ākārasya bāhya vastunaḥ avastunaḥ vā sphuraṇam adhyavasāya arthaḥ yadi vā su a ākāre bāhya āropaḥ bāhye vā su a ākāra āropaḥ su a ākāra bāhyayoḥ yojanāḥ tayoḥ ekīkaraṇam eka pratipattiḥ abhedena pratipattiḥ bheda āgrahaḥ adhyavasāya arthaḥ iti vikalpāḥ 
RKNĀ_133.28–133.30	 tatra na tāvat ādimau pakṣau kalpanām arthaḥ svarūpe sarvasya eva sphuraṇasya nirvikalpa tvāt avasāya anupapattiḥ itarathāḥ nirvikalpaka jñāna abhāva prasaṅgāt alīka sphuraṇam tu prāk pratyākhyātam sati api sphuraṇe asphuṭa tvāt nirvikalpakam etat dvi candra ādi jñāna vat astu sva grāhye tat nirvikalpakam bāhye tu adhyavaseye adhyavasāyaḥ iti ced na tad sambandha abhāvātaḥ tad apratibhāsāt ca anyathā ati prasaṅgāt iti ukta prāyam bāhya vastu svarūpa sphuraṇe tu pratyakṣa pratipattiḥ eva asau iti kaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ avastu sphuraṇam punar tridhā vikalpya prāk eva pratyākhyātam 
RKNĀ_134.4–134.8	 su a ākāre tu bāhya āropaḥ na sambhavati eva tathā hi jñānam kenacid ākāreṇa satyena alīkena vā upajātam nāma bāhya āropaḥ tu tad ākāre tad kṛtaḥ anya kṛtaḥ vā syāt tad kṛta tve na tāvat tad kāle eva vyāpāra antaram anubhūyate iti kutas tad ā āropaḥ kāla antare ca svayam eva asat kasya vyāpāraḥ syāt dvitīya pakṣe jñāna antaram api na ākārāra uparāga saṅginīm utpattim antareṇa vyāpāra antareṇa kvacid kiñcitkaram nāma tat etat arvācīna jñāna sadṛśa ākāra gocarīkaraṇe api na bāhya āropa vyāpāram aparam spṛśati tad ākāra leśa anukāram apahāya na ca śabdāmukhīkaraṇam atiriktaḥ vyāpāraḥ śabda ākārasya api svarūpaḥ eva antarbhāvāt iti na ākārāt anyaḥ jñāna vyāpāraḥ āropyamāṇaḥ ca asau arthaḥ bāhyaḥ tatra buddhau yadi svarūpeṇa sphurati satya pratītiḥ eva asau kaḥ āropaḥ atha na parisphurati tathā api kaḥ āropaḥ sphuraṇe vā adhikaraṇa bhūta sva ākāra atiriktasya āropyamāṇa ākārasya api pratibhāsa prasaṅgaḥ 
RKNĀ_134.16	 tad ākāra sphuraṇam eva tasya sphuraṇam iti ced na tasya āropa viṣaya tvāt na hi marīci sphuraṇam eva jala sphuraṇam iti na su a ākāre bāhya āropaḥ atas eva bāhye su a ākāra āropaḥ na asti āropaviṣayasya bāhyasya asphuraṇāt tatas eva su a ākāra bāhyayoḥ yojanā api asambhavinī yogyayoḥ apratibhāsāt na ca ekīkaraṇam adhyavasāyaḥ kaḥ ayam ekīkaraṇa arthaḥ yadi eka tāpatau prayojaka tvam tadāra upya āropaviṣayayoḥ kadācid ekībhāva abhāvāt asambhavaḥ eva na hi śaśa viṣāṇe kāraṇam kiñcid na ca pūrvam anekam eka tām eti iti kṣaṇika vādinaḥ sāṃpratam artha antara utpatti mātram tu syāt na ca tad upalabdhi gocaraḥ anyatra āropaviṣayāt su a ākārāt na ca tāvatā api arthasya kiñcid iti katham ekīkaraṇam 
RKNĀ_134.25–134.27	 atha eka pratītiḥ adhyavasāyaḥ tathā api na dvayoḥ eka pratipattiḥ adhyavaseya anubhava abhāvāt na ca dvayoḥ pratītiḥ iti eva adhyavasāyaḥ nīla pīta vat na ca abhedena pratītiḥ adhyavasāyaḥ yatas paryudāsa pakṣe aikya pratītiḥ uktā bhavati sā ca prayuktāḥ adhyavaseya pratyabhāvāt bhedena pratīti niṣedha mātre api na bāhyasya pratītiḥ uktā iti kutas tad adhyavasāyaḥ yadi hi bāhyam prakāśeta eka tvena aneka tvena vā satā asatā vā pratītiḥ iti yuktam 
RKNĀ_134.31–135.1	 sarva ākāra tad svarūpa tiraskāreṇa sā pratītiḥ iti eka pratītiḥ iti ced tad svarūpa tiraskāre tarhi tad apratibhāsanam eva kasyacid aṃśasya pratibhāsanāt iti ced na niraṃśa tvāt vastunaḥ sarva ātmanā pratibhāsaḥ apratibhāsaḥ vā iti śāstram eva atra vistareṇa parīkṣyate na ca bheda āgrahaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ vaktavyaḥ tathā hi kim bāhye gṛhyamāṇe agrahyamāṇe vā na ca prathamaḥ pakṣaḥ bāhya grahaṇasya pratikṣipta tvāt grahaṇe vā adhyavasāyasya pratyakṣatā prasaṅgāt agṛhyamāṇe tu bāhye pravṛtti niyamaḥ na syāt anyeṣām api tadānīm agrahaṇāt anyatra api pravṛtti prasaṅgāt 
RKNĀ_135.5	 trilocanaḥ api ittham adhyavasāyam dūṣayati kaḥ ayam adhyavasāyaḥ kim grahaṇam ahosvit karaṇam uta yojanā atha samāropaḥ tatra su ābhāsam anartham artham katham gṛhṇīyāt kuryāt vā vikalpaḥ na hi nīlam pītam śakyam grahītum kartum vā śilpa kuśalena api na api agṛhītena sva lakṣaṇena su a ākāram yojayitum arhati vikalpaḥ na ca sva lakṣaṇam vikalpa grahaṇa gocaraḥ na ca su a ākāram anartham artham āropayati na tāvat agṛhīta sva ākāraḥ śakyaḥ āropayitum iti tad grahaṇam eṣita vayam tatra kim gṛhītvā āropayati atha yadā eva su a ākāram gṛhṇati tadā eva āropayati na ādyaḥ na hi kṣaṇikam vikalpa vijñānam kramavantau grahaṇa samāropau kartum arhati uttarasmin tu kalpe avikalpa sva saṃvedana pratyakṣāt vikalpa ākārāt ahaṅkāra āspadād anahaṅkāra āspadam samāropyamāṇaḥ vikalpena sva gocaraḥ na śakyaḥ abhinnaḥ pratipattum na api bāhya sva lakṣaṇa eka tvena śakyaḥ pratipattum vikalpa ākāre sva lakṣaṇasya bāhyasya apratibhā āsanāt iti 
RKNĀ_135.16	 vācaspatiḥ api adhyavasāyam pratikṣipati anartham su a ābhāsam artham adhyavasyati iti nirvacanīyam etat nanu ayam āropayati iti kim vikalpasya svarūpa anubhavaḥ eva āropaḥ uta vyāpāra antaram svarūpa anubhavāt na tāvat pūrvaḥ kalpaḥ anubhava samāropayoḥ vikalpa avikalpa rūpa tayā drava kaṭhina vat tādātmya anupapatteḥ vyāpāra antara tve tu kramaḥ samāna kāla tā vā na tāvat kramaḥ kṣaṇikasya vijñānasya kramavat vyāpāra ayogāt akṣaṇika vādinām api buddhi karmaṇoḥ viramya vyāpāra anupapatteḥ na kramavat vyāpāra sambhavaḥ anubhava samāropau samāna kālau iti ced bhavatu samāna kāla tvam kevalam ātmā svabhāva sthitaḥ eva vedyaḥ para bhāvena vedane sva rūpa vedanā anupapatteḥ tathā ca ātmā jñānasya grāhya grāhaka ākāraḥ anubhūtaḥ arthaḥ ca samāropitaḥ na tu ātmā vedyamānaḥ samāropitaḥ na arthaḥ samāropyamāṇaḥ pratyakṣa vedyaḥ sa ca samāropaḥ sataḥ asataḥ vā grahaṇam eva na ca jñāna atiriktasya grahaṇam sambhavati iti upapāditam 
RKNĀ_135.27	 sva pratibhāsasya bāhyāt bheda agrahaḥ bāhya samāropaḥ tatas bāhye vṛttiḥ iti ced sa kim gṛhyamāṇe bāhye na vā na tāvat gṛhyamāṇe uktam hi etat na tad agrahaṇam sambhavati iti agṛhyamāṇe tu bheda agrahe na pravṛtti niyamaḥ syāt anyeṣām api tadānīm agrahāt anyatra api pravṛtti prasaṅgāt iti tasmāt yathā yathā ayam adhyavasāyaḥ cintyate tathā tathā viśīryate eva tathā vikalpa āropa abhimāna graha niścaya ādayaḥ api adhyavasāya vat su a ākāra paryavasitāḥ eva sphurantaḥ bāhyasya vārtā mātram api na jānanti iti adhyavasāya svabhāvāḥ eva śabda pravṛtti nimitta bhede api tat katham yukti āgama abahis bhūtaḥ anātma asphuraṇam ācakṣīta 
RKNĀ_136.3	 nanu evam vikalpa ādīnām asambhave api anātma prakāśaka tvā anabhyupagame sarva jana prasiddha vidhi pratiṣedha vyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgaḥ iti loka virodhaḥ vikalpaḥ iti adhyavasāyaḥ iti āropaḥ iti abhimānaḥ iti grahaḥ iti niścayaḥ iti ādikam śāstre pratipadam pratipāditam tad siddham ca bahis artha ādikam abhyupagatam iti ācārya virodhaḥ nyāya virodhaḥ ca tathā hi sarvaiḥ eva prakāśaiḥ aviparīta svarūpa saṃvedanāt bhrānteḥ atyantam abhāvaḥ syāt tatas ca sarva sattvāḥ sadā eva samyaksambuddhāḥ bhaveyuḥ 
RKNĀ_136.9	 vikalpikā buddhiḥ brāntiḥ sva pratibhāse anarthe artha adhyavasāyāt iti ced katham avasīyamānaḥ tayā saḥ arthaḥ na prakāśate prakāśamānaḥ vā katham asau tasyām na prakāśate atha prakāśataḥ eva tadā arthasya tādātmya prasaṅgaḥ asati ca arthe sā na syāt abhūt māndhātā bhaviṣyati śaṅkhaḥ asti ātmā nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti sarva ātmanā ca niścayaḥ syāt gauḥ iti spaṣṭena ca svena lakṣaṇena prakāśeta sva lakṣaṇe ca saṅketa ayogāt vikalpikā eva sā buddhiḥ na syāt tasmāt aśeṣa go vyakti sādhāraṇena go tvena go buddhiḥ alīkena sa abhilāpena viplavāt prakhyāti iti tathā prakāśanam asyāḥ gavārtha avasāyaḥ iti eṣṭavyam evam hi ete doṣāḥ na syuḥ apratibhāsamānasya api sva lakṣaṇasya bhrāntyā avasāyāt iti 
RKNĀ_136.18–136.23	 atra abhidhīyate na tāvat loka śāstra virodhau agṛhīte api bāhye pravṛtti nivṛtti ādi samarthanāt sva parava ādi duratikrama adhyavasāya svarūpa nirvacanāt nyāya virodhasya tu gandhaḥ api na asti tathā hi kā punar ayam bhrāntiḥ asat khyātiḥ atasmin tad grahaḥ vā yad abhāvāt idānīm eva muktiḥ āsajyate na tāvat ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ asat khyāteḥ pratyākhyānāt yat āhuḥ guru vaḥyasya svarūpa nirbhāsaḥ bādhakāt yadi tat na sat bādhake api kaḥ āśvāsaḥ svarūpa antara bhāsini anya svarūpa upanayāt tad svarūpa nivāraṇam tatra api saṃśayaḥ jātaḥ pūrva bādha upalabdhitaḥ iyam eva agrahe bādhā na ādya jasya aparā yadi asyāḥ pūrvā eva bhavatu rūpa nirbhāsanam samam na anyā ca bhāvinī iti atra pramāṇam kiñcid asti vaḥ api svarūpa nirbhāse yadā bādhaka sambhavaḥ anirbhāse svarūpasya hetu śodhana viplave bādha śaṅkā vinirbhāse api evam ced viplavaḥ mahān iti 
RKNĀ_137.3–137.6^1	 śāstre ca atasmin tad grahāt sva pratibhāse anarthe artha adhyavasāyāt dṛśya vikalpyayoḥ ekīkaraṇāt bhrāntiḥ uktāḥ tām ayam samarthayitum asamarthaḥ svātantryeṇa alīka sphuraṇam bhrāntiḥ iti kāvyam viracayya vistārayati nanu atasmin tad grahaḥ api bhramaḥ su a ākāra paryavasita jñānāt atiriktaḥ bahubhiḥ bahudhā vicārya pratyākhyātaḥ tat katham tasmin api pakṣe na bhrānti kṣatiḥ yena idānīm eva mukti prasaṅgaḥ na syāt iti ced tat etat bhagavataḥ bhāṣya kārasya mata vidveṣa viṣa vyākula vikrośitam atikātarayati kṛpā para vaśadhiyaḥ tathā hi samanantara pratyaya bala āyātasva pratibhāsa viśeṣa vedana mātrāt agṛhīte api paratra pravṛtti ākṣepaḥ adhyavasāyaḥ na ca asau pūrva ukta vāc jālaiḥ pratihantum śakyaḥ sarva prāṇabhṛtām pratyātma vidita tvāt kaiścid api anudbhinna tvāt ayam eva ca saṃsāraḥ tad kṣayaḥ mokṣaḥ iti kva idānīm eva tad vārtā api tathā hi vicitra an ādi vāsanā vaśāt prabodhaka pratyaya viśeṣa apekṣayā vikalpaḥ kenacid ākāreṇa upajāyamānaḥ eva bahirmukha pravṛtti anukūlam artha kriyā smaraṇa abhilāṣa ādi prabandham ādhatte 
RKNĀ_137.6^2	 tatas puruṣa artha kriyā arthinaḥ bahis artha anurūpāṇi pravṛtti nivṛtti avadhāraṇāni bhavanti pṛthagjana santāna jñāna kṣaṇānām tādṛśaḥ hetu phala bhāvasya niyata tvāt aniścita artha sambandha vikalpa kāle api sat asat tā nirṇaya ādi pravṛtti prasavaḥ tatra yat ubhayathā pravṛtti sādhana sāmarthyam asya sva hetu bala āyātam ayam eva pravṛtti viṣaya tva āropaḥ adhyavasāya apara nāmā yathā candra ādi jñānasya bhrāntasya abhrāntasya vā tad darśana avasāya jananam eva grahaṇa vyāpāraḥ sva vid api iyam artha vid eva kāryataḥ draṣṭavyā iti nyāyāt tathā vikalpasya api agniḥ atra ityādinā ākāreṇa utpadyamānasya pravṛtti ākṣepaka tvam eva bāhya avasānam nāma yathā ca nirvikalpa dvi candra ādi ākāra tā eva tathā avasāya sādhanī evam avasāyasya api tādṛśa ākāra tā eva viṣaya antara vimukha pravṛtti sādhanī 
RKNĀ_137.25	 nanu tathā ca tat ca tena pratipādyate na ca tad jñāne tat prakāśate iti śapathena api na saṃpratyayaḥ iti ced asambaddham etat na hi adhyavasāyāt bāhyasya paṭa ādeḥ vastunaḥ bādhaka avatārāt pūrva sandigdha vastu bhāvasya kṣaṇikā ādeḥ avastunaḥ vā śaśaviṣāṇa ādeḥ asphuraṇe api siddhi pratibandhaḥ brahmaṇā api pratividhātum śakyaḥ dvividhaḥ hi viṣaya vyavahāraḥ pratibhāsāt adhyavasāyāt ca tat iha pratibhāsa abhāve api para apoḍha sva lakṣaṇa ādeḥ adhyavasāya mātreṇa viṣaya tvam uktam sarvathā nirviṣaya tve pravṛtti nivṛtti ādi sakala vyavahāra uccheda prasaṅgāt tatas ca tena ca tat pratipādyate na ca jñāne tad prakāśaḥ iti saṅgatiḥ asti eva prakāśya prakāśaka bhāva abhāve api adhyavaseya adhyavasāyaka bhāvena api viṣaya viṣayi bhāva upapatteḥ 
RKNĀ_138.1	 nanu yadi na adhyavaseya pratītiḥ tadāgṛhīte api sva lakṣaṇa ādau pravṛttiḥ iti sarvatra aviśeṣeṇa prasajyeta sarvatra agṛhīta tvena viśeṣa abhāvāt tatas ca prāptiḥ api nābhimatasya niyamena iti anumānam api viplutam atra brūmaḥ yadi adhyavaseyam agṛhītam viśvam api agṛhītam tathā api niyata viṣayā eva pravṛttiḥ na sarvatra tathābhūta samanantara pratyaya bala āyāta niyata ākāra tayā niyata śakti tvāt vikalapasya niyata śaktayaḥ bhāvāḥ hi pramāṇa pariniṣṭhita svabhāvāḥ na śakti sāṅkarya paryanuyoga bhājaḥ asat utpatti vat sarvatra asattve api hi bījāt aṅkurasya eva utpattiḥ tatra eva tasya śakteḥ pramāṇena nirūpaṇāt tathā iha api hutavaha ākārasya vikalpasya dāha pāka ādi artha kriyā arthinaḥ tad smaraṇavataḥ hutavaha viṣayāyām eva pravṛttau sāmarthyam pramāṇa pratītam katham ati prasaṅga bhāgi pratyāsatti cintāyām ca tāttvikasya api vahneḥ jvalat bhāsvara ākāra tvam vikalpa ullikhitasya api iti tāvatā tatra eva pravartana śaktiḥ jvalana vikalpasya na jala ādau 
RKNĀ_138.12^1	 nanu ca sādṛśya āropeṇa kim su a ākārasya bāhye su a ākāre vā bāhyasya āropaḥ ubhayathā api asaṅgatiḥ āropya āra upaviṣayayoḥ su a ākāra bāhyayoḥ dvayoḥ grahaṇa asambhavāt iti ced na vayam āropeṇa pravṛttim brūmaḥ kim tarhi sva vāsanā paripāka vaśāt upajāyamānā eva sā buddhiḥ apaśyanti api bāhyam bāhye pravṛttim ātanoti iti viplutā eva saṃsāra ātmikā ca yat śāstram na jñāne tulyam utpattitaḥ dhiyaḥ tathāvidhāyāḥ iti tasmāt na rūpya ādi vat āropa dvāreṇa pravṛttiḥ api tu tathāvidha ākāra utpatti pratibaddha śakti niyamāt na ca vicārakasya vastu adarśana niścayāt apravṛttiḥ saṅgacchate
